
α.1.1 UKkutt8wongash Jeremiah wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, sephausuen ut Anathoth, ut wutohkit Benjamin.
E.1.1 The words of Jeremiah the son of Hilkiah, of the priests that were in Anathoth in the land of Benjamin:

α.1.2 Ukkutt8wonk Jehovah peyaónuk ut ukkesukodtumut Josiah wunnaumonuh Ammon Judae ketass8t nabo nishwe kodtumwae nanawunnuadt.
E.1.2 To whom the word of the LORD came in the days of Josiah the son of Amon king of Judah, in the thirteenth year of his reign.

α.1.3 Peyuam8 wonk ut ukkesukodtumut Jehoiakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t: nô pajeh wehqshik nabo nequtte kodtum8m Zedechiah wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, nô pajeh missinóhkonae monchanónat Jerusalem, ut napanna tahshe nepâuzsaut.
E.1.3 It came also in the days of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, unto the end of the eleventh year of Zedekiah the son of Josiah king of Judah, unto the carrying away of Jerusalem captive in the fifth month.

α.1.4 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaónukqun, n8wau,
E.1.4 Then the word of the LORD came unto me, saying,

α.1.5 Asq kahkenawahenoun ut menogkusseet, k8wahenup, kah asquam sohham8an wutch ôontomukqut, k8neetupanatamwáhenup, kah kukkehtimunup kukquoshodtumwaenúuneat en wutohtimoinnahtu.
E.1.5 Before I formed thee in the belly I knew thee; and before thou camest forth out of the womb I sanctified thee, and I ordained thee a prophet unto the nations.

α.1.6 Neit nussip, Woi Lord Jehovah nuttónteóh ket8hkon, newutche nen Peisses.
E.1.6 Then said I, Ah, Lord GOD! behold, I cannot speak: for I am a child.

α.1.7 Qut Jehovah nuttugqun, n8wóhkon, nen peisses, newutche piṣh kuttom wame uttoh ánan8mun, kah uttoh áne ann8nun, piṣh kussin.
E.1.7 But the LORD said unto me, Say not, I am a child: for thou shalt go to all that I shall send thee, and whatsoever I command thee thou shalt speak.

α.1.8 Wabesuontamúhkon wuskesuk8óash: newutche k8weetomsh, k[u]ppohquohwhununat, wussin Jehovah.
E.1.8 Be not afraid of their faces: for I am with thee to deliver thee, saith the LORD.

α.1.9 Neit Jehovah summagunum wunnutcheg, kah mussinnum nutt8n, kah Jehovah nuttugqun, kusseh nupponam nukkutt8wongash ut kutt8nut.
E.1.9 Then the LORD put forth his hand, and touched my mouth. And the LORD said unto me, Behold, I have put my words in thy mouth.

α.1.10 Naish, yeu kesukok kenanawunnumwahesh wutohtimóneash, kah ketass8tam8ongash, kodohchâbuhkohhamunat, kah soqunnumunat, kah pagwatauunat, kah kepuhkonat, weekuhkonat, kah ohteuhkonat.
E.1.10 See, I have this day set thee over the nations and over the kingdoms, to root out, and to pull down, and to destroy, and to throw down, to build, and to plant.

α.1.11 Nano, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaónuk, n8wau, Jeremiah te[a]gwas kenaum? kah nussip, nunnaum Almonuntugque souobpunk.
E.1.11 Moreover the word of the LORD came unto me, saying, Jeremiah, what seest thou? And I said, I see a rod of an almond tree.

α.1.12 Neit Jehovah nuttugkup, k8nenaum; newutche nukkenuppéhteo nukk8tonk ussenat.
E.1.12 Then said the LORD unto me, Thou hast well seen: for I will hasten my word to perform it.

α.1.13 Kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nahohtôeu nuppeyaonuk n8wau, teagwas kenaum? kah nussip, nunnau wussue ohkuk, kah wuskesuk nogwohteau nanummiyeu.
E.1.13 And the word of the LORD came unto me the second time, saying, What seest thou? And I said, I see a seething pot; and the face thereof is toward the north.

α.1.14 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, wutch nummiyeu mahcuk piṣh pohqusheau ut wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit.
E.1.14 Then the LORD said unto me, Out of the north an evil shall break forth upon all the inhabitants of the land.

α.1.15 Newutche kusseh, n8wehquetum wame nanumie tahs8tam8e teateashiyeuongash, wussin Lord, kah nag piṣh peyaog, kah nag piṣh nishnoh pasuk ponam wutappuonk ahhut petutteamuk ut Jerusaleme squontamut, kah ayeuuhkonitue wame pummenutonganit, nahut weenu, kah ayeuuhkonittue wame Judae keitotanash.
E.1.15 For, lo, I will call all the families of the kingdoms of the north, saith the LORD; and they shall come, and they shall set every one his throne at the entering of the gates of Jerusalem, and against all the walls thereof round about, and against all the cities of Judah.

α.1.16 Kah nukket8hkontam n8sittum8ongash, ayeuuhkonittue nagoh, pa[p]aume wame ummatchseonganooash neg ohquanumukqueaneg, kah chikohsumauwáog weetemungquok o[n]kotagig manitt8og, kah wowussittumwog nehenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuonganooash.
E.1.16 And I will utter my judgments against them touching all their wickedness, who have forsaken me, and have burned incense unto other gods, and worshipped the works of their own hands.

α.1.17 Newutche puttukquobpinoush kusseg, kah neepaush, kah nag us wame ne anan8nun: chepshúhko[n] ut wuskesuk8wóut, ishkont kuss8quttahwhush ut anaquabhettit.
E.1.17 Thou therefore gird up thy loins, and arise, and speak unto them all that I command thee: be not dismayed at their faces, lest I confound thee before them.

α.1.18 Newutche kusseh, yeu kesukok kutogqhesh pummeneutausue keitotanat, & brasse pummeneutongash ayeuuhkonittue mamusse ohke, ayeuuhkonittue Judae ketass8tamwog, ayeuuhkonittue wussontimóm8uh[,] ayeuuhkonittue wussephausueneum8uh, kah ayeuuhkonittúe ohkee missinninnúog.
E.1.18 For, behold, I have made thee this day a defenced city, and an iron pillar, and brasen walls against the whole land, against the kings of Judah, against the princes thereof, against the priests thereof, and against the people of the land.

α.1.19 Kah nag piṣh kutayeuhkonukquog, qut matta piṣh kussohkunkk8og: newutche k8wettomsh wussin Jehovah, kuppohquohwununat.
E.1.19 And they shall fight against thee; but they shall not prevail against thee; for I am with thee, saith the LORD, to deliver thee.

α.2.1 NAno wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
E.2.1 Moreover the word of the LORD came to me, saying,

α.2.2 Monchish, kah mishont8ash ut wehtauogkut Jerusalem, n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, kummehquanumouṣh, k8skenúe womoausuonk, k8weetauânumwae womoausuonk, asuhkiean ut touohkomukqut, ut mat ohteuhkausue ohkeit.
E.2.2 Go and cry in the ears of Jerusalem, saying, Thus saith the LORD; I remember thee, the kindness of thy youth, the love of thine espousals, when thou wentest after me in the wilderness, in a land that was not sown.

α.2.3 Israel wunneetupanatamweyeuop ut Lordut, kah ukk[a]keneumunne pénaeetuonk: wame neh mahchipwónukqutcheh piṣh matchenehéoog, machuk piṣh nukkuhkongquog wussin Jehovah.
E.2.3 Israel was holiness unto the LORD, and the firstfruits of his increase: all that devour him shall offend; evil shall come upon them, saith the LORD.

α.2.4 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi wek Jakob, kah wame teateashiyeuonga[s]h ut wekit Israel.
E.2.4 Hear ye the word of the LORD, O house of Jacob, and all the families of the house of Israel:

α.2.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah, teagwe matcheseonk k8sh8wóog nunnámteunk, waj nô8sukoihettit, kah asuhkomwog tahn8cheyeuuk, kah tahn8cheyeu8og?
E.2.5 Thus saith the LORD, What iniquity have your fathers found in me, that they are gone far from me, and have walked after vanity, and are become vain?

α.2.6 Kah matta n8wo8og, uttiyeu woh Jehovah noh kohkuhk8unukqueog wutch Egypte ohkeit? noh pannuppe sagkompagunogkup touohkomuk, papashpe touushinne kah pasohthegane ohkit, papashpe kunkohteadteáeu kah nupp8ongane onkauohtáe ohkeit, papashpe ohke, ne matta howan woh panupwushog, kah uttoh matta howan wadohkeg.
E.2.6 Neither said they, Where is the LORD that brought us up out of the land of Egypt, that led us through the wilderness, through a land of deserts and of pits, through a land of drought, and of the shadow of death, through a land that no man passed through, and where no man dwelt?

α.2.7 Kah kuppas8unumw8 ut misségene ohkeit, meechinat ne meechummúonk, kah ne noh adt wunnegit: qut petutteáog, kenishketeomwop nutohke, kah kutunkquontam8wáhtomw8 nutohtóonk.
E.2.7 And I brought you into a plentiful country, to eat the fruit thereof and the goodness thereof; but when ye entered, ye defiled my land, and made mine heritage an abomination.

α.2.8 Sephausuenuog matta n8wo8og, uttiyeuoh Jehovah? kah neg weoggehheoncheg naumatuonk, nag matta n8wahik8og: Pastorsog wonk nuppann[e]setunkquog, kah quoshodtumwaenuog, quoshodtumwog nashpe Baaloh; kah asuhkomwog niṣh matta wadchiéhettégish.
E.2.8 The priests said not, Where is the LORD? and they that handle the law knew me not: the pastors also transgressed against me, and the prophets prophesied by Baal, and walked after things that do not profit.

α.2.9 Newaj, ashpumme keket8kauunog, wussin Jehovah, kah keneechan8óog wunneechan8oh nukkeket8kauóog.
E.2.9 Wherefore I will yet plead with you, saith the LORD, and with your children's children will I plead.

α.2.10 Newutche paumhkash Chittimme munnuhhanaṣh, kah naish, kah ann8teamsh en Kedar, kah menuhke natwontaṣh, kah naiṣh ne nnák.
E.2.10 For pass over the isles of Chittim, and see; and send unto Kedar, and consider diligently, and see if there be such a thing.

α.2.11 Sun wutohtimóin ôsowunáog ummanitt8m8oh, qut onch neg matta manitt88og? qut nummissinninnúmog ôs8wunnumwog wussohsum8ongan8, ne matta nompe wutcheihetteg.
E.2.11 Hath a nation changed their gods, which are yet no gods? but my people have changed their glory for that which doth not profit.

α.2.12 Yeu chepshontam8k, woi kesukquog, kah mishu wabesek, kah mishe touussinok, wussin Jehovah.
E.2.12 Be astonished, O ye heavens, at this, and be horribly afraid, be ye very desolate, saith the LORD.

α.2.13 Newutche nummissinninnumog usseog neesinaṣh machukiṣh: nag nutohquanumukquog nen pâmachúane tohkekomue, kah nag wunnehthamóog wônogquash, poksháe woonogquaṣh ne matta woh ohtan8g nippe.
E.2.13 For my people have committed two evils; they have forsaken me the fountain of living waters, and hewed them out cisterns, broken cisterns, that can hold no water.

α.2.14 Sun Israel wuttinneumun? sun noh missináe neetu? tohwutch mukk8kinit?
E.2.14 Is Israel a servant? is he a homeborn slave? why is he spoiled?

α.2.15 Wuske qunnon8og mishont8wae mehnehte[a]og, kah mahchumwéhtôog ohke: ukkeitotanaṣh chikohtaaṣh, matta wutohkeina[t].
E.2.15 The young lions roared upon him, and yelled, and they made his land waste: his cities are burned without inhabitant.

α.2.16 Wunnaumonuh wonk Noph kah Tahapanes, nag pohquenumwog kuppuhkuk8e chetuhquab.
E.2.16 Also the children of Noph and Tahapanes have broken the crown of thy head.

α.2.17 Sunnummatta yeu kuppaudtauònas kuhhog, waj ohquánumadt kum-Manitt8m Jehovah, sagkompágunukquean en mayut?
E.2.17 Hast thou not procured this unto thyself, in that thou hast forsaken the LORD thy God, when he led thee by the way?

α.2.18 Kah yeuyeu toh|kutussen ut Egipte mayut, wuttattamunat wunnippeaṣh Sihor? asuh toh kutussen ut Assyriae mayut, wuttattamunat sepupogquaṣh?
E.2.18 And now what hast thou to do in the way of Egypt, to drink the waters of Sihor? or what hast thou to do in the way of Assyria, to drink the waters of the river?

α.2.19 Nehenwonche kummatcheseonk piṣh kussasamatuhhuk, kah kutt8nequssinn8wongaṣh piṣh kutáushk[ó]mukqunaṣh: newutche wahteaush, kah naish, ne matchit kah weesogkon kenukkenònat Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, kah n8wabesuonitteáonk matta ohtáno kuhhogkat, wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.2.19 Thine own wickedness shall correct thee, and thy backslidings shall reprove thee: know therefore and see that it is an evil thing and bitter, that thou hast forsaken the LORD thy God, and that my fear is not in thee, saith the Lord GOD of hosts.

α.2.20 Newutche nôadt nuppohquetahwhomp keyoakum, kah nuppaskukkomup keneepissuongaṣh, kah kussip, matta nuppannesu: nanwiyean kah nanwun8dsquaosean nishnoh kussohkôi, kah nishnoh ut ashkuhquamut.
E.2.20 For of old time I have broken thy yoke, and burst thy bands; and thou saidst, I will not transgress; when upon every high hill and under every green tree thou wanderest, playing the harlot.

α.2.21 Qut onch kutohtekônunup wunnégenne weenomwussippog, papannuppe wunnamuhkut[é]e wuskannem: uttoh kuttin neit quinnuppein nano matchékinne penoe weenomwussippog en nuhhogkat.
E.2.21 Yet I had planted thee a noble vine, wholly a right seed: how then art thou turned into the degenerate plant of a strange vine unto me?

α.2.22 Newutche uttohkônogque kukkitsumwin nashpe nitre, kah kumm8chekiyimunat sope, onch kummatcheseonk kuhkinneasin ut anaquabeh wussin Lord Jehovah.
E.2.22 For though thou wash thee with nitre, and take thee much soap, yet thine iniquity is marked before me, saith the Lord GOD.

α.2.23 Uttoh woh kuttin unn8won, matta nunnishkhetteoh, matta nutasuhkauoh Baalim? naish kummay ut 8noikoiyeuut, wahteaush uttoh aséan: ken kenupshae dromedary papaumwushadt ummayash.
E.2.23 How canst thou say, I am not polluted, I have not gone after Baalim?  see thy way in the valley, know what thou hast done: thou art a swift dromedary traversing her ways;

α.2.24 Touohkomukque asse, nukkodchu touohkomuk, assanómau wabanoh tapeneogish, tapeneog howan ukqushkinuh? wame neg natinneahwhoncheg, matta sauwunâou wuhhogkuh, ut wunnepâuzsómut piṣh wunnamheouh.
E.2.24 A wild ass used to the wilderness, that snuffeth up the wind at her pleasure; in her occasion who can turn her away? all they that seek her will not weary themselves; in her month they shall find her.

α.2.25 Nanawehteoush kusseet matta mokkussinnohhôsin8ut, kah kukquttunk wutch kuhkutt8nat: qut kussip, na matta annoósuonganinno, matchaog, newutche n8womon penuowhteaog, kah nag m8hche nutasuhkauóog.
E.2.25 Withhold thy foot from being unshod, and thy throat from thirst: but thou saidst, There is no hope: no; for I have loved strangers, and after them will I go.

α.2.26 Neane komm8towaen akodchik namehit: nene Israel wek akodchum8, nag ukketass8tam8m8uh, wussontimom8uh, kah wussephausueneum8uh, kah ukquoshodtumwaenúm8uh.
E.2.26 As the thief is ashamed when he is found, so is the house of Israel ashamed; they, their kings, their princes, and their priests, and their prophets.

α.2.27 Adtamwéhettit weehquanunk ken n8sh[ú]n: kah qussuk, keneechansup; newutche|n[a]g nukquinnuppinumunkquog uppusquan8, qut matta wuskes[u]k8: qut wuttaméhpunáhettit, piṣh n8waog, omohkish kah wadchâninnean.
E.2.27 Saying to a stock, Thou art my father; and to a stone, Thou hast brought me forth: for they have turned their back unto me, and not their face: but in the time of their trouble they will say, Arise, and save us.

α.2.28 Qut uttiyeug kummatt8mog neg kezheácheg? neg omohkehettich, woh neg wadchanukquean w[a]dtaméhpunáon: newutche na adtahshik kukkeitotanash, ne wuttinniinneau kummanitt8mog woi Judah.
E.2.28 But where are thy gods that thou hast made thee? let them arise, if they can save thee in the time of thy trouble: for according to the number of thy cities are thy gods, O Judah.

α.2.29 Tohwaj keket8kieóg? kenaau wame kuppanneséhtayimw8 wussin Jehovah.
E.2.29 Wherefore will ye plead with me? ye all have transgressed against me, saith the LORD.

α.2.30 Tahn8che nuttogkom keneech[â]n8oog, nag matta attumunum8og sasamatahwhuttuonk: nehenwonche kuttogkodtegan8 mahchipp8 kukquoshodtumwaéneumog, onauh pagwohteae qunnono[u].
E.2.30 In vain have I smitten your children; they received no correction: your own sword hath devoured your prophets, like a destroying lion.

α.2.31 Woi pometuonk, naish wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, sun nuttouohkomuk8imis ut Israel? pohkenâe ohke? tohwutch nummissinninnúmog n8wahettit, nenawun nussontimôumun, matta wonk kuppeyaónunómun?
E.2.31 O generation, see ye the word of the LORD. Have I been a wilderness unto Israel? a land of darkness? wherefore say my people, We are lords; we will come no more unto thee?

α.2.32 Sun woh peenomp wanánatam 8nhogk8unaṣh, asuh weetauwadteaénin wuthogqunnumaongaṣh? qut onch nummissinninnúmog n8wanánumuk ánu[ā]nittu kesukkodtaṣh.
E.2.32 Can a maid forget her ornaments, or a bride her attire? yet my people have forgotten me days without number.

α.2.33 Tohwutch m8sittahhaman kummay natinnehamunat womonittuonk? newaj wonk kuhk8tomauadt matchet8wog kummayaṣh.
E.2.33 Why trimmest thou thy way to seek love? therefore hast thou also taught the wicked ones thy ways.

α.2.34 Ut sissippoe kuthogk8wonganit wonk namehteauun wusqueheonk kuttummunge mat woskhúog: matta nummiskom8un keme natinteaon, qut ut wame yeush.
E.2.34 Also in thy skirts is found the blood of the souls of the poor innocents: I have not found it by secret search, but upon all these.

α.2.35 Onch kuttinn8wam, newutche matta n8woskhuwoh, wunnamuhkut ummusquanitteaonk piṣh qushkemo wutch nuhhogkat: kusseh, kukkeket8hkoush, newutche kussim, matta nummatchesu.
E.2.35 Yet thou sayest, Because I am innocent, surely his anger shall turn from me. Behold, I will plead with thee, because thou sayest, I have not sinned.

α.2.36 Tohwaj m8cheke papaumsháan kutôs8wunumunat kummayash? ken wonk piṣh kutakodchawahik Egypt, neane akojheup Assyria.
E.2.36 Why gaddest thou about so much to change thy way? thou also shalt be ashamed of Egypt, as thou wast ashamed of Assyria.

α.2.37 Nux, pish kussohwéhtau, kah kenutchegash ohtag kuppuhkukqut: newutche Jehovah pogketam kuppabahtantamóongaṣh, kah nish matta pish k8niéhikk8unáṣh.
E.2.37 Yea, thou shalt go forth from him, and thine hands upon thine head: for the LORD hath rejected thy confidences, and thou shalt not prosper in them.

α.3.1 NOOwaog, wosketomp pogkenont ummittamwussoh, kah noh nukkonont, kah mittamwussit onkatog, sun woh wonk noh en qushkeu: sunnummatta ohke woh mishe nishketeauun? qut ken kenanwun8dsquáus monaog womónadcheg: qut onch quinnuppish en nuhhogkat, wussin Lord.
E.3.1 They say, If a man put away his wife, and she go from him, and become another man's, shall he return unto her again? shall not that land be greatly polluted? but thou hast played the harlot with many lovers; yet return again to me, saith the LORD.

α.3.2 Tohshiniṣh kuskesukquash en qunuhqui ayeuonganehtu, kah naish uttoh kittin matta k8weepámutteanás: ut mayut kutaskwhonóog, onatuh Arabian ut touohkomukqut, kah kenishketeop ohke, nashpe kenanwun8dsquaôsuongaṣh, kah nashpe kummatcheseongaṣh.
E.3.2 Lift up thine eyes unto the high places, and see where thou hast not been lien with. In the ways hast thou sat for them, as the Arabian in the wilderness; and thou hast polluted the land with thy whoredoms and with thy wickedness.

α.3.3 Newaj sokanonaṣh kogkôunumuk, kah kutogque pehtùquom nanwu[n]8dsquoôsuenuut, kussekeneam akodchinat.
E.3.3 Therefore the showers have been withholden, and there hath been no latter rain; and thou hadst a whore's forehead, thou refusedst to be ashamed.

α.3.4 Sunnummatta yeu wutch kummauunnitteiyeu, n8sh, ken n8skenue nanawunnuaenéum?
E.3.4 Wilt thou not from this time cry unto me, My father, thou art the guide of my youth?

α.3.5 Sun piṣh nagwutteánum ummusquantamóonk, sun piṣh wunnagwutteánumun pajeh wohkukquoshik? kusseh, kussip kah kutussep machukish neahunukukqunnittean.
E.3.5 Will he reserve his anger for ever? will he keep it to the end?  Behold, thou hast spoken and done evil things as thou couldest.

α.3.6 Jehovah wonk nuttugkup, pamontog Josiah ketass8t, sun kenaum uttoh asit asóeposue Israel? noh kukkuhq[e]u en nishnoh kussohkôi wadchu, kah ut agwe nishnoh askunkquomut, kah na wuttit nanwun8dsquaôsin.
E.3.6 The LORD said also unto me in the days of Josiah the king, Hast thou seen that which backsliding Israel hath done? she is gone up upon every high mountain and under every green tree, and there hath played the harlot.

α.3.7 Kah nussip mahche yeush wame usseit, quinnuppish en nuhhogkat: qut noh matta qushkeu, kah wunass8muwae weetompassuin Judah wunnaumun.
E.3.7 And I said after she had done all these things, Turn thou unto me. But she returned not. And her treacherous sister Judah saw it.

α.3.8 Kah nunnaumunah, aquompak, wutche wame newaj omponcheposue Israel mamussit, nuppogkenóp, kah nuttinninnumauop pogkenittue wussukwhonk: qut onch wunass8muwae weetikkusquoh Judah, matta wabeseupoh, qut monchup, kah nanwun8dsquaausip wonk.
E.3.8 And I saw, when for all the causes whereby backsliding Israel committed adultery I had put her away, and given her a bill of divorce; yet her treacherous sister Judah feared not, but went and played the harlot also.

α.3.9 Kah niyeup, nashpe mataunchemoe, wunnanwun8dsquaosuonk, nishketeauop ohke, kah mamussup qussukquanash kah wehquanunkquamaṣh.
E.3.9 And it came to pass through the lightness of her whoredom, that she defiled the land, and committed adultery with stones and with stocks.

α.3.10 Qut onch wame yeush, wunass8muwáe weetompasu Judah, matta quinnuppu en nuhhogkat nashpe mamusse wuttah, qut eiantukiyeue, wussin Jehovah.
E.3.10 And yet for all this her treacherous sister Judah hath not turned unto me with her whole heart, but feignedly, saith the LORD.

α.3.11 Kah Jehovah nuttugkup, assôeposue Israel anue sampwe ogquanumau wuhhogkuh, onk wunass8muwáe Judah.
E.3.11 And the LORD said unto me, The backsliding Israel hath justified herself more than treacherous Judah.

α.3.12 Monchish kah yeush wahteauwahuaṣh kut8wongaṣh nogque nanumiyeu, kah n8wash, qushkiṣh ken asôepôsue Israel, n8wau Lord, matta ken8konkaúun8mw8 nummusquantam8onk: newutche nummómonaneteam, wussin Jehovah, matta nunnagwutteánum8 nummusquanittam8onk.
E.3.12 Go and proclaim these words toward the north, and say, Return, thou backsliding Israel, saith the LORD; and I will not cause mine anger to fall upon you: for I am merciful, saith the LORD, and I will not keep anger for ever.

α.3.13 Webe samp8ash kummatcheseonk, kuppanneséhtáu Jehovah kum-Manitt8m; kah kusseáhham kummayash en penuwohteaut, ut agwe nishnoh ashkuhquamut, kah matta ken8sweetam8mw8 n8wadtauatonkqussuon, n8wau Lord.
E.3.13 Only acknowledge thine iniquity, that thou hast transgressed against the LORD thy God, and hast scattered thy ways to the strangers under every green tree, and ye have not obeyed my voice, saith the LORD.

α.3.14 Qushkek, woi asôep8sue mukkiog, wussin Lord, newutche k8weetauómunumw8: kah keneemununumw8, pasuk en pasuk otanat, kah kenehneesinunnénaôont, kah pish kuppas8unumw8 Zion.
E.3.14 Turn, O backsliding children, saith the LORD; for I am married unto you: and I will take you one of a city, and two of a family, and I will bring you to Zion:

α.3.15 Kah kittinnumauunumw8 pastorsog neaunak nuttah, neg sohkom8nukqueog wahteauonk kah wohwohtam8onk.
E.3.15 And I will give you pastors according to mine heart, which shall feed you with knowledge and understanding.

α.3.16 Kah piṣh n$nih, muttaán8óg, kah nanom8naóg ut ohkeit: yeush ut kesukodtash n8wau Jehovah, nag matta piṣh wonk n8wo8og, 8n8wae wut-arkum Jehovah: matta piṣh waantam8un, matta pish mehquontam8un, matta pish nátauwohtau8un, asuh matta piṣh wonkusséin.
E.3.16 And it shall come to pass, when ye be multiplied and increased in the land, in those days, saith the LORD, they shall say no more, The ark of the covenant of the LORD: neither shall it come to mind: neither shall they remember it; neither shall they visit it; neither shall that be done any more.

α.3.17 Na ahquompak piṣh hettamwog Jerusalem, wutass8tamappuonk Lord, kah wame wutahtimoneaṣh en piṣh miyaém8aṣh, en 8wesuonganit Jehovah, en Jerusalem: kah matta piṣh wonk asuhkom8og uppehchuánumwe matche wuttahhou.
E.3.17 At that time they shall call Jerusalem the throne of the LORD; and all the nations shall be gathered unto it, to the name of the LORD, to Jerusalem: neither shall they walk any more after the imagination of their evil heart.

α.3.18 Yeush ut kesukodtash wek Judah, piṣh weechaáog wek Israel, kah nag piṣh mo[à]e peyaog wutch nánumohkit, en ohkit numauogkup k8sh8wóog wutche ohtóonk.
E.3.18 In those days the house of Judah shall walk with the house of Israel, and they shall come together out of the land of the north to the land that I have given for an inheritance unto your fathers.

α.3.19 Qut nussip, uttoh woh kuttin kenugke ponunu[n] mukkiésut, kah kittinninnumauunat wunne ohke, wunne wutohtoongan8 mataànukeg wutohtimoneash? kah nussip, piṣh kuttehenneh, n8sh, kah matta piṣh kenukkoss8h.
E.3.19 But I said, How shall I put thee among the children, and give thee a pleasant land, a goodly heritage of the hosts of nations? and I said, Thou shalt call me, My father; and shalt not turn away from me.

α.3.20 Wunnamuhkut, neane mittamwussin wunass8muwáe nukkonont wessukeh, netatuppe kuttin wunass8muwae unnehhinneau, woi wek Israel wussin Jehovah.
E.3.20 Surely as a wife treacherously departeth from her husband, so have ye dealt treacherously with me, O house of Israel, saith the LORD.

α.3.21 Wadtauatonkqussuonk n8tunkup ut qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, mauonk, kah uppeantam8ongash wunneechanoh Israel: newutche woónkitteauog ummayeu, k[a]h nag wannanumaog Lord um-Manitt8m8h.
E.3.21 A voice was heard upon the high places, weeping and supplications of the children of Israel: for they have perverted their way, and they have forgotten the LORD their God.

α.3.22 Qushkek kenaau asouhp8sue mukkiog, kah piṣh nunneetskehteoh kutasôep8suongan8oash: kusseh kuppeyaónunumun, newutche ken Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
E.3.22 Return, ye backsliding children, and I will heal your backslidings. Behold, we come unto thee; for thou art the LORD our God.

α.3.23 Wunnamuhkut tahn8che wadchanittuonk annoontamun wutch wadchuut, kah wutch mataánukish wadchuash, wunnamuhkut, ut Jehovah num$Manitt8mut wadchanaongan8 Israel ohteau.
E.3.23 Truly in vain is salvation hoped for from the hills, and from the multitude of mountains: truly in the LORD our God is the salvation of Israel.

α.3.24 Newutche akodchuonk mahcheteo wutanakausuongan8 n8shunônog, wutch n8skenúunneanónut: uffloksum8ash, kah wutheardsum8ash, wunnaumonauh kah wuttôn8uh.
E.3.24 For shame hath devoured the labour of our fathers from our youth; their flocks and their herds, their sons and their daughters.

α.3.25 Nussepsinumun nutogkojchuwonganunónut, kah nutchepshaonganun nunnuhkuhkonkumun: newutche nummatcheneheómun Jehovah num-Manitt8muh: nenawun kah n8shunonog, wutch n8skenúunneanónut pajeh yeu kesukok, kah matta n8sweetam8mun 8wadtautatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
E.3.25 We lie down in our shame, and our confusion covereth us: for we have sinned against the LORD our God, we and our fathers, from our youth even unto this day, and have not obeyed the voice of the LORD our God.

α.4.1 QUshkean, woi Israel, wussin Jehovah, qushkish en nuhhogkat, kah am[a]unuman kenishkeneunkquodt8mash wutch anaquabeh, neit matta piṣh kutontsappu.
E.4.1 If thou wilt return, O Israel, saith the LORD, return unto me: and if thou wilt put away thine abominations out of my sight, then shalt thou not remove.

α.4.2 Kah piṣh kutchadchekeyeuwam, Lord pomantog, ut wunnamuhkutéyeuuk, wut wussittum8onganit, kah ut sampweusseonganit, kah wutohtimóneash piṣh wunánumáog wuhhogkauh, ut wuhhogkat, kah ut wuhhogkat piṣh woweenauwaog.
E.4.2 And thou shalt swear, The LORD liveth, in truth, in judgment, and in righteousness; and the nations shall bless themselves in him, and in him shall they glory.

α.4.3 Newutche Jehovah yeu wuttinnon Judae, kah Jerusaleme wosketompuh, anaskham8k kenukkonohkomuk8, kah tanohketéhteók asinnekôusséhtu.
E.4.3 For thus saith the LORD to the men of Judah and Jerusalem, Break up your fallow ground, and sow not among thorns.

α.4.4 Quôshquss8k kuhhogkaóog en JEhovahut, kah amaunum8k woskechee wuttahh8wae kodtuhquabeyeu, kenaau Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, ishkont nummusquanitteaonk ogque sohham8m8 n8taut, kah chikohteau ne woh mat howan ontham8g, wutche kummatcheseongan8oash.
E.4.4 Circumcise yourselves to the LORD, and take away the foreskins of your heart, ye men of Judah and inhabitants of Jerusalem: lest my fury come forth like fire, and burn that none can quench it, because of the evil of your doings.

α.4.5 Wahteauwahuwak ut Judah, kah n8tamwáhuwak ut Jerusalem, kah n8wak, puhpéquagk ut ohkeit: mishont8wak, miyaegk, kah n8wak, moek, kah ontuh pummenutausue keitotanéhtu.
E.4.5 Declare ye in Judah, and publish in Jerusalem; and say, Blow ye the trumpet in the land: cry, gather together, and say, Assemble yourselves, and let us go into the defenced cities.

α.4.6 Neepattau8k muttauákinash nogque Zion, menehketeau8k, pitchinnoéhteok, newutche nuppaudto machuk wutch nanumiyeu, kah mishe paguanuonk.
E.4.6 Set up the standard toward Zion: retire, stay not: for I will bring evil from the north, and a great destruction.

α.4.7 Qunnonou kuhkuhqueu wutch ukkuppiyeumut; kah noh pagwanont gentilsoh appu mayut: sohham wutch wutayeuonganit, wttauwushitteauunat kutohke, kah kutotanáoash piṣh mahchim8ash, matta wutohkeinat.
E.4.7 The lion is come up from his thicket, and the destroyer of the Gentiles is on his way; he is gone forth from his place to make thy land desolate; and thy cities shall be laid waste, without an inhabitant.

α.4.8 Yeu wutche, puttukquobpussuontam8k man8tionak, mau8k, kah 8n8k, newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk Jehovah matta qushkemun8 wutch kuhhogkanónut.
E.4.8 For this gird you with sackcloth, lament and howl: for the fierce anger of the LORD is not turned back from us.

α.4.9 Kah piṣh nnih ne kesukok, wussin Jehovah, ketass8t wuttah piṣh nupp8m8, kah wuttahhou sontimoog kah sephausuenuog piṣh chepsheau, kah quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh monchanatamwog.
E.4.9 And it shall come to pass at that day, saith the LORD, that the heart of the king shall perish, and the heart of the princes; and the priests shall be astonished, and the prophets shall wonder.

α.4.10 Neit nussip, woi Lord Jehovah, wunnamuhkut, kummishe yeug as8kekomâog missinninnuog, kah Jerusalem, kussip, piṣh k8nohteamw8, qut togkodteg missigquonont keteahogkou
E.4.10 Then said I, Ah, Lord GOD! surely thou hast greatly deceived this people and Jerusalem, saying, Ye shall have peace; whereas the sword reacheth unto the soul.

α.4.11 Na ahquompak piṣh unnôog yeug missinninnúog, kah Jerusalem, ponkque wuttin wutch qunuhqui ayeuonganit, ut touohkomuk, en nogque wutton8óont nummissinninnúmog, matta páuunontusseneat, asuh pahketeàuunat.
E.4.11 At that time shall it be said to this people and to Jerusalem, A dry wind of the high places in the wilderness toward the daughter of my people, not to fan, nor to cleanse,

α.4.12 Pokkodche wuttin, wutch yeush ayeuongash, piṣh nuppeyaónuk: yeuyeu wonk nutayeuuhkonittue kut8kontamauóog wussittumoonk.
E.4.12 Even a full wind from those places shall come unto me: now also will I give sentence against them.

α.4.13 Kusseh, noh piṣh ogque kuhkuhqueu matohqshit, kah wutchariotsumash piṣh onatuhyeuash pemsquaut: wuthorsesumoh anue kenupshaog onk neg wompsikukquaog: missi nutonkapunnaongan8, newutche nummatchhetteamun.
E.4.13 Behold, he shall come up as clouds, and his chariots shall be as a whirlwind: his horses are swifter than eagles. Woe unto us! for we are spoiled.

α.4.14 Woi Jerusalem, kutchishittaush kuttah, wutch matchetowonganit, onk woh k8wadchanit: toh utt8che piṣh tahn8che kuttenantam8ongash kutappehtunk?
E.4.14 O Jerusalem, wash thine heart from wickedness, that thou mayest be saved. How long shall thy vain thoughts lodge within thee?

α.4.15 Newutche wadtauatonkqussuonk wahteauahuau wutch Dan, kah n8tamwahuwau onkapunáonk wutch Ephraimme wadchuut.
E.4.15 For a voice declareth from Dan, and publisheth affliction from mount Ephraim.

α.4.16 N8tamwáhuk wutohtimóneash, kusseh, ayeuuhkonittue wahteauwahuk Jerusalem, askuhwheteaenuog 8mwog nôadtit wutohtimoneat, kah ayeuuhkonittue mishont8waontamwog Judae keitotanash.
E.4.16 Make ye mention to the nations; behold, publish against Jerusalem, that watchers come from a far country, and give out their voice against the cities of Judah.

α.4.17 Onatuh nanwohkontogig ohteuk wutayeuuhkontamuneau waeénu: newutche ayeuuhkonittue nutcheketunk, wussin Jehovah
E.4.17 As keepers of a field, are they against her round about; because she hath been rebellious against me, saith the LORD.

α.4.18 Kummay kah kutusseongash, kuppautunkqunash yeush, yeu kummatcheetowonk newutche wesogkon, newutche mussishin kuttahhut.
E.4.18 Thy way and thy doings have procured these things unto thee; this is thy wickedness, because it is bitter, because it reacheth unto thine heart.

α.4.19 Nunnogkus, nunnogkus, nutonkquomom ut nuttahhut, nuttah mishont8wau ut nuttinnómiyeumut, n8nanum chequnappin, newutche ken8tamup, woi nukketeahogkou, ummishont8waonk monopuhpeg, ayeuteáont8waonk.
E.4.19 My bowels, my bowels! I am pained at my very heart; my heart maketh a noise in me; I cannot hold my peace, because thou hast heard, O my soul, the sound of the trumpet, the alarm of war.

α.4.20 Paguanuonk asuhkaue pagwanuonganit mishont8wóm8, newutche mamusse ohke matchehteauun: kenuppe neekash matchehteauunash, kah nutonkwonganog kenuppe.
E.4.20 Destruction upon destruction is cried; for the whole land is spoiled: suddenly are my tents spoiled, and my curtains in a moment.

α.4.21 Toh utt8che woh nunnaumun muttaag, kah n8tamunat monopuhpékque mishont8waonk?
E.4.21 How long shall I see the standard, and hear the sound of the trumpet?

α.4.22 Newutche numissinninnúmog mattammag88og, matta n8wahik8og, nag as8tue mukkiog, kah matta wohwohtam8og: waantamwog matchesenat, qut wunnesenat matta wahteau8og.
E.4.22 For my people is foolish, they have not known me; they are sottish children, and they have none understanding: they are wise to do evil, but to do good they have no knowledge.

α.4.23 Nukkehkeneamup ohke kah kusseh, matta kuhkénauwéhteósin8, kah monteagwuninno: & kesukquosh, & mat wequaiyeuméog.
E.4.23 I beheld the earth, and, lo, it was without form, and void; and the heavens, and they had no light.

α.4.24 Nukkehkinneamup wadchuash, & kusseh, nag nunnukshaog, kah wame wadchuash keme ontohtaash.
E.4.24 I beheld the mountains, and, lo, they trembled, and all the hills moved lightly.

α.4.25 Nummomunneamup kah kusseh na matta wosketompaun8, kah wame kesukque puppinshasog wussem8og.
E.4.25 I beheld, and, lo, there was no man, and all the birds of the heavens were fled.

α.4.26 Nummonunneamup, kah kusseh, mishummeechume ayeuonk touohkomukqueyeu8, kah wame nish keitotanaṣh pohquetahhamunaṣh ut anquabit Jehovah, kah nashpe ummishe musquantamôonk.
E.4.26 I beheld, and, lo, the fruitful place was a wilderness, and all the cities thereof were broken down at the presence of the LORD, and by his fierce anger.

α.4.27 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, mamusse ohke piṣh touwushin, qut onch matta n8wame mohtupanôog.
E.4.27 For thus hath the LORD said, The whole land shall be desolate; yet will I not make a full end.

α.4.28 Yeu 8ch pish ohke mauun, kah kesukquash wohqut pish m8iyeuaṣh: newutche nussin, nuppogkodtantamun, & matta nutaiuskoianatam8, & matta nukqushkinnum8un.
E.4.28 For this shall the earth mourn, and the heavens above be black; because I have spoken it, I have purposed it, and will not repent, neither will I turn back from it.

α.4.29 Mamusse keitotan piṣh wusseem8 wutche ummishont8waongan8 horsesoh na8mukqutcheg kah wadohtompéitcheg, nag piṣh petutteaog kuppáhtu, kah piṣh tohk8tauaog kussampskôiyeuut: nishnoh keitotan piṣh ahquontamun, kah matta wosketomp wutaiyéin.
E.4.29 The whole city shall flee for the noise of the horsemen and bowmen; they shall go into thickets, and climb up upon the rocks: every city shall be forsaken, and not a man dwell therein.

α.4.30 Kah matchéhenumuk, toh piṣh kutussen? tokonogque kuthogqunneat waneemsquag, tohkonogque gold k8n8whósuohtineat, tohkonogque kenenekinum8e wussukhumunat kuskesuk, tahn8che piṣh k8nekuhhog, womonukqueanig piṣh kussekanunkquog, piṣh kukkodtinneánukquog.
E.4.30 And when thou art spoiled, what wilt thou do? Though thou clothest thyself with crimson, though thou deckest thee with ornaments of gold, though thou rentest thy face with painting, in vain shalt thou make thyself fair; thy lovers will despise thee, they will seek thy life.

α.4.31 Newutche nutogquesittamup wuttauatonkqussuonk mittamwossis kodtauwekheont, kah ogque wutonkquommom8onk noh weske neechadt, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk wuttaunoh Zion, noh mawémont wuhhogkuh, noh sepaginuk wunnutchegash, n8wau, missi nutonkapunnáonk yeuyeu, newutche nukketeahogkou sauwunum wutche nushehteaenúog.
E.4.31 For I have heard a voice as of a woman in travail, and the anguish as of her that bringeth forth her first child, the voice of the daughter of Zion, that bewaileth herself, that spreadeth her hands, saying, Woe is me now! for my soul is wearied because of murderers.

α.5.1 AH[a]úhsukque u[s]ishunk ut pannuppe Jerusaleme toumáogquehtu, kah yeuyeu naum8k kah wahteau8k, kah nuttinneohteagk na$ut mishe ayeuonganehtu: woh naméheadt wosketomp, noh asein wussittum[ò]onk, kah piṣh nutahquontamwòntamun
E.5.1 Run ye to and fro through the streets of Jerusalem, and see now, and know, and seek in the broad places thereof, if ye can find a man, if there be any that executeth judgment, that seeketh the truth; and I will pardon it.

α.5.2 Kah tohkônogque wussinneau, Lord pomantog, wunnamuhkut pann8wae chadchekeyeuwaog.
E.5.2 And though they say, The LORD liveth; surely they swear falsely.

α.5.3 Woi Jehovah, sunnummatta kuskesukquash ohtano wunnamuhkuteyeuuk? nag kuttogkomóog, qut nag neuantam8og, nag kummahtupanòog, qut sekeneamwog attumunumun sasamatawhuttuonk, nag anue menehketeoog wuskesuk8oaṣh onk ne qussuk, sekenamwog qushke[u].
E.5.3 O LORD, are not thine eyes upon the truth? thou hast stricken them, but they have not grieved; thou hast consumed them, but they have refused to receive correction: they have made their faces harder than a rock; they have refused to return.

α.5.4 Newaj n8wau, wunnamuhkut yeug matchekuog, as8tuog, newutche mat wahteau8og umm[a]y Jehovah; asuh 8sittum8onk um-Manitt8m8oh.
E.5.4 Therefore I said, Surely these are poor; they are foolish: for they know not the way of the LORD, nor the judgment of their God.

α.5.5 Nutauon masugkenukeg, kah nag nukken8naog, newutche neg wahteauog ummay Jehovah, kah 8sittum8onk um-Manitt8m8uh: qut yeug papannuppe pokqshanáog yoakoh, kah paskúhkomwog kenepsuongash.
E.5.5 I will get me unto the great men, and will speak unto them; for they have known the way of the LORD, and the judgment of their God: but these have altogether broken the yoke, and burst the bonds.

α.5.6 Newaj piṣh qunnonou wutch touohkomukqut pagwanon, kah wunnonkquae mukquoshim piṣh ummatchhheuh; Leopard piṣh askuhhum ukkeitotanáoaṣh: nishnoh pasuk na waj sohhog piṣh sokshanau, newutche uppanneseonganoaṣh monaaṣh, kah wutasôep8suongan88aṣh nano m8naaṣh.
E.5.6 Wherefore a lion out of the forest shall slay them, and a wolf of the evenings shall spoil them, a leopard shall watch over their cities: every one that goeth out thence shall be torn in pieces: because their transgressions are many, and their backslidings are increased.

α.5.7 Uttoh woh kuttin yeu ahquontamauunun: kummukkiésumwog nutohquanumunk, & chadchekeimáog neh mat manitt8enégeh: nag wamepwuhheog, neit mamussuog, & miaweog ut nanwun8dsquasenuog wek8ôut
E.5.7 How shall I pardon thee for this? thy children have forsaken me, and sworn by them that are no gods: when I had fed them to the full, they then committed adultery, and assembled themselves by troops in the harlots' houses.

α.5.8 Nag tatuppeyeu8og sohkom8nae horsesut nompoáeu, nishnoh pasuk kogkeahchewánumau ummittamwussoh weetatteamungoh.
E.5.8 They were as fed horses in the morning: every one neighed after his neighbour's wife.

α.5.9 Sunnummatta yeush pish nunnátauwohtauòunaṣh, wussin Jehovah, kah sunnummatta piṣh kukketeahogkou ann8tauòntam8 yeu ânak wutohtimoin?
E.5.9 Shall I not visit for these things? saith the LORD: and shall not my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?

α.5.10 Kuhkuhquegk uppummeneutonganit, kah pagwohteagk, qut ahque wámeneán8k, amaunumau wutonkk8asuongaṣh, newutche nish matta wuttaiheaṣh Jehovah.
E.5.10 Go ye up upon her walls, and destroy; but make not a full end: take away her battlements; for they are not the LORD's.

α.5.11 Newutch wek Israel, kah wek Judah, ayeuuhkonittue ahche n8nass8mukquog wussin Jehovah.
E.5.11 For the house of Israel and the house of Judah have dealt very treacherously against me, saith the LORD.

α.5.12 Pann8waheáog Jehovah, kah n8waog, noh matta, kah machuk matta piṣh nunnuhkukkongk8mun, kah matta piṣh naum8mun togkodteg kah muhshagquodt.
E.5.12 They have belied the LORD, and said, It is not he; neither shall evil come upon us; neither shall we see sword nor famine:

α.5.13 Kah quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh wabanu8og, kah wuttinn8waonk matta appehtunk8og: yeu piṣh unneheóneau.
E.5.13 And the prophets shall become wind, and the word is not in them: thus shall it be done unto them.

α.5.14 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord God ayeuuhteanit, newutche yeu kutt8onk kussinneau, kusseh nuttinn8waongaṣh nunn8taúhteam ut kutt8nut, kah yeug missinninnuog wuttuhqunnú8og, kah piṣh ummahchipwunneuh.
E.5.14 Wherefore thus saith the LORD God of hosts, Because ye speak this word, behold, I will make my words in thy mouth fire, and this people wood, and it shall devour them.

α.5.15 Kusseh, kuppaudtauunumw8 wutohtim[ó]in wutch nôadtit, woi wek Israel, wussin Lord: ne menuhki wutohtimóin, ne kehchiyeue wutohtimóin, neg ukkutt8wongan8 mo wahteau8un, kah matta k8wohtam8 uttoh an8wahettit.
E.5.15 Lo, I will bring a nation upon you from far, O house of Israel, saith the LORD: it is a mighty nation, it is an ancient nation, a nation whose language thou knowest not, neither understandest what they say.

α.5.16 Uppetan[o]nou ne pohquohshine wenohke, nag wame menuhkesuenúog.
E.5.16 Their quiver is as an open sepulchre, they are all mighty men.

α.5.17 Kah nag pish meechwog kukkepenum8onk, kah kuppetukqunnunk, ne woh kenaumonog kah kuttaunog meechhetteup: pish m8whóog kuf-flocksumoh, kah kut-herdsumoh: nag piṣh mahchipp8og k8weenomwussippogquash, kah figsuhtugquash: nag piṣh matcheketeauog pummeneutausue kukkeitotanaṣh, uttoh adt pabahtantaman, nashpe togkodteg.
E.5.17 And they shall eat up thine harvest, and thy bread, which thy sons and thy daughters should eat: they shall eat up thy flocks and thine herds: they shall eat up thy vines and thy fig trees: they shall impoverish thy fenced cities, wherein thou trustedst, with the sword.

α.5.18 Qut onch ut yeush kesukkodt[a]ṣh wussin Lord, matta kutóshkoméh[e]n8mw8.
E.5.18 Nevertheless in those days, saith the LORD, I will not make a full end with you.

α.5.19 Kah pish n$nih, piṣh n8waog, tohwutch yeush wame unnéhenog Lord num-Manitt8mun? neit pish nag kenamp8hamauóog; neane ohquanumeógkup, kah k8wowussumómw8 pen8e mánitt8og ut kutohk8wóut, ne kuttattuppe piṣh wuttinneumuhkauóneau pen8wohteaog, ut ohkeit ne matta wadtiheéóg.
E.5.19 And it shall come to pass, when ye shall say, Wherefore doeth the LORD our God all these things unto us? then shalt thou answer them, Like as ye have forsaken me, and served strange gods in your land, so shall ye serve strangers in a land that is not your's.

α.5.20 Yeu wahteauwáhuwagk ut wekit Jakob, kah n8tamwahuagk ut Judah, n8wagk,
E.5.20 Declare this in the house of Jacob, and publish it in Judah, saying,

α.5.21 Yeu n8tam8k yeuyeu, woi mattammag8weógish missinninnuog, kah matta wohwohtam8gig, neg wuskesukqutcheg qut matta naum8og, neg wohtauogkutcheg, kah matta n8tamóog.
E.5.21 Hear now this, O foolish people, and without understanding; which have eyes, and see not; which have ears, and hear not:

α.5.22 Sun matta k8wabesúonumw8 wussin Jehovah? sun matta kenunukushomw8 ut anaquabeh, noh wanohtunk nagunt wutche kuhkuhheg ut ketahhannit, nashpe michemohtae kuhk8waonk, matta woh anùwushómun8, kah tôhkonogque wuttugk8moh 8wahwáabpénin, qut onch matta sohkom8uneau, tôhkonogque mishont8wóneau, qut onch matta wutaneukom8uneau?
E.5.22 Fear ye not me? saith the LORD: will ye not tremble at my presence, which have placed the sand for the bound of the sea by a perpetual decree, that it cannot pass it: and though the waves thereof toss themselves, yet can they not prevail; though they roar, yet can they not pass over it?

α.5.23 Qut yeug missinninnuog ontsogquéhtamwutteaháog, kah cheketamwutteahaog: ontsogquehtamwog kah moncheog.
E.5.23 But this people hath a revolting and a rebellious heart; they are revolted and gone.

α.5.24 Kah matta n8wawog ut wuttahh8wout, yeuyeu qushontuh Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, noh sokenonteadt, negonáe kah maumachish ut wutaquompiyeumut: kenanawehteunkqun kuhquttum8e kepenum8e weekaṣh.
E.5.24 Neither say they in their heart, Let us now fear the LORD our God, that giveth rain, both the former and the latter, in his season: he reserveth unto us the appointed weeks of the harvest.

α.5.25 Kummatcheseonganooaṣh yeuṣh wutamaunumunáoaṣh, kah kummatcheseonganooaṣh kukkushpâdtamunk8 wanegukish.
E.5.25 Your iniquities have turned away these things, and your sins have withholden good things from you.

α.5.26 Newutche ut kenugke nummissinninnumog, matchetoweenuog wáhsháog: nag unnaskwheteaog noh wânashont ahpehanoh[,] ponaog ápehanoh, puttawhôog wosketompuh.
E.5.26 For among my people are found wicked men: they lay wait, as he that setteth snares; they set a trap, they catch men.

α.5.27 Onatuh wadshiùhquneg numwabhettit psuksesog, ne ne numwohteau wekuwoont as8kekodteam8onk, ne waje nag mussugkenhettit, kah weenauweetuog.
E.5.27 As a cage is full of birds, so are their houses full of deceit: therefore they are become great, and waxen rich.

α.5.28 Nag nano wunogk8og, wunampamukqussuog, nux paumuhkomwog wutusseongan8oash matchet8wog, matta wussittumoog pissaumatuonk, uppissaumatuonk touies, qut onch wunayeuog: kah wussampiyeum qunauwahikquit matta 8sittum8uneau.
E.5.28 They are waxen fat, they shine: yea, they overpass the deeds of the wicked: they judge not the cause, the cause of the fatherless, yet they prosper; and the right of the needy do they not judge.

α.5.29 Sun matta woh yeush n8ch nátauwahuwaunash wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta woh nukketeahogkou ann8tantam8 yeu ának wutohtimóin?
E.5.29 Shall I not visit for these things? saith the LORD: shall not my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?

α.5.30 Monchanatamwéyeu8k kah úhquejishánumukquok ne ussen yeu ut ohkeit.
E.5.30 A wonderful and horrible thing is committed in the land;

α.5.31 Quoshodtumwaenuog pann8wae quoshodtumwog, kah sephausuenuog nánawunnuwáog nag nashpe, kah missinninnùog womontamuneau ne n$niyeuut: kah toh woh kutussemw8 ut wohkukquoshik.
E.5.31 The prophets prophesy falsely, and the priests bear rule by their means; and my people love to have it so: and what will ye do in the end thereof?

α.6.1 WOi kenaau wunneechanoh Benjamin, moek k8seemunneaut wuch nashaue Jerusalem, kah puhpequohto8k monopuhpeg ut Tekoa: kah ponam8k kuhkinneasue n8teau ut Beth-haccerem, newutche machuk nogquodt wutch nanummiyeu kah mishe paguanuonk.
E.6.1 O ye children of Benjamin, gather yourselves to flee out of the midst of Jerusalem, and blow the trumpet in Tekoa, and set up a sign of fire in Bethhaccerem: for evil appeareth out of the north, and great destruction.

α.6.2 Nutogquéheop wutta[u]noh Zion tapeneunkqussit kah wanegit mittumwossis.
E.6.2 I have likened the daughter of Zion to a comely and delicate woman.

α.6.3 Nanaushepsaenùh weeche uf$flocksumóuh pish uppeyonóuh: pish nag ayeuuhkonittue 8wéenikomukquonóuh: nag pish nishnoh pasuk tanadtupp8og ut wutayeuonganit.
E.6.3 The shepherds with their flocks shall come unto her; they shall pitch their tents against her round about; they shall feed every one in his place.

α.6.4 Ayeuuhkonittue quagwoshwunum[ó]k matómpog: omohkek, kah kuhkuhquehtuh puhshaquadt: missi nutonkapunnaonganun, newutche kesukod paumushóm8, newutche wunnonkquae onkauóhteau sepagkém8.
E.6.4 Prepare ye war against her; arise, and let us go up at noon. Woe unto us! for the day goeth away, for the shadows of the evening are stretched out.

α.6.5 Omohkek, neepoushádtuh, kah pagwatauuttuh ummishikkomukquash.
E.6.5 Arise, and let us go by night, and let us destroy her palaces.

α.6.6 Newutche yeu wussinah Lord ayeuteanit, kouéhtham8k mehtugquash, kah ayeuuhkonittue pogkétinómukquae wadchukok Jerusalem, yeu keitotan woh nadtauahtómuk: noh mamusse sunukkuhchahh8waonk wunnashomut ohteau.
E.6.6 For thus hath the LORD of hosts said, Hew ye down trees, and cast a mount against Jerusalem: this is the city to be visited; she is wholly oppression in the midst of her.

α.6.7 Neane tohkekom sohham8teunk wunnippem, neweyane sohwhôkon ummatcheseonk, chekeusseonk kah mukk8kinnuwáonk nish n8tamunaṣh ut wuhhogkat: neuantamóonk kah n8chumwuttahwhuttuongaṣh nagwutteohtaaṣh anaquabeh.
E.6.7 As a fountain casteth out her waters, so she casteth out her wickedness: violence and spoil is heard in her; before me continually is grief and wounds.

α.6.8 Kuhk8tomaúununach, woi Jerusalem, ishkont nukketeahogkou kenukkonuk, ishkont kuttauwushinnewahesh, ohke ne matta wadohkeémuk.
E.6.8 Be thou instructed, O Jerusalem, lest my soul depart from thee; lest I make thee desolate, a land not inhabited.

α.6.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuuhteaunit, nag piṣh pannuppe mukkupushquaog Israelle sekqshoncheg, onatuh weenomwussippog: ogque ompontinuṣh kenutcheg en man8taut noh máwuneadt weenominneaṣh.
E.6.9 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, They shall throughly glean the remnant of Israel as a vine: turn back thine hand as a grapegatherer into the baskets.

α.6.10 Howan woh k6on8nog, kah âmómog, onk woh n8tamwog? kusseh, wehtauogk8 matta quoshqussausin8, kah n8nanumóog kuhkeitamun: kusseh, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah ogquontamwog ashpunâmut: matta wuttapeneam8uneau.
E.6.10 To whom shall I speak, and give warning, that they may hear? behold, their ear is uncircumcised, and they cannot hearken: behold, the word of the LORD is unto them a reproach; they have no delight in it.

α.6.11 Newaj numwabetunkqueh ummusquantam8onk Jehovah: nussauunum kogkôunumunát: nussokanumauóneau mukkiog poquadchit, kah ummoeu mukkinneongan8out wuskenuog, newutche wessukkiin weeche mittamwussoh piṣh neemunau, kutchise weeche noh mahtauntog.
E.6.11 Therefore I am full of the fury of the LORD; I am weary with holding in: I will pour it out upon the children abroad, and upon the assembly of young men together: for even the husband with the wife shall be taken, the aged with him that is full of days.

α.6.12 Kah wekuóash pish quinnuppem8ash en onkatoganit, kah weeche wutohtekonoash kah ummittamwuss8oh moeu: newutche nussummagunum nunnutcheg ut wadohkitcheg ohkeit wussin Jehovah.
E.6.12 And their houses shall be turned unto others, with their fields and wives together: for I will stretch out my hand upon the inhabitants of the land, saith the LORD.

α.6.13 Newutche wutch peississit pajeh noh masugkenuk, nishnoh pasuk n8suhkom hohchewontamóonk: kah wutch quoshodtumwaenúut, pajeh sephausuenúut, nishnoh pasuk pann8wae ussu.
E.6.13 For from the least of them even unto the greatest of them every one is given to covetousness; and from the prophet even unto the priest every one dealeth falsely.

α.6.14 Meeshane neetskehteóog wonk woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8uh nummissinninnúmog, n8waog, Wunohteagk, wunohteagk, matta wunohteaonganin8g.
E.6.14 They have healed also the hurt of the daughter of my people slightly, saying, Peace, peace; when there is no peace.

α.6.15 Sun nag akodchuog ussehettit unkqueneunkquok? matchaog, matta akodchuog, kah onteauog pen8quoshun, newaj pish penusháhettit kenugke nag panushoncheg, uttoh adt natauwáheog, pish kepshaog wussin Jehovah.
E.6.15 Were they ashamed when they had committed abomination? nay, they were not at all ashamed, neither could they blush: therefore they shall fall among them that fall: at the time that I visit them they shall be cast down, saith the LORD.

α.6.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neepo8k maikontu, káh naum8k kah nat8tomwehteag kah nukkone mayash, uttiyeu wunneguk may, kah ne pomushagk, kah pish kenampteomw8 keteahogkoune anwosin8onk: qut nag n8waog matta ne nuppomushaunan.
E.6.16 Thus saith the LORD, Stand ye in the ways, and see, and ask for the old paths, where is the good way, and walk therein, and ye shall find rest for your souls. But they said, We will not walk therein.

α.6.17 Kah wonk nupponaskqhukqueogig, n8wahettit, kuhkeitam8k monopehpegane wadtauatonqussuonk: qut nag n8waog matta nukkeiketam8unan.
E.6.17 Also I set watchmen over you, saying, Hearken to the sound of the trumpet. But they said, We will not hearken.

α.6.18 Newutche n8tam8k kenaau wutohtimoneash kah wahteau8k woi mukkineonk, uttoh ánag ut kenugke nagoh.
E.6.18 Therefore hear, ye nations, and know, O congregation, what is among them.

α.6.19 N8tash woi ohke, kusseh nuppaudtoh machuk yeu ut ayeuonganit, wuttenantamog meechummuongash, newutche matta kuhkeitam8og nukkutt8wongash, asuh nuttinnaumatuonk, qut uppogketamuneau.
E.6.19 Hear, O earth: behold, I will bring evil upon this people, even the fruit of their thoughts, because they have not hearkened unto my words, nor to my law, but rejected it.

α.6.20 Teag wutch weetemungquok peyogque wutch Sheba? kah weekemungquoke weekinaskq, wutch n8adtut wutohtimoneat kutchikohtae mag8onganoash matta tapeneunkquottinn8ash, kah kussephausuongan8oash matta weetemungquottin8ash ut nuhhogkat.
E.6.20 To what purpose cometh there to me incense from Sheba, and the sweet cane from a far country? your burnt offerings are not acceptable, nor your sacrifices sweet unto me.

α.6.21 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah, kusseh, nupponam togkussittassunoonk ut anaquabhettit yeug missinninnuog, kah wut8shineunk kah wunnaumoninneunk pish moae uppenushadtamuneau: weetatteamunganin kah weetompoh pish paguanog.
E.6.21 Therefore thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will lay stumblingblocks before this people, and the fathers and the sons together shall fall upon them; the neighbour and his friend shall perish.

α.6.22 Yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh missinninnuog 8mwog nanumohkit, kah missi wutohtimoin pish tahshinumun sussippoe ohkeit.
E.6.22 Thus saith the LORD, Behold, a people cometh from the north country, and a great nation shall be raised from the sides of the earth.

α.6.23 Nag pish kogkonaog ohtompeh kah qunuhtug: nag onkapunohteaenu8og, kah wanne ummonaneteaonganeog: wuttauatonkqussuonk ogque mishotn8wau mehtahhannit, kah nayeumukquog horsesoh: ogque wunappuog ayeuuhkonukquean, woi wuttaunoh Zion.
E.6.23 They shall lay hold on bow and spear; they are cruel, and have no mercy; their voice roareth like the sea; and they ride upon horses, set in array as men for war against thee, O daughter of Zion.

α.6.24 N8tamumunnomup woweenodtumoonk, nunnutcheganunonash nano n8chumwiyeuash, kah mishonkquómom8onk nuttohqunukumun kah ogque onkquommomm8onk muttamwossis kodtauweekheont.
E.6.24 We have heard the fame thereof: our hands wax feeble: anguish hath taken hold of us, and pain, as of a woman in travail.

α.6.25 Sohham8teòk en ohteahkonit, kah pomusháhte[ó]k may$ut, newutche wuttogkodteg matwau, kah wabesuonk waéenu.
E.6.25 Go not forth into the field, nor walk by the way; for the sword of the enemy and fear is on every side.

α.6.26 Woi wuttaunoh nummissinninnumog puttukquobpissuwontamók man8tiônak, kah pummuquáish pukqukontu: ogquohpâusish mauwemat kenukquttegheon, ahche wesogkone maumuttam8onk, newutche matchehuwaénin teanuk pish kenuhkuhkongqun.
E.6.26 O daughter of my people, gird thee with sackcloth, and wallow thyself in ashes: make thee mourning, as for an only son, most bitter lamentation: for the spoiler shall suddenly come upon us.

α.6.27 Kutogque ponush qunuhquikomukqut, kah wonkônous ut kenugke nummissinninnumut; onk woh k8wahteoh, kah kukqutchteoh ummayeu.
E.6.27 I have set thee for a tower and a fortress among my people, that thou mayest know and try their way.

α.6.28 Nag wame onkquanittamwe ontsogquehtamog, kehkomuwae pomusháog: neg wompohshog kah misséhchuog, neg wame anuskuwanùog.
E.6.28 They are all grievous revolters, walking with slanders: they are brass and iron; they are all corrupters.

α.6.29 Popotowegaṣh chikohtaash, mahmuttattag mohtutteau ut n8taut: sôbossumwaen tahn8ch sâbohsôsu, newutche matchet8wog matta amaunóog.
E.6.29 The bellows are burned, the lead is consumed of the fire; the founder melteth in vain: for the wicked are not plucked away.

α.6.30 Nishke silver wosketompaog piṣh wuttehenóneau, newutche Lord uppogkenuh.
E.6.30 Reprobate silver shall men call them, because the LORD hath rejected them.

α.7.1 WUttinn8waonk ne paômukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
E.7.1 The word that came to Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.7.2 Neepaush ussquontamut wekit Jehovah, kah naut yeu wahteauwahuash kutt8wonk, kah n8waṣh, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame kenaau Judaéog, neg petutteacheg yeush usquontamaṣh, wowussumónat Jehovah.
E.7.2 Stand in the gate of the LORD's house, and proclaim there this word, and say, Hear the word of the LORD, all ye of Judah, that enter in at these gates to worship the LORD.

α.7.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah ut ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, onchteo8k kummayeuoaṣh, kah kutusseonganuoaṣh, kah yeu k8to[n]kéhinuneau ayeuonk.
E.7.3 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, Amend your ways and your doings, and I will cause you to dwell in this place.

α.7.4 Pabahtantam8hteók pann8wae kutt8wongaṣh, n8w[a]og, wut-templeum Jehovah, wut-templum Jehovah, wut-templum Jehovah yeush.
E.7.4 Trust ye not in lying words, saying, The temple of the LORD, The temple of the LORD, The temple of the LORD, are these.

α.7.5 Newutche papannuppe oncheteaôg kum$mayeuóaṣh, kah kutusseongan8óaṣh; papannuppe usseog wussittumóonk nashauwe wosketomp, kah weetatteamunguh.
E.7.5 For if ye throughly amend your ways and your doings; if ye throughly execute judgment between a man and his neighbour;

α.7.6 Matta sunukkutchahôóg pen8wot, touwies, kah sekousq, kah matta seaham8óg mat woskehuwáe musqueheonk yeu ut ayeuonganit, kah matta asuhkauôog onkatogig manittoog, wutch k8woskhetteaongan8.
E.7.6 If ye oppress not the stranger, the fatherless, and the widow, and shed not innocent blood in this place, neither walk after other gods to your hurt:

α.7.7 Neit yeu k8tohk[e]hinuneau ayeuonk, ut ohkeit ne anumauogkup k8sh8oog micheme kah micheme.
E.7.7 Then will I cause you to dwell in this place, in the land that I gave to your fathers, for ever and ever.

α.7.8 Kusseh kuppab[a]htantamumw8 pann8wae kutt8wongash, nish matta woh wadchiyeumukish.
E.7.8 Behold, ye trust in lying words, that cannot profit.

α.7.9 Sun kukkomm8tomw8, kenushteomw8, kah kummamussimw8, kah kuppann8wae chadchekeyeuomw8, kah kutchikossumauómw8 weetemungquok Baal, kah kutásuhkauomw8 onkatogig manitt8og, neg matta woheogig.
E.7.9 Will ye steal, murder, and commit adultery, and swear falsely, and burn incense unto Baal, and walk after other gods whom ye know not;

α.7.10 Kah sun kuppeyomw8, kah keneepomw8 anaqu[a]beh yeu ut wetuómut, ne as8weetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, kah kussimw8, nuppohquoahwhunnitteamun ussenat wame yeush nishkeneunkquokiṣh?
E.7.10 And come and stand before me in this house, which is called by my name, and say, We are delivered to do all these abominations?

α.7.11 Yeu weetu ne as8wetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, sun ne 8wekineau mukk8kinnuwaenuog ut anaquabeog? kusseh, nen nunnaumun wussin Jehovah.
E.7.11 Is this house, which is called by my name, become a den of robbers in your eyes? Behold, even I have seen it, saith the LORD.

α.7.12 Qut yeuyeu unk nutáyeuonganit ne ohtagkup Shiloh, uttoh negonne ponamomp n8wesuonk, kah naum8k uttoh ánteau wutche ummatcheseongan8 nummissinninnumog Israel.
E.7.12 But go ye now unto my place which was in Shiloh, where I set my name at the first, and see what I did to it for the wickedness of my people Israel.

α.7.13 Kah yeuyeu newutche k8wame yeush ussenáoaṣh anakausuongaṣh, wussin Jehovah, kah kukken8numwop, nompoáeu omohkéon, kah kódt8kôon, qut matta ken8tamómw8, kah k8wehkomunumwop, qut matta kenamp8hamomw8:
E.7.13 And now, because ye have done all these works, saith the LORD, and I spake unto you, rising up early and speaking, but ye heard not; and I called you, but ye answered not;

α.7.14 Newaj unnehteau yeu weetu, ne as8wetamuk wutche n8wesuonk, ne pabuhtantamóg, kah ayeuonk ne anumauogkup kenaau kah k8sh8óog, ne ánteauomp Shiloh.
E.7.14 Therefore will I do unto this house, which is called by my name, wherein ye trust, and unto the place which I gave to you and to your fathers, as I have done to Shiloh.

α.7.15 Kah kussohwhôkôunumw8 wutch anaquabeh, neane sohwohteaomp wame kematt8oóg, mamusse Ephraime wuskannem.
E.7.15 And I will cast you out of my sight, as I have cast out all your brethren, even the whole seed of Ephraim.

α.7.16 Newutche peantamwanshúhkon yeug missinninnuog, kah ahque tahshinumwansh mauonk asuh peantamóonk, kah ahque nag ken8tamwansh en nuhhogkat, newutche matta ken8tauun8.
E.7.16 Therefore pray not thou for this people, neither lift up cry nor prayer for them, neither make intercession to me: for I will not hear thee.

α.7.17 Sun matta kenaum8 toh ussehettit ut Judae keitotanehtu: & ut Jerusaleme taumaogquehtu?
E.7.17 Seest thou not what they do in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem?

α.7.18 Mukkiesog mukkinnumwog wuttuhqunaṣh, kah wut8shineunk m[o]utt[à]numwog, kah mittamwussissog tuttuhpunumwog ayimauwónat petukqunegaṣh wutche keichissonkusq kesukqut, kah sokenumauónat wuttattamoe mag8ongaṣh ut onkatoge manitt8h, woh numm8m8squehikqunnaóut.
E.7.18 The children gather wood, and the fathers kindle the fire, and the women knead their dough, to make cakes to the queen of heaven, and to pour out drink offerings unto other gods, that they may provoke me to anger.

α.7.19 Sun nag numm8m8squehikquog, wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta m8m8squeheauóog wuhhogkauh, chepshonat ut nehenwonche wuskesuk8óut.
E.7.19 Do they provoke me to anger? saith the LORD: do they not provoke themselves to the confusion of their own faces?

α.7.20 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh, nummusquantam8onk kah nummishe musquantam8onk pish sokanumun yeu ut ayeuonganit, ut wosketompaut, kah ut puppinashimwut, kah ut ohteuhkóne mehtugqut, kah ut ohkee meechummuonganit, kah pish chikohteau, kah matta pish ontham8un.
E.7.20 Therefore thus saith the Lord GOD; Behold, mine anger and my fury shall be poured out upon this place, upon man, and upon beast, and upon the trees of the field, and upon the fruit of the ground; and it shall burn, and shall not be quenched.

α.7.21 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, ponam8k kutchikohtae mag8ongan8oash, en kussephausuongan8out, kah meech8k weyaus.
E.7.21 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Put your burnt offerings unto your sacrifices, and eat flesh.

α.7.22 Newutche matta nukken8nomp k8sh8woog, kah matta nutann8noog ne kesukok pas8og wutch ohkit Egypt, papaume chikohtae mag8ongash, asuh sephausuongaṣh.
E.7.22 For I spake not unto your fathers, nor commanded them in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt, concerning burnt offerings or sacrifices:

α.7.23 Qut yeu nutann8nonah, nussip, n8swehtam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah nen piṣh kum-Manitt8mw8, kah kenaau piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah pomushagk wame mayut ne ánunn8nunóg, onk woh k8niyimw8.
E.7.23 But this thing commanded I them, saying, Obey my voice, and I will be your God, and ye shall be my people: and walk ye in all the ways that I have commanded you, that it may be well unto you.

α.7.24 Qut nag matta n8tam8og, kah matta ahchúsittam8og, qut pomusháadtamwog ut matche metahh8wae kogáhquttuonganit, kah pittuanum8onganit, kah nag as[ô]ushaog, kah matta kutchittohshau8og.
E.7.24 But they hearkened not, nor inclined their ear, but walked in the counsels and in the imagination of their evil heart, and went backward, and not forward.

α.7.25 Nadteuh ne kesukok k8sh8wóog sohhamwehettit wutch ohkit Egypt, nô pajeh yeu kesukok, n8wame ann8nomp en kuhhogkaut quoshodtumwae nuttinninnúmog, asekesukokiṣh, nompoáeu omohkeonish, kah ann8nogish.
E.7.25 Since the day that your fathers came forth out of the land of Egypt unto this day I have even sent unto you all my servants the prophets, daily rising up early and sending them:

α.7.26 Qut onch matta nukkeihketunk8og, asuh nutahch[ú]wusṣittonk8og, ut nag menehkehteôog wusṣittuppukan8, ánue ne matchesúmaog 8sh8oh.
E.7.26 Yet they hearkened not unto me, nor inclined their ear, but hardened their neck: they did worse than their fathers.

α.7.27 Newutche wame yeush kutt8wongash pish kuttinnonáoash, qut nag matta ken8tunk8og, pish wonk k8weehkomôog, qut matta kenamp8hamunk8og.
E.7.27 Therefore thou shalt speak all these words unto them; but they will not hearken to thee: thou shalt also call unto them; but they will not answer thee.

α.7.28 Qut pish kuttinóog, yeu wutohtimoin matta n8swetam8gig 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, kah matta attumunum8 sasamatuhwhuttuonk: wanamuhkutéyeuuk nehtauun, kah tummesumun wutch wutt8n8wóut.
E.7.28 But thou shalt say unto them, This is a nation that obeyeth not the voice of the LORD their God, nor receiveth correction: truth is perished, and is cut off from their mouth.

α.7.29 M8sumush woi Jerusalem, kah pogketash[.] kah maumatash ut qunuhqueu ayeuonganéhtu[;] newutche Jehovah uppogketamun, kah nukkodtum ne m8squantog pometuonk.
E.7.29 Cut off thine hair, O Jerusalem, and cast it away, and take up a lamentation on high places; for the LORD hath rejected and forsaken the generation of his wrath.

α.7.30 Newutche wunneechanoh Judah matcheseoh ut anaquabeh, wussin Jehovah; nag ponumwog wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8ash, wetuómut ne [à]hettamuk wutch n8wesuonk, nishketeauunat.
E.7.30 For the children of Judah have done evil in my sight, saith the LORD: they have set their abominations in the house which is called by my name, to pollute it.

α.7.31 Kah nag ayimwog qunuhqui ayeuongash ut Tophet, ne ohtag wut8n8ohkôiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnom, chikoswónat wunnaumonáuh kah wuttaun8uh n8taut, ne matta anann8nog, asuh peyaumun8 nuttahhut.
E.7.31 And they have built the high places of Tophet, which is in the valley of the son of Hinnom, to burn their sons and their daughters in the fire; which I commanded them not, neither came it into my heart.

α.7.32 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, wussin Lord, matta pish wonk hettam8unat Tophet, asuh wut8n8uhkoiyeum wunnaumonuh Hinnom, qut sheteae 8nóuhkôi, newutche nag pish posekinóog ut Tophet, nô pajeh mat momishkán8g.
E.7.32 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that it shall no more be called Tophet, nor the valley of the son of Hinnom, but the valley of slaughter: for they shall bury in Tophet, till there be no place.

α.7.33 Kah wuhhogkauh yeug missinninnúog piṣh ne ummechuongan8 kesukque puppinsháog, kah wutche ohkee puppinashimwog, kah matta pish howan wutáma8hkauoh.
E.7.33 And the carcases of this people shall be meat for the fowls of the heaven, and for the beasts of the earth; and none shall fray them away.

α.7.34 Neit nutchéqunapéhteoh wutch Judae keitotanaṣh, kah Jerusaleme taumáogquehtu, weekontamwe wadtauaonkqussuonk, wussentomwaen 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah weetauwadteáen 8wadtauatonkqussuonk: newutche ohke piṣh tauwushin.
E.7.34 Then will I cause to cease from the cities of Judah, and from the streets of Jerusalem, the voice of mirth, and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride: for the land shall be desolate.

α.8.1 NA ahquompag, wussin Jehovah, nag pish sohh8wuttauog wuskonash Judae ketass8tamwog kah wuskonoash wussontimom8oh, kah wuskon8ash sephausuenuog, kah wuskon8aṣh quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wuskon8aṣh wadohkitcheg JErusalem, wutch 8weenohkéenóut.
E.8.1 At that time, saith the LORD, they shall bring out the bones of the kings of Judah, and the bones of his princes, and the bones of the priests, and the bones of the prophets, and the bones of the inhabitants of Jerusalem, out of their graves:

α.8.2 Kah nag pish wussephamunáoaṣh anaquoshik nep[á]uz, kah nanepaoushadt, kah wame kesukque kenauwameonk neh womonáhetticheh, kah neh wadtinninneumuhkauwáhetticheh, kah neh asuhkauáhetticheh, kah neh natinneawáhettiche, kah neh wâsumáhetticheh: niṣh matta piṣh mukkinum8unaṣh, asuh posekinum8unaṣh, niṣh piṣh annohkeyeu8aṣh ut wosket ohkit.
E.8.2 And they shall spread them before the sun, and the moon, and all the host of heaven, whom they have loved, and whom they have served, and after whom they have walked, and whom they have sought, and whom they have worshipped: they shall not be gathered, nor be buried; they shall be for dung upon the face of the earth.

α.8.3 Kah nupp8onk piṣh pepenauau ánue onk ne pomantamóonk, nashpe neg wame seqshoncheg yeu ut matcheteatashiyeuonganit, neg ashqushoncheg ut wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh ann8kauog, wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.8.3 And death shall be chosen rather than life by all the residue of them that remain of this evil family, which remain in all the places whither I have driven them, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.8.4 Nano piṣh kuttinnóog, yeu wussin Jehovah, sun nag woh penushaog, kah matta omohkéog? sun woh amaeu, kah matta qushkeu?
E.8.4 Moreover thou shalt say unto them, Thus saith the LORD; Shall they fall, and not arise? shall he turn away, and not return?

α.8.5 Tohwaj yeug Jerusaleme missinninnúog assôep8shettit, nashpe machemohtag assôep8suonk? menuhkenumwog as8kek[ó]dteam8onk, sekeneamwog qushkenat.
E.8.5 Why then is this people of Jerusalem slidden back by a perpetual backsliding? they hold fast deceit, they refuse to return.

α.8.6 Nukkeiketamup, kah n8tamup, qut nag matta sampwe n8wa8wog, wanne howan aiuskoiantam8 ummatcheseonk, anowadt, toh nutussen? nishnoh pasuk en quinnuppu ummayut, neane horse quogqueit en ayeuuhkonat.
E.8.6 I hearkened and heard, but they spake not aright: no man repented him of his wickedness, saying, What have I done? every one turned to his course, as the horse rusheth into the battle.

α.8.7 Nux kesukque Stork wahteau kuhquttume wutútt8cheiyeum, kah wuskuhwhunan, kah ta[nu]ag, kah maméshashques kuhkinneasuog, ne woh utt8che peyahettit: qut nummissinninnḿog matta wahteau8og 8sittum8onk Jehovah.
E.8.7 Yea, the stork in the heaven knoweth her appointed times; and the turtle and the crane and the swallow observe the time of their coming; but my people know not the judgment of the LORD.

α.8.8 Uttoh kittin n8wónean n8waantamumun, kah wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah n8wetomukqun? kusseh, wunnamuhkut tahn8che wutáyimun, uppennum8uh Scribsog tahn8cheyeu8.
E.8.8 How do ye say, We are wise, and the law of the LORD is with us? Lo, certainly in vain made he it; the pen of the scribes is in vain.

α.8.9 Waantamwog akodchuog, chepshaog kah tohqun[ó]og, kusseh, nag pogketamwog wuttinn8w[á]onk Jehovah, kah teagwe waantamóonk apehtunkqhettit?
E.8.9 The wise men are ashamed, they are dismayed and taken: lo, they have rejected the word of the LORD; and what wisdom is in them?

α.8.10 Newaj mag8 ummittamwuss8uh en onkatoganit, kah wutohteuhkón8ash en nag woh ohtunkeg: newutche nishnoh pasuk wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk n8swuhkom hohchewontamoonk, wutch quoshodtumwáenuut pajeh sephausuwáenuut, niṣh$noh pasuk pann8wae usseu.
E.8.10 Therefore will I give their wives unto others, and their fields to them that shall inherit them: for every one from the least even unto the greatest is given to covetousness, from the prophet even unto the priest every one dealeth falsely.

α.8.11 Newutche nag meshanne neetsketuog woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, n8waog, wunohteagk wunohteagk, matta wunohteaonganin8g.
E.8.11 For they have healed the hurt of the daughter of my people slightly, saying, Peace, peace; when there is no peace.

α.8.12 Sun nag akodchuog nishkeneunkquok ussehettit? matchag, wanneh mo akodchuog kah matta pen8quosho8og, newaj piṣh penusháhettit kenugke neg panushoncheg, ne adt8che nadtauwáhet piṣh penuhkonog wussin Jehovah.
E.8.12 Were they ashamed when they had committed abomination? nay, they were not at all ashamed, neither could they blush: therefore shall they fall among them that fall: in the time of their visitation they shall be cast down, saith the LORD.

α.8.13 Wunnamuhkut nag piṣh nummahtupanóog wussin Jehovah, matta piṣh weenomininno wenómwussippog, asuh figsash ut figsuhtugqut, kah wunnepog piṣh uhp8teau: kah piṣh áninnumauogish, piṣh uppaumukongqunáoash.
E.8.13 I will surely consume them, saith the LORD: there shall be no grapes on the vine, nor figs on the fig tree, and the leaf shall fade; and the things that I have given them shall pass away from them.

α.8.14 Tohwutch chequnappeog? miyáek, kah petutteadtuh pummenútausue keitotanahtu, kah naut chequnapitteuh, newutche Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, kutchequnaphikqun, kah k8tattamwáhikqun weeswee[e]pog, newutche nummatcheneheomun Jehovah.
E.8.14 Why do we sit still? assemble yourselves, and let us enter into the defenced cities, and let us be silent there: for the LORD our God hath put us to silence, and given us water of gall to drink, because we have sinned against the LORD.

α.8.15 Nukkenompadtamumun wunohteaonk, qut matta wunnegininn8, kah wunnáyeue aquompi kah kusseh wuttamehpunáonk.
E.8.15 We looked for peace, but no good came; and for a time of health, and behold trouble!

α.8.16 Chequttumhettit horsesog mo wuttissittauog Dan: mamusse ohke nunnuksinea[u] wadauatonkqussue nehnehteanit ummenuhkeseumoh, newutche peyaog, k[à]h mahchep8og ohke, kah wame ne noh ohtag, keitotan kah wame neg nag wadohkitcheg.
E.8.16 The snorting of his horses was heard from Dan: the whole land trembled at the sound of the neighing of his strong ones; for they are come, and have devoured the land, and all that is in it; the city, and those that dwell therein.

α.8.17 Newutche kusseh nutann8n ask8kog kah kokatricesog ut kenugke kenaau, neg woh mat monehtauwooncheg, kah neg piṣh kussogkepak8óog, n8wau Lord.
E.8.17 For, behold, I will send serpents, cockatrices, among you, which will not be charmed, and they shall bite you, saith the LORD.

α.8.18 Ayeukonittue tapene[á]uwontamun ohquanumoonk, nuttah nupp8m8 ut nuttinnómiyeumut.
E.8.18 When I would comfort myself against sorrow, my heart is faint in me.

α.8.19 Kusseh 8wadtauatonkqussuongane mauongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, newutche neg wadohkitcheg nôadtut wutohtimóneat: sunnummatta Jehovah appu Zion? sunnummatta ukkehtass8tamomoh apehtunk8? tohwutch nag m8m8squehettit nashpe wuttinnukontunkanouh, kah nashpe penowe tahn8cheyeugish [j]
E.8.19 Behold the voice of the cry of the daughter of my people because of them that dwell in a far country: Is not the LORD in Zion? is not her king in her? Why have they provoked me to anger with their graven images, and with strange vanities?

α.8.20 Kepenum8onk pámsheau, nepun wohkukquoshin, kah matta n8wadchanitteamun.
E.8.20 The harvest is past, the summer is ended, and we are not saved.

α.8.21 Newutche woskeheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, n8woskhit numm8es: chepshaonk nuttohqunuk.
E.8.21 For the hurt of the daughter of my people am I hurt; I am black; astonishment hath taken hold on me.

α.8.22 Sunn$na$matta balmun8 ut Gilead? sun$na$mat ponaskétuwosuenúun8? tohwaj mat uppomantam8ongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, mat keteohtaómun.
E.8.22 Is there no balm in Gilead; is there no physician there? why then is not the health of the daughter of my people recovered?

α.9.1 WOi napehnont nuppuhkuk nippeyeu88, kah nissuppegwe tohkekommú8k nuskesukquash: onk woh nummau kesukodae kah nukkonae, wutche nashoncheg wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
E.9.1 Oh that my head were waters, and mine eyes a fountain of tears, that I might weep day and night for the slain of the daughter of my people!

α.9.2 Napehnont ohtau ut touohkomuk, pomushaenuog ukkoueongan8, onk woh nunnukon nummissinninnúmog, & woh nutámaéhtauóog: newutche nag wame mamussuwaenuog, ummóeongan8 wanass8muwácheg.
E.9.2 Oh that I had in the wilderness a lodging place of wayfaring men; that I might leave my people, and go from them! for they be all adulterers, an assembly of treacherous men.

α.9.3 Kah nag ogque wutunkkinnumw8weenanú8 ohtompe, pann8wonat: qut nag matta wutt8wehtamóog wutch wánamuhkutéyeuuk ut ohkeit: newutche ohhontseog w[u]tch machuk en machukut, kah matta n8wáhik8og wussin Jehovah.
E.9.3 And they bend their tongues like their bow for lies: but they are not valiant for the truth upon the earth; for they proceed from evil to evil, and they know not me, saith the LORD.

α.9.4 Nunnukqussek wutch nishnoh wosketomp weetatteamungoh, kah pabuhtánumúhteok howae weemattin: newutche nishnoh 8weemattin 8wománumoh, kah nishnoh weetatteamunganin, kekómuwae pomusheau.
E.9.4 Take ye heed every one of his neighbour, and trust ye not in any brother: for every brother will utterly supplant, and every neighbour will walk with slanders.

α.9.5 Kah nag as8kekomáog nishnoh weetatteamungan8oh, kah matta eyeu wunnamuhkutéyeuuk, kuhk8t[u]mwontamwog weenannú pann8wonat, kah sauwunnaog wuhhogkauh matchesenat.
E.9.5 And they will deceive every one his neighbour, and will not speak the truth: they have taught their tongue to speak lies, and weary themselves to commit iniquity.

α.9.6 K8tohtuonk ohteau nôeu as8kekodteam8onk, nashpe as8ke[k]odteam8onk sekeneamwog n8wahikqunnaóont wussin Jehovah,
E.9.6 Thine habitation is in the midst of deceit; through deceit they refuse to know me, saith the LORD.

α.9.7 Newájeh yeu n8wadt Lord ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nag nummáhtuppaswóog, kah nukqutchheaog: newutche toh woh nuttinneh wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
E.9.7 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, Behold, I will melt them, and try them; for how shall I do for the daughter of my people?

α.9.8 Weenan8 onatuh kôuhquodt pámemuk, as8kekodteám8eyeum8: how[a]n wunohteae ken8nau weetatteamungoh ut wutt8nut, qut wuttahhut wutaskwhónuh.
E.9.8 Their tongue is as an arrow shot out; it speaketh deceit: one speaketh peaceably to his neighbour with his mouth, but in heart he layeth his wait.

α.9.9 Sunnummatta woh yeush n8ch natauwahuwáunash, wussin Jehovah? sun matta woh nukketeahogou an8tantàm8 yeu ânag wutohtimóin?
E.9.9 Shall I not visit them for these things? saith the LORD: shall not my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?

α.9.10 Wutche wadchuash nunnemunum mauonk kah maumuttam8onk, kah wutch touohkomukque ayeuonk maumuttam8onk, newutche nag mahchukkissuog, ne waj matta howan nah paumukáuonk, kah woh mo wosketompaog n8tam8og 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neetassuog, naneeswe kesukque puppinshasog, kah puppinashimwog, wussem8og kah monchasháog.
E.9.10 For the mountains will I take up a weeping and wailing, and for the habitations of the wilderness a lamentation, because they are burned up, so that none can pass through them; neither can men hear the voice of the cattle; both the fowl of the heavens and the beast are fled; they are gone.

α.9.11 Kah nunnanomwonkquadtoh Jerusalem, kah dragonsog wek8, kah nuttauushitteoh Judae keitotanash, matta wutohkeinat.
E.9.11 And I will make Jerusalem heaps, and a den of dragons; and I will make the cities of Judah desolate, without an inhabitant.

α.9.12 Howan noh waantog yeu woh wohtog, kah howan noh wutt8n Jehovah kôn8nukqut, onk woh 8wahteauwáhuwon tohwaj ohke mahchum8g; kah ogque mahtutteau touohkomuk, matta howan ukqushkodteáunat?
E.9.12 Who is the wise man, that may understand this? and who is he to whom the mouth of the LORD hath spoken, that he may declare it, for what the land perisheth and is burned up like a wilderness, that none passeth through?

α.9.13 Kah Jehovah n8wau, newutche ohquanumaog nuttinnaum[á]tuonk, ne ponamon anaquabhettit, kah matta n8sweetamóog n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah matta ne pomusháuneau.
E.9.13 And the LORD saith, Because they have forsaken my law which I set before them, and have not obeyed my voice, neither walked therein;

α.9.14 Qut nag asuhkomwog nehenwonche metahh8wae uppehtuánum8ongan8; kah Baalim, ne 8sh8oh kuhk8tomungqhetteup.
E.9.14 But have walked after the imagination of their own heart, and after Baalim, which their fathers taught them:

α.9.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nag nussohkom8unoog, yeug missinninnúog wormw8d, kah n8tattamweheoog weeswe.
E.9.15 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will feed them, even this people, with wormwood, and give them water of gall to drink.
