α.9.16 Nusseahwhóog wonk kenugke pen8wotheáut, nag asuh 8sh8oh matta waheáhettegeh: kah nutas[ù]hkaue n8sukqunôog togkodteg, nô pajeh nummohtupp[á]nonaóont.
E.9.16 I will scatter them also among the heathen, whom neither they nor their fathers have known: and I will send a sword after them, till I have consumed them.

α.9.17 Yeu wussin Lord ayéuteaunit, natwontam8k, kah wehkomok maumuttamwe mittamwossissog, onk woh nag peyaog kah wehkom nohtôe maumuttogig, onk woh peyaog.
E.9.17 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, Consider ye, and call for the mourning women, that they may come; and send for cunning women, that they may come:

α.9.18 Kah kenupshahettich, kah maumuttamwanshikqutteuh, onk woh kuss8ksuppégwoshómun, kah woh sohwutchúan nippe wutch kuskesukqunónut.
E.9.18 And let them make haste, and take up a wailing for us, that our eyes may run down with tears, and our eyelids gush out with waters.

α.9.19 Newutche wuttauatonkqussue maumuttam8onk wutch n8tamun Zion, uttoh kittin matchehetteanan? nummishe chepshómun, newutche nu[n]nukkodtumumun ohke, newuthe nutayeuonganunonash nuppogkenukumun.
E.9.19 For a voice of wailing is heard out of Zion, How are we spoiled! we are greatly confounded, because we have forsaken the land, because our dwellings have cast us out.

α.9.20 Qut onch n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Lord, woi kenaau mittamwossissog, kah kuhtauog88ash attumunumhettich wutt8ne wuttinn8waonk, kah kuhk8tamok kuttaun8wóog maumuttamun, kah nishnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, maumuttam8onk.
E.9.20 Yet hear the word of the LORD, O ye women, and let your ear receive the word of his mouth, and teach your daughters wailing, and every one her neighbour lamentation.

α.9.21 Newutche nupp8onk pajeh kuhkúhqueu nukkenogkunnégunó[u]t, kah petutteom8 nummishekomukqunónut, tummehtahwhonát mukkiog wutch poquadchit, kah wuskenúog toumáogquehtu.
E.9.21 For death is come up into our windows, and is entered into our palaces, to cut off the children from without, and the young men from the streets.

α.9.22 Ket8kash, yeu wussin Lord, nupp8e wuhhogkáuh wosketompaog piṣh ogque penushaog an[n]óhkeit m8sohteuhkónit, kah ogque wunnukquttinutchánit kepenumwain, kah matta pish howan ummukkinum8unash.
E.9.22 Speak, Thus saith the LORD, Even the carcases of men shall fall as dung upon the open field, and as the handful after the harvestman, and none shall gather them.

α.9.23 Yeu wussin Lord, waantamwaen ahque woweenoaj ut 8waantam8onganit, kah menuhkesuen, ahque woweenóaj ut ummenuhkesuonganit, weenauwetuen woweenoáhkitch ut 8weenauaweetuonganit.
E.9.23 Thus saith the LORD, Let not the wise man glory in his wisdom, neither let the mighty man glory in his might, let not the rich man glory in his riches:

α.9.24 Qut noh waeenoadt, yeu$ut waeenoaj, noh n8wohwohtunk, kah n8wahik, nen Jehovah[ú]8, asee womoausuonk, wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit, newutche yeush nuttapeneaumunash wussin Jehovah.
E.9.24 But let him that glorieth glory in this, that he understandeth and knoweth me, that I am the LORD which exercise lovingkindness, judgment, and righteousness, in the earth: for in these things I delight, saith the LORD.

α.9.25 Kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8ásh, n8wau Jehovah, nussasámatahwhônaóont wame neg quosqusaúsitcheg, kenugke matta quosqussausegig.
E.9.25 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will punish all them which are circumcised with the uncircumcised;

α.9.26 Egypt, kah Judah, kah Edom, kah wunneechanoh Ammon, [h]ah Moab, kah wame neg aongkoue apitcheg, neg ayitcheg touohkomuk: newutche wame yeush wutohtimoneaṣh matta quosqushôsin8aṣh, kah wame wek Israel matta quosqushausuwutteahou8og.
E.9.26 Egypt, and Judah, and Edom, and the children of Ammon, and Moab, and all that are in the utmost corners, that dwell in the wilderness: for all these nations are uncircumcised, and all the house of Israel are uncircumcised in the heart.

α.10.1 NOOtam8k kutt8onk ne Jehovah ánukqueog, woi wek Israel.
E.10.1 Hear ye the word which the LORD speaketh unto you, O house of Israel:

α.10.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, nehtuhtam8hteogk ummayou penuohteaog: kah chepshontam8hteogk kesukque kuhkinneasuongaṣh, newutche pen8wohteáog niṣh wutchepshontamunnáoaṣh.
E.10.2 Thus saith the LORD, Learn not the way of the heathen, and be not dismayed at the signs of heaven; for the heathen are dismayed at them.

α.10.3 Newutche wuttinniyeuongan8oaṣh tahn8cheyeu8aṣh: newutche pasuk tummehtam mehtug wutch touohkomuk, (wunnutchegane anakausuonk anakausuwaen) nashpe togkunk.
E.10.3 For the customs of the people are vain: for one cutteth a tree out of the forest, the work of the hands of the workman, with the axe.

α.10.4 Nag wunnohh8suog nashpe silver kah gold, kah ummenuhketunaoaṣh nashpe kenunkwhongaṣh, kah hammersaṣh woh mo ontohtáun8ut.
E.10.4 They deck it with silver and with gold; they fasten it with nails and with hammers, that it move not.

α.10.5 Ogque samp8kompauog palmuhtugqut, qut matta ket8kau8og: neg woh kenunóog, newutche matta pomushauóog: qushûhteógk, newutche mo woskéhuwówog, asuh woh mo 8nénehuóog
E.10.5 They are upright as the palm tree, but speak not: they must needs be borne, because they cannot go. Be not afraid of them; for they cannot do evil, neither also is it in them to do good.

α.10.6 Newutche matta howan ku[ttin]unkou woi Jehovah, kummissugken, kah k8wesuonk mishe menuhki.
E.10.6 Forasmuch as there is none like unto thee, O LORD; thou art great, and thy name is great in might.

α.10.7 Howan woh mat quoshuk8an woi wutohtimóune ketass8t? newutche wutchayeum8 kuhhogkat: newutche ut kenugke wame wutohtimóune waantamwog, kah ut wame wutass8tam8ongan8out, wanne howan kuttinnunk8.
E.10.7 Who would not fear thee, O King of nations? for to thee doth it appertain: forasmuch as among all the wise men of the nations, and in all their kingdoms, there is none like unto thee.

α.10.8 Qut papannuppe puppinashumóog kah as8tuog: nunneukontunk tahn8cheeyeu kuhk8tomwehteaonk.
E.10.8 But they are altogether brutish and foolish: the stock is a doctrine of vanities.

α.10.9 Sepagenumwe silvere kodchuhkiyeuaṣh wutaaunaṣh Tarshish, kah gold wutch Uphaz, wutanakausuonk anakausuwaen kah sabasumwaenin wunnutcheg: 8nôagk kah purple wuthogk8un8oaṣh, niṣh wame wutanakausuongan8 nehtoe anausuenúog,
E.10.9 Silver spread into plates is brought from Tarshish, and gold from Uphaz, the work of the workman, and of the hands of the founder: blue and purple is their clothing: they are all the work of cunning men.

α.10.10 Qut Jehovah wunnamuhkutée Manitt88, noh pomantamwae God, kah machemapit ketass8t[:] musquantog, ohke piṣh nunnksheau, kah wutohtimoneaṣh matta piṣh tapenumóog appuwontamun ummishe musquantam8onk.
E.10.10 But the LORD is the true God, he is the living God, and an everlasting king: at his wrath the earth shall tremble, and the nations shall not be able to abide his indignation.

α.10.11 Yeu woh nag kuttinoneau, manittoog neg matta kesteo8gig kesukquaṣh kah ohke, neg piṣh pagwanuog wutche ohkeit, kah wutch agwe yeush kesukquaṣh.
E.10.11 Thus shall ye say unto them, The gods that have not made the heavens and the earth, even they shall perish from the earth, and from under these heavens.

α.10.12 Noh nashpe ayikup ohke ummenuhkesuonk, noh menuhketeau muttaok mashpe 8waantam8onk, kah sepágenumup kesukquaṣh nashpe 8waantam8onk.
E.10.12 He hath made the earth by his power, he hath established the world by his wisdom, and hath stretched out the heavens by his discretion.

α.10.13 Máhshant8adt, muttáununkquodt nippeaṣh ut kesukqut, k[á]h waabeteau óuwan ushpem8ut, wutch weekqshik ohke: ukkutshamwunéhteau nashpe sokanon, kah sohh8wunau waban8h wutche wunnompak8une komukqut.
E.10.13 When he uttereth his voice, there is a multitude of waters in the heavens, and he causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; he maketh lightnings with rain, and bringeth forth the wind out of his treasures.

α.10.14 Nishnog wosketomp puppinashim88 ut 8wahteauonganit: nishnoh sôbassumwaénin chepshau nashpe nukkeukontunk: newutche wussabassumwe nunneukontunkoh pann8waeyeu8, kah matta wunnashaonganéoh.
E.10.14 Every man is brutish in his knowledge: every founder is confounded by the graven image: for his molten image is falsehood, and there is no breath in them.

α.10.15 Nag tahn8cheyeu8og, kah panneusseae anakausuongaṣh, nadtauwahit pish matcheheóog.
E.10.15 They are vanity, and the work of errors: in the time of their visitation they shall perish.

α.10.16 Wutchippiyeum Jakob matta nah tatuppéin8: newutche noh kakenauwehteunk wame teanteoqussiniṣh, kah Israel wutohtauongane souobpunk, Jehovah ayeuteanit ne 8wesuonk.
E.10.16 The portion of Jacob is not like them: for he is the former of all things; and Israel is the rod of his inheritance: The LORD of hosts is his name.

α.10.17 Miy[á]numók maumachiaṣh wutch ohkeit, woi wadohkéan wonkon8sinit.
E.10.17 Gather up thy wares out of the land, O inhabitant of the fortress.

α.10.18 Newutche yéu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nuss8wompagunuh pasukqut wadohkitcheg ohkeit, k[á]h nukquequenauánumwahheóog, onk woh ne wuttinne nemehtinneau.
E.10.18 For thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will sling out the inhabitants of the land at this once, and will distress them, that they may find it so.

α.10.19 Missi nutonkapunáonk wutche n8woskkitteáonk, nunn8chumwetáhwhutteaonk uhqueneunkquodt, qut nussip, wunnamuhkut yeu onkquanumóonk, kah m8che mos nummuk8ammattamun.
E.10.19 Woe is me for my hurt! my wound is grievous; but I said, Truly this is a grief, and I must bear it.

α.10.20 Neek matchehteauun, kah nuppémuneóhtanaṣh wame poskisháaṣh: nummukkiesumog nussohwehtunkquog, kah nag matta appeog, kah matta wonk howan nussépagunumunk8 nek, kah n8nohtunkoh nutunkwheganuh.
E.10.20 My tabernacle is spoiled, and all my cords are broken: my children are gone forth of me, and they are not: there is none to stretch forth my tent any more, and to set up my curtains.

α.10.21 Newutche Pastorsog puppinashimweyeu8og, kah natinnewho8og Jehovah: ne$waj matta piṣh wunnihettit, kah wame uf-flockum piṣh seáhwhóog.
E.10.21 For the pastors are become brutish, and have not sought the LORD: therefore they shall not prosper, and all their flocks shall be scattered.

α.10.22 Kusseh, aunchem8kae wadtauatonkqussuonk peyom8, kah mishe wogkouéonk wutch nanumohkit, touushinnúwáhtinat Judae keitotanaṣh, kah dragonnekommukquaṣh.
E.10.22 Behold, the noise of the bruit is come, and a great commotion out of the north country, to make the cities of Judah desolate, and a den of dragons.

α.10.23 Woi Lord, n8wahteoh ummay wosketomp matta wunnehenwoncheiyeum: mat ohtano wosketompaut, noh paumushadt, sampwutteauunat wuttaunehtuongash.
E.10.23 O LORD, I know that the way of man is not in himself: it is not in man that walketh to direct his steps.

α.10.24 Woi Jehovah, sasamatahwheh, qut nashpe wussittumóonk, matta ut kummusquanittam8onganit, ishkont mat toh kuttintuppehu.
E.10.24 O LORD, correct me, but with judgment; not in thine anger, lest thou bring me to nothing.

α.10.25 Sokenumau kummusquanitteaonk pen8wohteaut neg matta wahikk8uneg, kah wutteateashiyeuongan8wóut neg matta wehquetum8gig k8wesuonk, newutche mahchipp8og Jakoboh, kah umm8hwhóuh, kah ummahtupanóuh, kah tauushit[t]eauwahtoog wutayeuonk.
E.10.25 Pour out thy fury upon the heathen that know thee not, and upon the families that call not on thy name: for they have eaten up Jacob, and devoured him, and consumed him, and have made his habitation desolate.

α.11.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
E.11.1 The word that came to Jeremiah from the LORD saying,

α.11.2 N8tam8k yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash, kah ken8nok Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem
E.11.2 Hear ye the words of this covenant, and speak unto the men of Judah, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem;

α.11.3 Kah nag us, yeu wussin Lord Jehovah ut Israel, matánumunach noh matta n8sweetam8g yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash.
E.11.3 And say thou unto them, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel; Cursed be the man that obeyeth not the words of this covenant,

α.11.4 Nish ann8nokkupash k8sh8wóog, ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypt, wutch missitchuogke sab[a]ssum8onganit, an8waon, n8swetam8k, n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah nish ussek, wame neanann8nunóg: neit pish kenaau nummissinninnúmog, kah nen piṣh kum-Manitt8m8.
E.11.4 Which I commanded your fathers in the day that I brought them forth out of the land of Egypt, from the iron furnace, saying, Obey my voice, and do them, according to all which I command you: so shall ye be my people, and I will be your God:

α.11.5 Onk woh nutussem chadchekeyeuwaonk, ne chadchekéimogkup k8sh8wóog, aninnumauónat ohke ne taumogok sogkodtunk kah hony, ne âunag yeu kesukok: neit nunnamp8hamuk kah nussip, ne n$naj woi Jehovah.
E.11.5 That I may perform the oath which I have sworn unto your fathers, to give them a land flowing with milk and honey, as it is this day. Then answered I, and said, So be it, O LORD.

α.11.6 Neit Lord nuttugkup n8tamwáhuash wame yeush kutt8wongash ut Judae keitotanehtu, kah Jerusaleme taumáogquehtu, n8wash, n8tam8k yeush wunn8wae kutt8wongash kah nish ussek.
E.11.6 Then the LORD said unto me, Proclaim all these words in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem, saying, Hear ye the words of this covenant, and do them.

α.11.7 Newutche nummenuhke chekeimomp k8showóog, ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypt, pajeh yeu kesukok, n$nompoae omohkeon, kah chadchekeyeuwaon, an8waon, n8swehtam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk.
E.11.7 For I earnestly protested unto your fathers in the day that I brought them up out of the land of Egypt, even unto this day, rising early and protesting, saying, Obey my voice.

α.11.8 Qut nag mat nosweetamóog, kah matta ahch8sittam8og, qut nishnoh pasuk pomushau ummatchetahhae wuttenantam8onganit: newaj nuhkunumauog wame yeu wunn8wae kutt8wongash, ne ánan8nog ussenat: qut nag matta wutussenáoash.
E.11.8 Yet they obeyed not, nor inclined their ear, but walked every one in the imagination of their evil heart: therefore I will bring upon them all the words of this covenant, which I commanded them to do: but they did them not.

α.11.9 Kah Lord nuttinnuk, nushehteáuss8waonk namehteauun ut kenugke Judae wosketompaog: kah kenugke wadohkitcheg Jerusalem.
E.11.9 And the LORD said unto me, A conspiracy is found among the men of Judah, and among the inhabitants of Jerusalem.

α.11.10 Nag qushkéog en ummatcheseongan8wòut negonne 8sh8uh, neg sekeneogig n8tamunat nuttinn8waongash: kah asuhkauáog onkatogek manitt8h, wowussumonat: Israelle wetu, kah Judae wetu nag pohquenumwog n8n8waonk, ne ayimauogkup 8sh8uh.
E.11.10 They are turned back to the iniquities of their forefathers, which refused to hear my words; and they went after other gods to serve them: the house of Israel and the house of Judah have broken my covenant which I made with their fathers.

α.11.11 Newaj yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauóog machuk, ne matta pish tapenumohetteg pohquohhamunat, kah tôhkonogque pish nummauunnitteunkqunneau, matta pish nunn8tau8og.
E.11.11 Therefore thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will bring evil upon them, which they shall not be able to escape; and though they shall cry unto me, I will not hearken unto them.

α.11.12 Neit Judae keitotanash kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem pish moncheog, kah mauunnitteauâog manitt8oh neh anumauáhetticheh weetemungquok, qut nag matta pish papaquanne 8wadchanuk8oh, wuttaméhpun[à]hettit.
E.11.12 Then shall the cities of Judah and inhabitants of Jerusalem go, and cry unto the gods unto whom they offer incense: but they shall not save them at all in the time of their trouble.

α.11.13 Newutche ne âdtahshik kukkeitotanash ne kum-manitt8mog, woi Judah, kah ne âdtahshik Jerusaleme toumaogquash k8nahtómw8 altarash en ne akodchuwéyeu8k, altarsash ne adt chikkohsumuk weetemungquok en Baal.
E.11.13 For according to the number of thy cities were thy gods, O Judah; and according to the number of the streets of Jerusalem have ye set up altars to that shameful thing, even altars to burn incense unto Baal.

α.11.14 Newutche peantamwanshuhkon yeug missinninnuog, kah tahshinnumwanshuhkon mauonk asuh peantamoonk: newutche matta pish nunn8tauoog maunnitt[t]eaihettit wutch wuttamehpunaonk.
E.11.14 Therefore pray not thou for this people, neither lift up a cry or prayer for them: for I will not hear them in the time that they cry unto me for their trouble.

α.11.15 Noh womonog, teag wutch appit neekit, mahche manishquaâsit m8náoh? kah wunneetupanatamwe weyaus kuppaumuhkunk: matcheseanish, kummiskouantam.
E.11.15 What hath my beloved to do in mine house, seeing she hath wrought lewdness with many, and the holy flesh is passed from thee? when thou doest evil, then thou rejoicest.

α.11.16 Lord kutussowenuk askuh[u]kquame olivuhtug, wunnegen, kah wunnummeechummu: nashpe mishe wogkouee mishont8waonk wutchikkossumun, kah wuttuhqunash pohqshaash.
E.11.16 The LORD called thy name, A green olive tree, fair, and of goodly fruit: with the noise of a great tumult he hath kindled fire upon it, and the branches of it are broken.

α.11.17 Newutche Jehovah ayeuteaunit, noh ahteuhkonukquean, ayeuuhkonittue kukken8tamunk machuk wutch ummatchitt8m Israelle weetu, kah Judae weetut, ne ayeuuhkonittue aseaunshehettit wuhhogkauh, numm8m8sqhikqunnaoont, aninnumauahetticheh weetemungquok Baaloh.
E.11.17 For the LORD of hosts, that planted thee, hath pronounced evil against thee, for the evil of the house of Israel and of the house of Judah, which they have done against themselves to provoke me to anger in offering incense unto Baal.

α.11.18 Kah Jehovah n8wahteauwahikqun, kah n8wahteauun; neit kenaitussip wutusseonganóoash.
E.11.18 And the LORD hath given me knowledge of it, and I know it: then thou shewedst me their doings.

α.11.19 Qut nuttatuppeyeuup Lamb, asuh ox, noh pas8ut nushonat, kah matta n8wahteau8h ayeuuhkonittue natwontamunkquog tashipinanittuongash, n8wahettit, nehtauudtuh mehtug nashpe ummeechummuonk, kah tummehtáhwhontuh wutch wutohtuout pomontogig, onk woh 8wesuonk matta wonk mequontam8un.
E.11.19 But I was like a lamb or an ox that is brought to the slaughter; and I knew not that they had devised devices against me, saying, Let us destroy the tree with the fruit thereof, and let us cut him off from the land of the living, that his name may be no more remembered.

α.11.20 Qut woi Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ken sampweusseáe wussittuman, ken quajheadt mutt8[u]nussog, kah metah: naumwáhe nag kutann8tauwaongan8, newutche k8wahteauwáhesh nuppissaumatuonk.
E.11.20 But, O LORD of hosts, that judgest righteously, that triest the reins and the heart, let me see thy vengeance on them: for unto thee have I revealed my cause.

α.11.21 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah papaume Anathothe wosketompaog, neg áchuwehteunkig kuppomantamóonk, n8wahettit, quoshodtuhkon ut 8wesuonganit Lord, onk woh mo kenupp8 nashpe nunnutcheganun.
E.11.21 Therefore thus saith the LORD of the men of Anathoth, that seek thy life, saying, Prophesy not in the name of the LORD, that thou die not by our hand:

α.11.22 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nag nussasamatahwhóog: wuskennuog piṣh nupwog nashpe togkodteganit, wunnaumonáoh kah wuttaun8oh pish nupwoh nashpe mahshagquodt:
E.11.22 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, Behold, I will punish them: the young men shall die by the sword; their sons and their daughters shall die by famine:

α.11.23 Kah matta piṣh ushqushau8og, newutche nunnuhkinnumau machuk ut Anathothe wosketompaog, nadtauwáheáe ukkodtum8m8.
E.11.23 And there shall be no remnant of them: for I will bring evil upon the men of Anathoth, even the year of their visitation.

α.12.1 KUssampweusseaénu, woi Lord, keket8kauunon, qut kéket8kauwunnittei papaume k8sittum8ongaṣh: tohwaj ummay matchetou wunayeum8uk? tohwaj wame nag wanaihettit ahche wanassúm8wáe ussécheg?
E.12.1 Righteous art thou, O LORD, when I plead with thee: yet let me talk with thee of thy judgments: Wherefore doth the way of the wicked prosper?  wherefore are all they happy that deal very treacherously?

α.12.2 Nag kutohtukónunk, nux, nag 8wadchabuk8og: nag neetuog, nux meechummu8og: ken kuppas8cheyeu8 wutt8n8wóut, kah kinnau8sukom wutt8unuss8uh.
E.12.2 Thou hast planted them, yea, they have taken root: they grow, yea, they bring forth fruit: thou art near in their mouth, and far from their reins.

α.12.3 Qut ken woi Jehovah, k8waheh, kenáip, kah kukqutchteóp nuttah en kuhhogkáiyeu: ogque sohwhun sheepsut wutche nashaongan8, kah quagquashweáh wutche paguwanittue kesukod.
E.12.3 But thou, O LORD, knowest me: thou hast seen me, and tried mine heart toward thee: pull them out like sheep for the slaughter, and prepare them for the day of slaughter.

α.12.4 Toh utt8che piṣh ohke mau8m8, kah wame ohteuhkonée herbsaṣh ohp8taaṣh, wutche ummatcheseongan8 neg na wadohkitcheg? puppinashimwog mahtsúog, kah psukesuk, newutche nag n8waog matta piṣh naum8 n8wohkukquóiyeumun.
E.12.4 How long shall the land mourn, and the herbs of every field wither, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein? the beasts are consumed, and the birds; because they said, He shall not see our last end.

α.12.5 Weechepohtómussoh mohtissita[h]shoncheg, kah nag sauunukquéan, neit toh woh kittin nunnôohkônon horses? kah wunohteáe ohkeit, ne pabuhtantamun, sauwunukquean, neit uttoh woh kittinheoh tômogkok ut Jordan?
E.12.5 If thou hast run with the footmen, and they have wearied thee, then how canst thou contend with horses? and if in the land of peace, wherein thou trustedst, they wearied thee, then how wilt thou do in the swelling of Jordan?

α.12.6 Newutche kemattog, kah k8sh wek, wutass8muwae kittinhukquog; nux, wehkomáog monanutcheh kutásuhkunkqunat: wunnamptauúhkon, tôhkonogque k8wówunónukumukqunat. 
E.12.6 For even thy brethren, and the house of thy father, even they have dealt treacherously with thee; yea, they have called a multitude after thee: believe them not, though they speak fair words unto thee.

α.12.7 Nunnukkodtum nek: nunnukkodtum nutohtóonk: neh nuttah womononcheh, noh nummagun wunu[n]tchegan8wout ummatwomoh.
E.12.7 I have forsaken mine house, I have left mine heritage; I have given the dearly beloved of my soul into the hand of her enemies.

α.12.8 Nutohtóonk tatuppeyeu8 ut nuhhogkat qunnonou$ut, nutayeuuhkonittue mishont8anumunk newaj sekeneam.
E.12.8 Mine heritage is unto me as a lion in the forest; it crieth out against me: therefore have I hated it.

α.12.9 Nutohtóonk tatuppeyeu8 ut nuhhogkat chohchohkésue psuksesut, waéene psuksesog wutayeuhkonóuh: peyunk, miyaek kenaau wame ohteakône puppinashimwog nónche mahchep8k.
E.12.9 Mine heritage is unto me as a speckled bird, the birds round about are against her; come ye, assemble all the beasts of the field, come to devour.

α.12.10 Monaog pastorsog pagwadtóog n8wenominneohteuk, nag tahtaskuhkomwog nutchippiyeum agwe wusseetowóut: n8ne chippáiyeum wuttauushine touohkomukquhkóneau.
E.12.10 Many pastors have destroyed my vineyard, they have trodden my portion under foot, they have made my pleasant portion a desolate wilderness.

α.12.11 Wuttauushitteauuneau, kah tâuushik nummauunnitteunkqun, mamusse ohke tauushitteáuun, newutche matta howan upponam8un wuttahhut.
E.12.11 They have made it desolate, and being desolate it mourneth unto me; the whole land is made desolate, because no man layeth it to heart.

α.12.12 Matchehteauwaenúog nuhkuhkomwog wame qunuhqui ayeuongaṣh papashpe touohkomukqut: newutche wuttogkodteg Jehovah piṣh pagwohteom8, wutch weekqshik ohke, onk ya$en aongkoue: wanne weyaus piṣh wunohteómun8.
E.12.12 The spoilers are come upon all high places through the wilderness: for the sword of the LORD shall devour from the one end of the land even to the other end of the land: no flesh shall have peace.

α.12.13 Ohkehteopanneg wheatash qut nag pish kepenumwog asinnekoussoh: ponaog wuhhogkauh onkquommamwunneat, matta wutchienat, kah nag pish akodchuwontamwog k8chiyeuonkan8oash newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk J[é]hovah.
E.12.13 They have sown wheat, but shall reap thorns: they have put themselves to pain, but shall not profit: and they shall be ashamed of your revenues because of the fierce anger of the LORD.

α.12.14 Yeu wutayeuuhkonittue unnon Jehovah wamé nummatchetowé weetatteamungoh, neg masinukeg oht[ó]onk ne ohtauaheog nummissinn[n]inneumoh Israel, kusseh nag, nukkodtinoog wutch wutohkeout, kah nukkodtinum week Judah wutch nag kenugke.
E.12.14 Thus saith the LORD against all mine evil neighbours, that touch the inheritance which I have caused my people Israel to inherit; Behold, I will pluck them out of their land, and pluck out the house of Judah from among them.

α.12.15 Kah pish n$nih, mahche kodtinog, pish nukqushkem kah pish nukkitteamonteanumoog, kah wonk nuppas8 nish$noh wosktomp ut wutohtoônganit, kah nish$noh pasuk ut wutohkeit.
E.12.15 And it shall come to pass, after that I have plucked them out I will return, and have compassion on them, and will bring them again, every man to his heritage, and every man to his land.

α.12.16 Kah pish n$nih nag menuhke kodnetuhtauwehettit ummayeuoash nummissinninnumog, chadchekeyeuonat nashpe n8wesuonk (Jehovah pomantam, neane kuhk8tomauwahettit nummissinninnumoh chadchekeyeuonat nashpe Baal) neit pish weekitteaog ut nasháuwe nummissinninnumut.
E.12.16 And it shall come to pass, if they will diligently learn the ways of my people, to swear by my name, The LORD liveth; as they taught my people to swear by Baal; then shall they be built in the midst of my people.

α.12.17 Qut matta nosweetamohetteg, pish nuppapukquané kodtinnumun kah pagu[á]tauun ne wutohtimoin, wussin Jehovah.
E.12.17 But if they will not obey, I will utterly pluck up and destroy that nation, saith the LORD.

α.13.1 YEu nuttugqun Jehovah, monchish, nanashweetash womponákinne puttukquobpus, kah ponsh kussegkonóhtugqut, kah ponam8hkon nippeit,
E.13.1 Thus saith the LORD unto me, Go and get thee a linen girdle, and put it upon thy loins, and put it not in water.

α.13.2 Neit nukquagquashwe[h]tamup puttugquobpus neaunag wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kah nupponamu[n]ah nusségonohtugqut.
E.13.2 So I got a girdle according to the word of the LORD, and put it on my loins.

α.13.3 Kah wuttinnowaonk Jehovah nahohtôeu nuppeyaónuk, n8wop,
E.13.3 And the word of the LORD came unto me the second time, saying,

α.13.4 Nemunush puttugquobpus ne quagquoshwehtamop, ne ohtag kussegonohtogqut, kah neepaush, âush Euphrates, na$ut adtahtaush ut qussukquane wónogqut.
E.13.4 Take the girdle that thou hast got, which is upon thy loins, and arise, go to Euphrates, and hide it there in a hole of the rock.

α.13.5 Neit nummonchip, kah nutadtahtauun ut kishke Euphrates, neanann8sit Jehovah.
E.13.5 So I went, and hid it by Euphrates, as the LORD commanded me.

α.13.6 Kah nnihyeup mahche m8chetikqunogkok, Lord nuttinuk, neepaush, àush Euphrates, kah na wuttinuh puttukquobpus, ne an8nop na$ut adtahtauunat[.]
E.13.6 And it came to pass after many days, that the LORD said unto me, Arise, go to Euphrates, and take the girdle from thence, which I commanded thee to hide there.

α.13.7 Neit nuttomp Euphrates, ka[g] nukkuthamun, kah n8tinum puttukquobpus ne adt adtahtauomp, kah kusseh, puttukquobpus anit, matta toh unnompâmunkquodtinn8.
E.13.7 Then I went to Euphrates, and digged, and took the girdle from the place where I had hid it: and, behold, the girdle was marred, it was profitable for nothing.

α.13.8 Neit wuttinn8wáonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, n8wau,
E.13.8 Then the word of the LORD came unto me, saying,

α.13.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah, yeu nuttinne matchehteauun uppehtuanumóonk Judah, kah ummishe pehtuanumóonk Jerusalem.
E.13.9 Thus saith the LORD, After this manner will I mar the pride of Judah, and the great pride of Jerusalem.

α.13.10 Yeug matcheetoe missinninnúog neg sekeneogig n8tamunat nuttinn8waongash, neg paumushácheg ut matche metahh8wae unnantam8onganit, kah ásuhkauóncheg onkatogeh manitt8h, nag wowussumonat, kah peantamauónat, nag pish tatuppeyeu8og yeu puttugquoppissinit, ne matta toh ánompâmukquodtin8g.
E.13.10 This evil people, which refuse to hear my words, which walk in the imagination of their heart, and walk after other gods, to serve them, and to worship them, shall even be as this girdle, which is good for nothing.

α.13.11 Newutche neane puttukquobpus ogquám8k wussegonóhtugqut wosketomp, ne nuttinne ogquamwehteauun nuhhogkat mamusse Israelle wek, kah mamusse Judae wek, wussin Jehovah, onk woh nag n8missinneumúneunk, kah wutch wesuonk, kah wutche waeenodtuonk, kah wutche sohsumóonk, qut nag matta n8tam8og.
E.13.11 For as the girdle cleaveth to the loins of a man, so have I caused to cleave unto me the whole house of Israel and the whole house of Judah, saith the LORD; that they might be unto me for a people, and for a name, and for a praise, and for a glory: but they would not hear.

α.13.12 Newutche pish unnádt yeu kutt8onk, yeu wussin Lord um$Manitt8moh Israel, nish$noh wisq pish numwohtauun wine, kah nag pish kuttugquog, sunnummatta nuppapannuppe wahteomun, nishnoh wisq piṣh numw[â]panau wine?
E.13.12 Therefore thou shalt speak unto them this word; Thus saith the LORD God of Israel, Every bottle shall be filled with wine: and they shall say unto thee, Do we not certainly know that every bottle shall be filled with wine?

α.13.13 Neit piṣh nag kuttinóog, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, pish nunnumwohtauóog wame wadohkitcheg yeu ohkeit, kehtass8tamwog neg apitcheg ut wutappuonganit David, kah sephausuenuog, kah quoshódtumwaénuog, kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, nashpe kogkeissippam8onk.
E.13.13 Then shalt thou say unto them, Thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will fill all the inhabitants of this land, even the kings that sit upon David's throne, and the priests, and the prophets, and all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, with drunkenness.

α.13.14 Kah nuppápashkuhkónunk, wut8shimóog, kah wunnaumonáuh moeu wussin Jehovah, matta nukkitteamonteanumoh, qut nag nuppaguanóog.
E.13.14 And I will dash them one against another, even the fathers and the sons together, saith the LORD: I will not pity, nor spare, nor have mercy, but destroy them.

α.13.15 N8tam8k kah kuhkeitam8k, pittuanumúhteok, newutche Jehovah wussin.
E.13.15 Hear ye, and give ear; be not proud: for the LORD hath spoken.

α.13.16 Sohsum8wáheuk Jehovah kum-Manitt8m8, asquam papohkina[n]teagkup, kah asquam kusseet8ash ta[g]shinheug pohkenae wadchuuhkontu, kah nadtauwompadtamóg wequai, ukquinnuppinnumun en nupp8onk, wutonkauontomut, ukkúhpogke po[h]kináhko[n]
E.13.16 Give glory to the LORD your God, before he cause darkness, and before your feet stumble upon the dark mountains, and, while ye look for light, he turn it into the shadow of death, and make it gross darkness.

α.13.17 Qut matta n8tam8og, nukketeahogkou pish keme mau wutche kuppehtuánum8ongan8, kah nuskesukquaṣh piṣh mauée mau8m8aṣh, kah penutchuanash nussippegwash, newutche uf-flockum Jehovah missinae monchadtauun.
E.13.17 But if ye will not hear it, my soul shall weep in secret places for your pride; and mine eye shall weep sore, and run down with tears, because the LORD's flock is carried away captive.

α.13.18 Us ketass8t, kah sonksquaut, hohpaheuk kuhhogkaoog, nummatappek, newutche k8puhkuhk88onk pish n8keem8, kutchetuhquabee sohsumoonk.
E.13.18 Say unto the king and to the queen, Humble yourselves, sit down: for your principalities shall come down, even the crown of your glory.

α.13.19 Sowaniyeue keitotanash pish kuppohhosuash kah mattá pish howan 8woshwunnum8unash, Judah pish missinnae monchanau, neg wame pish mamusse missinohko[n]unk.
E.13.19 The cities of the south shall be shut up, and none shall open them: Judah shall be carried away captive all of it, it shall be wholly carried away captive.

α.13.20 Táhshinum8k kuskesuk8oash, kah nok neg wagig nanumiyeu, uttiyeu flock ne ut anumauunumuk, ne wanégik flock?
E.13.20 Lift up your eyes, and behold them that come from the north: where is the flock that was given thee, thy beautiful flock?

α.13.21 Toh pish kussim sasamatahhukquean, (newutché nag kukkuhk8tomauoog ummummugquompainneaout k8puhkuhqunneat) sunnummatta pish onkquanum8onk kutogque tohqunnumunat mittamwossis neechadt?
E.13.21 What wilt thou say when he shall punish thee? for thou hast taught them to be captains, and as chief over thee: shall not sorrows take thee, as a woman in travail?

α.13.22 Kah n8waan ut kuttahhut, tohwutch yeush nuhkuhkiit, wutché mohsag kummatcheseonk kussissippoe hogk8onk waahsheau, kah kogquanash pôhshkohtaash.
E.13.22 And if thou say in thine heart, Wherefore come these things upon me?  For the greatness of thine iniquity are thy skirts discovered, and thy heels made bare.

α.13.23 M8adthogk8nas sun woh 8wompheuh wuttuhquab, asuh Leópard wutchohchohkesuongash? neit kenaau wonk woh k8nhukquneau, nag wutteae matcheseog.
E.13.23 Can the Ethiopian change his skin, or the leopard his spots? then may ye also do good, that are accustomed to do evil.

α.13.24 Newaj ogquesewahhog sequékepenum8onganit, ne pamshunk nashpe touohkomukque waban.
E.13.24 Therefore will I scatter them as the stubble that passeth away by the wind of the wilderness.

α.13.25 Yeu kuttittanohkitteaonk, kukquthum8e chippiyeum nashpe neen, wussin Lord, newutche k8wannanumeh, kuppabuhtantam pann8waonk.
E.13.25 This is thy lot, the portion of thy measures from me, saith the LORD; because thou hast forgotten me, and trusted in falsehood.

α.13.26 Newaj naumwahuwi kussissippoe hogk8 ut woskeche kesukqut, onk woh kúkkosuonk nogquodt.
E.13.26 Therefore will I discover thy skirts upon thy face, that thy shame may appear.

α.13.27 Nunnaumup kummamussuongash, kah kukkogkeinw8dsquaongash, kah kenishkeneungque mánisquaôsuongash, kah kutuhquneunkquodt8mash, ut ohteuhkonue wádchuuhkontu: missi kutonkapunaónk woi Jerusalem, sun mátta pish kuppahkhetteoh? uttoh adt8che woh nnag?
E.13.27 I have seen thine adulteries, and thy neighings, the lewdness of thy whoredom, and thine abominations on the hills in the fields. Woe unto thee, O Jerusalem! wilt thou not be made clean? when shall it once be?

α.14.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah, ne pauhônukqut Jéremiah papaume mahshagquodt.
E.14.1 The word of the LORD that came to Jeremiah concerning the dearth.

α.14.2 Judah mau, kah 8squontamash mahchim8, m8esuog pajeh ohkeit, kah ummauonk Jerusalem kuhkuhquem8.
E.14.2 Judah mourneth, and the gates thereof languish; they are black unto the ground; and the cry of Jerusalem is gone up.

α.14.3 Kah ukkehtauwom8uh ann8naog uppeissesum8uh en nippekontu, nag peyaog pasahtheganehtu, kah mat namehteauoog nippe, nag qushkeog mahchayeue wishquadt nag akodchuog, kah chepshaog, kah puttogquequohh8og.
E.14.3 And their nobles have sent their little ones to the waters: they came to the pits, and found no water; they returned with their vessels empty; they were ashamed and confounded, and covered their heads.

α.14.4 Néwutche ohke passohteaem8, newutche matta sokanonunn8 óhkeit, anaskhamwaenuog akodchuog, nag onkhumwog uppuhkuk88ash.
E.14.4 Because the ground is chapt, for there was no rain in the earth, the plowmen were ashamed, they covered their heads.

α.14.5 Nux, quenegq wonk neechau ut ohteuhkonit, kah wunnukkonuh, newutche matta moskehtuun8.
E.14.5 Yea, the hind also calved in the field, and forsook it, because there was no grass.

α.14.6 Kah touohkomukque assesog neneepattag qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, nag assonómáog waban onatuh dragonsog: wuskesuk88ash nupp8m8aṣh newutche matta moskehtuun8
E.14.6 And the wild asses did stand in the high places, they snuffed up the wind like dragons; their eyes did fail, because there was no grass.

α.14.7 Woi Jehovah, tôhkonogque nummatcheseonganunonaṣh n8wauwaónukqunnanonaṣh, ne ussish wutche k8wesuonk: newutche nutassôéhpósuonganunonaṣh monataṣh, kummatchenéhennumun.
E.14.7 O LORD, though our iniquities testify against us, do thou it for thy name's sake: for our backslidings are many; we have sinned against thee.

α.14.8 Woi ken wutannoósuonk Israel, 8wadchanuwaénumoh wuttamehpunadt: tohwutch ya[n]éewéan penuwohteaut ut ohkeit, kah onatuh pomushaénin, noh quánupit nóquttukqunóhteat?
E.14.8 O the hope of Israel, the saviour thereof in time of trouble, why shouldest thou be as a stranger in the land, and as a wayfaring man that turneth aside to tarry for a night?

α.14.9 Tohwutch woh yanéeuwéan noh chepshont, onatuh menuhkesuen noh matta woh pohquohham8k? qut onch woi ken Jehovah nunnashómunonat kutap, kah nutuss8wénitteamun k8wesuonk, ahque nukóhsinan.
E.14.9 Why shouldest thou be as a man astonied, as a mighty man that cannot save? yet thou, O LORD, art in the midst of us, and we are called by thy name; leave us not.

α.14.10 Yeu wuttinnon Jehovah, yeúh missinninnúh, yeuh wuttinne womantamuneau nanwiyin, matta quihtittam8og wusseet8oàsh, newaj Jehovah matta tapeneáwonk, yeuyeu mehquontam nag ummatcheseongan8oaṣh, kah natawóhtou ummatcheseonganooaṣh.
E.14.10 Thus saith the LORD unto this people, Thus have they loved to wander, they have not refrained their feet, therefore the LORD doth not accept them; he will now remember their iniquity, and visit their sins.

α.14.11 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, peantamwanshúhkon yeug missinninnuog, wutche 8niyeuongan8.
E.14.11 Then said the LORD unto me, Pray not for this people for their good.

α.14.12 Mat meetséhetteg matta nunn8tam8 ummauongan8, kah maghettit chikohtae mag8ongash kah mag8onk, matta nuttapeneauóog: qut nag nuppaguanóog nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mashagquod, kah nashpe pagwanúonk.
E.14.12 When they fast, I will not hear their cry; and when they offer burnt offering and an oblation, I will not accept them: but I will consume them by the sword, and by the famine, and by the pestilence.

α.14.13 Neit nussip, woi Lord Jehovah, kusseh, quoshodtumwaenuog wuttinóuh, matta pish kenaum8m8 togkodteg, kah matta pish kummishagqunneów8, qut kuttinnumauunumw8 wunnamuhkutée wunohteáonk, yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.14.13 Then said I, Ah, Lord GOD! behold, the prophets say unto them, Ye shall not see the sword, neither shall ye have famine; but I will give you assured peace in this place.

α.14.14 Neit J[e]hovah nuttinuk, quoshodtumwaenuog pann8wae quoshodtumwog ut n8wesuonganit, matta nag nutann8nóog, kah matta nutann8konóog, kah matta nukken8noog; nag nukquoshae missohhamun8óog pann8wae monomansuonk kah mosinunkquodt, kah monteagwuninn8g, kah wuttahh8wae as8kekodteam8ongan8.
E.14.14 Then the LORD said unto me, The prophets prophesy lies in my name: I sent them not, neither have I commanded them, neither spake unto them: they prophesy unto you a false vision and divination, and a thing of nought, and the deceit of their heart.

α.14.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume quoshodtumwaenúog neg quoshodtukeg ut n8wesuonganit, kah matta nutann8nóog, onch nag n8waog, togkodteg kah mahshagquodt matta pish yeu o[h]tano ohkeit, nashpe togkodteg kah mahshagquodt yeug quoshodtumwaenuog piṣh paguan8og.
E.14.15 Therefore thus saith the LORD concerning the prophets that prophesy in my name, and I sent them not, yet they say, Sword and famine shall not be in this land; By sword and famine shall those prophets be consumed.

α.14.16 Kah missinninnúog neh kohk8tomauwáhetticheh, nag piṣh sohw[e]ôkonunk ut Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu newutche mahshagquodt, kah togkodteg, kah matt piṣh howan uppósekinuh, asuh um̃ittamwuss8oh, asuh wunnaumonáuh, asuh wuttaun8oh, newutche nussókanónukk[ó]ntam ummatcheseongan8oaṣh.
E.14.16 And the people to whom they prophesy shall be cast out in the streets of Jerusalem because of the famine and the sword; and they shall have none to bury them, them, their wives, nor their sons, nor their daughters: for I will pour their wickedness upon them.

α.14.17 Newutche yeu kutt8onk piṣh kuttinnóneau, nuskesukquaṣh nuhkonáe kah kesukodtae pomitchuaj nussippegwash, kah matta tahshéyeuitch: newutche peenompáe wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog, pokshanáog nashpe mishe pokshaonk, kah nashpe ahche unkqunneunkquodte togkodtuonk.
E.14.17 Therefore thou shalt say this word unto them; Let mine eyes run down with tears night and day, and let them not cease: for the virgin daughter of my people is broken with a great breach, with a very grievous blow.

α.14.18 Sohhaman en ohteuhkonit, neit kusseh, náhshitcheg nashpe togkodteg; petutteaon otan, neit kusseh, neg mahchinacheg nashpe mahshagquodt: nux naneeswe quoshodtumwaen, kah sephausuwaen quinnuppuhkomwog ohkeit ne matta wahteauhetteg.
E.14.18 If I go forth into the field, then behold the slain with the sword!  and if I enter into the city, then behold them that are sick with famine!  yea, both the prophet and the priest go about into a land that they know not.

α.14.19 Sun ken papaquanne kuppogken Judah? sun kukketeahogkou uhquontam Zion? tohwutch togkomeog, kah matta n8neetskehuwaenúm8mun? natauwompadtamumun wunohteaonk, kah matta wunnegeninno, kah neetskehettue ahquompi, kah kusseh wuttaméhpunáonk.
E.14.19 Hast thou utterly rejected Judah? hath thy soul lothed Zion? why hast thou smitten us, and there is no healing for us? we looked for peace, and there is no good; and for the time of healing, and behold trouble!

α.14.20 Nussamp8womun, woi Jehovah, nummatcheseonganun, kah ummatcheseongan8 n8shunónog, newutche kummatchenéhenumun.
E.14.20 We acknowledge, O LORD, our wickedness, and the iniquity of our fathers: for we have sinned against thee.

α.14.21 Ahque unkquanuminnean wutche k8wesuonk mishanontogkon kussohsumoe appuonk, mehquontaṣh: ahque pohquenumaiinnean k8n8waonganun.
E.14.21 Do not abhor us, for thy name's sake, do not disgrace the throne of thy glory: remember, break not thy covenant with us.

α.14.22 Sun howae kenugke tahwunn8cheyeum8 Gentilsog, noh woh sokanonukôsit? asuh sun woh kesukquash sokanónitteam8ash? sunnummatta ken, noh woi Lord num-manitt8mun? ne waj pahtussuónunog, newutche wame yeush ken kesteauunash.
E.14.22 Are there any among the vanities of the Gentiles that can cause rain? or can the heavens give showers? art not thou he, O LORD our God?  therefore we will wait upon thee: for thou hast made all these things.

α.15.1 NEit Lord nuttinuk, tohkônogque Moses kah Samuel wunneepauun anaquabeh, onch nuttah matta ómun8 nogque en yeug missinninnuog: nag sohwhôteash wutch anaquabeh, kah sohhamwéhettich.
E.15.1 Then said the LORD unto me, Though Moses and Samuel stood before me, yet my mind could not be toward this people: cast them out of my sight, and let them go forth.

α.15.2 Kah piṣh n$nih, nag unnukquean, uttoh nuttin sohhamunán? neit piṣh nag kuttinóog, yeu wussin Lord, neg wadchiitcheg nushittuonganit, en nuppunát: kah neg wadchiitcheg togkodteganit, en togkodteganit, kah neg wadchiitcheg mahshagquodtut en mahshagqu[ó]dtut, kah neg wadchiitcheg missinnáiinneat, en missinnáinneat.
E.15.2 And it shall come to pass, if they say unto thee, Whither shall we go forth? then thou shalt tell them, Thus saith the LORD; Such as are for death, to death; and such as are for the sword, to the sword; and such as are for the famine, to the famine; and such as are for the captivity, to the captivity.

α.15.3 Kah nukkuhquttumauóog yauwechippaiyeuash, wussin Lord, togkodteg nushittinneat kah anumwog nehnekikôsineàt, kah kesukque puppinashasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwog en mahchipwunneat kah pagwohkonat.
E.15.3 And I will appoint over them four kinds, saith the LORD: the sword to slay, and the dogs to tear, and the fowls of the heaven, and the beasts of the earth, to devour and destroy.

α.15.4 Kah ontappehéoog, en wame ohkée as8tam8onganit, newutche Manasseh wunnaumonuh Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, wutche ne ásip ut Jerusalem.
E.15.4 And I will cause them to be removed into all kingdoms of the earth, because of Manasseh the son of Hezekiah king of Judah, for that which he did in Jerusalem.

α.15.5 Newutche howan woh kódtumonteanumukquean woi Jerusalem? kah howan woh kummauunnitteauwánshik, asuh howan woh páhchadt 8wahteauunat tôh aniyean.
E.15.5 For who shall have pity upon thee, O Jerusalem? or who shall bemoan thee? or who shall go aside to ask how thou doest?

α.15.6 Kutohquanumeh wussin Lord, kutassóushám: ne$waj summagunum nuhpit ayeuuhkonittue ken, kah kenushish, nussauunum aiuskoianatamunat.
E.15.6 Thou hast forsaken me, saith the LORD, thou art gone backward: therefore will I stretch out my hand against thee, and destroy thee; I am weary with repenting.

α.15.7 Nag nuppáuanomóog nashpe pauunóntunk, ut ohkee squontaméhtu: nummukk8kinóog wunneechan8oh, nuppagwan nummissinninnúmog, newutche matta qushkéog wutch ummayeuóut.
E.15.7 And I will fan them with a fan in the gates of the land; I will bereave them of children, I will destroy my people since they return not from their ways.

α.15.8 Wussekousquóm8uh nano m8naoh en nuhhogkat onk ne ketahhanne nagunt: nunnuhkinnumauóog, ayeuuhkonittue wutókasin, wuskenuog, pohshuhqu[á]e mukk8kinnuaenúog: nukkenuppe quentamwaheon, kah wabesuonganú88k ut keitotanat.
E.15.8 Their widows are increased to me above the sand of the seas: I have brought upon them against the mother of the young men a spoiler at noonday: I have caused him to fall upon it suddenly, and terrors upon the city.

α.15.9 Noh nesausuk tahsuoh neechadt mahchimm8, nupp8, wunnuppauzs8moh wayaoh ash kesuk88k: mahche akodchu kah chepshau, kah nag ashqshoncheg nupponoog togkodteganit, anquabhettit ummatwom8oh, wussin Jehovah.
E.15.9 She that hath borne seven languisheth: she hath given up the ghost; her sun is gone down while it was yet day: she hath been ashamed and confounded: and the residue of them will I deliver to the sword before their enemies, saith the LORD.

α.15.10 Missi nutonkapunaonk, woi nokas, newutche keneekitteah penuanittue wosketomp, kah mekonteaenin ut mamusse ohkeit: matt[t]a nunnanamohkouehhuwoh ontsompadtamoonk, asah matta howan ontsompadtam8e nagoh kouhuk8, qut onch nish$noh pasuk nummatanumwe unnukquog.
E.15.10 Woe is me, my mother, that thou hast borne me a man of strife and a man of contention to the whole earth! I have neither lent on usury, nor men have lent to me on usury; yet every one of them doth curse me.

α.15.11 Lord n8wop wunnamuhkut pish k8nenanumukqutteauunun matwau matche ahquompak, kah wuttamehpunae ahquompag.
E.15.11 The LORD said, Verily it shall be well with thy remnant; verily I will cause the enemy to entreat thee well in the time of evil and in the time of affliction.

α.15.12 Sun pish missehchuog poksheau nanumiyeue missehchuog, kah menuhkequog?
E.15.12 Shall iron break the northern iron and the steel?

α.15.13 Kuttinneetuonk kah kenompakouunash, matta tahnoadtue nummag ut mukk8kinnuonganit, wutche wame kummatcheseongan8oash, en wame kussissippoiyeumut.
E.15.13 Thy substance and thy treasures will I give to the spoil without price, and that for all thy sins, even in all thy borders.

α.15.14 Kah kuppannupwushahush nashpe kummatwomog en ohkeit ne mo wahteauouan: newutche n8teau nashquneau ut nummusquanittam8onganit, ne pish chogohsukqueog.
E.15.14 And I will make thee to pass with thine enemies into a land which thou knowest not: for a fire is kindled in mine anger, which shall burn upon you.

α.15.15 Woi Jehovah k8wahteoh, mehquanumeh, kah natauwaheh, kah ann8tauwa[n]sheh waskhikqueoneg, amanehkon nashpe kussepepahtoonk: wahteaush, wutche ken nutchequnehtam auskontuonk.
E.15.15 O LORD, thou knowest: remember me, and visit me, and revenge me of my persecutors; take me not away in thy longsuffering: know that for thy sake I have suffered rebuke.

α.15.16 Kukutt8wongash namehteauunash, kah nash nummeech[in]apash, kah kukkutt8onk kah nummoskouantamwahik n8weekontamwutteah[a]hik: newutche nuttissowes k8wesuonk, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh ayeuhteaog.
E.15.16 Thy words were found, and I did eat them; and thy word was unto me the joy and rejoicing of mine heart: for I am called by thy name, O LORD God of hosts.

α.15.17 Matta nutappeup ummoeongan8ont momontohsuenuog: kah matta n8weekontam8p: nunnussappip newutche kenutcheg: newutche kenumwohtoh jishontamoonk.
E.15.17 I sat not in the assembly of the mockers, nor rejoiced; I sat alone because of thy hand: for thou hast filled me with indignation.

α.15.18 Tohwutch nagwutteohtag nutonkquomom8onk? kah nunn8chumweteawutteaonk matta neetskehteauouun sekeneam8m8 neetkehteauunat? sun pish pannuppe kutogquanumeh pann8waenuut, ut nunohtae nippeut.
E.15.18 Why is my pain perpetual, and my wound incurable, which refuseth to be healed? wilt thou be altogether unto me as a liar, and as waters that fail?

α.15.19 Newutche yeu n8wau Jehovah, qushkean, neit pish wonk kuppas8ush, kah pish keneepau anaquabeh kah amaunuman mahshoadtitcheg wutch kenugke nishkeneunkqussitcheg, pish kuttatuppeyeu nutt8nut: nag qushkehettich en kuhhogkaiyeu, qut n[á] en qushkehkon.
E.15.19 Therefore thus saith the LORD, If thou return, then will I bring thee again, and thou shalt stand before me: and if thou take forth the precious from the vile, thou shalt be as my mouth: let them return unto thee; but return not thou unto them.

α.15.20 Kah kutayeuush pummenutohsue brasse wonkonous en yeug missinninnuog, kah nag pish kutayeuuhkonukquog, qut nag pish matta kussohkunk8og: newutche nen k8weetomsh k8wadchanukqunat, kah kuppohquohwhunukqunat, wussin Jehovah.
E.15.20 And I will make thee unto this people a fenced brasen wall: and they shall fight against thee, but they shall not prevail against thee: for I am with thee to save thee and to deliver thee, saith the LORD.

α.15.21 Kah kuppohquohwhunush wutch wunnutcheganit matcheetou, kah kummanouwhush wutch wunnutcheganit unkqueneunkqussit.
E.15.21 And I will deliver thee out of the hand of the wicked, and I will redeem thee out of the hand of the terrible.

α.16.1 WOnk wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
E.16.1 The word of the LORD came also unto me, saying,

α.16.2 Matta pish k8mittamwussissu, kah matta pish k8naumoniyeu asuh k8tauniyeu, yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.16.2 Thou shalt not take thee a wife, neither shalt thou have sons or daughters in this place.

α.16.3 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, papaume wunnaumoniinneunk, kah papaume wuttauneunk neg nekitcheg yeu ut ayeuonganit kah papaume okas8oh neh neekhukqhetticheh, kah papaume wut8shineunk waneechânukkônukquehetticheh yeu ut ohkeit.
E.16.3 For thus saith the LORD concerning the sons and concerning the daughters that are born in this place, and concerning their mothers that bare them, and concerning their fathers that begat them in this land;

α.16.4 Nag pish onkquommom8e nupwog, nag matta pish mauemóog, asuh matta pish posekinóog: qut nag pish tatuppeyeu8og anóhke ut woskeche ohkeit, kah nag pish mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah wuhhogkauh ummeetsuongan8 kesukque puppinshaog, kah ohkée puppinashimwog.
E.16.4 They shall die of grievous deaths; they shall not be lamented; neither shall they be buried; but they shall be as dung upon the face of the earth: and they shall be consumed by the sword, and by famine; and their carcases shall be meat for the fowls of heaven, and for the beasts of the earth.

α.16.5 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, petutteúhkon mauongane wetu[ô]mut, kah ahque aush ut maumuttamunat asuh mohkon: newutche nutamaunum n8nohteaonk wutch yeug missinninnuog, wussin Jehovah, womoausuonk kah monaneteaongash.
E.16.5 For thus saith the LORD, Enter not into the house of mourning, neither go to lament nor bemoan them: for I have taken away my peace from this people, saith the LORD, even lovingkindness and mercies.

α.16.6 Naneeswe matikkenukeg kah papeissiṣsitcheg pish nupwog yeu ut ohkeit: matta pish posekinóog, kah wosketompaog matta pish ummauemouh, kah matta pish neekswóunáuh wuhhogkuh, asuh mukukkontupauóog.
E.16.6 Both the great and the small shall die in this land: they shall not be buried, neither shall men lament for them, nor cut themselves, nor make themselves bald for them:

α.16.7 Asuh matta pish wosketompaog nehneekinauoog maumuttamunat, taphe[ò]nat wuhhogkauh: asuh pish mat wosketompaog 8tattamwaheouh taphettue wuttattamwaitche wutche wut8shin, kah wutohkasin.
E.16.7 Neither shall men tear themselves for them in mourning, to comfort them for the dead; neither shall men give them the cup of consolation to drink for their father or for their mother.

α.16.8 Wonk matta pish kuppetutteoh mishadtupp8e-kommukqut, nag weetappemónat, meetsinat asuh wuttattamunat.
E.16.8 Thou shalt not also go into the house of feasting, to sit with them to eat and to drink.

α.16.9 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, n8wohkukquoshitteóh, yeu wutch ayeuonganit ut anaquabeóg kah pomantamóg, pôáe wodtauatonkquossuonk, weekontamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk wessentamwaénin, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauwadteaénin.
E.16.9 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will cause to cease out of this place in your eyes, and in your days, the voice of mirth, and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride.

α.16.10 Kah piṣh nnih wahteauwaheadt yeug missinninnuog wame yeush kutt8wongash, kah nag unnukquean, tohwaj Jehovah kutt8hkontog wame yeu mohsag machuk ayeuuhkone nenawun? kah teagwas nummatcheseonganun, asuh teagwas nummatcheseonganun, asuh teagwas nuppanneseonganun, ne ayeuhkonittue unnéhheungkut Jehovah num-Manitt8mun?
E.16.10 And it shall come to pass, when thou shalt shew this people all these words, and they shall say unto thee, Wherefore hath the LORD pronounced all this great evil against us? or what is our iniquity? or what is our sin that we have committed against the LORD our God?

α.16.11 Neit nag piṣh kuttinnóog, newutche k8sh8oog nutohquanumuk, wussin Jehovah, kah asuhkauaog onkatogeh manitt8h, kah wuttinneumuhkauóuh, kah wowussumouh, kah nutohquanumukquog, kah matta nanawehheauóog nuttinnaumatuonk.
E.16.11 Then shalt thou say unto them, Because your fathers have forsaken me, saith the LORD, and have walked after other gods, and have served them, and have worshipped them, and have forsaken me, and have not kept my law;

α.16.12 Kah nag anue matcheseúmaog k8sh8uh (newutche kusseh kutasuhkomumw8 nishnoh pasuk ummatchitteaháe unnántam8onk, onk woh nag mat nukkuhkeitonk8og)
E.16.12 And ye have done worse than your fathers; for, behold, ye walk every one after the imagination of his evil heart, that they may not hearken unto me:

α.16.13 Newaj sohwòhkónunóg yeu wutch ohkeit, en ohkeit ne mo wahteau8óg, asuh k8sh8óog: kah na piṣh kuttit wowussumóneau penowe manitt8og kesukodae kah nukkonae, kah na kuttit matta kitteamonteanumunn[n]eau.
E.16.13 Therefore will I cast you out of this land into a land that ye know not, neither ye nor your fathers; and there shall ye serve other gods day and night; where I will not shew you favour.

α.16.14 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8ash wussin Lord, matta piṣh wonk unn8wáun, Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp wunnaumonuh Israel wutch Egypt.
E.16.14 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that it shall no more be said, The LORD liveth, that brought up the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt;

α.16.15 Qut Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp wunnaumonuh Israel wutch nanumohkeit, kah wame ohketu uttoh an8hkauomp: kah piṣh wonk nuppas8óog wutohtuóut ne anumauogkup 8sh8oh.
E.16.15 But, The LORD liveth, that brought up the children of Israel from the land of the north, and from all the lands whither he had driven them: and I will bring them again into their land that I gave unto their fathers.

α.16.16 Kusseh, nutann8n monacheg n8tamágwaénúog, wussin Jehovah, kah nag piṣh nah wunn8tamagquonóuh, kah nahohtoeu piṣh nutann8n monacheg adchaenúog, kah nag piṣh wutadchanóuh wutch nishnoh wadchu, kah wutch nishnoh wadchuém: kah wutch hassunónogqut.
E.16.16 Behold, I will send for many fishers, saith the LORD, and they shall fish them; and after will I send for many hunters, and they shall hunt them from every mountain, and from every hill, and out of the holes of the rocks.

α.16.17 Newutche nuskesukquash ohtaash wame ummayeuóut: niṣh matta adtahtâunóash wutch kuskesukqut: kah umm[at]ch[e]seongan8 matta adtahtôsin8 wutch nuskesukqut.
E.16.17 For mine eyes are upon all their ways: they are not hid from my face, neither is their iniquity hid from mine eyes.

α.16.18 Kah negonne nutonkquadtantam ummatcheseonganoash, kah uppanneseongash papsku, newutche nishketeóog nutohke: n[à]g numwohtoog nutohtóonk nashpe nupp8e muhhogkunk jishanumukquokish kah unkqueneunkquokish.
E.16.18 And first I will recompense their iniquity and their sin double; because they have defiled my land, they have filled mine inheritance with the carcases of their detestable and abominable things.

α.16.19 Woi Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk kah n8wonkônous, kah nutushpho[u]áonk wuttaméhpunae kesukodtut, Gentilsog piṣh kuppeyaonuk wutch weehqshik ohke, kah piṣh n8waog, wunnamuhkut n8shunónog nompappéhtamwog pann8waongash, tahn8cheyeu8k, kah niṣh matta wadchiyeumukish.
E.16.19 O LORD, my strength, and my fortress, and my refuge in the day of affliction, the Gentiles shall come unto thee from the ends of the earth, and shall say, Surely our fathers have inherited lies, vanity, and things wherein there is no profit.

α.16.20 Sun woh wosketomp ummanitt8muhkauau wuhhogkuh, kah nag matta manitto8og?
E.16.20 Shall a man make gods unto himself, and they are no gods?

α.16.21 Newutche kusseh, pasukqut piṣh n8wahteauwaheoog: n8wahteauwahéoog nunnutcheg, nummenuhkesuonk, kah piṣh wahteauog nuttissowis Jehovah.
E.16.21 Therefore, behold, I will this once cause them to know, I will cause them to know mine hand and my might; and they shall know that my name is The LORD.

α.17.1 UMmatcheseonk Judah wussukwhósu nashpe moóshogque pen: kah nashpe wuhk8nuk diamond: ne kogóhksimun ut wuttahh8wae tableut, kah ut kutaltarume askonit.
E.17.1 The sin of Judah is written with a pen of iron, and with the point of a diamond: it is graven upon the table of their heart, and upon the horns of your altars;

α.17.2 Wunneechan8uh mehquantamunit wutaltarumooash kah ukkuppiyeum8oash kishke ashkunkquamut ut wadchuut.
E.17.2 Whilst their children remember their altars and their groves by the green trees upon the high hills.

α.17.3 Woi n8wadcheum ut ohteuhkonit, nummag wáme kittinneetuonk kah wame kenompakouunash mukk8kenittinneat, kah kukqunuhqui ayeuongash wutch matcheseonk pannuppe wame kussussippôiyeumut.
E.17.3 O my mountain in the field, I will give thy substance and all thy treasures to the spoil, and thy high places for sin, throughout all thy borders.

α.17.4 Kah ken pish matta kutappu ut kutohtoonganit ne anumauunomp, kah k8tinninneumuhkausuáhush ut kummatwomut, en ohkeit ne mo wahteáuoan: newutche kenashqunanum n8teau ut nummusquanittam8onganit, ne pish micheme chikohtag.
E.17.4 And thou, even thyself, shalt discontinue from thine heritage that I gave thee; and I will cause thee to serve thine enemies in the land which thou knowest not: for ye have kindled a fire in mine anger, which shall burn for ever.

α.17.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah, matanumunach noh pabahtanumont wosketompuh, kah wahpittenteadt weyaus, kah noh wuttah amaehtauont Jehovah.
E.17.5 Thus saith the LORD; Cursed be the man that trusteth in man, and maketh flesh his arm, and whose heart departeth from the LORD.

α.17.6 Newutche pish tatuppeyeu8 kunkohteadtag touohkomukqut, kah matta pish naum8 peyom88k wanegik, qut noh pish wutohtuontam kunkohteadtaeu ayeuongash ut touohkomukqut, ut salte ohkeit, kah matta wutohkein.
E.17.6 For he shall be like the heath in the desert, and shall not see when good cometh; but shall inhabit the parched places in the wilderness, in a salt land and not inhabited.

α.17.7 Wunnanumau wosketomp noh pabuhtanttanumont Jehovah, kah noh annaonont Jehovah.
E.17.7 Blessed is the man that trusteth in the LORD, and whose hope the LORD is.

α.17.8 Newutche noh pish tatuppeyeu8 mehtug ohketeamuk ut kishke nippeit, kah noh sepagodchabukkaem8uk ut kishke sepuut kah matta pish naum8, kussittau peyom8uk, qut 8neepog pish ashkoshqui, kah matta pish wuttamhik8 kunkohteadtae kodtum8, kah matta pish wohkukquoshininn8 tanneganit meechum.
E.17.8 For he shall be as a tree planted by the waters, and that spreadeth out her roots by the river, and shall not see when heat cometh, but her leaf shall be green; and shall not be careful in the year of drought, neither shall cease from yielding fruit.

α.17.9 Metah anue as8kekodteam8wontam onk wame teanteaguasinish kah unkqueneunkummatcheetou, howan woh 8wahteauun.
E.17.9 The heart is deceitful above all things, and desperately wicked: who can know it?

α.17.10 Nen Jehovah natinneuhkontam metah, nukqutcheh mutt8unussog, aninnumauonat nish$noh wosketomp neaunak ummayash, kah neaunak wutusseongane meechummuonk.
E.17.10 I the LORD search the heart, I try the reins, even to give every man according to his ways, and according to the fruit of his doings.

α.17.11 Onatuh pahpahkis ahtenásuk kah matta pwohkhôyeog: netatuppe noh weenauwekit qut matta sampwe, pish wunnukkodtumunash ut nashauwe ukkesukodtumut, kah ut 8wohkukquóiyeumut pish mattammagweyeu8.
E.17.11 As the partridge sitteth on eggs, and hatcheth them not; so he that getteth riches, and not by right, shall leave them in the midst of his days, and at his end shall be a fool.

α.17.12 Sohsumoe qunùhqueu appuonk wutch waj kutchissik ne nus-Sanctuarie ayeuonk.
E.17.12 A glorious high throne from the beginning is the place of our sanctuary.

α.17.13 Woi Jehovah, wutannoósuonguh Israel, wame neg ohquanumukqueáneg pish akodchuog, kah nag pahchaôsitcheg pish wusukwhosuog ut ohkeit, newutche nag nukkonáog Jehovah, noh tohkekommue pomantamwae nippe.
E.17.13 O LORD, the hope of Israel, all that forsake thee shall be ashamed, and they that depart from me shall be written in the earth, because they have forsaken the LORD, the fountain of living waters.

α.17.14 Neetskeheh woi Jehovah, kah pish nunneetskes: wadchaneh kah pish n8wadchanit: newutche ken waeenomog.
E.17.14 Heal me, O LORD, and I shall be healed; save me, and I shall be saved: for thou art my praise.

α.17.15 Kusseh, nag nuttugquog, uttiyeu wuttinn8waonk Lord? yeuyeu peyóm8utch.
E.17.15 Behold, they say unto me, Where is the word of the LORD? let it come now.

α.17.16 Qut nen, matta nukken8natu Pastoreuuneat kutasukauununat, kah matta nukkodtantam8 unkqunneunkquodte kesukod, k8wahteóh: ne sohham8m8uk wutch nussisset8nut, ne sampwiyeup ut anaquabean.
E.17.16 As for me, I have not hastened from being a pastor to follow thee: neither have I desired the woeful day; thou knowest: that which came out of my lips was right before thee.

α.17.17 OOwabesuonganehkon en kuhhogkat, ken nutannoósuonk ut matche kesukodtut.
E.17.17 Be not a terror unto me: thou art my hope in the day of evil.

α.17.18 Nag chepshahettich neg kodwoskehúkqueaneg, qut nen ahque chepshónti: nag quequénauánumwéhettich, qut nen ahque queuénauánumwuttei: núhkinumau matchik kesuk, kah nag pagwas nashpe papsku pagwanuonk,
E.17.18 Let them be confounded that persecute me, but let not me be confounded: let them be dismayed, but let not me be dismayed: bring upon them the day of evil, and destroy them with double destruction.

α.17.19 Jehovah yeu nuttugqun, monchish kah neepaush 8squontam8out wunneechan8oh missinninnuog, uttoh adt Judae ketass8tamwog petutteahettit, kah ne waj sohhamwehettit, kah ut wame Jerusaleme squontamehtu.
E.17.19 Thus said the LORD unto me; Go and stand in the gate of the children of the people, whereby the kings of Judah come in, and by the which they go out, and in all the gates of Jerusalem;

α.17.20 Kah nag us, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wame Judah, kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, neg petutteacheg yeu ut squontaméhtu.
E.17.20 And say unto them, Hear ye the word of the LORD, ye kings of Judah, and all Judah, and all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, that enter in by these gates:

α.17.21 Yeu wussin Lord, nunnukqussek kuhhogkaóog, kah weasséhteogk sabboth$dayeu: asuh petukkodta8hteok ut Jerusalemeh squontamut.
E.17.21 Thus saith the LORD; Take heed to yourselves, and bear no burden on the sabbath day, nor bring it in by the gates of Jerusalem;

α.17.22 Asuh sohh8wuttóhteók weanun wutch kekuóut sabboth$dayeu. Asuh toh usséhteok, qut wunneetupanátamwáhteó8k sabboth$day neánann8nogkup k8shuóog.
E.17.22 Neither carry forth a burden out of your houses on the sabbath day, neither do ye any work, but hallow ye the sabbath day, as I commanded your fathers.

α.17.23 Qut nag matta wunosweetam8uneau, ásuh mat ahchusittamoog, qut nag chetauwussittippukoñaeog, onk woh mo n8tam8og asuh matta attumunum8og kuhk8tomoadtuonk.
E.17.23 But they obeyed not, neither inclined their ear, but made their neck stiff, that they might not hear, nor receive instruction.

α.17.24 Kah pish n$nih, menuhke kuhkeitieog wussin Jehovah, matta petukkodtau8unat weanun yeu ut kutotanae squontamut Sabbothdayeu, qut wunneetupanatamwahteo8k Sabboth$day, mat na$ut anakauseuinat.
E.17.24 And it shall come to pass, if ye diligently hearken unto me, saith the LORD, to bring in no burden through the gates of this city on the sabbath day, but hallow the sabbath day, to do no work therein;

α.17.25 Neit pish kehtass8tamwog, kah sontimoog petutteaog ut yeu otanae squontamtu appinneat wutappuonganit David, nayeumukquehettit chariotsash kah horsesog, nag wussontimom8uk Judae wosketompaog kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kah yeu kutotan pish michemohteau.
E.17.25 Then shall there enter into the gates of this city kings and princes sitting upon the throne of David, riding in chariots and on horses, they, and their princes, the men of Judah, and the inhabitants of Jerusalem: and this city shall remain for ever.

α.17.26 Kah nag pish 8mwog Judae keiotanehtu, kah wutch ayeuonganehtu ut kishke Jerusalem, kah wutch Benjamine ohkeit, kah wutch mukoshquttaut, kah wutch wadchuuhkontu, kah wutch sowaniyeu, paudtauehettit chikohtae mag8ongash, kah sephausuongash, kah meetsue sephausuongash, kah incense kah padtauwehettit woweenodtumwe sephausuongash en wekit Jehovah.
E.17.26 And they shall come from the cities of Judah, and from the places about Jerusalem, and from the land of Benjamin, and from the plain, and from the mountains, and from the south, bringing burnt offerings, and sacrifices, and meat offerings, and incense, and bringing sacrifices of praise, unto the house of the LORD.

α.17.27 Qut matta kukkéhtieog, wunn[é]etupanatamwahtinneat Sabbath$day, kah matta nayeutam8unat weanun, petutteahettit ut Jerusalemme squontamut Sabbathdayeu: neit pish nunnashqussum n8teau na$ut squontamash, kah pish mahchikkossum8m8 Jerusalemme mishikkomukquash, kah matta pish onthamm8un.
E.17.27 But if ye will not hearken unto me to hallow the sabbath day, and not to bear a burden, even entering in at the gates of Jerusalem on the sabbath day; then will I kindle a fire in the gates thereof, and it shall devour the palaces of Jerusalem, and it shall not be quenched.

α.18.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah wutch Lordut, n8wau.
E.18.1 The word which came to Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.18.2 Neepaush kah w8msish en ohkuhkitteaen weékit kah na nuttit n8tamwahuwon nukkutt8wongash.
E.18.2 Arise, and go down to the potter's house, and there I will cause thee to hear my words.

α.18.3 Neit n8womsip en ohkuhketeaen wekit, kah kusseh, wuttittannehteauun wheelut.
E.18.3 Then I went down to the potter's house, and, behold, he wrought a work on the wheels.

α.18.4 Kah wisq ne kezteunk wutch man8nskut, ne matchehteausu ut wunnutcheganit ohkuhqutteaenin: neit wonk ayim penowe wisq: uttoh an 8nontug ohukuhqutteaenin.
E.18.4 And the vessel that he made of clay was marred in the hand of the potter: so he made it again another vessel, as seemed good to the potter to make it.

α.18.5 Neit wuttinn8wao[u]k Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, n8wau.
E.18.5 Then the word of the LORD came to me, saying,

α.18.6 Woi Israelle week, sun woh mat kuttinhenn8mw8 neane yeuoh ohkuhketeanin wussin Lord, kusseh, neane man8nsk appit ut wunnutcheganit ohkuhketeaenin, ne kuttatuppe appinneau nunnutcheganit, woi Israelle wek.
E.18.6 O house of Israel, cannot I do with you as this potter? saith the LORD. Behold, as the clay is in the potter's hand, so are ye in mine hand, O house of Israel.

α.18.7 Na utt8che unn8waon papaume wutohtimoin, kah papaume tahs8tamoonk, pohqunumunat, kah n8kenumunat, kah paguatauunat.
E.18.7 At what instant I shall speak concerning a nation, and concerning a kingdom, to pluck up, and to pull down, and to destroy it;

α.18.8 Tohneit ne wutohtimoin, ne ayeuuhkonittue kón8tam, quinnuppehettit wutch ummatchet8m8out, pish nutaiuskoiantam ne machuk ayeuuhkonittue ananumog.
E.18.8 If that nation, against whom I have pronounced, turn from their evil, I will repent of the evil that I thought to do unto them.

α.18.9 Kah uttoh adt8cheyeu8g ne an8wi papaume wutohtimoin, kah papaume tahs8tamoonk, ayimunat, kah ohteuhkonat.
E.18.9 And at what instant I shall speak concerning a nation, and concerning a kingdom, to build and to plant it;

α.18.10 Matchesehettit ut anaquabeh, matta n8swehtam8hetteg n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, neit pish nutaiuskoiantam ne wanegik ne anogkup k8niyeuhhennumw8.
E.18.10 If it do evil in my sight, that it obey not my voice, then I will repent of the good, wherewith I said I would benefit them.

α.18.11 Newutche yeuyeu ehhoh, ken8s Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, kutayeuuhkonittue ayimauunumw8 machuk, kah kutayeuuhkonittue natwontamauonumw8 natwontamoonk: qushkek yeuyeu nish$noh pasuk wutch ummatche mayit, kah wunnehteo8k kummayeuoash.
E.18.11 Now therefore go to, speak to the men of Judah, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, saying, Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I frame evil against you, and devise a device against you: return ye now every one from his evil way, and make your ways and your doings good.

α.18.12 Kah nag n8waog, matta annoósuonganun8: qut nutásukomumun nehenwonche natwontam8onganunonash, kah nish$noh pasuk nenawun nutussemun ummatche metahh8wae unnantam8onk.
E.18.12 And they said, There is no hope: but we will walk after our own devices, and we will every one do the imagination of his evil heart.

α.18.13 Newutche yeu wussin Lord, nat8tamok yeuyeu kenugke penuwohteaog, howan noh n8tog ne ônagish Israelle penomp ussen ne onkquanumukquok.
E.18.13 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Ask ye now among the heathen, who hath heard such things: the virgin of Israel hath done a very horrible thing.

α.18.14 Sun woh wosketomp nukkonau Lebanone k8noh, ne wóm8uk ohteahkone qussukquanit? asuh kussitchuáne sonkuppogash ne wam8uk pen8e ayeuonganit sun woh nukkodtumunash?
E.18.14 Will a man leave the snow of Lebanon which cometh from the rock of the field? or shall the cold flowing waters that come from another place be forsaken?

α.18.15 Newutche nummissinninúmog n8wanánumuk, nag chikohsumwog weetemungquok en tahn8cheyeu8uk, kah nah wuttogkussittahssumóuh ut ummayeuóut, wutch nukkóne mayut, pomushónat mayit nish mo wunnegenunogish.
E.18.15 Because my people hath forgotten me, they have burned incense to vanity, and they have caused them to stumble in their ways from the ancient paths, to walk in paths, in a way not cast up;

α.18.16 Touwishinnuwóhtineat wutohkeyeu, kah michemohtae nuttohhentupantam8onk: nish$noh pasuk noh na paumshadt pish chepshau, kah nunnukkuhquoshau.
E.18.16 To make their land desolate, and a perpetual hissing; every one that passeth thereby shall be astonished, and wag his head.

α.18.17 Nag nusseahwhóog onatuh nashpe wutchepwash ut anaquabit matwau: nunnahtinoog muppusk, qut matta muskesuk, wutonkapunáe kesukodtum8óut.
E.18.17 I will scatter them as with an east wind before the enemy; I will shew them the back, and not the face, in the day of their calamity.

α.18.18 Neit nag n8waog, peyunk, ayeuuhkonittue natwontamauóntuh natwontam8ongash Jeremiah; newutche naumatuonk matta pish wannehheau wutch sephausuenuut,  asuh kogáhquttuonk, wutch waantamwenuut, kah wuttinn8waonk wutch quoshodtumwaenuut: peyunk, togkommontuh meena[n], kah ahque tohhentupontammuttuh teagwe ukkutt8wonk.
E.18.18 Then said they, Come and let us devise devices against Jeremiah; for the law shall not perish from the priest, nor counsel from the wise, nor the word from the prophet. Come, and let us smite him with the tongue, and let us not give heed to any of his words.

α.18.19 Kuhkeihtah woi Jehovah, kah n8tash 8wadtauato[u]kqussuongan8 neg mekonukqueaneg.
E.18.19 Give heed to me, O LORD, and hearken to the voice of them that contend with me.

α.18.20 Sun woh machuk onkquttantamun wanegik? newutche nag pasáhthamwog wutch nukketeahogkou: mehquontash nunneepop ut anaquabe[a]n, nag wunnee n8wanshánaoont, kah quinnuppenumunat kummusquantam8onk nag wutch.
E.18.20 Shall evil be recompensed for good? for they have digged a pit for my soul. Remember that I stood before thee to speak good for them, and to turn away thy wrath from them.

α.18.21 Newutche p8nin wunneechan8oh ne mohshagquodtut, kah sohkenash 8sqheongan8 nashpe chekeushae togkodteg, kah ummittumwuss8oh amaunumauunach wunneechan8oh, kah sekousquainitch, kah 8wosketompóm8uh nushinach, kah wuskenúm8uh nushunaj mattompagwe togkodteg.
E.18.21 Therefore deliver up their children to the famine, and pour out their blood by the force of the sword; and let their wives be bereaved of their children, and be widows; and let their men be put to death; let their young men be slain by the sword in battle.

α.18.22 Mauonk n8tamunach wutch week8woont, tiadche nuhkinnumauadt m8chequshaoh, newutche nag pahsohthamwog nuttohqunukqunnaoont, kah adtahshaog appehanoh wutche nusseetash.
E.18.22 Let a cry be heard from their houses, when thou shalt bring a troop suddenly upon them: for they have digged a pit to take me, and hid snares for my feet.

α.18.23 Qut woi Jehovah, k8wahteoh wame ukkogahquetuongan8 ayeuuhkonittue nen, nunnushikqunnaoont, ahque ahquontamau ummatcheseongan8, kah jishkhogkon, uppanneseonk wutch anaquabean, qut kepuhkonunaj ut anaquabean, unneh musquantaman.
E.18.23 Yet, LORD, thou knowest all their counsel against me to slay me: forgive not their iniquity, neither blot out their sin from thy sight, but let them be overthrown before thee; deal thus with them in the time of thine anger.

α.19.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, monchish neemunush ahkuhqutteaenin wutohkee wisq, kah neemun kutchisog wutch missinninnuut kah kutchisog wutch sephausuenuut.
E.19.1 Thus saith the LORD, Go and get a potter's earthen bottle, and take of the ancients of the people, and of the ancients of the priests;

α.19.2 Kah en sohhom8k wut8nuhkoiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnon, ne ohtag ahhut petutteamuk chepwiyeue squontamut, kah naut wahteauwahuush kutt8wongash, nish pish anonish.
E.19.2 And go forth unto the valley of the son of Hinnom, which is by the entry of the east gate, and proclaim there the words that I shall tell thee,

α.19.3 Kah n8wash, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah woi Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, yeu wussin Jehvoah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel kusseh, ne nuppaudtauun yeuut ayeuonganit, ne howan n8tog wuhtauogash pish nupp8m8ash.
E.19.3 And say, Hear ye the word of the LORD, O kings of Judah, and inhabitants of Jerusalem; Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will bring evil upon this place, the which whosoever heareth, his ears shall tingle.

α.19.4 Newutche nag nunnukkonukquog, kah penuwohteatoog yeu ayeuonk kah ne wuttit chikohsumauoneau weetemungquok penowe Manitto, neh matta nagumau asuh 8sh8oh, waheahettegeh, asuh Judae ketass8tamwog, kah wohtoog yeuut ayeuonganit mat woskehuwae wusqueheunk
E.19.4 Because they have forsaken me, and have estranged this place, and have burned incense in it unto other gods, whom neither they nor their fathers have known, nor the kings of Judah, and have filled this place with the blood of innocents;

α.19.5 Nag wonk ayimauwaog qunuhqui ayeuongash Baal, chikkoswonat wunnaumonaoh nashpe n8tau wutche chikohtae mag8ongash en Baalut, ne matta anunn8team8 asuh ân8wau, asuh matta anantam8.
E.19.5 They have built also the high places of Baal, to burn their sons with fire for burnt offerings unto Baal, which I commanded not, nor spake it, neither came it into my mind:

α.19.6 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, n8wau Jehovah, yeu ayeuonk matta pish wonk hettam8un Tophet, asuh wut8nouhkoiyeum wunnaumonuh Hinnon, qut nushehteae 8nouhkoi.
E.19.6 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that this place shall no more be called Tophet, nor The valley of the son of Hinnom, but The valley of slaughter.

α.19.7 Kah tahnunn8cheahtauun ukkogahquttuonk Judah kah Jerusalem yeu ut ayeuonganit, kah nuppenushah[h]eoog anaquabenit ummatwom8uh, kah nashpe wunnutchegan8wout neg kodnushehteacheg, kah nupp8e wuhhogkauh nummeechumuhkauona[oh] kesukque puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwog.
E.19.7 And I will make void the counsel of Judah and Jerusalem in this place; and I will cause them to fall by the sword before their enemies, and by the hands of them that seek their lives: and their carcases will I give to be meat for the fowls of the heaven, and for the beasts of the earth.

α.19.8 K[a]h nuttauwushitteauun yeu otan, kah [n]ummeshonantamwahtea[n]un, nish$noh pasuk noh na paumshadt pish chepshau, kah ummeshanontamun, newutche wame unninneaongash naut.
E.19.8 And I will make this city desolate, and an hissing; every one that passeth thereby shall be astonished and hiss because of all the plagues thereof.

α.19.9 Kah nummeechuwaheaog 8weyaus8 wunnaumonauh, kah 8weyaus8 wuttaun8oh kah nag pish meechwog nish$noh pasuk 8weyausum8 weetompuh, weenuhkomuk nannakompananuttimuk, uttohad ummatwom8uh, kah neg kodnushoncheg pish wunnanakompananouh.
E.19.9 And I will cause them to eat the flesh of their sons and the flesh of their daughters, and they shall eat every one the flesh of his friend in the siege and straitness, wherewith their enemies, and they that seek their lives, shall straiten them.

α.19.10 Neit pish kuppohquetahham wisq ut anaquabhettit weechogqueaneg.
E.19.10 Then shalt thou break the bottle in the sight of the men that go with thee,

α.19.11 Neit pish nag kuttinoog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuuhteaunit, ne nuttinne pohquenumun yeug missinninnuog, kah yeu keitotan, onatuh howan pohkshadtunk ohkuhquehteaen wisq, ne [w]atta woh wonk nompe wunnehteauomuk, kah nag pish upposekinouh, ut Tophet, Nô pajeh mat wuttape posekinausinneaoónt.
E.19.11 And shalt say unto them, Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Even so will I break this people and this city, as one breaketh a potter's vessel, that cannot be made whole again: and they shall bury them in Tophet, till there be no place to bury.

α.19.12 Yeu nuttinteauun yeu ayeuonk wussin Jehovah, kah en nag na wadohkitcheg kah nutogquehteoh wutotaneau Tophetut.
E.19.12 Thus will I do unto this place, saith the LORD, and to the inhabitants thereof, and even make this city as Tophet:

α.19.13 Kah Jerusálemme wetuomash kah Judae tahs8tamwog wekuoash pish ogque nishketeauunash Tophet: newutche wame wekuoash uttoh ut woskeche chikohsumauwahettit weetemungquok en wame kesukque kenauwameonk & sokanumauwaog wuttattamoe mag8ongash penowe Manitt8ut.
E.19.13 And the houses of Jerusalem, and the houses of the kings of Judah, shall be defiled as the place of Tophet, because of all the houses upon whose roofs they have burned incense unto all the host of heaven, and have poured out drink offerings unto other gods.

α.19.14 Neit Jeremiah 8m Tophet, uttoh Jehovah anan8nomp quoshodtamunat, kah neepau ut chippinnutongane wekit Jéhovah kah unnau wame missinninnuh.
E.19.14 Then came Jeremiah from Tophet, whither the LORD had sent him to prophesy; and he stood in the court of the LORD's house; and said to all the people,

α.19.15 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um[-]manitt8moh Israel kusseh, nunnuhkinnumau yeu keitotan kah ut wame wutotanamesash machuk ne ayeuuhkonittue ane kn8tam, newutche menehketeauog wussittippukan8oash, onk woh mo, n8tam8og nuttinn8waongash.
