E.19.15 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will bring upon this city and upon all her towns all the evil that I have pronounced against it, because they have hardened their necks, that they might not hear my words.

α.20.1 NEit Pashur wunnaumonuh Immer sephausuen noh kehche nanawunnuaenin wonk ut wekit Jehovah n8tam quoshodtuk Jeremiah yeush.
E.20.1 Now Pashur the son of Immer the priest, who was also chief governor in the house of the LORD, heard that Jeremiah prophesied these things.

α.20.2 Neit Pashur togkomau Jerémiahoh quoshodtumwaenuh, kah upponuh stocksut ne ohtag ut Benjaminne qunuhqui squontamut, ne kishkohtag wekit Jehovah.
E.20.2 Then Pashur smote Jeremiah the prophet, and put him in the stocks that were in the high gate of Benjamin, which was by the house of the LORD.

α.20.3 Kah nnih na wonk kesukok Pashur sohh8wunau Jeremiahoh wutch stocksut, neit Jeremiah wuttinuh Lord matta kuttehenuk8h Pashur qut Magoz$missabib.
E.20.3 And it came to pass on the morrow, that Pashur brought forth Jeremiah out of the stocks. Then said Jeremiah unto him, The LORD hath not called thy name Pashur, but Magormissabib.

α.20.4 Newutche yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, kutayimaush chepshaonk en kuhhogkat, kah en wame ketompaut, kah nag pish penushadtamwog nashpe wuttogkodtegan8 ummatwom8uh, kah kuskesukquash pish wunnaumun, kah nummag wame Judah en wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish kummissinohkone monchanuk en Babilon, & noh pish wunnushoh nashpe togkodteg.
E.20.4 For thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will make thee a terror to thyself, and to all thy friends: and they shall fall by the sword of their enemies, and thine eyes shall behold it: and I will give all Judah into the hand of the king of Babylon, and he shall carry them captive into Babylon, and shall slay them with the sword.

α.20.5 Nano, nummag wame ummenuhkesuonk yeu keitotan, kah wame wutanakausuonganooash kah wame ummishoade maumachiyeumash, kah wame wunnompak8un8oash Judae ketass8tamwog, nummagunash wunnutchegan8wout ummatwom8uh, neg pish mak8kinoncheg, kah pish neemunoog, kah uss8unoog Babilon.
E.20.5 Moreover I will deliver all the strength of this city, and all the labours thereof, and all the precious things thereof, and all the treasures of the kings of Judah will I give into the hand of their enemies, which shall spoil them, and take them, and carry them to Babylon.

α.20.6 Kah k[é]n Pashur, kah wame neg apitcheg kékit, pish missinno8og, kah ken pish kuppeam Babilon, kah na pish kuttit nuppun kah na pish kuttit posekinnitteam, ken kah wame ketompaog, neg pann8wae quoshodtumauadtcheg.
E.20.6 And thou, Pashur, and all that dwell in thine house shall go into captivity: and thou shalt come to Babylon, and there thou shalt die, and shalt be buried there, thou, and all thy friends, to whom thou hast prophesied lies.

α.20.7 Woi Jehovah, kuppuhch8uneh, kah nuppuhch8unit, ken kutanue menuhkusumeh, kah kussohkos: asekésukokish nutahanehtont, nish$noh pasuk nutoontohkonuk.
E.20.7 O LORD, thou hast deceived me, and I was deceived; thou art stronger than I, and hast prevailed: I am in derision daily, every one mocketh me.

α.20.8 Newutchen nádteuh kôdt8an, nummishont8wop, nummishont8wop, chekeeu usseonk kah mukk8kinnuwaonk newutche wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nutushpunanittean, kah asekesukokish nutahanehtont.
E.20.8 For since I spake, I cried out, I cried violence and spoil; because the word of the LORD was made a reproach unto me, and a derision, daily.

α.20.9 Neit nussip, matta wonk nummissohwhôh, asuh wonk nussu ut 8wésuonganit: qut wuttinn8waonk ut nuttahhut, tatuppeyeu8 nashqunáe n8taut, kuppuhhôsu ut nuskon$ut, kah nussauunumup kehchithon, kah matta nukkehchittohhou.
E.20.9 Then I said, I will not make mention of him, nor speak any more in his name. But his word was in mine heart as a burning fire shut up in my bones, and I was weary with forbearing, and I could not stay.

α.20.10 Newutche n8tamup nukkehkomukqunat monaog, wabesuonk waeenu, unnehtunkquodt, n8waog, kah nuttinnehtonkqunn8hteamun: wame neetompaog askuhhamwog nukk8qunukshaonk, n8waog, pagwodche woh ôsumau, kah woh kussohkauóun, kah woh kutann8tauóun.
E.20.10 For I heard the defaming of many, fear on every side. Report, say they, and we will report it. All my familiars watched for my halting, saying, Peradventure he will be enticed, and we shall prevail against him, and we shall take our revenge on him.

α.20.11 Qut Jehovah n8weetomuk, onatuh mohsheunkqueneunkqussit: newaj piṣh waskhukqueoneg togkussittassunéhettit, kah nag piṣh matta sohkohseog, nag piṣh mishe akodchuog, newutche nag matta piṣh wunniyéog, nag ummicheme chepshaongan8 matta piṣh wunántam8un.
E.20.11 But the LORD is with me as a mighty terrible one: therefore my persecutors shall stumble, and they shall not prevail: they shall be greatly ashamed; for they shall not prosper: their everlasting confusion shall never be forgotten.

α.20.12 Qut, woi Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ken quajheadt sampweusseaénin kah kenaau mutt8unussog kah metah, naumutti kutann8tôsuonk nag ut: newutche en kuh[k]ogkat n8wohshinum nuppissau$matuonk.
E.20.12 But, O LORD of hosts, that triest the righteous, and seest the reins and the heart, let me see thy vengeance on them: for unto thee have I opened my cause.

α.20.13 Ket8humok Jehovah, waeenomók Jehovah, newutche pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunoh matcheku, wutch wunnutcheganit matcheseaen.
E.20.13 Sing unto the LORD, praise ye the LORD: for he hath delivered the soul of the poor from the hand of evildoers.

α.20.14 Matanumwe uttamunach ne kesukod adt neekeomp: ahque wunanittamunach ne kesukok n8hkas neechanukquéan
E.20.14 Cursed be the day wherein I was born: let not the day wherein my mother bare me be blessed.

α.20.15 Mat[á]numwe ununach noh wosketomp, noh paudtaunchem8óno[n]t n8shoh, n8wadt, mukkutchouks keneekitteont, ahche wekontamwahikqun.
E.20.15 Cursed be the man who brought tidings to my father, saying, A man child is born unto thee; making him very glad.

α.20.16 Kah noh wosketomp tatuppeyeu8itch keitotanaṣh nish Jehovah kepuhteajiṣh, kah matta aiuskoianatam8: kah n8taj mauonk nompoáeu, kah mishont8waonk puhshequadt.
E.20.16 And let that man be as the cities which the LORD overthrew, and repented not: and let him hear the cry in the morning, and the shouting at noontide;

α.20.17 Newutche matta nunnushhuk8 wutch ôontomukqut, asuh woh nokas n8weenohkeinneat, kah wutôontomuk woh nagwutteae n8wompikquoeuwónukqunat.
E.20.17 Because he slew me not from the womb; or that my mother might have been my grave, and her womb to be always great with me.

α.20.18 Tohwutch sohhamos wutch ôontomukqut, naumunat anakausuonk kah unkquanumóonk, onk woh nukkesukodtum akodchue pámsheau?
E.20.18 Wherefore came I forth out of the womb to see labour and sorrow, that my days should be consumed with shame?

α.21.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, Zedekiah ketass8t ann8nont Pashur wunnaumonuh Melchiah, kah Zephaniah wunnaumonuh Maaseiah sephausuen, n8waog,
E.21.1 The word which came unto Jeremiah from the LORD, when king Zedekiah sent unto him Pashur the son of Melchiah, and Zephaniah the son of Maaseiah the priest, saying,

α.21.2 K8wehquetumoush nat8tamwontamaiinneam Jehovah (newutche Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t nummatompagúhkonukquog) tohneit Jehovah unnehikquéog neaunak wame ummonchanatamwe anakausuongaṣh, onk woh nutamaehtunkqun
E.21.2 Enquire, I pray thee, of the LORD for us; for Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon maketh war against us; if so be that the LORD will deal with us according to all his wondrous works, that he may go up from us.

α.21.3 Neit Jeremiah nah wuttinuh, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau Zedekiah.
E.21.3 Then said Jeremiah unto them, Thus shall ye say to Zedekiah:

α.21.4 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, Nukqushkinum kenauwameongaṣh ohtágiṣh ut kenutchegan8wóut, niṣh nashpe ayeuuhkónog Babylone ketass8t, kah Caldeansog, neg wéenuhkongqueógig ut poquadchit pummeneutunkanit, kah nummukkinóog ut noeu yeu keitotanat.
E.21.4 Thus saith the LORD God of Israel; Behold, I will turn back the weapons of war that are in your hands, wherewith ye fight against the king of Babylon, and against the Chaldeans, which besiege you without the walls, and I will assemble them into the midst of this city.

α.21.5 Kah nen wonk kutayeuúhkonumw8, nashpe summagunnumwe menutcheg, kah nashpe menuhki muhpit, musquantamwe kah chenauausue, kah mishe musquantamwe.
E.21.5 And I myself will fight against you with an outstretched hand and with a strong arm, even in anger, and in fury, and in great wrath.

α.21.6 Kah nuttogkom neg apitcheg yeu keitotanat, naneswe wosketomp & pupinashim: nag piṣh nupwog nashpe mishe anninneaonk
E.21.6 And I will smite the inhabitants of this city, both man and beast: they shall die of a great pestilence.

α.21.7 Kah ompetag wussin Jehovah nummag Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah wuttinneumoh, kah missinninnuog, kah neg sekqshoncheg yeu otanat wutch enninneaonganit, wutch togkodteganit, kah wutch mashagquodtut, ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut ummatwom8uh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kodnushoncheg, kah nah piṣh wuttogkomuh en kenag togkodteg matta piṣh owóhquánumuh, asuh ukkitteamonteanumoh, asuh monánumoh.
E.21.7 And afterward, saith the LORD, I will deliver Zedekiah king of Judah, and his servants, and the people, and such as are left in this city from the pestilence, from the sword, and from the famine, into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, and into the hand of their enemies, and into the hand of those that seek their life: and he shall smite them with the edge of the sword; he shall not spare them, neither have pity, nor have mercy.

α.21.8 Kah piṣh kuttin yeug missinninnúog, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nupponam anaquabeog, pomantamóe may, kah nupp8e may.
E.21.8 And unto this people thou shalt say, Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I set before you the way of life, and the way of death.

α.21.9 Noh apit yue keitotanat, piṣh nashpe nupp8 togkodteganit, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk: qut noh sohhog kah agẃehtauont Caldeansoh, neg wéenuhkongqueógig, noh piṣh pomantam, kah uppomantamoonk pish ne tohqunuk.
E.21.9 He that abideth in this city shall die by the sword, and by the famine, and by the pestilence: but he that goeth out, and falleth to the Chaldeans that besiege you, he shall live, and his life shall be unto him for a prey.

α.21.10 Newutche ayeuuhkonittue ponam nuskesuk yeu otan wutche machuk, kah matta wutch wanegik, wussin Jehovah; kah piṣh aninnumauon en wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wutchikohsumun ut n8taut.
E.21.10 For I have set my face against this city for evil, and not for good, saith the LORD: it shall be given into the hand of the king of Babylon, and he shall burn it with fire.

α.21.11 Kah papaume wek Judae ketass8t, n8wash, n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk.
E.21.11 And touching the house of the king of Judah, say, Hear ye the word of the LORD;

α.21.12 Woi David wek, yeu wussin Lord, ussek wussittumóonk nompoáeu, kah pohquohwuttók noh mogk8kinit wutch wunnutcheganit noh magk8kinuadt, ishkont nummusquantam8onk ogque sohham8m8 n8taut, kah chikohteau, ne$waj howan woh mo ontham8k: newutche kummatche usseongan8oaṣh.
E.21.12 O house of David, thus saith the LORD; Execute judgment in the morning, and deliver him that is spoiled out of the hand of the oppressor, lest my fury go out like fire, and burn that none can quench it, because of the evil of your doings.

α.21.13 Kusseh, kutayeuuhkonṣh woi wadohkean 8nouhkôiyeuut, kah mukoshquttae qussukquanit, wussin Lrod, neg 8n8wacheg, howan woh ayeuuhkonukquean? asuh howan woh petutteadt nutáyeuonganunónut?
E.21.13 Behold, I am against thee, O inhabitant of the valley, and rock of the plain, saith the LORD; which say, Who shall come down against us? or who shall enter into our habitations?

α.21.14 Qut kussasamatahwhunumw8, neánummeechumik kutusseongan8aṣh, wussin Jehovah: kah nunnashqunanum n8teau, ut wuttouohkomukkouóut, kah piṣh mahchekussum8m8 wame teanteáqussiniṣh, ut waéenu.
E.21.14 But I will punish you according to the fruit of your doings, saith the LORD: and I will kindle a fire in the forest thereof, and it shall devour all things round about it.

α.22.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, womsish en Judae ketass8t wekit, kah naut n8wash yeu kutt8wonk,
E.22.1 Thus saith the LORD; Go down to the house of the king of Judah, and speak there this word,

α.22.2 Kah n8wash, N8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi Judae ketass8t, ken ápean wutappuonganit David, ken kah kuttinneumog, kah kummissinninnúmog neg petutteacheg yeuh squontamehtu.
E.22.2 And say, Hear the word of the LORD, O king of Judah, that sittest upon the throne of David, thou, and thy servants, and thy people that enter in by these gates:

α.22.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah, ussek wussittumóonk, kah sampweusseonk, kah pohquohwhus noh mak8kinit wutch wunnutcheganit magk8kinnúadt, kah matchenehuwáhte[ò]gk, chekéenéheúhteógk pen8wot, touwiés, asuh sekousq, asuh soksquohthádteok mat woskehuwae musqueheonk yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.22.3 Thus saith the LORD; Execute ye judgment and righteousness, and deliver the spoiled out of the hand of the oppressor: and do no wrong, do no violence to the stranger, the fatherless, nor the widow, neither shed innocent blood in this place.

α.22.4 Newutche yeu wunnamu[h]kut usseóg, neit piṣh petukkon[e]au yeu ut squontamut, ketass8tamwog, appinneat wutappuonganit David, nayeumukqunat chariotsaṣh, kah horsesog, nagum kah wuttinneumoh, kah ummissinninnumoh.
E.22.4 For if ye do this thing indeed, then shall there enter in by the gates of this house kings sitting upon the throne of David, riding in chariots and on horses, he, and his servants, and his people.

α.22.5 Qut mata yeuṣh n8tam8og kut8wongaṣh, nutchadchekeyeuwam nashpe nen, wussin Jehovah, yeu weetu piṣh touushitteauun.
E.22.5 But if ye will not hear these words, I swear by myself, saith the LORD, that this house shall become a desolation.

α.22.6 Newutche yeu Lord wuttittamun Judae ketass8t weekit, ken Gilead, ut nuhhogkat, kah uppuhkuk Lebanon, qut wunnamuhkut kuttouohkomukqúhkonuṣh, kah keitotanaṣh niṣh matta wadohteumukiṣh.
E.22.6 For thus saith the LORD unto the king's house of Judah; Thou art Gilead unto me, and the head of Lebanon: yet surely I will make thee a wilderness, and cities which are not inhabited.

α.22.7 Kah kutayeuuhkonittue qu[a]gwoshwéhtamouṣh pagwohteaenuog, nisnoh pasuk ahtou wutauwohteaonk, kah nag piṣh tummehtahwhôog k8ne Cedarsum8uh, kah wuttinnuhkonáuh n8taut.
E.22.7 And I will prepare destroyers against thee, every one with his weapons: and they shall cut down thy choice cedars, and cast them into the fire.

α.22.8 Kah monataṣh wutohtimoneaṣh piṣh paumuhkomwog yeu keitotan, kah nag piṣh unnaog nishnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, tohwaj Jehovah yeu unnehteunk yeu missi keitotan?
E.22.8 And many nations shall pass by this city, and they shall say every man to his neighbour, Wherefore hath the LORD done thus unto this great city?

α.22.9 Kah nag piṣh namp8hamwog, newutche nukkodtumwog 8n8waonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, & wowussumáog onkatogeh manitt8oh, kah wuttinneumuhkauóuh.
E.22.9 Then they shall answer, Because they have forsaken the covenant of the LORD their God, and worshipped other gods, and served them.

α.22.10 Mauemúhteogk napukeg, asuh maumuttamóunúhteógk; qut mishe mauunnitteaunsheuk noh moncheit, newutche matta piṣh wonk qushkeu, asuh naum8 ne adt neekit ohke
E.22.10 Weep ye not for the dead, neither bemoan him: but weep sore for him that goeth away: for he shall return no more, nor see his native country.

α.22.11 Newutche yeu wussin Lord papaume Shallum wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, noh nompe nanawunnuómont Josiahoh 8shoh, noh sohhog yeu wutch ayeuonganit, matta na piṣh wonk en qushku.
E.22.11 For thus saith the LORD touching Shallum the son of Josiah king of Judah, which reigned instead of Josiah his father, which went forth out of this place; He shall not return thither any more:

α.22.12 Qut piṣh na wuttit nuppunin uttoh adt missinohteahettit, kah matta piṣh wonk naum8 yeu ohke.
E.22.12 But he shall die in the place whither they have led him captive, and shall see this land no more.

α.22.13 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh ayig weetu nashpe mat sampweusseonk, kah 8chambersaṣh nashpe wo[ô]nkagk, noh attumunuk weetatteamunguh wutanakausuonk, kah matta onkquatauonk, kah matta wutôadtúhkauoh wutanakausuonk.
E.22.13 Woe unto him that buildeth his house by unrighteousness, and his chambers by wrong; that useth his neighbour's service without wages, and giveth him not for his work;

α.22.14 Noh an8wadt nutayim mishe kehchikkomuk, kah mogke kishke chambersaṣh, kah wunnussum kenogkenegash, kah appuhquau chikkupoh, kah musquadtsôsu.
E.22.14 That saith, I will build me a wide house and large chambers, and cutteth him out windows; and it is cieled with cedar, and painted with vermilion.

α.22.15 Sun woh kenanawunnuam newutche kutabpuhquomp chikkuppog? sunnummatta k8sh meetseis kah wuttattam8us, kah usseis wussittumóonk, kah sampweusseonk, neit 8niyeuwontamun?
E.22.15 Shalt thou reign, because thou closest thyself in cedar? did not thy father eat and drink, and do judgment and justice, and then it was well with him?

α.22.16 Wussittum uppissaumatonk matcheku, kah quenauhikquit, neit 8niyeuhikqun; sunnummatta yeu n8wahetteaonk wussin Jehovah.
E.22.16 He judged the cause of the poor and needy; then it was well with him: was not this to know me? saith the LORD.

α.22.17 Qut kuskesukquaṣh kah kuttah webe wutch hahchewontamóonk, kah soksquadthamunat mat woskehuwae musqueheonk, kah sunukqutchahwhuttuonk, kah chekée ussenat.
E.22.17 But thine eyes and thine heart are not but for thy covetousness, and for to shed innocent blood, and for oppression, and for violence, to do it.

α.22.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, matta piṣh ummauemóuh, woi neemat, woi neetompas: matta piṣh ummauém8uh n8wahettit, woi lord, woi wussohsumóonk.
E.22.18 Therefore thus saith the LORD concerning Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah; They shall not lament for him, saying, Ah my brother! or, Ah sister! they shall not lament for him, saying, Ah lord! or, Ah his glory!

α.22.19 Piṣh posekinau ne posekinit asse, pamontonchimáhettit, kah sohwohteahettit en áongkoue Jerusaleme squontamehtu.
E.22.19 He shall be buried with the burial of an ass, drawn and cast forth beyond the gates of Jerusalem.

α.22.20 Kuhkuhquiṣh Lebanon, maush, kah mishont8aṣh ut Bashan, kah maush ut ôsukonganit; newutche wame womonadtcheg paguanóog.
E.22.20 Go up to Lebanon, and cry; and lift up thy voice in Bashan, and cry from the passages: for all thy lovers are destroyed.

α.22.21 Kukkinnonup wanniyéan, qut kussip, matta nunn8tam, yeu kuttinniyeuonk wutch k8skenuunneat, matta ken8swetam8unat n8wadtau[a]tonkqussuonk.
E.22.21 I spake unto thee in thy prosperity; but thou saidst, I will not hear. This hath been thy manner from thy youth, that thou obeyedst not my voice.

α.22.22 Waban piṣh mahchipp8 wame Pastorsoh, kah womonacheg piṣh missinoóog, wunnamuhkut piṣh neit kutakoj, kah piṣh kutchepsham wutch wame kummatcheseongaṣh.
E.22.22 The wind shall eat up all thy pastors, and thy lovers shall go into captivity: surely then shalt thou be ashamed and confounded for all thy wickedness.

α.22.23 Woi ken wadohkean Lebanon, wâdsháhteáan ut chikkupuhtukqut, uttoh piṣh kuttin wunneetupanatamwéin onkquommom8ongaṣh yeanâhkukkongquean, wutonkquommom8ongaṣh mittamwossis neechadt.
E.22.23 O inhabitant of Lebanon, that makest thy nest in the cedars, how gracious shalt thou be when pangs come upon thee, the pain as of a woman in travail!

α.22.24 Pomantamon wussin Jehovah, Coniah wunnaumonuh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t tôhkonogque nompak8unnú8 ut nuttinohkôunit, onch na k8ch kodtinunun.
E.22.24 As I live, saith the LORD, though Coniah the son of Jehoiakim king of Judah were the signet upon my right hand, yet would I pluck thee thence;

α.22.25 Kah kuttinnumaush ut wunnutchegan8w[ô]ut neg kodnushikqueaneg, kah en wunnutchegan8wout neg wuskesuk8 quohtaman, ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8wout Caldeansog.
E.22.25 And I will give thee into the hand of them that seek thy life, and into the hand of them whose face thou fearest, even into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, and into the hand of the Chaldeans.

α.22.26 Kah kussohwhokonsh, kah kokas noh nekhikquean, ut onkatogke ohkeit ne mo adt nekean kah na pish kuttit nuppun.
E.22.26 And I will cast thee out, and thy mother that bare thee, into another country, where ye were not born; and there shall ye die.

α.22.27 Qut ohkeit na kodtantamwehettit en qushkenat na matta pish wuttin qushkeineau.
E.22.27 But to the land whereunto they desire to return, thither shall they not return.

α.22.28 Sun yeuoh wosketomp Coniah sekeneauou pokshae nunnukontunkoh: sun noh wishquiyeu ne adt mat wekontam8onganun8g? tohwutch nag sohwohteaog, nagum kah 8skannemunneoh, kah pogketamwog en ohkeit ne matta wahteauhétteg[?]
E.22.28 Is this man Coniah a despised broken idol? is he a vessel wherein is no pleasure? wherefore are they cast out, he and his seed, and are cast into a land which they know not?

α.22.29 Woi ohke, ohke, ohke[,] n8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah.
E.22.29 O earth, earth, earth, hear the word of the LORD.

α.22.30 Yeu wussin Lord, wussukhamok yeuoh wosketomp, matta wunnechaneg wosketomp noh matta woh waniegk ut ukkesukkodtumut: newutche matta wosketomp 8m8oh 8skannemunit pish wunniyeoh: appinneat wutappuonganit David, kah nano nanawunnuadt ut Judah.
E.22.30 Thus saith the LORD, Write ye this man childless, a man that shall not prosper in his days: for no man of his seed shall prosper, sitting upon the throne of David, and ruling any more in Judah.

α.23.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 Pastorsog, neg pagwohteacheg kah seahwhoncheg wuttittanadtupp8ongan8 nusshepsumog wussin Jehovah.
E.23.1 Woe be unto the pastors that destroy and scatter the sheep of my pasture! saith the LORD.

α.23.2 Newutche yeu wussin Lord um-Manitt8m8uh Israel, ayeuuhkonittue Pastorsog neg assamoncheg nummissinninnumoh kusseahwhomw8 nufflockum, kah kutama8hkauoog, kah matta nag kenatauwaheoog, kusseh natauwahettue kupponamauonumw8 kummatche usseongan8oash wussin Jehovah.
E.23.2 Therefore thus saith the LORD God of Israel against the pastors that feed my people; Ye have scattered my flock, and driven them away, and have not visited them: behold, I will visit upon you the evil of your doings, saith the LORD.

α.23.3 Kah nummukkin sekqshoncheg ut nuf[-]flockumut wutchwame wutohtimoinash uttoh ann8hkauog, kah wonk nuppas8oog, ut wutchippinneutunkan8out, kah nag pish mishimmeechummuog, kah nano monaog.
E.23.3 And I will gather the remnant of my flock out of all countries whither I have driven them, and will bring them again to their folds; and they shall be fruitful and increase.

α.23.4 Kah nuttahshinnumauoog nanashipsaenuog, neg pish sohkom8unoncheg, kah nag matta pish wonk wabeseog asuh chepshau8og, asuh matta pish waneteau8og pasuk8 wussin Jehovah.
E.23.4 And I will set up shepherds over them which shall feed them: and they shall fear no more, nor be dismayed, neither shall they be lacking, saith the LORD.

α.23.5 Kusseh, kesukodtásh peyaum8ash wussin Lord, nutomohkinumau David sampweusseae wuttuhk, kah ketass8t pish nanawunnuau, kah pish wunayeu, kah pish usseu wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit.
E.23.5 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will raise unto David a righteous Branch, and a King shall reign and prosper, and shall execute judgment and justice in the earth.

α.23.6 Ut ukkesukodtumut Judah pish wadchanau, kah Israel pish wunayeu, kah yeu 8wesuonk ne pish ahen[l]t: JEHOVAH NUSSAMPWE USSEONGANIIN.
E.23.6 In his days Judah shall be saved, and Israel shall dwell safely: and this is his name whereby he shall be called, THE LORD OUR RIGHTEOUSNESS.

α.23.7 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8ash wussin Jehovah, nag matta pish wonk unn8wo8og, Lord pomantam noh sohh8wunomp Israélloh wutch ohkit Egypt.
E.23.7 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that they shall no more say, The LORD liveth, which brought up the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt;

α.23.8 Qut Lord pômantam, noh sohh8wunomp kah sagkompagunomp 8skannem Israelle week, wutch nanumohkeit, kah wutch wame wutohtimoneat uttoh ann8hkauog, kah nag pish ayeu[ô]g nehenwonché wutohkeyeuout.
E.23.8 But, The LORD liveth, which brought up and which led the seed of the house of Israel out of the north country, and from all countries whither I had driven them; and they shall dwell in their own land.

α.23.9 Nuttah ut nuttinnomiyeumut pokshau newutche quoshodtumwaenuog, wame nuskonash nunnukshaash: nuttatuppeyeu kogkeussippamwaenuut (kah neaneyeu wosketomp aneukongquit wine) newutche Jehovah, kah wutche 8neetupa[n]atamwe unn8waongash.
E.23.9 Mine heart within me is broken because of the prophets; all my bones shake; I am like a drunken man, and like a man whom wine hath overcome, because of the LORD, and because of the words of his holiness.

α.23.10 Newutche ohke wunnumwapeneau mamussuénuog, newutche nashpe chadchekeyeuwaonk, ohke mau8m8, wunneayeuongash ut touohkomuk nunohtaash, kah wuttinniyeuongan8 matchit, kah wutchekeusseongan8 matta sampwan8.
E.23.10 For the land is full of adulterers; for because of swearing the land mourneth; the pleasant places of the wilderness are dried up, and their course is evil, and their force is not right.

α.23.11 Newutche naneeswe quoshodtumwaen kah sephausuwaen nishkeneungqussuog, nux, ut nekit namehteauun ummatcheseonk wussin Jehovah.
E.23.11 For both prophet and priest are profane; yea, in my house have I found their wickedness, saith the LORD.

α.23.12 Newutche pish ummayou tatuppeyeu8 ut wuhhogkaout t8neque mayash ut pohkenahtu: nag pish kutchittoushaog, kah na$ut penushaog: newutche pish nuppaudtauoog machut natauwahae kodtum8m8 wussin Jehovah.
E.23.12 Wherefore their way shall be unto them as slippery ways in the darkness: they shall be driven on, and fall therein: for I will bring evil upon them, even the year of their visitation, saith the LORD.

α.23.13 Kah nunnaum wutass8tuongan8 quoshodtumwaenuog ut Samaria: nag quoshodtamwog ut Baal, kah panneseaheaog Israelloh nummissinninnumoh.
E.23.13 And I have seen folly in the prophets of Samaria; they prophesied in Baal, and caused my people Israel to err.

α.23.14 Kah wonk nunnaum nishkeneunkquok ut Jerusaleme quoshodtumawenuut, mamussuog, pomushaog pann8wonganit, menehketeauog wonk wunnutchegan8oaṣh matchesecheg, onk matta howan woh qushku wutch ummatcheseonganit: nag wame tatuppeyeuog ut nuhhogkat Sodom, kah wadohkitcheg naut tatuppeyeu8og Gomorrah.
E.23.14 I have seen also in the prophets of Jerusalem an horrible thing: they commit adultery, and walk in lies: they strengthen also the hands of evildoers, that none doth return from his wickedness; they are all of them unto me as Sodom, and the inhabitants thereof as Gomorrah.

α.23.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit papaume quoshodtumwaenuog, kusseh, nussohkom8un[ó]og wormw8d, kah 8tattamwaheóuh weesweeu nippe: newutche wutch Jerusaleme quoshodumwaenúog, eiantukeiyeuonk sohham8m8 en wame wutohtimóineat.
E.23.15 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts concerning the prophets; Behold, I will feed them with wormwood, and make them drink the water of gall: for from the prophets of Jerusalem is profaneness gone forth into all the land.

α.23.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, n8tam8hteók ukkutt8ongan8oaṣh quoshodtumwaenuog, neg missohhamunkqueógig; nag tohken8cheáhik8oog: nag n8waog monomansuonk wutch nehenwonche wuttahh8wóut, kah matta wuch wutt8nut Jehovah.
E.23.16 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, Hearken not unto the words of the prophets that prophesy unto you: they make you vain: they speak a vision of their own heart, and not out of the mouth of the LORD.

α.23.17 Nag ash wuttinóuh neh sekeneunkqueaneh: Jehovah n8wau, piṣh k8nohteamw8, kah unnáog nishnoh pasuk8, noh ásuhkog nehenwonche wuttahh8wae unnantam8onk; wanne machuk piṣh kenuhkuhkongk8mw8.
E.23.17 They say still unto them that despise me, The LORD hath said, Ye shall have peace; and they say unto every one that walketh after the imagination of his own heart, No evil shall come upon you.

α.23.18 Newutche howan neepauwit ukkogúhqutteam8onganit Jehovah, kah wahteunk, kah n8tog wuttinn8waonk? howan kahkinneasit ukkutt8wonk n8tog?
E.23.18 For who hath stood in the counsel of the LORD, and hath perceived and heard his word? who hath marked his word, and heard it?

α.23.19 Kusseh, Jehovah uppemsquohhumoh sohham8m8 ut musquantam8onganit, unkqueneunkque pemsquoh, piṣh unkqueneunkque penushau ut uppuhkukqut matcheetou.
E.23.19 Behold, a whirlwind of the LORD is gone forth in fury, even a grievous whirlwind: it shall fall grievously upon the head of the wicked.

α.23.20 Ummusquantam8onk Jehovah matta piṣh qushkemun8, nô pajeh kestauunat, kah pakodche ussenat wuttahh8wae unnantam8ongaṣh: ut maumachiṣh kesukodtut, piṣh kuppannuppeyeue natwontamuneau.
E.23.20 The anger of the LORD shall not return, until he have executed, and till he have performed the thoughts of his heart: in the latter days ye shall consider it perfectly.

α.23.21 Matta yeug nutann8nóog quoshodtumwaénuog, qut quogqueog: matta nag nukken8náog, qut nag quoshodtumwog.
E.23.21 I have not sent these prophets, yet they ran: I have not spoken to them, yet they prophesied.

α.23.22 Qut neepauwéhettis nukkogáhqutteam8onganit, kah n8tamwáheáhettis nummissinninnúmoh nuttinn8waongaṣh, neit woh nag qushk8panneg wutch ummatchemayyeuóut, kah wutch ummatcheseongan8óut.
E.23.22 But if they had stood in my counsel, and had caused my people to hear my words, then they should have turned them from their evil way, and from the evil of their doings.

α.23.23 Sun nen paswe Manit wussin Jehovah, kah matta nô|adt Manit?
E.23.23 Am I a God at hand, saith the LORD, and not a God afar off?

α.23.24 Sun woh howan adtahshau wuhhogkuh, ut asampamukquodtut, onk woh mo nunnauoh wussin Jehovah? sunnummatta nunnumwohto8h kesuk kah ohke wussin Jehovah?
E.23.24 Can any hide himself in secret places that I shall not see him? saith the LORD. Do not I fill heaven and earth? saith the LORD.

α.23.25 Nunn8tauomp toh quoshodtumwaenuog an8wahetteup, pann8wayeuongash quoshodtumwehettit ut n8wesuonganit, n8wahettit, nuttinnukquom, nuttinnukquom.
E.23.25 I have heard what the prophets said, that prophesy lies in my name, saying, I have dreamed, I have dreamed.

α.23.26 Toh utt8che piṣh yeu ohteau wuttahh8wout quoshodtumwaenuog, neg pann8waongash quoshódtukeg? nux, nag quoshodtumwog wuttahh8wae as8kekodteam8onganooash;
E.23.26 How long shall this be in the heart of the prophets that prophesy lies? yea, they are prophets of the deceit of their own heart;

α.23.27 Nag unnantamwog wanantamwáheonat nummissinninnúmog n8wesuonk, nashpe wuttinnukquomuwonganooash, neg ánoncheg nishno[h] pasuk weetatteamunguh, neane 8sh8uh wananatamohettit n8wesuonk wutche Baal.
E.23.27 Which think to cause my people to forget my name by their dreams which they tell every man to his neighbour, as their fathers have forgotten my name for Baal.

α.23.28 Quoshodtumwaenin noh anukquonk, unn8w[á]j unnukquom8onk, kah noh ohtunk nuttinn8waonk, unn8waj nuttinn8waonk, pabuhtanumwe: teagwas wussadteamunash ut wheatut? wussin Jehovah.
E.23.28 The prophet that hath a dream, let him tell a dream; and he that hath my word, let him speak my word faithfully. What is the chaff to the wheat? saith the LORD.

α.23.29 Sunnummatta nuttinn8waonk tatuppéyeuunn8 n8taut? wussin Jehovah, kah onatuh hammer, ne sogquetahham8m8uk qussuk?
E.23.29 Is not my word like as a fire? saith the LORD; and like a hammer that breaketh the rock in pieces?

α.23.30 Newutche kusseh, nen nutáyeuuhkon quoshodtumwaenuog, wussin Jehovah, neg kôm8tukeg nuttinn8w[á]onk niṣh$noh pasuk wutch weetatteamunganit.
E.23.30 Therefore, behold, I am against the prophets, saith the LORD, that steal my words every one from his neighbour.

α.23.31 Kusseh, nen nutáyeuuhkon quoshodtumwaenuog, wussin Jehovah, neg m8sitteunkeg weenannu8 kah an8wahettit, noh wussin.
E.23.31 Behold, I am against the prophets, saith the LORD, that use their tongues, and say, He saith.

α.23.32 Kusseh, nag nutáyeuuhkonoog quoshae missohhogig pann8wae unnukquom8ongash wussin Lord, kah wussinneau, kah panne usseáheáog nummissinninnúmog nashpe uppann8waongan8oash, kah nashpe wunnonkan8ongan8, qut matta nutann8noog, asuh nuttinann8nóuneau: newaj piṣh mat wunáyeuheahetteg yeuh missinninnúh wussin Jehovah.
E.23.32 Behold, I am against them that prophesy false dreams, saith the LORD, and do tell them, and cause my people to err by their lies, and by their lightness; yet I sent them not, nor commanded them: therefore they shall not profit this people at all, saith the LORD.

α.23.33 Kah yeug missinninnúog, asuh quoshodtumwaen, asuh sephausuwaen, nat8tamungquean, n8wahettit, teagwas 8weéanun Lord? neit nag piṣh kuttinòog, teagwe weanun? nen kutohquanumunumw8 wussin Jehovah,
E.23.33 And when this people, or the prophet, or a priest, shall ask thee, saying, What is the burden of the LORD? thou shalt then say unto them, What burden? I will even forsake you, saith the LORD.

α.23.34 Kah quoshodtumwaen, kah sephausuwaen, kah missinninnumog neg an8wacheg, 8wéanun Jehovah, nussasamatuh noh wosketomp, kah wek.
E.23.34 And as for the prophet, and the priest, and the people, that shall say, The burden of the LORD, I will even punish that man and his house.

α.23.35 Yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau niṣhnoh pasuk weetatteamungoh, kah nishnoh pasuk wematoh, toh unnunnamp8ham Jehovah, kah toh n8wau Jehovah?
E.23.35 Thus shall ye say every one to his neighbour, and every one to his brother, What hath the LORD answered? and, What hath the LORD spoken?

α.23.36 Kah 8weanun Jehovah matta piṣh wonk kummiṣhamm8uneau: newutche niṣh$noh howan ukkutt8wonk ne piṣh 8weanun, newutche k8woonkitteamw8 ukkutt8wongash pomantamwae God; Jehovah ayeuteaunit num$Manitt8mun.
E.23.36 And the burden of the LORD shall ye mention no more: for every man's word shall be his burden; for ye have perverted the words of the living God, of the LORD of hosts our God.

α.23.37 Yeu pish kuttinnon quoshodtumwaenin, toh kuttin namp8hamunk Jehovah, kah Jehovah toh n8wau?
E.23.37 Thus shalt thou say to the prophet, What hath the LORD answered thee? and, What hath the LORD spoken?

α.23.38 Qut newutche kussimw8, 8weanun Jehovah, newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah, newutche yeu kussinneau kutt8onk, 8weanun Jehovah, kah nunnegont8wop en kuhhogkaout, nussip, matta pish kussimw8 8weanun Jehovah.
E.23.38 But since ye say, The burden of the LORD; therefore thus saith the LORD; Because ye say this word, The burden of the LORD, and I have sent unto you, saying, Ye shall not say, The burden of the LORD;

α.23.39 Newutche kusseh, nen papaquánne k8wananumunumw8, kah kutohquanumunumw8, kah keitotan aninnumauunog, kah k8sh8woog, kah kuppogkenunnumw8 wutch anaquabeh.
E.23.39 Therefore, behold, I, even I, will utterly forget you, and I will forsake you, and the city that I gave you and your fathers, and cast you out of my presence:

α.23.40 Kah kuppaudtauunumw8 machemoht[a]g spu[n]adtuonk, kah machemohtag akodchuonk matta pish wanatam8muk.
E.23.40 And I will bring an everlasting reproach upon you, and a perpetual shame, which shall not be forgotten.

α.24.1 LOrd nukkuhk8tomunkqunuh, kah kusseh, neesunnútogkodtash figsash ponamunash anaquohtag wut-Templum Jehovah, Nebuchadnezar Babilone ketass8t mahche missinohkonittue monchanont Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, kah Judae sontimoog, kah weekitteaenuog kah Smithsog wutch Jerusalem, kah uppas8uh Babilon.
E.24.1 The LORD shewed me, and, behold, two baskets of figs were set before the temple of the LORD, after that Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon had carried away captive Jeconiah the son of Jehoiakim king of Judah, and the princes of Judah, with the carpenters and smiths, from Jerusalem, and had brought them to Babylon.

α.24.2 Pasuk Man8t ohteau wunnegenash figsash, ogqueneunkquodtash figsash nish negonne kesa[n]8tagish: kah onkatog Man8t matchetaṣh figsash, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchittaṣh.
E.24.2 One basket had very good figs, even like the figs that are first ripe: and the other basket had very naughty figs, which could not be eaten, they were so bad.

α.24.3 Neit Jehovah nuttinuk, teagwas kenaum Jeremiah? kah nussip, figsaṣh: wunnegenash figsash, ahche wunnegenaṣh, kah machukiṣh ahche matchitaṣh, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchitaṣh.
E.24.3 Then said the LORD unto me, What seest thou, Jeremiah? And I said, Figs; the good figs, very good; and the evil, very evil, that cannot be eaten, they are so evil.

α.24.4 Neit wonk wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
E.24.4 Again the word of the LORD came unto me, saying,

α.24.5 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, ogqueneunkquotaṣh yeuṣh wanegukiṣh figs[a]ṣh, ne nuttinne waheoneau, neg masinohteamukeg wutch Judah, neg ann8t[è]amwéoneg yeu wutch ayeuonganit en wutohtuóut Caldeansoh wutche wanegik.
E.24.5 Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel; Like these good figs, so will I acknowledge them that are carried away captive of Judah, whom I have sent out of this place into the land of the Chaldeans for their good.

α.24.6 Newutche nag nummonunneauóog wutch wanegik, kah nag wonk nupp8oog yeu ut ohkeit, kah nag n8weekikkonóog, kah matta nunn8kinóog, kah nag nutohteuhkonunk, kah matta nukkodadchabukinóog.
E.24.6 For I will set mine eyes upon them for good, and I will bring them again to this land: and I will build them, and not pull them down; and I will plant them, and not pluck them up.

α.24.7 Kah nag nuttinnumauáog metah n8wahikquna[ó]ut, nen noh Jehovah, kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah nag nen um-Manitt8m8uh: newutche nag piṣh quinnuppeog ut nuhhogkat nashpe mamusse wuttahhou.
E.24.7 And I will give them an heart to know me, that I am the LORD: and they shall be my people, and I will be their God: for they shall return unto me with their whole heart.

α.24.8 Kah onatuh matche figsaṣh, niṣh woh mo meech8mukiṣh newutche mamatchitash (wunnamuhkut yeu wussin Jehovah) ne nuttinne aninnumauón Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah wussontimom8uh, kah ashqshoncheg ut Jerusalem, [á]shqshoncheg yeu ut ohkeit, kah neg wadohkitche Egypte ohkeit.
E.24.8 And as the evil figs, which cannot be eaten, they are so evil; surely thus saith the LORD, So will I give Zedekiah the king of Judah, and his princes, and the residue of Jerusalem, that remain in this land, and them that dwell in the land of Egypt:

α.24.9 Kah nag nuttinnumauóog ontahtauunat wame ass8tam8ongaṣh ohkeit, wutche woskeheaongan8, kehkomónat ushpunnamonat momontauonat, kah matchenánumáe unnonat ut wame ayeuonganehtu toh an8hkauog.
E.24.9 And I will deliver them to be removed into all the kingdoms of the earth for their hurt, to be a reproach and a proverb, a taunt and a curse, in all places whither I shall drive them.

α.24.10 Kah nutann8tam togkodteg, kah mahshagquodt, kah unninneaonk kenugke nagoh, nô pajeh mahchimwunneaóont wutch ohkeit, ne anumauogkup, kah 8sh8oh.
E.24.10 And I will send the sword, the famine, and the pestilence, among them, till they be consumed from off the land that I gave unto them and to their fathers.

α.25.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah papaume wame Judae missinninnúog, weyaue kodtum8m Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, ne 8skekodtum8g Nebuchad[r]ezzar Babylone ketass8t.
E.25.1 The word that came to Jeremiah concerning all the people of Judah in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, that was the first year of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon;

α.25.2 Ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen kôn8nompuh wame Judae missinninnúh, kah en wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, n8wau,
E.25.2 The which Jeremiah the prophet spake unto all the people of Judah, and to all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, saying,

α.25.3 Wutch nabo wunnishwe kodtum8mut Josiah wunnaumonuh Ammon Judae ketass8t, pajeh yeu kesukok (ne neesneechage nishwe kodtum8) wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk, kah kuttinnonunnáop, nompoáe omohkeon kah kodt8hkôon, qut matta kukkeihketam8uneau.
E.25.3 From the thirteenth year of Josiah the son of Amon king of Judah, even unto this day, that is the three and twentieth year, the word of the LORD hath come unto me, and I have spoken unto you, rising early and speaking; but ye have not hearkened.

α.25.4 Kah Jehovah nutann8nuk en wame kuhhogkaôut quoshodtumwaenûh wuttinninnúmoh, nompoáe omohkeon, kah ann8teamwean, qut matta ken8tam8m8, kah matta kenaúohtauogaemw8 n8tamunat.
E.25.4 And the LORD hath sent unto you all his servants the prophets, rising early and sending them; but ye have not hearkened, nor inclined your ear to hear.

α.25.5 Nag n8waog, qushkek wonk yeuyeu nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut, kah wutche kummatche usseonganit, kah ayekq ut ohkeit ne Jehovah aninnumunkqueog, kah k8sh8out micheme kah micheme.
E.25.5 They said, Turn ye again now every one from his evil way, and from the evil of your doings, and dwell in the land that the LORD hath given unto you and to your fathers for ever and ever:

α.25.6 Kah asuhkauúhteogk onkatogig manitt8og wuttinneumuhkauónat kah wowussumónat, kah ahque m8m8sqhegk en musquantam8onganit, nashpe kenutchegane anakausuongan8oash, kah matta piṣh k8woskhennomw8.
E.25.6 And go not after other gods to serve them, and to worship them, and provoke me not to anger with the works of your hands; and I will do you no hurt.

α.25.7 Qut matta kukkeiketiomw8 wussin Lord, onk woh kumm8hm8sqhinneaóut musquanitamunat nashpe kenutchegane anakausuonganóoaṣh, en k8woskhitteaongan8.
E.25.7 Yet ye have not hearkened unto me, saith the LORD; that ye might provoke me to anger with the works of your hands to your own hurt.

α.25.8 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, newutche matta ken8tam8mw8 nuttinn8waongaṣh.
E.25.8 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts; Because ye have not heard my words,

α.25.9 Kusseh, nutann8n kah nunneemun wame nannummiyeue teateashiyeuongash, wussin Jehovah, kah Nebuchadrezzar Babylone ketass8t nuttinninneum, k[a]h nag nutayeuuhkonittue pas8oog yeu ohkeit, kah ayeuuhkonittue neg na wadohkitcheg, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeush wutohtim[ó]ineaṣh waeenu, kah nag nuppapaquane pagwanóog, kah nutch[é]pshaheoog, kah nummishannánumweheaog, kah machemohtag touwushin.
E.25.9 Behold, I will send and take all the families of the north, saith the LORD, and Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon, my servant, and will bring them against this land, and against the inhabitants thereof, and against all these nations round about, and will utterly destroy them, and make them an astonishment, and an hissing, and perpetual desolations.

α.25.10 Nano, nag nutamaunumauóog póanittam8e wadatauatonkqussuonk kah weekontamóe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, wesseentamwaenin, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauadteaenin, wadtauatonkque togguhwhonganompskosh kah 8wequai8m wequananteg.
E.25.10 Moreover I will take from them the voice of mirth, and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride, the sound of the millstones, and the light of the candle.

α.25.11 Kah yeu mamusse ohke piṣh touwushin, kah chepshaonganú8, kah yeush wutohtimóinneaṣh piṣh wuttinneumuhkauáog Babylone ketass8tamwoh nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae.
E.25.11 And this whole land shall be a desolation, and an astonishment; and these nations shall serve the king of Babylon seventy years.

α.25.12 Kah piṣh n$nih nesausuk tahshinchag kodtum8aṣh mahtshunk, nussasamatoh Babylone ketass8t, kah ne wutohtim[ó]in, wussin Lord, wutch ummatcheseongan8, kah wutohtu Caldeansog, kah ne nummicheme touwushitteauwáhtauun.
E.25.12 And it shall come to pass, when seventy years are accomplished, that I will punish the king of Babylon, and that nation, saith the LORD, for their iniquity, and the land of the Chaldeans, and will make it perpetual desolations.

α.25.13 K[á]h nunnuhkinumau ne ohke wame nukkutt8wongaṣh ne áne ken8tam, wame ne ánsukwhosik yeu b8k, ne Jeremiah ayeuu[k]konittue quoshodtumwohtunk wame wutohtimóneaṣh.
E.25.13 And I will bring upon that land all my words which I have pronounced against it, even all that is written in this book, which Jeremiah hath prophesied against all the nations.

α.25.14 Newutche monatash wutohtimóneash, kah mogass8tamwog piṣh na 8chiinneauh wonk; kah nag piṣh nuttinunkquottauóog neaunak wutusseongan8aṣh, kah neaunak nehenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuonganooaṣh.
E.25.14 For many nations and great kings shall serve themselves of them also: and I will recompense them according to their deeds, and according to the works of their own hands.

α.25.15 Newutche yeu nuttugqun Lord um-Manitt8m8uh Israel, neemunush musquanittamwe wine wuttattamwaitch wutch nunnutcheganit, kah wame wutohtimóneash uttoh anann8nun wuttattamwáh.
E.25.15 For thus saith the LORD God of Israel unto me; Take the wine cup of this fury at my hand, and cause all the nations, to whom I send thee, to drink it.

α.25.16 Kah nag piṣh wuttattamwog, kah wogkouéog, kah kogkéyeuwaog, newutche togkodteg ne an8tam nag en kenugke.
E.25.16 And they shall drink, and be moved, and be mad, because of the sword that I will send among them.

α.25.17 Neit neemununup cup wutch Jehovah wunnutcheganit, kah wame wutohtimóneash n8tattamwaheoneáu, n$noh Jehovah ánunn8nukqueh.
E.25.17 Then took I the cup at the LORD's hand, and made all the nations to drink, unto whom the LORD had sent me:

α.25.18 Jerusalem, kah Judae keitotanaṣh, kah ukkeitass8tamóm8oh, kah wussontimóm8oh, n[á]g ayeuónaóut touwussinóonk, chepshaonk, mishanánittuonk, kah matchenanittuonk (neane yeu kesukok.)
E.25.18 To wit, Jerusalem, and the cities of Judah, and the kings thereof, and the princes thereof, to make them a desolation, an astonishment, an hissing, and a curse; as it is this day;

α.25.19 Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t, kah wuttinneumoh, kah wussontimomoh, kah wame ummissinninnúmoh.
E.25.19 Pharaoh king of Egypt, and his servants, and his princes, and all his people;

α.25.20 Kah wame kenukshae missinninnuog, kah wame ketass8tamwog ohkeit Uz, kah wame ketass8tamwog ohkeit Philistiansog, kah Ashkelon, kah Azzah, kah Ekron, kah sekqshoncheg ut Ashdod.
E.25.20 And all the mingled people, and all the kings of the land of Uz, and all the kings of the land of the Philistines, and Ashkelon, and Azzah, and Ekron, and the remnant of Ashdod,

α.25.21 Edom, kah Moab, kah wunnaumonuh Ammon.
E.25.21 Edom, and Moab, and the children of Ammon,

α.25.22 Kah wame Tyre ketass8tamwog, kah wame Zidon[é]e ketass8tamwog, kah munnáhhannu ketass8tamwog ut aongkoue ketahhanit.
E.25.22 And all the kings of Tyrus, and all the kings of Zidon, and the kings of the isles which are beyond the sea,

α.25.23 Dedan, kah tema, kah Buz, kah wame neg apitcheg aonkgoue adt nashik.
E.25.23 Dedan, and Tema, and Buz, and all that are in the utmost corners,

α.25.24 Kah wame Arabie ketass8tamwog, kah wame ukketass8tamómoh kenukshae missinninnúog apitcheg touohkomukqut.
E.25.24 And all the kings of Arabia, and all the kings of the mingled people that dwell in the desert,

α.25.25 Wame Zimrie ketass8tamwog, kah wame Elame ketass8tamwog, kah wame Medse ketass8tamwog.
E.25.25 And all the kings of Zimri, and all the kings of Elam, and all the kings of the Medes,

α.25.26 Kah wame nannummiyeue ketass8tamwog, nô apitcheg, kah páswoppitcheg, môeu, kah wame ass8tam8ongaṣh muttaohkeit, niṣh woskeche ut ohkeit, kah Sheshache ketass8t piṣh wutahtôe wuttattam8moh
E.25.26 And all the kings of the north, far and near, one with another, and all the kingdoms of the world, which are upon the face of the earth: and the king of Sheshach shall drink after them.

α.25.27 Newaj pish nag unnádt, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, wuttattum8k, kah kogkeiussippam8k, kah menadtam8k, kah kepshunk, kah omohkéhteók, newutche togkodteg ne ân8tam en kenugke kuhhogkaou.
E.25.27 Therefore thou shalt say unto them, Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Drink ye, and be drunken, and spue, and fall, and rise no more, because of the sword which I will send among you.

α.25.28 Kah piṣh n$nih, sekenamohettit nemunumunat wuttattamwaitch wutch kenutcheganit wuttattamunat, neit nag piṣh kuttinóog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnamuhkut piṣh k8tattamw8.
E.25.28 And it shall be, if they refuse to take the cup at thine hand to drink, then shalt thou say unto them, Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Ye shall certainly drink.

α.25.29 Newutche kusseh, nunn8che nuhkinnum machuk ut keitotanat, ne as8wésik wutche n8wesuonk, kah sun woh kuppapaquanne matta sasamatáhwhutteomw8? matta piṣh mat sasamatáhwhutteomw8: newutche n8wehquttum togkodteg ut wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit, wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.25.29 For, lo, I begin to bring evil on the city which is called by my name, and should ye be utterly unpunished? Ye shall not be unpunished: for I will call for a sword upon all the inhabitants of the earth, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.25.30 Newutche ayeuuhkonittue quoshódtumau wame yeush kutt8wongash, kah nag us, Jehovah piṣh mishont8wau wutch wohqut, kah kussont8wau wutch 8neetupanatamwe appuonganit, piṣh menuhke mishont8wau ut wutappuonganit, piṣh ogque mishont8wau neg tahtahshkuhkogig weenomineash, ayeuuhkonittue wame wadohkitcheg ohkeit.
E.25.30 Therefore prophesy thou against them all these words, and say unto them, The LORD shall roar from on high, and utter his voice from his holy habitation; he shall mightily roar upon his habitation; he shall give a shout, as they that tread the grapes, against all the inhabitants of the earth.

α.25.31 Mishont8waonk piṣh peyaum8 wehqshik ohke: newutche Jehovah penuantam wutohtimoneash: piṣh kéketehtam wame weyaus, neh machetinutcheh ummagunuh en togkodteganit wussin Jehovah.
E.25.31 A noise shall come even to the ends of the earth; for the LORD hath a controversy with the nations, he will plead with all flesh; he will give them that are wicked to the sword, saith the LORD.

α.25.32 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, machuk piṣh sohham8m8 wutch wutohtimoinneat en wutohtimoinneat, kah mishe pemsquoh piṣh waabu wutch weehqshik ohke.
E.25.32 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, Behold, evil shall go forth from nation to nation, and a great whirlwind shall be raised up from the coasts of the earth.

α.25.33 Kah nashoncheh Jehovah, ne kesukok, piṣh wutch wee[h]qshik muttaok onk yaan weehqshik: nag matta piṣh maumuttam8[on]óog, asuh mukkinóog, asuh posekinóog, nag piṣh anohkeyeu8og ut ohkeit.
E.25.33 And the slain of the LORD shall be at that day from one end of the earth even unto the other end of the earth: they shall not be lamented, neither gathered, nor buried; they shall be dung upon the ground.

α.25.34 Mishont8wak kenaau nanaushepsaénuog, kah mau8k, kah ôiyômegk pukquee, kenaau negonneweógish ut flokut: newutch kenushitteae kesukodtoash, kah naswaiyeue pakodjteausuash, kah piṣh kutogque penushomw8 wunne wishquadt.
E.25.34 Howl, ye shepherds, and cry; and wallow yourselves in the ashes, ye principal of the flock: for the days of your slaughter and of your dispersions are accomplished; and ye shall fall like a pleasant vessel.

α.25.35 Kah nanaushepsaenuog matta piṣh ohtoog toh woh ashphow[á]hettit: asuh negonnewutcheg ut flokut pohquohhamunat.
E.25.35 And the shepherds shall have no way to flee, nor the principal of the flock to escape.

α.25.36 OOwadtauatonkqussue mauongan8 nanaushepsaenuog, kah wutt8noongan8 negoneyeuutcheg ut flockut, newutche Jehovah matchehteou wuttittanadtupp8ongan8.
E.25.36 A voice of the cry of the shepherds, and an howling of the principal of the flock, shall be heard: for the LORD hath spoiled their pasture.

α.25.37 Kah wunohteáe áyeuongaṣh tuméhthamun[a]ṣh, newutche ummishe musquanitteaonk Lord.
E.25.37 And the peaceable habitations are cut down because of the fierce anger of the LORD.

α.25.38 Ahquontam ukkuppiyeum onatuh qunnónou, newutche nag wutohkou touwushin, newutche wutchekee usseonk sunukkutchóhh8waénin, kah newutche wutunkque musquanitteaonk.
E.25.38 He hath forsaken his covert, as the lion: for their land is desolate because of the fierceness of the oppressor, and because of his fierce anger.

α.26.1 NOOche nanawuñuadt Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, wuttinn8waonk 8m88 Jehovah$ut, n8wau,
E.26.1 In the beginning of the reign of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah came this word from the LORD, saying,

α.26.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neepaush chippinneutunkanit ut Jehovah wekit, kah ken8s wame Judae keitotanash, neg paoncheg waussumónat ut wekit Jehovah, wame kutt8wongash nish an8nonish nag unnónaóut: ass[a]nukon pasuk kutt8onk.
E.26.2 Thus saith the LORD; Stand in the court of the LORD's house, and speak unto all the cities of Judah, which come to worship in the LORD's house, all the words that I command thee to speak unto them; diminish not a word:

α.26.3 N8tamwehettit, kah nishnoh pasuk qushkeit wutch ummatche mayut, onk woh nutaiuskoiantam ne machuk kodnéhheog, newutche ummatche usseongan8oaṣh.
E.26.3 If so be they will hearken, and turn every man from his evil way, that I may repent me of the evil, which I purpose to do unto them because of the evil of their doings.

α.26.4 Kah piṣh nag kuttinóog yeu wussin Jehovah, matta kukkehtiéog, pomusháonónat naumatuonk noh|pónog anaquabeog.
E.26.4 And thou shalt say unto them, Thus saith the LORD; If ye will not hearken to me, to walk in my law, which I have set before you,

α.26.5 N8tamunat ukkutt8wongan8oaṣh quoshodtumwaénue nuttinneumog, neg ann8nogig en kuhhogkaóut, naneeswe nompoáe omohkeon, kah ann8nog (qut matta ken8tamomw8.)
E.26.5 To hearken to the words of my servants the prophets, whom I sent unto you, both rising up early, and sending them, but ye have not hearkened;

α.26.6 Neit yeu wetu nutogquehteauun Shiloh, kah yeu keitotan nummatanatamwe hettamwátauun ut wame ohkee wutohtimoneaṣh.
E.26.6 Then will I make this house like Shiloh, and will make this city a curse to all the nations of the earth.

α.26.7 Neit sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wame missinninnuog n8tauáog Jeremiahoh wussinneat yeush kutt8wongash ut wekit Jehovah.
E.26.7 So the priests and the prophets and all the people heard Jeremiah speaking these words in the house of the LORD.

α.26.8 Kah n$niyeup mahche Jeremiah unn8wadt wame Jehovah neanunn8nont, ken8nónat wame missinninnuog: sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog, kah wame missinninnuog wuttohqunoush, n8waog, wunnamuhkut pish kenup.
E.26.8 Now it came to pass, when Jeremiah had made an end of speaking all that the LORD had commanded him to speak unto all the people, that the priests and the prophets and all the people took him, saying, Thou shalt surely die.

α.26.9 Tohwutch quoshódtuman ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, unn8waan, yeu wetu piṣh tatuppeyeu8 Shiloh, kah yeu keitotan piṣh touwushin, amtta ayéyinat: kah wame missinninnuog ayeuuhkonittue miyaéhtauwaog Jeremiahoh, ut wekit Jehovah.
E.26.9 Why hast thou prophesied in the name of the LORD, saying, This house shall be like Shiloh, and this city shall be desolate without an inhabitant?  And all the people were gathered against Jeremiah in the house of the LORD.

α.26.10 Judae sontimòog yeush n8tamwéhettit, neit nag kuhkuhqueog wutch ketass8t wekit en wekit Jehovah, kah nag appuog ut ahhut petutteamuk wuskesquont ut wekit Jehovah.
E.26.10 When the princes of Judah heard these things, then they came up from the king's house unto the house of the LORD, and sat down in the entry of the new gate of the LORD's house.

α.26.11 Neit sephausuenuog kah quoshodtumwaenuog ken8naog sontimoh, kah wame missinninnúh n8waog: yeuoh wosketomp tumuhhouau nupp8onk, newutch yeuoh ayeuuhkonittue quoshaeu missohham yeu keitotan, neane n8tamóg ut kuhtauogk8w[ô]ut.
E.26.11 Then spake the priests and the prophets unto the princes and to all the people, saying, This man is worthy to die; for he hath prophesied against this city, as ye have heard with your ears.

α.26.12 Neit Jeremiah ken8nau wame sontimoh, kah wame missinninnúh, n8wau, Jehovah nutann8nuk ayeuuhkonittue quoshóe missohhamunat yeu wetu, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeu keitotan, wame kutt8wongash niṣh n8tamógish.
E.26.12 Then spake Jeremiah unto all the princes and to all the people, saying, The LORD sent me to prophesy against this house and against this city all the words that ye have heard.

α.26.13 Newutche yeuyeu sampweteau8k kummay8woash kah kutusseonganóoash, kah n8swehtam8k 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8, kah Jehovah piṣh aiuskoiantam ne machuk ayeuuhkonittue pogkóduttumunkqueóg.
E.26.13 Therefore now amend your ways and your doings, and obey the voice of the LORD your God; and the LORD will repent him of the evil that he hath pronounced against you.

α.26.14 Qut nen, kusseh, nutap kenutchegan8wout: unnéhhek uttoh an tápeneámók.
E.26.14 As for me, behold, I am in your hand: do with me as seemeth good and meet unto you.

α.26.15 Qut wahteau8k wunnamuhkut, nushéóg, wunnamuhkut piṣh kenuhkenumauómw8 mat woskehuwae musqueheonk ut kuhhogkaóut, kah yeuut otanat, & neg na wadohkitcheg: newutche wunnamuhkut Jehovah nutann8nuk en kuhhogkaout, unn8wonat wame yeush ut kuttauogk8wout.
E.26.15 But know ye for certain, that if ye put me to death, ye shall surely bring innocent blood upon yourselves, and upon this city, and upon the inhabitants thereof: for of a truth the LORD hath sent me unto you to speak all these words in your ears.

α.26.16 Neit sontimoog kah wame missinninnúog, unnaog sephausuenuh, kah quoshodtumwaénúh, yeuoh matta tumuhhouóou nuppun: newutche kukken8nukqun ut 8wesuonganit Lord kum$Manitt8mun.
E.26.16 Then said the princes and all the people unto the priests and to the prophets; This man is not worthy to die: for he hath spoken to us in the name of the LORD our God.

α.26.17 Neit nawhutch eldersog ne ohkeit, neepoog kah ken8naog wame mukkinnée missinninnúh, n8waog,
E.26.17 Then rose up certain of the elders of the land, and spake to all the assembly of the people, saying,

α.26.18 Micah wut-Moràshit, quoshodtumup pomontog Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, kah ken8nau wame Judae missinninnuh, n8wau, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Zion piṣh ogque anaskhamun ohteuhkonit, kah Jerusalem piṣh nanómukqueau; kah weetuome wadchu, touohkomukque qunuhqui ayeuongash.
E.26.18 Micah the Morasthite prophesied in the days of Hezekiah king of Judah, and spake to all the people of Judah, saying, Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Zion shall be plowed like a field, and Jerusalem shall become heaps, and the mountain of the house as the high places of a forest.

α.26.19 Hezechiah kah wame Judah wunnushóóussohhoh? sunnummatta wabesuonauous Lord, kah wehquetumauop Lord kah Lord aiuskoiantamup ne machuk, nean pogkodtittumauomp? ne woh nashpe kuppaudtauónan kukketeahogkôununónog mahshe matchuk.
E.26.19 Did Hezekiah king of Judah and all Judah put him at all to death?  did he not fear the LORD, and besought the LORD, and the LORD repented him of the evil which he had pronounced against them? Thus might we procure great evil against our souls.

α.26.20 Wonk na mo wosketomp noh quoshoe missohhogkup ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, Urijah wunnaumonuh Shemajah, wutche[i] Kirajth$jearim: noh quoshae mussohhogkup ayeuuhkonittue yeu keitotan, kah ayeuuhkonittue yeu ohke, neaunak wame ukkutt8wongash Jeremiah.
E.26.20 And there was also a man that prophesied in the name of the LORD, Urijah the son of Shemaiah of Kirjathjearim, who prophesied against this city and against this land according to all the words of Jeremiah.

α.26.21 Kah Jehojakim ketass8t, kah wame ummenuhkesuenumoh, kah wame sontimóog n8tamwehettit ukkutt8wongash, ketass8t ukkod-nushoh: qut Urijah n8tog, wabesúp, kah wussemop, kah auop Egypt.
E.26.21 And when Jehoiakim the king, with all his mighty men, and all the princes, heard his words, the king sought to put him to death: but when Urijah heard it, he was afraid, and fled, and went into Egypt;

α.26.22 Kah Jehojakim ketass8t ann8nau wosketompuh en Egypt, Elnathan wunnaumonuh Achbor, kah wosketompoh weechok en Egypt.
E.26.22 And Jehoiakim the king sent men into Egypt, namely, Elnathan the son of Achbor, and certain men with him into Egypt.

α.26.23 Kah sohh8unaog Urijah wutch Egypt, kah uppas8ouh Jehojakimit ketass8t, kah wunnushoh nashpe togkodteg, kahwuttinnohkonoh nupp8e wuhhogkuh en 8weenohkeout missinninnuog.
E.26.23 And they fetched forth Urijah out of Egypt, and brought him unto Jehoiakim the king; who slew him with the sword, and cast his dead body into the graves of the common people.

α.26.24 Qut wunnutcheg Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan weetomau Jeremiahoh, matta woh umag8unat en wunnutchegan8óut missinninnúog, wunnushonaout.
E.26.24 Nevertheless the hand of Ahikam the son of Shaphan was with Jeremiah, that they should not give him into the hand of the people to put him to death.

α.27.1 NOOche nanauwunnuadt Jehovjakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, yeu kutt8wonk peyaonukqun Jeremiah wutch Lordut, n8wau,
E.27.1 In the beginning of the reign of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah came this word unto Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.27.2 Yeu Jehovah nuttugqun, ayimau kuhhog kishpissuongash kah yoakash, kah ponsh kussittuppukanit,
E.27.2 Thus saith the LORD to me; Make thee bonds and yokes, and put them upon thy neck,

α.27.3 Kah niṣh negonshhuash en Edome ketass8tamwut, kah en Moabe ketass8tamwut, kah en Amonitse ketass8tamwut, kah Tyruse ketass8tamwut, kah Zidone ketass8tamwut, ut wunnutchegan8out onn8naenuog neg paoncheg Jerusalem, en Zedechiahut Judae ketass8t.
E.27.3 And send them to the king of Edom, and to the king of Moab, and to the king of the Ammonites, and to the king of Tyrus, and to the king of Zidon, by the hand of the messengers which come to Jerusalem unto Zedekiah king of Judah;

α.27.4 Kah nag us wuttinnon[a]oont wussontimóm8oh: yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau wussontimóm8og,
E.27.4 And command them to say unto their masters, Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Thus shall ye say unto your masters;

α.27.5 Nutayim ohke, wosketomp kah puppinashim neg apitcheg wosketohkeit, nashpe ummishe menuhkesuonk, kah nashpe summagunumwe nuhput, kah nuttinnumauón uttoh woh kod aninnumaúog.
E.27.5 I have made the earth, the man and the beast that are upon the ground, by my great power and by my outstretched arm, and have given it unto whom it seemed meet unto me.

α.27.6 Kah yeuyeu wame yeush wutohtimoneash nummagunash en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, nuttinneum, kah ohteuhkone puppinashimwog wonk nuttinninnumau, 8tinninneumuhkongqunat.
E.27.6 And now have I given all these lands into the hand of Nebuchadnezzar the king of Babylon, my servant; and the beasts of the field have I given him also to serve him.

α.27.7 Kah wame wutohtimoneash pish 8tinninneumuhkauouh, kah wunnaumonuh, kah wunnaumonuh wunnaumonuh, nô pajeh wutohkeé ahquompiyeum peyaum8uk: kah neit monateash wutohtimoneash kah mogke ketass8tamwog pish 8chiyeuounouh.
E.27.7 And all nations shall serve him, and his son, and his son's son, until the very time of his land come: and then many nations and great kings shall serve themselves of him.

α.27.8 Kah pish n$nih, ne wutohtimoin, kah ass8tamoonk ne matta wadtinninneumuhkauog nenan Nebucadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah matta agwe ponamog wussittuppuk 8weyokum Babilone ketass8t, ne wutohtimoin pish nussásamatahhamun, wussin Lord, nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, nô pajeh nummohtupanonaoont nashpe wunnutcheg.
E.27.8 And it shall come to pass, that the nation and kingdom which will not serve the same Nebuchadnezzar the king of Babylon, and that will not put their neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon, that nation will I punish, saith the LORD, with the sword, and with the famine, and with the pestilence, until I have consumed them by his hand.

α.27.9 Newutche ahque n8tau, kukquoshodtumwaenumog, asuh quoshae missohhamwaenuog, asuh kuttinnukquomweneum8woog, asuh kuppauwom8oog, asuh kummoneteum8oog, neg ànukqueogig, n8waog, matta pish k8tinninneumuhkauomw8 Babilone ketass8t.
E.27.9 Therefore hearken not ye to your prophets, nor to your diviners, nor to your dreamers, nor to your enchanters, nor to your sorcerers, which speak unto you, saying, Ye shall not serve the king of Babylon:

α.27.10 Newutche nag kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog, nòadtit kuttin ontashikq[a]nnaoont wutch kutohtuout, ônk woh kussohh8kauununnaoont, onk woh kenuppunaoont.
E.27.10 For they prophesy a lie unto you, to remove you far from your land; and that I should drive you out, and ye should perish.

α.27.11 Qut wutohtimoneash neg paudtunkeg wussittipukan8 ut agwe weyokumut Babilone ketass8t, kah wadtinneumuhkauoncheg yeug nutappeheoog nehenwonche wutohtkeyeuout, wussin Lord, kah nag pish wutohteuhkoneau, kah pish na 8tohkinneau.
E.27.11 But the nations that bring their neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon, and serve him, those will I let remain still in their own land, saith the LORD; and they shall till it, and dwell therein.

α.27.12 Kah wonk nuttin Zedéchiah Judae ketass8t neaunak wame yeush kutt8wongash nussip, paudto8k kussittippukanash ut agwe weyokum Babilone ketass8t, kah noh wuttinneumuhkok, kah ummissinninnumoh kah pomantam8k.
E.27.12 I spake also to Zedekiah king of Judah according to all these words, saying, Bring your necks under the yoke of the king of Babylon, and serve him and his people, and live.

α.27.13 Tohwaj nuppog, ken kah kummissinninnumog nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk neane ayeuuhkonittue ken8tog Jehovah wutohtimoin noh matta wadtinninnumuhkauonk Babilone ketass8t?
E.27.13 Why will ye die, thou and thy people, by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence, as the LORD hath spoken against the nation that will not serve the king of Babylon?

α.27.14 Newutche kuhkeitam8hteok wuttinn8waongan8oash quoshodtumwaeenuog, neg kon8nukqueogig, n8wahettit, matta pish k8tinninneumuhkauomw8 Babilone ketass8t: newutch kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog.
E.27.14 Therefore hearken not unto the words of the prophets that speak unto you, saying, Ye shall not serve the king of Babylon: for they prophesy a lie unto you.

α.27.15 Newutche mag nag nutann8noog, wussin Jehovah, qut onch pann8wae quoshodtumwog ut n8wesuonganit, onk woh kussohh8kauunumw8, onk woh kuppagwanyimw8 kenaau kah quoshodtumwaenuog ne quoshae missohhamunkqueogig.
E.27.15 For I have not sent them, saith the LORD, yet they prophesy a lie in my name; that I might drive you out, and that ye might perish, ye, and the prophets that prophesy unto you.

α.27.16 Kah wonk nukken8nomp sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnuog, nussip, yeu wussin Jehovah, n8tam8hteok ukkutt8wongan8oash kukquoshodtumwaeneum8oog neg quoshae missohhamunkqueogig, n8waog, kusseh, wishquash ut Jehovah wekit, pish teanuk nompe paudtauunash wutch Babilon, Newutche nag kuppann8wae quoshodtumunk8oog.
E.27.16 Also I spake to the priests and to all this people, saying, Thus saith the LORD; Hearken not to the words of your prophets that prophesy unto you, saying, Behold, the vessels of the LORD's house shall now shortly be brought again from Babylon: for they prophesy a lie unto you.

α.27.17 Nag ahque n8tau: wuttinneumuhkok Babilone ketass8t, kah pomantam8k: tohwutch woh yeu keitotan mahchumwushik?
E.27.17 Hearken not unto them; serve the king of Babylon, and live: wherefore should this city be laid waste?

α.27.18 Qut tohneit nag quoshodtumwaenuhettit, kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah toh$neit nah weetomont, peantamauwahettich yeuyeu Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nish wishquash sequshunkish ut wekit Jehovah, kah weekit Judae ketass8t, kah ut Jerusalem, onk woh mo 8mun8ash Babilon.
E.27.18 But if they be prophets, and if the word of the LORD be with them, let them now make intercession to the LORD of hosts, that the vessels which are left in the house of the LORD, and in the house of the king of Judah, and at Jerusalem, go not to Babylon.

α.27.19 Newutche yeu n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit, papaume pillarsash, kah papaume keitoh, kah papaume agweyeu8gish, kah papaume ashqshunkish wishquash, nish|ohtagish yeu otanat.
E.27.19 For thus saith the LORD of hosts concerning the pillars, and concerning the sea, and concerning the bases, and concerning the residue of the vessels that remain in this city.

α.27.20 Nish Nebuchadnezar Babilone ketass8t mat neemunum8gkupash, masinohtead Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehojachin Judae ketass8t, wutch Jerusaleme en Babilon kah wame Judae kah Jerusalem sontimoog.
E.27.20 Which Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon took not, when he carried away captive Jeconiah the son of Jehoiakim king of Judah from Jerusalem to Babylon, and all the nobles of Judah and Jerusalem;

α.27.21 Nux yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel papaume wishquash nish ashqshunkish ut Jehovah wekit, k[á]h ut wekit Judae ketass8t kah Jerusalém.
E.27.21 Yea, thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, concerning the vessels that remain in the house of the LORD, and in the house of the king of Judah and of Jerusalem;

α.27.22 Nash pish uss8tauunash Babylon, kah na pish ohteau nô pajeh ne kesukok nag natauwaheog wussin Lord, neit pish wonk nukkuhkuhk8uttauunash, kah nompatauunash yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.27.22 They shall be carried to Babylon, and there shall they be until the day that I visit them, saith the LORD; then will I bring them up, and restore them to this place.

α.28.1 KAh n$niyeup ne nan kodtumuk n8che nánawunnuadt Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, yaue kodtum8g, kah napanna adtahs8it nepauz, Hananiah wunnaumonuh Azur quoshodtumwaen, noh wadchiit Gibeon, nukk[e]n8nuk ut Jehovah wekit, ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnúog, n8wau,
E.28.1 And it came to pass the same year, in the beginning of the reign of Zedekiah king of Judah, in the fourth year, and in the fifth month, that Hananiah the son of Azur the prophet, which was of Gibeon, spake unto me in the house of the LORD, in the presence of the priests and of all the people, saying,

α.28.2 Yeu wussin Lord ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel n8wau, nuppohqshan weyoakumoh Babilone ketass8t.
E.28.2 Thus speaketh the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, saying, I have broken the yoke of the king of Babylon.

α.28.3 Wuttuhshit yeu neeneese kodtum8, piṣh wonk nuppaudto yeuut ayeuonganit wame wishquash wadchikiish Jehovah wekit, niṣh Nebucad-nezzer Babilone ketass8t amaunukupash yeu wutch ayeuonganit, kah as8tunkupash Babilon.
E.28.3 Within two full years will I bring again into this place all the vessels of the LORD's house, that Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon took away from this place, and carried them to Babylon:

α.28.4 Kah wonk nuppasou yeuut ayeuonganit Jeconiah wunnaumonuh Jehoiachim Judae ketass8t, weeche wame missinóog neg aumpanneg Babilon wussin Jehovah, newutche nuppokshadtoh weyokum Babilone ketass8t
E.28.4 And I will bring again to this place Jeconiah the son of Jehoiakim king of Judah, with all the captives of Judah, that went into Babylon, saith the LORD: for I will break the yoke of the king of Babylon.

α.28.5 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaén unnau quoshodtumwaenúh Hananiah ut anaquabhettit sephausuenuog, kah ut anaquabhettit wame missinninnúog, neg neepauutcheg wekit Lord.
E.28.5 Then the prophet Jeremiah said unto the prophet Hananiah in the presence of the priests, and in the presence of all the people that stood in the house of the LORD,

α.28.6 Quoshodtumwaen Jeremiah n8wau, Amen, Jehovah ne usseiteh, Lord usseitch wuttinn8waongash niṣh quoshae missohhogish, paudtauunat wonk wishquash wadchiigish wekit Jehovah kah neg wame másinóhteamukuppanneg, wutch Babilon, yeuut ayeuonganit.
E.28.6 Even the prophet Jeremiah said, Amen: the LORD do so: the LORD perform thy words which thou hast prophesied, to bring again the vessels of the LORD's house, and all that is carried away captive, from Babylon into this place.

α.28.7 Qut yeuyeu n8tash yeu kutt8wonk an8wi ut kehtauogkut, kah ut wuhtauogkut wame missinninnúh.
E.28.7 Nevertheless hear thou now this word that I speak in thine ears, and in the ears of all the people;

α.28.8 Quoshodtumwaenuog neg negonuhkiitcheg, & neg negonuhkunkqueaneg n8adt, nag ayeuuhkonittue quoshoe missohhamwontamwog monaash wutohtimoneash, kah kehche ass8tam8ongash, papaume mattompagq, kah papaume machuk, kah papaume enninneaonl.
E.28.8 The prophets that have been before me and before thee of old prophesied both against many countries, and against great kingdoms, of war, and of evil, and of pestilence.

α.28.9 Quoshodtumwaen noh quoshae missohhog wunohteaonk, wuttinn8waonk quoshodtumwaen nnák, neit quoshodtumwaen piṣh waheau, wunnamuhkut Jehovah wutañ8nuh.
E.28.9 The prophet which prophesieth of peace, when the word of the prophet shall come to pass, then shall the prophet be known, that the LORD hath truly sent him.

α.28.10 Neit Hannaniah quoshodtumwaen, nemunau yoakoh wutch Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen wussittuppukanit, kah uppohqenumun.
E.28.10 Then Hananiah the prophet took the yoke from off the prophet Jeremiah's neck, and brake it.

α.28.11 Kah Hannaniah kutt8, ut wame anaquabhettit missinninnúog n8wau, yeu wussin Lord, ne nuttinne pohquenon weyokumoh Nebuchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t, wutch wussittippukan8wóut wame wutohtimóneunk, ash naneese kodtumun8kup, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen monchu.
E.28.11 And Hananiah spake in the presence of all the people, saying, Thus saith the LORD; Even so will I break the yoke of Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon from the neck of all nations within the space of two full years. And the prophet Jeremiah went his way.

α.28.12 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen (mahche Hananiah quoshodtumwaen pohquenont yoakoh wutch wussittippukanit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen) n8wau,
E.28.12 Then the word of the LORD came unto Jeremiah the prophet, after that Hananiah the prophet had broken the yoke from off the neck of the prophet Jeremiah, saying,

α.28.13 Monch, us Hannaniah n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, ken kuppohquenum mehtugque yokash, qut nag piṣ[k] kenompe ayimauoog mussehchuogque yoakoh.
E.28.13 Go and tell Hananiah, saying, Thus saith the LORD; Thou hast broken the yokes of wood; but thou shalt make for them yokes of iron.

α.28.14 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel nupponam misséhchuogque yoak wussittippukan8óut wame wutohtimóinneunk, onk woh nag wuttinneumuhkauaog Nebucchad-nezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah nag piṣh 8tinninneumuhkauouh kah wonk nuttinninnumau wonk ohteuhkone puppinashimwoh.
E.28.14 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; I have put a yoke of iron upon the neck of all these nations, that they may serve Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon; and they shall serve him: and I have given him the beasts of the field also.

α.28.15 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen unnau Hananiahoh quoshodtumwaen: yeuyeu n8tash Hananiah, Jehovah matta kut[á]nn8nuk8h, qut yeug missinninnúog kuppabahtantamwaheóog pann8waonk.
E.28.15 Then said the prophet Jeremiah unto Hananiah the prophet, Hear now, Hananiah; The LORD hath not sent thee; but thou makest this people to trust in a lie.

α.28.16 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, kuppogkenush wutch wosket-ohkit: yeu kodtumuk piṣh kenup newutche kukkuhk8tomwehteam cheketauónat Lord.
E.28.16 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will cast thee from off the face of the earth: this year thou shalt die, because thou hast taught rebellion against the LORD.

α.28.17 Neit Hannaniah quoshodumwaen nup ne nan kodtumuk, nabo nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz.
E.28.17 So Hananiah the prophet died the same year in the seventh month.

α.29.1 YEuyeu yeush wussukwhosue kutt8wongash, nish Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen negonshhuadche wutch Jerusalem, en ashqshoncheg eldersog, neg masinóhteámukeg, kah en sephausuénuut, kah en quoshodtumwaenuut, kahen wame missinninnuut, neh Nebuchhádnezzar másinohteacheh wutch Jerusalem en Babilon.
E.29.1 Now these are the words of the letter that Jeremiah the prophet sent from Jerusalem unto the residue of the elders which were carried away captives, and to the priests, and to the prophets, and to all the people whom Nebuchadnezzar had carried away captive from Jerusalem to Babylon;

α.29.2 (Ne mahche Jeconiah ketass8t, kah sonksq, kah eunuchsog, kah Judae kah Jerusaleme sontimoog, kah weekitteaenuog, kah smithsog mahche amaeog wutch Jerusalem)
E.29.2 (After that Jeconiah the king, and the queen, and the eunuchs, the princes of Judah and Jerusalem, and the carpenters, and the smiths, were departed from Jerusalem;)

α.29.3 Nashpe wunnutcheganit Elasah wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Gemariah wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, neh Zedechiah Judae ketass8t ánan8noncheh Babilon, en Nebucchadnezzar Babilone ketass8t n8wau,
E.29.3 By the hand of Elasah the son of Shaphan, and Gemariah the son of Hilkiah, (whom Zedekiah king of Judah sent unto Babylon to Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon) saying,

α.29.4 Yeu wuttinnon Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um$Manitt8moh Israel, wame neh másinóhteamukeh, neg masináhhuwáheogig wutch Jerusalem en Babilon.
E.29.4 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, unto all that are carried away captives, whom I have caused to be carried away from Jerusalem unto Babylon;

α.29.5 Wekikunk kah ne ayék, kah ohteuhkontam8k tanohketeaongash, kah meech8k ne nóh adtanegik.
E.29.5 Build ye houses, and dwell in them; and plant gardens, and eat the fruit of them;

α.29.6 Ummittamwussek, kah wunnaumonaek kah wuttaunek, kah ummittamwussuhkók kenaumona[o]og, kah 8wessukkauhkok kuttaun8oog, onk woh nag wunnaumoniyeuog kah wuttaunuog, onk woh na kuttit monôneau, kah matta kutogguhs8mw8.
E.29.6 Take ye wives, and beget sons and daughters; and take wives for your sons, and give your daughters to husbands, that they may bear sons and daughters; that ye may be increased there, and not diminished.

α.29.7 Kah nattinneham8k 8nohteaonk ne keitotan uttoh an missinóhkonittuáhinóg, kah peantamwanshúk Jehovahut, newutche ne piṣh k8nohteamw8 wunohteom8uk.
E.29.7 And seek the peace of the city whither I have caused you to be carried away captives, and pray unto the LORD for it: for in the peace thereof shall ye have peace.

α.29.8 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kukquosh[ó]dtumwaenúmog, kah quoshoe missohhogig, neg apitcheg kenashom8óut as8kekodteamuk8teok, kah kuhkeihtam8hteok kuttinukquom8ongan8oash, nish anukquo[m]ogish.
E.29.8 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Let not your prophets and your diviners, that be in the midst of you, deceive you, neither hearken to your dreams which ye cause to be dreamed.

α.29.9 Newutche nag pann8waeu kukquoshoe missohhamunk8oog ut n8wesuonganit: matta nag nutann8noog wussin Lord.
E.29.9 For they prophesy falsely unto you in my name: I have not sent them, saith the LORD.

α.29.10 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, mahche nesausuk tahshinchage kodtum8ash mahtshunk ut Babilon, pish kenatauwahunumw8, kah pish nutussem n8ne kutt8onk en kuhhogkaoont, kukquinnuppekompauwah[eo]un naoont yeu en ayeuonganit.
E.29.10 For thus saith the LORD, That after seventy years be accomplished at Babylon I will visit you, and perform my good word toward you, in causing you to return to this place.

α.29.11 Newutche n8wahteoh unnanetam8ongash, nish ananatamonish en kuhhogkaout, wussin Jehovah, wunohteae unnantam8ongash, kah matta machuk, kuttinnumauununaoont pahtussuwontamoe wohkukquoshin.
E.29.11 For I know the thoughts that I think toward you, saith the LORD, thoughts of peace, and not of evil, to give you an expected end.

α.29.12 Neit pish kuppeantamaiimw8, kah pish kummonchem8, kah pish kuppeantamiimw8, kah pish ken8tauunumw8.
E.29.12 Then shall ye call upon me, and ye shall go and pray unto me, and I will hearken unto you.

α.29.13 Kah pish kenatinneahimw8, kah pish kummishkiimw8, natinneahwheog nashpe mamusse kuttahhou.
