E.29.13 And ye shall seek me, and find me, when ye shall search for me with all your heart.

α.29.14 Kah pish kenamhimw8 8wau Jehovah, kah pish nukquinnuppinum kummissinnoongan8, kah kummukkinunumw8 wutch wame wutohtimoinneat, kah wutch wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh ann8hkauunog, wussin Jehovah kah wonk pish kuppas8unumw8, ut ayeuonganit ne$waj missinohkonuwahinogkup.
E.29.14 And I will be found of you, saith the LORD: and I will turn away your captivity, and I will gather you from all the nations, and from all the places whither I have driven you, saith the LORD; and I will bring you again into the place whence I caused you to be carried away captive.

α.29.15 Newutche kussimwop, Jehovah kuttahshinumunkq[un] quoshodtumwaenuh ut Babylon,
E.29.15 Because ye have said, The LORD hath raised us up prophets in Babylon;

α.29.16 Yeu wussin Jehováh papaume ketass8t noh quenapit wutappuonganit David, kah papaume wame missinninnuog neg apitcheg ne otanat, kah papaume kematt8oog neg matta weeche sohham8muk8ogig en missinnainneut.
E.29.16 Know that thus saith the LORD of the king that sitteth upon the throne of David, and of all the people that dwelleth in this city, and of your brethren that are not gone forth with you into captivity;

α.29.17 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauoog togkodteg, mahshagquodt kah enninneaonk kah nutogqheoog nishkeneunkque figsut, nish woh mo meech8mukish newutche matchitash.
E.29.17 Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Behold, I will send upon them the sword, the famine, and the pestilence, and will make them like vile figs, that cannot be eaten, they are so evil.

α.29.18 Kah nag nunn8sittahwhoog, nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe máhshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, kah nag nupponoog ontsappinneat en wame ass8tam8ongash ut muttaohkit: mattanumwae unnonaoont, kah chepshónaóont & mishonánumónaoont, kah kekomonaoont ut kenugke wame wutohtimoneat uttoh ann8hkauog.
E.29.18 And I will persecute them with the sword, with the famine, and with the pestilence, and will deliver them to be removed to all the kingdoms of the earth, to be a curse, and an astonishment, and an hissing, and a reproach, among all the nations whither I have driven them:

α.29.19 Newutche matta kukkeitamoog nukkutt8wongash wussin Jehovah, nish negons[h]huwaánish nashpe quoshodtumwae nuttinnumog, nompoae omohkeon, kah ann8nog qut matta ken8tam8mw8 wussin Jehovah.
E.29.19 Because they have not hearkened to my words, saith the LORD, which I sent unto them by my servants the prophets, rising up early and sending them; but ye would not hear, saith the LORD.

α.29.20 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame kenaau missinoog neg ann8nogeg wutch Jerusalem en Babylon.
E.29.20 Hear ye therefore the word of the LORD, all ye of the captivity, whom I have sent from Jerusalem to Babylon:

α.29.21 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume Ahab wunnaumonuh Kolajah, kah papaume Zedechiah wunnaumonuh Maasejah, nag quoshae missohhogig pann8waonk ut n8wesuonganit, kuss[é]h, nag nupponôog ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchad-nezzar Babilone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wunnushoh ut anaquabeóg.
E.29.21 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, of Ahab the son of Kolaiah, and of Zedekiah the son of Maaseiah, which prophesy a lie unto you in my name; Behold, I will deliver them into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon; and he shall slay them before your eyes;

α.29.22 Kah nag papaume matanumwe uttuonk piṣh neemunnuma[u]óog wame Judae masin[á]itcheg, apitcheg Babilon, n8waog, Jehovah ogquehikqush Zedechiahut, kah Ahabut, neh Babilone ketass8t app8sipuh ut n8taut.
E.29.22 And of them shall be taken up a curse by all the captivity of Judah which are in Babylon, saying, The LORD make thee like Zedekiah and like Ahab, whom the king of Babylon roasted in the fire;

α.29.23 Newutche usseog nishkeneunkqussuonk ut Israel, kah mamussuog weetatteamunganóuh ummittamwuss8oh, kah n8waog pann8wae kutt8wongash ut n8wesuonganit, niṣh matta ann8nóogish nen n8wahteauunnash kah n8wauwaénuh, wussin Jehovah.
E.29.23 Because they have committed villany in Israel, and have committed adultery with their neighbours' wives, and have spoken lying words in my name, which I have not commanded them; even I know, and am a witness, saith the LORD.

α.29.24 Yeu wonk piṣh kuttinnon Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, n8wash,
E.29.24 Thus shalt thou also speak to Shemaiah the Nehelamite, saying,

α.29.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel n8wau, newutche negonshhuau lettersash ut k8wesuonganit en wame missinninnuut neg apitcheg Jerusalem, kah en Shephaniahut wunnaumonuh Maasejah sephausuwaen, en wame sephausuwaénuut, kussip,
E.29.25 Thus speaketh the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, saying, Because thou hast sent letters in thy name unto all the people that are at Jerusalem, and to Zephaniah the son of Maaseiah the priest, and to all the priests, saying,

α.29.26 Jehovah kenompe sephausuwaenuwahik Jehojada sephausuwaen, onk woh kenaau aninnohsuenuog ut wekit Lord, wutch niṣh$noh pasuk noh kâgkéadt, kah quoshodtumwaenuwáheont wuhhogkuh, onk woh kukkupshagkin, kah ut stoksut.
E.29.26 The LORD hath made thee priest in the stead of Jehoiada the priest, that ye should be officers in the house of the LORD, for every man that is mad, and maketh himself a prophet, that thou shouldest put him in prison, and in the stocks.

α.29.27 Newutche yeuyeu, tohwutch mat auskomóad Jeremiah, wut-Anathoth, noh quoshodtumwaenuwáheont wuhhogkuh en kuhhogkaóut?
E.29.27 Now therefore why hast thou not reproved Jeremiah of Anathoth, which maketh himself a prophet to you?

α.29.28 Newutche newaj negonshhuau en kuhhogkanónut ut Babilon, n8wau, yeu missinno8onk sepeyeu8, wekekunk & ne ayék, ohkehteagk tanohketeaongash, kah meech8k ne adtannegik.
E.29.28 For therefore he sent unto us in Babylon, saying, This captivity is long: build ye houses, and dwell in them; and plant gardens, and eat the fruit of them.

α.29.29 Kah Zephaniah sephausuaen yeu wutogketamun wussukwheg, ut wuhtauogkit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
E.29.29 And Zephaniah the priest read this letter in the ears of Jeremiah the prophet.

α.29.30 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah n8wau,
E.29.30 Then came the word of the LORD unto Jeremiah, saying,

α.29.31 Aunchem8kae negonshhuash wame missinóog n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah, papaume Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, newutche Shemajah kukquoshoe missohhamwa[n]shikkou, kah matta nutann8nuh, kah kuppabuhtanumwahikou pann8waonk;
E.29.31 Send to all them of the captivity, saying, Thus saith the LORD concerning Shemaiah the Nehelamite; Because that Shemaiah hath prophesied unto you, and I sent him not, and he caused you to trust in a lie:

α.29.32 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nussasametah Shemajah wut-Nehelamit, kah 8skanneumuneoh: matta piṣh 8wosketomp8moh ayeoh kenugke yeug missinninnúog, kah matta piṣh naum8 wanegik, ne piṣh aseaunshau nummissinninnúmog wussin Jehovah, newutche kuhk8tomwehteau cheketauónat Jehovah.
E.29.32 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will punish Shemaiah the Nehelamite, and his seed: he shall not have a man to dwell among this people; neither shall he behold the good that I will do for my people, saith the LORD; because he hath taught rebellion against the LORD.

α.30.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhônukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut, n8wau,
E.30.1 The word that came to Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.30.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, wame kutt8wongash nish ánunonish, wussukhumush ut b8kut.
E.30.2 Thus speaketh the LORD God of Israel, saying, Write thee all the words that I have spoken unto thee in a book.

α.30.3 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8, wussin Jehovah, wonk nuppaudto ummissinnoongan8 Israelle kah Judae nummissinninnumog, wussin Jehovah, kah wonk nukqushkeáheaog en ohkeit ne anumauogkup 8sh8uh, kah nag pish wutoht[à]uuneau.
E.30.3 For, lo, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will bring again the captivity of my people Israel and Judah, saith the LORD: and I will cause them to return to the land that I gave to their fathers, and they shall possess it.

α.30.4 Kah yeush kutt8ongash nish Jehovah an8wopash papaume Israelloh kah papaume Judahoh.
E.30.4 And these are the words that the LORD spake concerning Israel and concerning Judah.

α.30.5 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah nunn8támumun nunnukshae kah wabesue wuttauatonkqussuonk, kah matta wunohteae.
E.30.5 For thus saith the LORD; We have heard a voice of trembling, of fear, and not of peace.

α.30.6 Nat8tamwehte8k yeuyeu, kah naum8k sun wosketomp onkquommom8e neechau? tohwaj naum niṣh$noh wosketomp wunnutchegash ogque ut wusseganit mittamwoṣsis neechadt, kah wame muskesukquaṣh quinnuppem8aṣh en wompekuṣhonat.
E.30.6 Ask ye now, and see whether a man doth travail with child? wherefore do I see every man with his hands on his loins, as a woman in travail, and all faces are turned into paleness?

α.30.7 Woi, newutche ne kesukok miṣsi, newaj wanne tatuppein8g: ne ahquompi ne adt Jakob wuttamehpunadt, qut piṣh na wutch wadchanon.
E.30.7 Alas! for that day is great, so that none is like it: it is even the time of Jacob's trouble, but he shall be saved out of it.

α.30.8 Newutch piṣh n$nih ne kesukok, wuṣsin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nuppohqun weyokumoh wutch kuṣsittippukanit, kah nuppashkukkom kukkenepissuongash, kah pen8wohteaog matta piṣh wonk 8chiéináuh naṣhpe nahoh.
E.30.8 For it shall come to pass in that day, saith the LORD of hosts, that I will break his yoke from off thy neck, and will burst thy bonds, and strangers shall no more serve themselves of him:

α.30.9 Qut nag piṣh wuttinneumuhkauáog Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh, kah Davidoh ukketass8tamomoh neh piṣh tahshinnumauogeh.
E.30.9 But they shall serve the LORD their God, and David their king, whom I will raise up unto them.

α.30.10 Newutche wabesehkon woi nuttinninneum Jakob, wuṣsin Jehovah, asuh chepshuhteogk woi Israel: newutche kusseh, piṣh k8wadchanṣh wutch noadtit, kah k8skannemuneog wutch ummiṣinae ohkeyeout, kah Jakob piṣh qushku kah piṣh anwohsin, & pish chequnappu, kah matta piṣh howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
E.30.10 Therefore fear thou not, O my servant Jacob, saith the LORD; neither be dismayed, O Israel: for, lo, I will save thee from afar, and thy seed from the land of their captivity; and Jacob shall return, and shall be in rest, and be quiet, and none shall make him afraid.

α.30.11 Newutche k8weetomsh wussin Jehovah k8wadchanunat tôkonogque n8wohkukquoshitteauun wame wutohtimoneash uttoh an seahwhun: qut onk matta k8wohkukquosumun8: qut quttuhham8e kussásamatohwhush, kah matta mamusse mat kussasamatahwhun8 kenukkonun8.
E.30.11 For I am with thee, saith the LORD, to save thee: though I make a full end of all nations whither I have scattered thee, yet I will not make a full end of thee: but I will correct thee in measure, and will not leave thee altogether unpunished.

α.30.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, ken8chumweteahwhutteaonk matta woh neetskehteauouun, kah k8wosketeawhutteaonk unkqueneunkquot.
E.30.12 For thus saith the LORD, Thy bruise is incurable, and thy wound is grievous.

α.30.13 Matta howan kukkeket8konshik8, onk woh kutasseepsu: wanne kutahtoou ne neetskehuwom8uk.
E.30.13 There is none to plead thy cause, that thou mayest be bound up: thou hast no healing medicines.

α.30.14 Wame womonacheg k8wananumuk, matta nag kenatinneahik8og, newutché ken8chumwehtoush nashpe matwae n8chumwetahwhuttuonk, nashpe wussasamatuhh8waonk unkqueneunkqussit, wutch mataanukish kummatcheseongash, newutche kummatcheseongash nano monat[a]sh.
E.30.14 All thy lovers have forgotten thee; they seek thee not; for I have wounded thee with the wound of an enemy, with the chastisement of a cruel one, for the multitude of thine iniquity; because thy sins were increased.

α.30.15 Tohwutch wuttuhpôsean kutunkquanumoonk? kutunkquanumoonk matta woh neetskehteauouun, newutche mataanukish kummatcheseongash, newutche kummatcheseongash nano monatash waj yeu unnehen.
E.30.15 Why criest thou for thine affliction? thy sorrow is incurable for the multitude of thine iniquity: because thy sins were increased, I have done these things unto thee.

α.30.16 Newaj wame neg mahchipp8wonukqueaneg, nag pish mahchipwutuog, kah wame ayeuuhkonuhqueaneg nag pish missinno8og, nish$noh pasuk, kah nag magk8kinukqueaneg, pish mukk8kinittuog, & wame neg chechekqunukqueaneg, pish chechequnaog.
E.30.16 Therefore all they that devour thee shall be devoured; and all thine adversaries, every one of them, shall go into captivity; and they that spoil thee shall be a spoil, and all that prey upon thee will I give for a prey.

α.30.17 Newutche kenompenumoush neetskehettuonk, kah keneetskehteoush ken8chumwetahwhutteaongash, wussin Lord, newutche nag kutuss8wenukquog pagkenit: n8wahettit, yeuoh Zion, matta howan natinneawhonkeh.
E.30.17 For I will restore health unto thee, and I will heal thee of thy wounds, saith the LORD; because they called thee an Outcast, saying, This is Zion, whom no man seeketh after.

α.30.18 Yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, wonk nuppaudtoh Jakob ummissinnae komukquash, kah nummonaneteam wutáyeuonganooash, kah keitotan pish ayimun ut nehenwonche 8wadchumut; kah mishikkomuk pish sepohteau neaunak wuttinniyeuonk.
E.30.18 Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will bring again the captivity of Jacob's tents, and have mercy on his dwellingplaces; and the city shall be builded upon her own heap, and the palace shall remain after the manner thereof.

α.30.19 Kah nag wutch pish sohham8m8 tabuttantamoonk, kah 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg pôacheg, kah nag nummuttaanheoog, kah nag matta pish ogguhs88og; nag wonk nussohsumwaheoog, kah n[a]g matta pish ogguhs8og.
E.30.19 And out of them shall proceed thanksgiving and the voice of them that make merry: and I will multiply them, and they shall not be few; I will also glorify them, and they shall not be small.

α.30.20 wunneechan8oh wonk pish tatuppeyeu8oh n8adt, ummukkinneongan8 pish menehketeauun ut anaquabeh: kah nussasamatoh wame neg sanakutchohwhoncheg.
E.30.20 Their children also shall be as aforetime, and their congregation shall be established before me, and I will punish all that oppress them.

α.30.21 Kah ukkencheiyeum8uh pish nehenwoncheyeu8og kah wunnanawunnuaeneum8oh pish wutch sohhamog wutch wunnasha[u]m8o[ut]: nkah nuppas8tshah, kah noh pish nuppas8su[k]unk: newutche howan yeuoh quoshauom8uk wuttah nuppas8sukunkqunat wussin Jehovah.
E.30.21 And their nobles shall be of themselves, and their governor shall proceed from the midst of them; and I will cause him to draw near, and he shall approach unto me: for who is this that engaged his heart to approach unto me? saith the LORD.

α.30.22 Kah kenaau pish nummiṣsinninnuog, kah nen kum-Manitt8mw8.
E.30.22 And ye shall be my people, and I will be your God.

α.30.23 Kusseh uppemsquohhumoh Jehovah chekee sohham, sepohtae pemsquoh, onkquomom8e pish appu uppuhkukqut matcheetou
E.30.23 Behold, the whirlwind of the LORD goeth forth with fury, a continuing whirlwind: it shall fall with pain upon the head of the wicked.

α.30.24 Ummishe musquanitteaonk Jehovah matta pish qushkemun8 nô pajeh mahche usseit, kah nó pajeh mahche ussenat wuttahh8wae unnantam8ongash: ut maumachish késukodtut pish kenatwontamumw8.
E.30.24 The fierce anger of the LORD shall not return, until he hath done it, and until he have performed the intents of his heart: in the latter days ye shall consider it.

α.31.1 NEnan ahquompag wuṣsin Jehovah nen um-Manitt8m8oh wame wutteateashiyeuongan8 Israel, kah nag pish num[-]miṣsinninnumog.
E.31.1 At the same time, saith the LORD, will I be the God of all the families of Israel, and they shall be my people.

α.31.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, missinninnuog neg ashquttahwhoncheh togkodteg namehteoog kitteamonteanittuonk ut touohkomukqut, Israel, nonche anwohsinw[a]heog.
E.31.2 Thus saith the LORD, The people which were left of the sword found grace in the wilderness; even Israel, when I went to cause him to rest.

α.31.3 Jehovah n8adt nunnaehtunk, n8wau, nux, kenashpe womonsh machemohtag womonittuonk: newaj nashpe womonittuonk kuppas8tshahesh.
E.31.3 The LORD hath appeared of old unto me, saying, Yea, I have loved thee with an everlasting love: therefore with lovingkindness have I drawn thee.

α.31.4 Wonk, k8weekekonsh, kah pish k8weekekonit woi Israelle penomp, pish wonk kenashpe wunn8whos kuttabretsash, kah pish kussohhom ut uppumukkaongan8oont neg weekontogeg.
E.31.4 Again I will build thee, and thou shalt be built, O virgin of Israel: thou shalt again be adorned with thy tabrets, and shalt go forth in the dances of them that make merry.

α.31.5 Pish wonk kutohketeam weenomwussippogwosh ut Samaria wadchutu, ohkehteaenuog pish wutohteakonaoash, kah nish pish nutogque meechinaoash nanweguk.
E.31.5 Thou shalt yet plant vines upon the mountains of Samaria: the planters shall plant, and shall eat them as common things.

α.31.6 Newutche pish kesukodu8, askuhwheteaenuog ut 8wadchumut Ephraim pish mishont8waog, neepok, kah kuhkuhquetuh en Zion en Jehovah num-Mánitt8mut.
E.31.6 For there shall be a day, that the watchmen upon the mount Ephraim shall cry, Arise ye, and let us go up to Zion unto the LORD our God.

α.31.7 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, weekontamwe ket8hamwanshuk Jákob, kah mishont8agk ut kenugke kehche wutohtimoinneat n8tamwahuwagk, tabuttántam8k, kah n8wak, woi Jehovah wadchán kummissinninnumog, sekqshoncheg ut Israel.
E.31.7 For thus saith the LORD; Sing with gladness for Jacob, and shout among the chief of the nations: publish ye, praise ye, and say, O LORD, save thy people, the remnant of Israel.

α.31.8 Kusseh, nag n8s8woog nanumohkeit, kah nag nummukkinoog wutch wekqshik óhke, kah nag kenugke pogkenukeg kah quanukquesitcheg, kah wompequae mittamwossis, kah noh neechadt moeu, m8chequshaog pish na wuttin quinnuppenau.
E.31.8 Behold, I will bring them from the north country, and gather them from the coasts of the earth, and with them the blind and the lame, the woman with child and her that travaileth with child together: a great company shall return thither.

α.31.9 Nag pish maue peyaog, kah nashpe peantam8ongash nussagkompa[n]oog: nuppannupwushaheáog sepupagwut, en sampwe mayut uttoh matta pish togkuṣsittassunehettég: newutche nen 8sh8oh Israel kah Ephraim noh mohtammegheog.
E.31.9 They shall come with weeping, and with supplications will I lead them: I will cause them to walk by the rivers of waters in a straight way, wherein they shall not stumble: for I am a father to Israel, and Ephraim is my firstborn.

α.31.10 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah woi kenáau wutohtimoinneunk, kah wahteauwahuagk en n8adte m[u]nahhannehtu, kah n8wak, noh seahwhont Israelloh pish ummoúnuh, kah pish wutogque nanawéheuh nanaushepsuenuut ufflokumut.
E.31.10 Hear the word of the LORD, O ye nations, and declare it in the isles afar off, and say, He that scattered Israel will gather him, and keep him, as a shepherd doth his flock.

α.31.11 Newutche Jehovah man8hwhau Jakoboh, kah wuttáphumauónuh neh anúe menuhkesumukqutcheh.
E.31.11 For the LORD hath redeemed Jacob, and ransomed him from the hand of him that was stronger than he.

α.31.12 Newaj piṣh peyahettit kah ket8hamóog ut kodtuhkóag Zion, kah nag piṣh moe kussitchuwanúog ut 8nétuwonganit Jehovah, wutch wheatash, kah wutche wine, kah wutche pummee, kah wutch floke kah hearde wuskoshimwesit: kah ukketeáhogkon8oh piṣh tatuppeyeu8oh sokenippontamwe tanohketeaonganit, kah matta piṣh wonk unkquanumoog.
E.31.12 Therefore they shall come and sing in the height of Zion, and shall flow together to the goodness of the LORD, for wheat, and for wine, and for oil, and for the young of the flock and of the herd: and their soul shall be as a watered garden; and they shall not sorrow any more at all.

α.31.13 Neit penomp piṣh pumukáeu muskauantam, naneeswe kehchiog kah wuskenuog moeu: newutche nukquinnuppinnum ummauongan8 en weekontam8onganit, kah nuttapheóog, kah nummuskauantamwaheoog mahche onkquanumwéhettit.
E.31.13 Then shall the virgin rejoice in the dance, both young men and old together: for I will turn their mourning into joy, and will comfort them, and make them rejoice from their sorrow.

α.31.14 Kah nuttapehteau ukketeahogkôunoh seph[á]usuwaen nashpe wees, kah nummissinninnúmog piṣh tapheóog wanegik, wussin Jehovah.
E.31.14 And I will satiate the soul of the priests with fatness, and my people shall be satisfied with my goodness, saith the LORD.

α.31.15 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wuttauatonkqussuonk n8tonkquod ut Ramah, maumuttam8onk, kah weesogohp[ó]suonk, Rachel mauémont wunneechanoh sekeneam taphettinneat wutch wunneechanoh, newutche nag matta ayeu8og.
E.31.15 Thus saith the LORD; A voice was heard in Ramah, lamentation, and bitter weeping; Rahel weeping for her children refused to be comforted for her children, because they were not.

α.31.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, quehtittaush kummauongane wadtauatonqussuonk, kah kuskesukque missippegwash, newutche kutanakausuonk piṣh onkquodtantamun, wussin Jehovah, kah nag piṣh wonk 8mwog wutohtuóut matwaug.
E.31.16 Thus saith the LORD; Refrain thy voice from weeping, and thine eyes from tears: for thy work shall be rewarded, saith the LORD; and they shall come again from the land of the enemy.

α.31.17 Kah ne annoósuonganú8 ut k8wóhkukquosininat, wussin Jehovah, onk woh keneechanog wonk peyaog ut nehenwonche wutohkeit.
E.31.17 And there is hope in thine end, saith the LORD, that thy children shall come again to their own border.

α.31.18 Wunnamuhkut nunn8tamup Ephraim maumuttamwaheont wuhhogkuh, kussasamatahheh, kah nussasamatahwhutteap; onatuh ox asquam yokhôsegk: quinnuppineh, kah piṣh nukquinnuppinit, newutche ken Jehovah num-Manitt8m.
E.31.18 I have surely heard Ephraim bemoaning himself thus; Thou hast chastised me, and I was chastised, as a bullock unaccustomed to the yoke: turn thou me, and I shall be turned; for thou art the LORD my God.

α.31.19 Wunnamuhkut mahche quinnuppinitteap, nutaiuskoiantamup: kah mahche kuhk8tomonteaon nupponketahhamup neehquau: nutakodchip, nux nutchepshomp, newutche nunnayeutamup n8skenue kehkomitteaonk.
E.31.19 Surely after that I was turned, I repented; and after that I was instructed, I smote upon my thigh: I was ashamed, yea, even confounded, because I did bear the reproach of my youth.

α.31.20 Sun Ephraim womonog nunnaumon? sun noh nuttapeneaue mukkies? newutche nadteah ayeuuhkonittue ken8nog, nummenuhke ash pumme mehquanum; newaj nunnogkis na[b] wutt[à]mánumont, wunnamuhkut piṣh nummonanum, wussin Jehovah.
E.31.20 Is Ephraim my dear son? is he a pleasant child? for since I spake against him, I do earnestly remember him still: therefore my bowels are troubled for him; I will surely have mercy upon him, saith the LORD.

α.31.21 Wunohtoush, maye kuhkinneasuongash: mishe numwonkquodtush: ponsh kuttah nogque toumáogquehtu, may ne ayôop: qushkish wonk woi Israelle penomp, qushkish wonk en kukkeitotanahtu.
E.31.21 Set thee up waymarks, make thee high heaps: set thine heart toward the highway, even the way which thou wentest: turn again, O virgin of Israel, turn again to these thy cities.

α.31.22 Toh kuttitt8che papaumṣham, woi ken as8ep8sue wuttaunin? newutch Lord kesteauun wuske ne teag ut ohkeit: mittamwossis piṣh quinuppekauau wosketompoh.
E.31.22 How long wilt thou go about, O thou backsliding daughter? for the LORD hath created a new thing in the earth, A woman shall compass a man.

α.31.23 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, aṣhpumme yeu piṣh auwohteaog kutt8onk ut ohkit Judah, kah ut ukkeitotanahtu, wonk paudtauon ummissinnoongan8, wunánumukquṣh Jehovah, woi sampweusseae ayeuonk, kah wunneetupanatamwe wadchu.
E.31.23 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; As yet they shall use this speech in the land of Judah and in the cities thereof, when I shall bring again their captivity; The LORD bless thee, O habitation of justice, and mountain of holiness.

α.31.24 Kah ohketeaenuog piṣh ayeuog Judah, kah ut wame ukkeitotanehtu moeu; kah nag sohwhuttunkeg flocksaṣh.
E.31.24 And there shall dwell in Judah itself, and in all the cities thereof together, husbandmen, and they that go forth with flocks.

α.31.25 Newutche nuttapeh sauunumwe keteahogkou, kah numwaméchumeh niṣh$noh neuantamwe keteahogkou.
E.31.25 For I have satiated the weary soul, and I have replenished every sorrowful soul.

α.31.26 Yeu ânag, nutt8hkep, nunnatauwompip, kah nukouéonk wunnegen ut nuhhogkat.
E.31.26 Upon this I awaked, and beheld; and my sleep was sweet unto me.

α.31.27 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8 wussin Jehovah, nutohketeam wek Israel kah wek Judah nashpe wosketompae wuskannem, kah nashpe puppinaṣhimwe wuskannem.
E.31.27 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will sow the house of Israel and the house of Judah with the seed of man, and with the seed of beast.

α.31.28 Kah piṣh n$nih, neane nag askuhwhekonog, nukkôdtinónat, kah pohqunónat, kah nukkepuhkonat, kah pagwanonat, kah onkapunuhkonat, ne nuttinne askuhwhekonóneáu weekekonat, ohteuhkonat, wussin Lord.
E.31.28 And it shall come to pass, that like as I have watched over them, to pluck up, and to break down, and to throw down, and to destroy, and to afflict; so will I watch over them, to build, and to plant, saith the LORD.

α.31.29 Ut yeuṣh kesukodtaṣh matta piṣh wonk n8wa8og, wut8shinneunk meechwog seáne weenominneaṣh, kah mukkiog wusketompeteáog.
E.31.29 In those days they shall say no more, The fathers have eaten a sour grape, and the children's teeth are set on edge.

α.31.30 Qut niṣh$noh pasuk piṣh nupp8wontam nehenwonche ummatcheseonk, niṣh$noh pasuk noh meechik seáne wenominneaṣh, piṣh wuskeompeteau.
E.31.30 But every one shall die for his own iniquity: every man that eateth the sour grape, his teeth shall be set on edge.

α.31.31 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8aṣh wussin Jehovah, piṣh nutáyimau wuske wunn8waonk wek Israel, kah wek Judah.
E.31.31 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will make a new covenant with the house of Israel, and with the house of Judah:

α.31.32 Matta neaunak wunn8waonk ne ayimauogkup 8sh8uh, ne kesukok ânunog wunnutchegan8out, sohh8wunónat wutch ohkeit Egypt, ne n8n8waonk pohquenumhettit, tôkonogque nen nag wásukó8uh wussin Jehovah.
E.31.32 Not according to the covenant that I made with their fathers in the day that I took them by the hand to bring them out of the land of Egypt; which my covenant they brake, although I was an husband unto them, saith the LORD:

α.31.33 Qut ne wunn8waonk ne áyimauog wek Israel, mahche yeuṣh kesukodtaṣh, wussin Jehovah, nuppon nuttinnaumatuonk wuttinnomiyeum8óut, kah n8sukkuhhumun ut wuttahh8wout, kah neen um-Manitt8moh, kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog.
E.31.33 But this shall be the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel; After those days, saith the LORD, I will put my law in their inward parts, and write it in their hearts; and will be their God, and they shall be my people.

α.31.34 Kah matta piṣh wonk kuhk8tomauó8 niṣh$noh pasuk weetatteamung, kah niṣh$noh pasuk wematoh, n8wonat wahúk Jehovah: newutche nag piṣh wame n8wahikquóg, wutch p[e]ississit pajeh másukkenuk wussin Jehovah, newutche nutahquontamauóog ummatcheseongan8, kah matta wonk nummequontam8 ummatcheseongan8.
E.31.34 And they shall teach no more every man his neighbour, and every man his brother, saying, Know the LORD: for they shall all know me, from the least of them unto the greatest of them, saith the LORD: for I will forgive their iniquity, and I will remember their sin no more.

α.31.35 Yeu wussin Lord, noh maguk nepauzsoh wutch kesukque wequai, kah nanepauh[s]hadt, & anogqse kuhquttum8ongash wutch nuhkonáe wequai; noh chachapenuk keitoh, tukk8og mahshont8wahetticheh, Jehóvah ayeuuhteanit ussowesu.
E.31.35 Thus saith the LORD, which giveth the sun for a light by day, and the ordinances of the moon and of the stars for a light by night, which divideth the sea when the waves thereof roar; The LORD of hosts is his name:

α.31.36 Yeush kuhk8wwaongash amaem8uk wutch anaquabeh wussin Jehovah, neit 8skannemuneoh Israel piṣh wohkukquoshinin wutohtimo88ut anaquabeh micheme.
E.31.36 If those ordinances depart from before me, saith the LORD, then the seed of Israel also shall cease from being a nation before me for ever.

α.31.37 Yeu wussin Jehovah tohneit kesuk wohqut woh quttuhhumuk, kah quenohtag ohke mishkomuk ut agque, nen piṣh wonk nuppogketam wame 8skannem Israel, wutch wame ne matche ussehettit, wussin Jehovah.
E.31.37 Thus saith the LORD; If heaven above can be measured, and the foundations of the earth searched out beneath, I will also cast off all the seed of Israel for all that they have done, saith the LORD.

α.31.38 Kusseh kesukkodtash peyaum8ash wussin Jehovah, keitotan piṣh ayimauau Jehovah, wutch qunnikommuk Hananeel, wehque [hâssá]nue squontamut.
E.31.38 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that the city shall be built to the LORD from the tower of Hananeel unto the gate of the corner.

α.31.39 Kah quttuhhumoe pemuneat piṣh na en piuhsuke summagunumun, ut wadchuut Gareb, kah piṣh weenisheáu wehque Gath.
E.31.39 And the measuring line shall yet go forth over against it upon the hill Gareb, and shall compass about to Goath.

α.31.40 Kah mamusse 8nôuhkoiyeu nupp8e muhhogkunk, kah pukque, kah ohteuhkonash wehque sepuissit Kidron, wehque adt nahshik horsese wutchepwoiyeue squont, piṣh wunneetupanatamweyeu8 en Lordut, matta piṣh pohqunnum8un, asuh wonk kepuhteaun micheme.
E.31.40 And the whole valley of the dead bodies, and of the ashes, and all the fields unto the brook of Kidron, unto the corner of the horse gate toward the east, shall be holy unto the LORD; it shall not be plucked up, nor thrown down any more for ever.

α.32.1 KUtt8onk ne p[á]uh[ô]nukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, ut uppiukque kodtum8mut Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, ne nabo shwosuk wutteáshe kodtum8m Nebuchad-nezar.
E.32.1 The word that came to Jeremiah from the LORD in the tenth year of Zedekiah king of Judah, which was the eighteenth year of Nebuchadrezzar.

α.32.2 Newutche neit ukkenauwameonk Babilone ketass8t weenuhkom Jerusalem: kah Jeremih quoshodtumwaen kuppuhhôsu ut chippinnutongane kuppishagkinittuonganit, ne ut wekit Judae ketass8t.
E.32.2 For then the king of Babylon's army besieged Jerusalem: and Jeremiah the prophet was shut up in the court of the prison, which was in the king of Judah's house.

α.32.3 Newutche Zedechiah Judae ketass8t ukkuppuhwhoh, n8wau, tohwaj quoshodtuman, n8w[a]an, yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nummag ne keitotan ut wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh piṣh wussohkomun?
E.32.3 For Zedekiah king of Judah had shut him up, saying, Wherefore dost thou prophesy, and say, Thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the king of Babylon, and he shall take it;

α.32.4 Kah Zedechiah Judae ketass8t matta piṣh pohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8óut Caledansog, qut wunnamuhkut noh piṣh ponau wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah mutt8n8e piṣh keket8koadtuog, kah piṣh wuskesuk88ash moninneadtum8ash.
E.32.4 And Zedekiah king of Judah shall not escape out of the hand of the Chaldeans, but shall surely be delivered into the hand of the king of Babylon, and shall speak with him mouth to mouth, and his eyes shall behold his eyes;

α.32.5 Kah noh piṣh uss8wunau Zedechiahhoh en Babilon, kah na piṣh wutappin nô pajeh nunnátauahónat, wussin Jehovah, tôkonogque kutáyeuuhkonon Caldeansog, matta piṣh kussohkôsu.
E.32.5 And he shall lead Zedekiah to Babylon, and there shall he be until I visit him, saith the LORD: though ye fight with the Chaldeans, ye shall not prosper.

α.32.6 Kah Jeremiah n8wau, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah nuppeyaonuk n8wau,
E.32.6 And Jeremiah said, The word of the LORD came unto me, saying,

α.32.7 Kusseh, Hanameel wunnaumonuh Shallum, kussusses, noh piṣh kuppeyaónuk, n8wau, adtôash nutohteuk ne ut Anathoth: ne wutche kussampwe adtôon.
E.32.7 Behold, Hanameel the son of Shallum thine uncle shall come unto thee saying, Buy thee my field that is in Anathoth: for the right of redemption is thine to buy it.

α.32.8 Neit Hanameel n8susses wunnaumonuh nuppeyaonuk ut kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit, neaunak wuttinn8waonk Lord, kah nuttinuk, [á]dtôash nutohteuk, k8wehquetumoush, ne ut An[a]thoth, ne ut wutohkit Benjamin; newutche sampwe ohto[ó]nk ne kuttaihe, kah adtoâonk kuttaihe, adt[ô]ash ken. Neit n8wahteóh ne wuttinn8waonk Jehovah.
E.32.8 So Hanameel mine uncle's son came to me in the court of the prison according to the word of the LORD, and said unto me, Buy my field, I pray thee, that is in Anathoth, which is in the country of Benjamin: for the right of inheritance is thine, and the redemption is thine; buy it for thyself. Then I knew that this was the word of the LORD.

α.32.9 Kah nuttaphumauop wutohteuk Hanameel nussusses wunnaumonuh, ut Aanathoth, kah nukquthamau teaugwash, nabo nesausuk tahshinash silvere shekelsash.
E.32.9 And I bought the field of Hanameel my uncle's son, that was in Anathoth, and weighed him the money, even seventeen shekels of silver.

α.32.10 Kah n8sukkuhhumup wussukwhosuongash, kah nukkehkinneas[ú]hkonah, kah n8wauwaeneúteáp, kah nukquthum[á]uop teagwash ut quttompagh8teganit.
E.32.10 And I subscribed the evidence, and sealed it, and took witnesses, and weighed him the money in the balances.

α.32.11 Neit nunneemunomp adtô[á]e wussukwhosuongash, naneeswe ne kahkinne[a]sukósik neaunak naumatuonk, kah uṣhuwaonk, kah ne wôshwohtag.
E.32.11 So I took the evidence of the purchase, both that which was sealed according to the law and custom, and that which was open:

α.32.12 Kah adtô[á]e wussukwhosuongash nuttinnumauomp Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah, wunnaumonuh Maasejah, ut anaquabit Hanameel nussusses wunnaumonuh, kah ut anaquabhettit wauwacheg, neg wásukkuhhukeg adtoáe wussukwhosuonk, ut anaquabhettit wame Jewsog, neg apitcheg kuppishagkinittue chippinnutunkanit.
E.32.12 And I gave the evidence of the purchase unto Baruch the son of Neriah, the son of Maaseiah, in the sight of Hanameel mine uncle's son, and in the presence of the witnesses that subscribed the book of the purchase, before all the Jews that sat in the court of the prison.

α.32.13 Kah nummeechumuhkonomp Baruch, ut anaquabhettit, nussip,
E.32.13 And I charged Baruch before them, saying,

α.32.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, yeush neemunush wussukwhosuongash, adtoae wussukwhosuongash, naneeswe ne sealhausik, kah ne woshwohtag wussukwhosuonk, kah ponsh ohkee wishqut, onk woh nish m8cheke kesukquohtaash.
E.32.14 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Take these evidences, this evidence of the purchase, both which is sealed, and this evidence which is open; and put them in an earthen vessel, that they may continue many days.

α.32.15 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit umManitt8moh Israel, weetuomash, kah ohtéuhkonash, kah wenominneohtekonash piṣh wonk ohtauunash yeuut ohkeit.
E.32.15 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Houses and fields and vineyards shall be possessed again in this land.

α.32.16 Kah mag8on adtoáe wussukwhosuongash en Barachut wunnaumonuh Neriah, nuppeantamauomp Jehovah, nussip,
E.32.16 Now when I had delivered the evidence of the purchase unto Baruch the son of Neriah, I prayed unto the LORD, saying,

α.32.17 Woi Lord Manit, kusseh, kukkezteoh kesuk kah ohke nashpe kummishe menuhkesuonk kah kussummagunnum8e kuhpit, kah monteag kussiogkéhik8.
E.32.17 Ah Lord GOD! behold, thou hast made the heaven and the earth by thy great power and stretched out arm, and there is nothing too hard for thee:

α.32.18 Kenáhtin womoausuonk muttannonganogkussuog, kah ummatcheseongan8oash 8sh8oh, kutonkquatantam ut upp8chenauóun8óut nahohtôeu wunneechan8oh, Masugkenuk, kah M[a]nuhkesit Manit, Jehovah ayeuteaunit ne 8wesuonk.
E.32.18 Thou shewest lovingkindness unto thousands, and recompensest the iniquity of the fathers into the bosom of their children after them: the Great, the Mighty God, the LORD of hosts, is his name,

α.32.19 Noh missugken ut kogohqutteamwunneat, kah menuhkesu ut anakausuonganit, (newutche kuskesukquash woshwohtaash ut wame ummayeu[ou]t wunnaumonuh wosktompaog, aninnumauonat nishnoh pasuk neaunak ummayash, kah neanummeechumuk wutusseongash)
E.32.19 Great in counsel, and mighty in work: for thine eyes are open upon all the ways of the sons of men: to give every one according to his ways, and according to the fruit of his doings:

α.32.20 Noh ponuk kuhkinneasuongash kah monchanatam8ongash ut ohkit Egypt, pajeh yeu késukok, kah ut Israel kah kenugke onkatogig wosketompaog, kah k8wesuonganuhkau ku[h]hog, onatuh ne kesukok.
E.32.20 Which hast set signs and wonders in the land of Egypt, even unto this day, and in Israel, and among other men; and hast made thee a name, as at this day;

α.32.21 Kah kussohh8wun Israelle kummissinninnumog wutch Egypte ohkeit, nashpe kuhkinneasuongash, kah nonchanatam8ongash, kah nashpe menuhkiyeue menutcheg kah nashpe summagunnum8e muhpit, kah nashpe mishe wabesuonk.
E.32.21 And hast brought forth thy people Israel out of the land of Egypt with signs, and with wonders, and with a strong hand, and with a stretched out arm, and with great terror;

α.32.22 Kah neg kittinnumau8og yeu ohke, ne chadchekeimop 8sh8oh kittinnumauónat, ohke ne tomogok sogkodtunk, kah hony.
E.32.22 And hast given them this land, which thou didst swear to their fathers to give them, a land flowing with milk and honey;

α.32.23 Kah nag petutteaog, kah wutahtauunneau, qut nag matta n8swehtam8og k8wadtauatonkqussuonk, asuh pomushontam8og kuttinnaumatuonk, nag monteag usséog nean ann8nadt wutussenaout, newaj wame ne machuk nuhkunumauadt.
E.32.23 And they came in, and possessed it; but they obeyed not thy voice, neither walked in thy law; they have done nothing of all that thou commandedst them to do: therefore thou hast caused all this evil to come upon them:

α.32.24 Kusseh, wadchukontamwog, nag peyaog keihtotanat sohkomunnaoont, kah keitotan magun wunnutchegan8out Coldeansog, neg ayeuuhkontogig, wutche togkodteg, kah mahshagquodt kah unninneaonk, kah uttoh an8waon n$nih, kah kusseh kenaumun.
E.32.24 Behold the mounts, they are come unto the city to take it; and the city is given into the hand of the Chaldeans, that fight against it, because of the sword, and of the famine, and of the pestilence: and what thou hast spoken is come to pass; and, behold, thou seest it.

α.32.25 Kah kutussip, woi Lord Jehovah, adtoash ohteuk wutch teagwash, kah wauwaenuog neemun: newutche keitotan magun en wunnutchegan8out Caldeansog.
E.32.25 And thou hast said unto me, O Lord GOD, Buy thee the field for money, and take witnesses; for the city is given into the hand of the Chaldeans.

α.32.26 Neit peyaonuk Jeremiah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, n8wau,
E.32.26 Then came the word of the LORD unto Jeremiah, saying,

α.32.27 Kusseh nen Jehovah um-Manitt8moh wame weyaus: sun ne teag nussioggehik?
E.32.27 Behold, I am the LORD, the God of all flesh: is there any thing too hard for me?

α.32.28 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, yeu nummagun keitotan en wunnutchegan8wout Caldeansog, kah en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzár Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish wussohkomun.
E.32.28 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the Chaldeans, and into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, and he shall take it:

α.32.29 Kah Caldeansog neg ayeuuhkontogig yeu keitotan, nag pish peyaog, kah pish chikohsumwog ne keitotan, kah chikohsumwog weetuomash nish ut woskeche sephamauwahetteup weetemungquok Baal, kah sokanumauw[á]hetteup wuttattamwe sephausuongash onkatogeh manittoh, m8m8sqhikqunnaoont.
E.32.29 And the Chaldeans, that fight against this city, shall come and set fire on this city, and burn it with the houses, upon whose roofs they have offered incense unto Baal, and poured out drink offerings unto other gods, to provoke me to anger.

α.32.30 Newutche wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah webe matcheseog ut anaquabeh wutch 8kenuunneaoont: newutche wunnaumonuh Israel webe numm8m8sqhikquog, nashpe wunnutchegane anakausuongan8, wussin Lord.
E.32.30 For the children of Israel and the children of Judah have only done evil before me from their youth: for the children of Israel have only provoked me to anger with the work of their hands, saith the LORD.

α.32.31 Newutche yeu keitotan nummusquantamwahikqun, kah nuppehchhikqun, wutch ne kesukok kezteauhettit, pajeh yeu kesukok, onk woh nutontahtauun wutch anaquabeh.
E.32.31 For this city hath been to me as a provocation of mine anger and of my fury from the day that they built it even unto this day; that I should remove it from before my face,

α.32.32 Wutche wame ummatchitt8m8 wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah, ne asehettit numm8m8sqhikqunnaout, nag, ukkehtass8tamóm8uh, wussontimom8uh, wussephausueneum8uh, kah ukquoshodtumwaeneum8uh, kah Judae wosketompaog kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem.
E.32.32 Because of all the evil of the children of Israel and of the children of Judah, which they have done to provoke me to anger, they, their kings, their princes, their priests, and their prophets, and the men of Judah, and the inhabitants of Jerusalem.

α.32.33 Kah quinnuppinnumwog uppisquan8 en nuhhogkat, qut matta wuskesuk8, tôhkônogque nukkuhk8tomauóneau nompoáeu omohkéonish, kah kuhk8tomauog, qut o[n]ch matta n8tam8og attumunumunat kuhk8tomóadtuonk.
E.32.33 And they have turned unto me the back, and not the face: though I taught them, rising up early and teaching them, yet they have not hearkened to receive instruction.

α.32.34 Qut nag ponamwog wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8, ne ahhettammuk nashpe n8wesuonk, nishketeauunat.
E.32.34 But they set their abominations in the house, which is called by my name, to defile it.

α.32.35 Kah nag ayimauáog qunúhqui ayeuongaṣh Baaloh, niṣh ut wut8nouhkôiyeumut wunnaumonuh Hinnom: wunnaumonáuh kah wuttaunoh pannupwusháheaog n8taut en Molechut, ne matta a[n]ann8náog, asuh matta paómun8g nuttenantam8onganit, nag woh yeu wutussenáout unkquanumukquok, matcheseáheónat Judah.
E.32.35 And they built the high places of Baal, which are in the valley of the son of Hinnom, to cause their sons and their daughters to pass through the fire unto Molech; which I commanded them not, neither came it into my mind, that they should do this abomination, to cause Judah to sin.

α.32.36 Kah yeu$yeu yeu$waj n8wadt Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume yeu keitotan, uttoh adt n8wáog, ne piṣh magun en wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mohshagquodt kah nashpe enninneaonk.
E.32.36 And now therefore thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel, concerning this city, whereof ye say, It shall be delivered into the hand of the king of Babylon by the sword, and by the famine, and by the pestilence;

α.32.37 Kusseh, nag nummukkinóog wutch wame wutohtimoneat, uttoh ann8hkauog musquanumog kah chenauosánumog, kah mishe musquantamon, kah wonk nuppas8óog yeu ayeuonganit, kah n8niyeuhéoog:
E.32.37 Behold, I will gather them out of all countries, whither I have driven them in mine anger, and in my fury, and in great wrath; and I will bring them again unto this place, and I will cause them to dwell safely:

α.32.38 Kah nag piṣh nummissinninnúmog, kah nen um-Manitt8m8uh.
E.32.38 And they shall be my people, and I will be their God:

α.32.39 Kah nag nuttinnumauóog pasuk metah, kah pasuk may, onk woh nag nukqushhukquog micheme, wutche 8niyeuongan8, kah wunneechan8oh nahohtôeu.
E.32.39 And I will give them one heart, and one way, that they may fear me for ever, for the good of them, and of their children after them:

α.32.40 Kah nutayimauoog machemohtag wunn8waonk, onk woh matta nukqushkehtauóog, n8neunneheonáóont, qut nupponum wuttahh8wout n8wabesuwónitteaonk onk woh nag mat nunnukkonuk8og.
E.32.40 And I will make an everlasting covenant with them, that I will not turn away from them, to do them good; but I will put my fear in their hearts, that they shall not depart from me.

α.32.41 Nux, nummuskouantamounóog n8neunneheonaóont, kah nag piṣh wunnamuhkut nutohteuhkonunk ut ohkeit, nashpe mamusse nuttah, kah mamusse nukketeahogkou.
E.32.41 Yea, I will rejoice over them to do them good, and I will plant them in this land assuredly with my whole heart and with my whole soul.

α.32.42 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, neane nuhkunumauog yeug missinninnúog wame yeu mishe machuk, ne nuttinne paudtauóneau wame wanegik ne quoshómogkup.
E.32.42 For thus saith the LORD; Like as I have brought all this great evil upon this people, so will I bring upon them all the good that I have promised them.

α.32.43 Kah ohteuhkonash pish taphumunash yeu ohkeit, uttoh ad n8waog, tne touwushin, wanne wosketompaun8, asuh puppinashimun8, ne magun ut wunnutchegan8out Caldeansog.
E.32.43 And fields shall be bought in this land, whereof ye say, It is desolate without man or beast; it is given into the hand of the Chaldeans.

α.32.44 Wosketómpaog pish adtoaog ohteuhkonash wutche teagwash, kah wussukhumwog wauwaongash, kah kuhkinneasukóntam8ongash, kah pish wauwaenuhteaog ut ohkeit Benjamin, kah ut ayeuonganehtu quinnuppe Jerusalem, kah ut Judae keitotanehtu, kah ut wadchae keitotanehtu, kah ut 8nouhkoiyeue keitotanehtu, kah ut sowanie keitotanehtu, newutche nukqushkeah missinoog wussin Jehovah.
E.32.44 Men shall buy fields for money, and subscribe evidences, and seal them, and take witnesses in the land of Benjamin, and in the places about Jerusalem, and in the cities of Judah, and in the cities of the mountains, and in the cities of the valley, and in the cities of the south: for I will cause their captivity to return, saith the LORD.

α.33.1 NAno wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, nahohtoeu (ashpamu kuppuhhausit kuppishagkinittue chippinneutunkanit) n8wau,
E.33.1 Moreover the word of the LORD came unto Jeremiah the second time, while he was yet shut up in the court of the prison, saying,

α.33.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah noh kesteunk, Jehovah noh kahkenauwehteunk, ummenuhkehtinat, Jehovah ne 8wesuonk.
E.33.2 Thus saith the LORD the maker thereof, the LORD that formed it, to establish it; the LORD is his name;

α.33.3 Wehkomeh, kah kenamp8hamoush, kah kukkuhk8tomoush mogagish kah mamenuhkagish, nish mo wahteau8anish.
E.33.3 Call unto me, and I will answer thee, and shew thee great and mighty things, which thou knowest not.

α.33.4 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, papaume weetuomash yeu ut keitotanat, kah papaume week8oash Judae ketass8tamwog nish kepuhteamukish nashpe wadchuuhkontam8ongash, kah nashpe togkodteg.
E.33.4 For thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel, concerning the houses of this city, and concerning the houses of the kings of Judah, which are thrown down by the mounts, and by the sword;

α.33.5 Nag peyaog ayeuuhkononat Caldeansog, qut ne nashpe numwohtauóneau nupp8e muhhogkuh, neg nohshogeg nashpe nummusquanitteaonk, kah nashpe nutchenauausuonk, kah wutche wame yeuṣh matcheseongaṣh nupputtogguhhum nuskesuk wutch yeu keitotanat.
E.33.5 They come to fight with the Chaldeans, but it is to fill them with the dead bodies of men, whom I have slain in mine anger and in my fury, and for all whose wickedness I have hid my face from this city.

α.33.6 Kusseh, nuppaudtauwontamun pomantamóonk, kah neetskehuwaonk, kah nag nunneetskeheaog, kah n8wahteauwahéoog monat wunoht[é]aonk kah wanamuhkutéyeuuk.
E.33.6 Behold, I will bring it health and cure, and I will cure them, and will reveal unto them the abundance of peace and truth.

α.33.7 Kah ummissinoóonk Judah ah ummissinoóonk Israel nukqushkeaheoog, kah nutogque wekitteahéoog weskeu.
E.33.7 And I will cause the captivity of Judah and the captivity of Israel to return, and will build them, as at the first.

α.33.8 Kah nuppahkhéoog wutch wame ummatcheseongan8óut, uttiyeu nashpe matchenéhehetteup, kah nutahquontamauóog wame ummatcheseongan8óaṣh, nish nashpe matchenehetticheh kah pannesehtiehetticheh.
E.33.8 And I will cleanse them from all their iniquity, whereby they have sinned against me; and I will pardon all their iniquities, whereby they have sinned, and whereby they have transgressed against me.

α.33.9 Kah piṣh ut nuhhogkat wekonatmwe wesuonk, waeenomáonk kah quttiánittuonk ut wame anaquabhettit wutohtimoneunk ut ohkeit, neg n8togiṣh wame wanegik ne ánheog: kah nag piṣh wabesuog kah nunnuksháog wutche wame wanegik, kah wutche wame wunáyeuonk, ne ánteau.
E.33.9 And it shall be to me a name of joy, a praise and an honour before all the nations of the earth, which shall hear all the good that I do unto them: and they shall fear and tremble for all the goodness and for all the prosperity that I procure unto it.

α.33.10 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wonk piṣh n8tamun yeu$ut ayeuonganit (ne an8waog ne touwushin matta wosketompaun8, kah matta puppinashimun8, ut Judae keitotan[e]htu, kah Jerusalemme toumaogquehtu, nish touushikiṣh wanne wosketom[a]un8, wanne wutohkeit, wanne puppinashimun8.)
E.33.10 Thus saith the LORD; Again there shall be heard in this place, which ye say shall be desolate without man and without beast, even in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem, that are desolate, without man, and without inhabitant, and without beast,

α.33.11 Muskouanatamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah weekontamwe wadtauatonkqussuonk, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk weetauadteaénin, 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 nag piṣh an8wacheg, tabuttantamok Jehôvah ayeuuhteaunit, newutche Jehov[a]h wunneetou, newutche ummonanitteaonk michemohteau, kah neg piṣh paudtunkeg tabuttantamoe sephausuonk ut wekit Jehovah: newutche nukqushkeáh ohkee missinoonk, neane wesku wussin Jehovah.
E.33.11 The voice of joy, and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride, the voice of them that shall say, Praise the LORD of hosts: for the LORD is good; for his mercy endureth for ever: and of them that shall bring the sacrifice of praise into the house of the LORD. For I will cause to return the captivity of the land, as at the first, saith the LORD.

α.33.12 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wonk yeu$ut ayeuonganit, ne touushik matta wosketompaun8ut, kah mat puppinashimun8, kah ut wame niṣh keitotanehtu piṣh wutáyeuongan8 nanaushepsaenuog, sepsinn8waheog ut flocksum8uh.
E.33.12 Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Again in this place, which is desolate without man and without beast, and in all the cities thereof, shall be an habitation of shepherds causing their flocks to lie down.

α.33.13 Ut wadchu[é] keitotanahtu, ut 8nouhkoiyeue otanahtu, kah sowaniyeue otanahtu, kah ut wutohkit Benjamin, kah ut ayeuonganéhtu quinnuppe Jerusalem, kah ut Judae otanahtu flocksog piṣh wonk pámwushaog ut agwe wunnutcheganit noh agkemont, wussin Jehovah.
E.33.13 In the cities of the mountains, in the cities of the vale, and in the cities of the south, and in the land of Benjamin, and in the places about Jerusalem, and in the cities of Judah, shall the flocks pass again under the hands of him that telleth them, saith the LORD.

α.33.14 Kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyom8aṣh, wussin Jehovah, nutussen ne wanegik ne quoshoái ut wekit Israel, kah ut wekit Judah.
E.33.14 Behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will perform that good thing which I have promised unto the house of Israel and to the house of Judah.

α.33.15 Ut yeush kesukodtaṣh, kah na ahquompag, nunneetuwáht[ó]h ut wekit David sampweusseae Wuttuhk, kah noh piṣh usseu wussittumóonk kah sampweusseonk ut ohkeit.
E.33.15 In those days, and at that time, will I cause the Branch of righteousness to grow up unto David; and he shall execute judgment and righteousness in the land.

α.33.16 Yeush ut kesukodtash Judah pish wadchanau, kah Jerusalem pish wadchanae wutayin, kah yeu pish ussowetamun, Jehovah nussampweusseonganun.
E.33.16 In those days shall Judah be saved, and Jerusalem shall dwell safely: and this is the name wherewith she shall be called, The LORD our righteousness.

α.33.17 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, David matta pish quena[u]ahik8 wosketompuh quenapinutche Israelle weke appuonganit.
E.33.17 For thus saith the LORD; David shall never want a man to sit upon the throne of the house of Israel;

α.33.18 Kah sephausuenuog kah Levitsog matta pish quenauehikk8og wosketompuh ut anaquabeh, magunat chikohtae sephausuongash, kah nashqussumunat metsue sephausuongash kah nagwutteáe sephausinneat.
E.33.18 Neither shall the priests the Levites want a man before me to offer burnt offerings, and to kindle meat offerings, and to do sacrifice continually.

α.33.19 Kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah n8wau,
E.33.19 And the word of the LORD came unto Jeremiah, saying,

α.33.20 Yeu wussin Jehovah pohquenumóg nukkesukodte wunn8waonk, kah nunnukkonae wunn8waonk, onk woh mo kesukodtino, kah nuhkonunn8, ut utt8cheyeu8ut.
E.33.20 Thus saith the LORD; If ye can break my covenant of the day, and my covenant of the night, and that there should not be day and night in their season;

α.33.21 Neit wonk woh n8n8waonganun David nuttinneum pohqunnumun, matta 8naumoniyeinat nanawunnuonat ut wuttappuonganit: kah n8n8waonganun Levitsog kah sephausuenuog nunohtompeantogomog.
E.33.21 Then may also my covenant be broken with David my servant, that he should not have a son to reign upon his throne; and with the Levites the priests, my ministers.

α.33.22 Neane kesukque kenauwameonk woh mo wáogketamomuk, kah kehtahhunomuk matta woh waeu quttuhhum8un, ne nuttinne mishehteauun 8skannem David nuttinneum, káh Levitsog neg wowussumukqueaneg.
E.33.22 As the host of heaven cannot be numbered, neither the sand of the sea measured: so will I multiply the seed of David my servant, and the Levites that minister unto me.

α.33.23 Nano wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, n8wau,
E.33.23 Moreover the word of the LORD came to Jeremiah, saying,

α.33.24 Sun matta kenatwontam8 yeug missinninnuog toh an8wahettit, n8wahettit, neesit teashiyeu8onk neh Jehovah pepenog, uppogkenuh? yeu wuttinne jishanumoneau nummissinninnumog onk woh matta wonk wutohtimoeinn8 ut anaquabhettit.
E.33.24 Considerest thou not what this people have spoken, saying, The two families which the LORD hath chosen, he hath even cast them off? thus they have despised my people, that they should be no more a nation before them.

α.33.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah, tohneit kesukodae kah nukkonae n8n8waonk matta ohtan8g, kah mátta kuhquttum8on kesukque kah ohkee kuhquttum8ongash.
E.33.25 Thus saith the LORD; If my covenant be not with day and night, and if I have not appointed the ordinances of heaven and earth;

α.33.26 Neit nuppogketam 8skannem Jakob kah David nuttinneum, newaj matta noh wuttinnum8 8skannem, wunnanauwunnumunnaoont 8skannemuneoh Abraham Isaak, kah Jakob: newutche nukqushkeahto ummissinn8ongan8, kah nag nummonanumoog.
E.33.26 Then will I cast away the seed of Jacob and David my servant, so that I will not take any of his seed to be rulers over the seed of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob: for I will cause their captivity to return, and have mercy on them.

α.34.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauonukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut (Nebuchadnezzer Babilone ketass8t, kah wame ukkenauwameumoh kah wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit, ut wunnanauúnnum8onganit, & wame missinninnuog ayeuuhkontamwog Jerusalem, & ayeuuhkonittue wame keitotanash na ohtagish) n8wau.
E.34.1 The word which came unto Jeremiah from the LORD, when Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, and all his army, and all the kingdoms of the earth of his dominion, and all the people, fought against Jerusalem, and against all the cities thereof, saying,

α.34.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel, monchish ken8s Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, kah us, yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh; yeu nummagun keitotan en wunnutcheganit Babilone ketass8t, kah noh pish wutchikkossumun ut n8taut.
E.34.2 Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel; Go and speak to Zedekiah king of Judah, and tell him, Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the king of Babylon, and he shall burn it with fire:

α.34.3 Kah ken matta pish kuppogquohham8 wutch wunnutcheganit: qut pish wunnamuhkut kuttohqunit, kah kuskesukquash pish naum wuskesukquash Babilone ketass8t, kah noh mutt8n8e kukken8nuk, kah pish kuttom Babilon.
E.34.3 And thou shalt not escape out of his hand, but shalt surely be taken, and delivered into his hand; and thine eyes shall behold the eyes of the king of Babylon, and he shall speak with thee mouth to mouth, and thou shalt go to Babylon.

α.34.4 Qut onch n8tash wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, woi Zedechiah Judae ketass8t: yeu wussin Lord papaume ken, matta pish kenupp8h, nashpe togkodteg.
E.34.4 Yet hear the word of the LORD, O Zedekiah king of Judah; Thus saith the LORD of thee, Thou shalt not die by the sword:

α.34.5 Qut pish k8nohteae nup, kah nashpe wutchikkossum8ongan8oash k8sh8oog, negonne ketass8tamwog, neg negonnekunkqueaneg, ne pish kitt[t]nne chikkohsumunkquneau, kah nag pish kummauwemukquog n8wahettit woi Lord: newutche nukkutt8kontam kutt8onk wussin Jehovah.
E.34.5 But thou shalt die in peace: and with the burnings of thy fathers, the former kings which were before thee, so shall they burn odours for thee; and they will lament thee, saying, Ah lord! for I have pronounced the word, saith the LORD.

α.34.6 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, wuttinnonash wame yeush kutt8ongash Zedechiahoh Judae ketass8t ut Jerusalem.
E.34.6 Then Jeremiah the prophet spake all these words unto Zedekiah king of Judah in Jerusalem,

α.34.7 Ukkenauwameonk Babilone ketass8t ayeuuhkontamunit Jerusalem, kah wame Judae keitotanash nish sequttahhamukish, Lachish kah Azekah: newutche yeush pummenutausue keitotanash ashpumohtáash wutch Judae keitotanat.
E.34.7 When the king of Babylon's army fought against Jerusalem, and against all the cities of Judah that were left, against Lachish, and against Azekah: for these defenced cities remained of the cities of Judah.

α.34.8 Yeu kutt8onk ne pauhonukup Jeremiah wutch Jehovah$ut, mahche Zedechiah wunn8wahettit wame missinninnuh neg, apitcheg Jerusalem, nag wahteauwahuonat chippinnu8onk.
E.34.8 This is the word that came unto Jeremiah from the LORD, after that the king Zedekiah had made a covenant with all the people which were at Jerusalem, to proclaim liberty unto them;

α.34.9 Nish$noh wosketmp woh chippinnuwaheau wosketompae wuttinninneumoh Hebrewyeu8it kah nish$noh wosketomp mittamwussisse wuttinninneumoh Hebrewyeu8it, wanne howan 8chieinneat Jewsue wematoh.
E.34.9 That every man should let his manservant, and every man his maidservant, being an Hebrew or an Hebrewess, go free; that none should serve himself of them, to wit, of a Jew his brother.

α.34.10 Kah wame sontimoog, kah wame missinninnuog neg wán8wacheg n8tamwehettit, nish$noh wosketomp woh chippinnewah[é]au wosketompae wuttinninnumoh, kah nishnoh mittumwossisse wuttinninneumoh, matta woh wonk 8chienaoont, neit n8swehtámwog kah ummoncheaheuh.
E.34.10 Now when all the princes, and all the people, which had entered into the covenant, heard that every one should let his manservant, and every one his maidservant, go free, that none should serve themselves of them any more, then they obeyed, and let them go.

α.34.11 Qut ompetak nag quinnuppeog kah ukqushkeaheóuh wuttinneum8ut kah ummaidum8uh neh chapinninnuwaheahetteupoh, kah wutagwapehheouh 8tinninneumunaóut.
E.34.11 But afterward they turned, and caused the servants and the handmaids, whom they had let go free, to return, and brought them into subjection for servants and for handmaids.

α.34.12 Newaj wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah n8wau,
E.34.12 Therefore the word of the LORD came to Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.34.13 Yeu wussin Lord um$Manitt8moh Israel, n8n8waheomp k8sh8óog ne kesukok sohh8wunog wutch Egypte ohkeit, wutch missinnae-kommukqut nussip,
E.34.13 Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel; I made a covenant with your fathers in the day that I brought them forth out of the land of Egypt, out of the house of bondmen, saying,

α.34.14 Wehqhshik nesausuk tahshe kodtumm8, nishnoh wosketomp moncheáheonch wemátoh Hebrewoh, noh kodtauwompámunuukkus: kah noh wuttinneumuhkonukquean nequtta tahshe kodtumwaeu, neit piṣh kutchippinninnuáh wutch kuhhogkat, qut k8sh8óog matta nukkeihketónk8, asuh nutáhchuwussittuonk8og.
E.34.14 At the end of seven years let ye go every man his brother an Hebrew, which hath been sold unto thee; and when he hath served thee six years, thou shalt let him go free from thee: but your fathers hearkened not unto me, neither inclined their ear.

α.34.15 Kuhquinnuppinitteamw8 yeuyeu, kah kutussemwop ne sampwag ut anaquabeh, wahteauwáhuwáóg chippinnú8onk nishnoh pasuk en weetatteamonganit, & k8n8wamwop ut anaquabeh, ut wetuomut ne áhettamuk nashpe n8wesuonk.
E.34.15 And ye were now turned, and had done right in my sight, in proclaiming liberty every man to his neighbour; and ye had made a covenant before me in the house which is called by my name:

α.34.16 Qut kukquinnuppemw8, kah kenishketeomw8 n8wesuonk, kah kukqushkeáheomw8 nishnoh wosketomp wuttinneumoh, kah nishnoh wosketomp ummaidumoh, neg chappinninnuwáheógkuppanneg, uttoh án kodtantamwéhettit, kah kutagwapéhe[ó]óog, k8tinninneumunneaóut kah k8maidumunneaóont.
E.34.16 But ye turned and polluted my name, and caused every man his servant, and every man his handmaid, whom he had set at liberty at their pleasure, to return, and brought them into subjection, to be unto you for servants and for handmaids.

α.34.17 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord, matta nukkehketi8mw8, wahteauwáhuónat chippinnú8onk, niṣhnoh pasuk weematoh, nishnoh pasuk wetatteamungoh: kusseh n8wahteauwáhuwam kutchippinninnu8ongan8 wussin Jehovah, en togkodteganit, en enneaonganit, kah en mahshogquodtut: kah kutontashinnumw8 en wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit.
E.34.17 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Ye have not hearkened unto me, in proclaiming liberty, every one to his brother, and every man to his neighbour: behold, I proclaim a liberty for you, saith the LORD, to the sword, to the pestilence, and to the famine; and I will make you to be removed into all the kingdoms of the earth.

α.34.18 Kah wosketompaog neg panneusséhtunkeg n8n8waonk neg matta asegek wunn8wae kutt8wongash niṣh áyimukish ut anaquabeh, póhshiswáhettit calfoh, kah pannupwusháhettit ut nôeu chippaiyeuut.
E.34.18 And I will give the men that have transgressed my covenant, which have not performed the words of the covenant which they had made before me, when they cut the calf in twain, and passed between the parts thereof,

α.34.19 Judae seontimoog, kah Jerusalemme sontimoog eunuchsog, kah sephausuenuog, kah wame missinninnúog ohkeit, neg pannupwushacheg nashaue calfe chippaiyeuut.
E.34.19 The princes of Judah, and the princes of Jerusalem, the eunuchs, and the priests, and all the people of the land, which passed between the parts of the calf;

α.34.20 Neg nummagununk en wunnutchegan8out ummatwomoh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kodnushoncheg, kah nupp8e wuhhogkauh ne piṣh ummeetsuongan8 kesukque puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimw[o]g.
E.34.20 I will even give them into the hand of their enemies, and into the hand of them that seek their life: and their dead bodies shall be for meat unto the fowls of the heaven, and to the beasts of the earth.

α.34.21 Kah Zedechiah Judae ketass8t kah wussontimomoh, neg nummagununk ut wunnutchegan8out ummatwom8uh, kah ut wunnutchegan8óut neg kod nushoncheg, kah ut wunnutchegan8out ukkenauwameongan8 Babilone ketass8t, neg kuhkuhquecheg wutch kuhhogkaóut.
E.34.21 And Zedekiah king of Judah and his princes will I give into the hand of their enemies, and into the hand of them that seek their life, and into the hand of the king of Babylon's army, which are gone up from you.

α.34.22 Kusseh, nag nutann8nóog, wussin Lord, kah nukqushkeaheóog yeu in otanat, kah nag piṣh wutayeuuhkontamuneau, kah piṣh wussohkomuneau, kah piṣh chikkossumuneau ut n8taut: kah Judae keitotanash nuttauwushitteauunash, matta wutohkeinneat.
E.34.22 Behold, I will command, saith the LORD, and cause them to return to this city; and they shall fight against it, and take it, and burn it with fire: and I will make the cities of Judah a desolation without an inhabitant.

α.35.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovah, ut ukkesukodtumut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t n8wau,
E.35.1 The word which came unto Jeremiah from the LORD in the days of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, saying,

α.35.2 Aush wekuout Rechabitsog, kah nag ken8s, kah nag petukos wekit Jehovah, ut pasuk chamberut, kah aninnumau wine wuttatumunat.
E.35.2 Go unto the house of the Rechabites, and speak unto them, and bring them into the house of the LORD, into one of the chambers, and give them wine to drink.

α.35.3 Neit nunnemunomp Jaazaniah wunnaumonuh Jeremiah, wunnaumonuh Habaziniah, kah weematoh, kah wame wunnaumonuh, kah mamusse wek8 Rechabitsog.
E.35.3 Then I took Jaazaniah the son of Jeremiah, the son of Habaziniah, and his brethren, and all his sons, and the whole house of the Rechabites;

α.35.4 Kah nuppetukonóog wekit Jehovah, ut wutchamberum8out wunnaumonuh Hanan wunnaumonuh Igdaliah Manittowomp, ne ohtag kishke wutchamberum8out sontimóog, ne waabe wutchamberumut Maasejah wunnaumonuh Shallum nanasquontamaenin,
E.35.4 And I brought them into the house of the LORD, into the chamber of the sons of Hanan, the son of Igdaliah, a man of God, which was by the chamber of the princes, which was above the chamber of Maaseiah the son of Shallum, the keeper of the door:

α.35.5 Kah nupponum anaquabhettit wunnaumonuh Rechabitse wetu, wishquahtu nanumwohteau wine, kah wuttattamwaitchuaṣh, kah nag nuttinnópanneg wuttattam8k wine.
E.35.5 And I set before the sons of the house of the Rechabites pots full of wine, and cups, and I said unto them, Drink ye wine.

α.35.6 Kah nag n8waog, matta n8tattam8mun wine: newutche Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab, nutann8nukqunnónup, n8wop, wuttattam8hteok wine kenaau asuh kenaumonáog micheme.
E.35.6 But they said, We will drink no wine: for Jonadab the son of Rechab our father commanded us, saying, Ye shall drink no wine, neither ye, nor your sons for ever:

α.35.7 Weekitteáhteogk, kah ohketeáhteogk, kah weenominneohketeahteogk, kah ahque ohtau8k: qut [n]isohke|pomantamog ayék weetuomut, onk woh kussepepomantamumw8 ut ohkeit ne adt penuwohteayeóg.
E.35.7 Neither shall ye build house, nor sow seed, nor plant vineyard, nor have any: but all your days ye shall dwell in tents; that ye may live many days in the land where ye be strangers.

α.35.8 Yeu nuttinne n8swetamunan 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab n8shun, wame neáne meechumuhkonukquéog, matta wuttattam8unat wine nisohke pomantamog, nenawun, nummittamwussinnonog, nunnaumonánonog, kah nuttaununónog.
E.35.8 Thus have we obeyed the voice of Jonadab the son of Rechab our father in all that he hath charged us, to drink no wine all our days, we, our wives, our sons, nor our daughters;

α.35.9 Matta n8wékekongk8unnanónut, ayinneat, kah matta n8weenominneohtekoneumun, matta n8tohteuhkoneumun, asuh n8skennémunneumun.
E.35.9 Nor to build houses for us to dwell in: neither have we vineyard, nor field, nor seed:

α.35.10 Qut nut[á]yimun wetuómut, kah nunn8swehtamumun, kah n8wame ussénan ne Jonadab n8shun ánann8nukqueog.
E.35.10 But we have dwelt in tents, and have obeyed, and done according to all that Jonadab our father commanded us.

α.35.11 Qut n$niyeup Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t kó[h]ku[h]quit yeu in ohkeit, nussi[m]unnonup, kah, ontuh Jerusalem, newutche n8wabesuóntamumun Syrianse kenauwameonk, kah Babylone kenauwameonk, ne$waj ayéog Jerusalem.
E.35.11 But it came to pass, when Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon came up into the land, that we said, Come, and let us go to Jerusalem for fear of the army of the Chaldeans, and for fear of the army of the Syrians: so we dwell at Jerusalem.

α.35.12 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah, kah n8wau,
E.35.12 Then came the word of the LORD unto Jeremiah, saying,

α.35.13 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, monchish, us Judae wosketompaog, kah wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, sunnummatta kuttattumunumomw8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk n8tamunat nukkutt8wongaṣh, wussin Jehovah.
E.35.13 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Go and tell the men of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem, Will ye not receive instruction to hearken to my words? saith the LORD.

α.35.14 Wuttinn8waongash Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab, neanann8nomp wunnaumonuh matta wuttattam8unat wine, wutusseneau, newutche pajeh yeu kesukok matta wuttattam8og, qut n8wehtamwog 8sh8oh wutann8team8onk: qut kukken8numw8, nompoáeu omohkeon kah kodt8hkôon, qut matta kukkehketiyeúmw8.
E.35.14 The words of Jonadab the son of Rechab, that he commanded his sons not to drink wine, are performed; for unto this day they drink none, but obey their father's commandment: notwithstanding I have spoken unto you, rising early and speaking; but ye hearkened not unto me.

α.35.15 Nutann8nop wonk en kuhhogkaóut wame nuttinninnumwog quoshodtumwaenuog, nompoáe omohkeon, kah nag ann8nog, nussip, yeuyeu qushkek nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut kah oncheteau8k kutusseongan8oaṣh, kah asuhkauúhteok onkatogig manitt8og nag wuttinneumuhkauónat, kah piṣh kutayimw8 ohkeit, ne anumauunóg, kah k8sh8wóog, qut matta kutahchuwussittam8mw8,asuh kukkeihketai8mw8.
E.35.15 I have sent also unto you all my servants the prophets, rising up early and sending them, saying, Return ye now every man from his evil way, and amend your doings, and go not after other gods to serve them, and ye shall dwell in the land which I have given to you and to your fathers: but ye have not inclined your ear, nor hearkened unto me.

α.35.16 Newutche wunnaumonuh Jonadab, wunnaumonuh Rechab, usseog wutann8team8onk 8sh8uh, ne ánann8nomp nahoh, qut yeug missinninnuog matta nukkehketunk8og.
E.35.16 Because the sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab have performed the commandment of their father, which he commanded them; but this people hath not hearkened unto me:

α.35.17 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumauôog Judah kah wame wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, wame machuk ne ayeuuhkone áne ken8nog: newutche nag nukken8nóog, qut nag matta n8tam8og, kah nag n8wehkomóog, qut namp8hamunk8og.
E.35.17 Therefore thus saith the LORD God of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will bring upon Judah and upon all the inhabitants of Jerusalem all the evil that I have pronounced against them: because I have spoken unto them, but they have not heard; and I have called unto them, but they have not answered.

α.35.18 Kah Jeremiah unnop wek8 Rechabitsog, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, newutche ken8swehtamumw8 wutann8team8onk Jonadab k8shw8, kah kenanawehteomw8 wame ukkuhk8waongaṣh, kah kutussemw8 wame neánan8nukqueóg.
E.35.18 And Jeremiah said unto the house of the Rechabites, Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Because ye have obeyed the commandment of Jonadab your father, and kept all his precepts, and done according unto all that he hath commanded you:

α.35.19 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, Jonadab wunnaumonuh Rechab matta piṣh quenanéhik8 wosketompuh nepauinneat anaquabeh micheme.
E.35.19 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Jonadab the son of Rechab shall not want a man to stand before me for ever.

α.36.1 KAh nniyeup ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, yeu kutt8onk uppeyaónukqun Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, n8wau,
E.36.1 And it came to pass in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, that this word came unto Jeremiah from the LORD, saying,

α.36.2 Nemunumush tuttuppequia[n]ôsuwu b8k, kah ne ut wawawussukwhuṣh, kutt8wongash nish ayeuuhkonittue ânogish Israel, kah Judah, kah wame wutohtimoneaṣh, wutch ne kesukok kôn8nunon, wutch ukkesukkodtumut Josiah pajeh yeu kesukok.
E.36.2 Take thee a roll of a book, and write therein all the words that I have spoken unto thee against Israel, and against Judah, and against all the nations, from the day I spake unto thee, from the days of Josiah, even unto this day.

α.36.3 Pagwodche wek Judah woh n8tam wame machuk ne kod néhheog, onk woh nag qushkeog nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut onk woh nutahquontam ummatcheseongan8, kah uppanneseongan8.
E.36.3 It may be that the house of Judah will hear all the evil which I purpose to do unto them; that they may return every man from his evil way; that I may forgive their iniquity and their sin.

α.36.4 Neit Jeremiah wehkomau Baruchoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, kah Baruch wussuhkhum wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, wame ukkutt8wongaṣh Jehovah, nish ánompaṣh, ut tuttuppequanausue b8kut.
E.36.4 Then Jeremiah called Baruch the son of Neriah: and Baruch wrote from the mouth of Jeremiah all the words of the LORD, which he had spoken unto him, upon a roll of a book.

α.36.5 Kah Jeremiah ann8nau Baruchoh, n8wau, nukkuphaus, matta woh nutóh weekit Jehovah.
E.36.5 And Jeremiah commanded Baruch, saying, I am shut up; I cannot go into the house of the LORD:

α.36.6 Newutche monchish, kah ogketash ut tuttuppequanausuut ne wásuhkuhhuman wutch nutt8nut, ukkutt8wongash Jehovah ut wu[h]tauogk8out missinninnuog, ut wekit Jehovah, ut matta meetsue kesukkodtut: kah niṣh piṣh wonk kutogketmunash, ut wame wuhtauogk8óut Judah neg sohhogeg wutch wutotanaóut.
E.36.6 Therefore go thou, and read in the roll, which thou hast written from my mouth, the words of the LORD in the ears of the people in the LORD's house upon the fasting day: and also thou shalt read them in the ears of all Judah that come out of their cities.

α.36.7 Pâguodcheh piṣh ponamwog uppeantam8ongan8 ut anaquabit Jehovah, kah piṣh qushkeog nishnoh pasuk wutch ummatche mayut, newutche missi ummusquanittam8onk kah wutchenauausuonk ne Jehov[a]h kôn8tog ayeuuhkonittue yeuh missinninnúh.
E.36.7 It may be they will present their supplication before the LORD, and will return every one from his evil way: for great is the anger and the fury that the LORD hath pronounced against this people.

α.36.8 Kah Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah wutussen neane wame ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ánann8nont, ogketamup ut b8kut wuttinn8waongash Jehovah, ut Jehovah wekit.
E.36.8 And Baruch the son of Neriah did according to all that Jeremiah the prophet commanded him, reading in the book the words of the LORD in the LORD's house.

α.36.9 Kah nniyeup napanna wutteashe kodtum8mut Jehoiakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, ut pasuk8gun adtas8it nepauz, nag wahteauwáhuwaog mat meetsuonk ut anaquabit Jehovah wutch wame missinninnúog ut Jerusalem, kah wutch wame missinninnúog neg wagig Judae keitotanahtu en Jerusalem.
E.36.9 And it came to pass in the fifth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, in the ninth month, that they proclaimed a fast before the LORD to all the people in Jerusalem, and to all the people that came from the cities of Judah unto Jerusalem.

α.36.10 Neit Baruch ogketamup b8k, ukkutt8wongash Jeremiah ut wekit Jehovah, ut wutchambarumut Gemariah wunnaumonuh Shaphan noh scribe, ut qunnunkquohtag chippinnutunkanit, ahhut petutteamuk wuske squontamut wekit Jehvoah, ut wuhtauogk8óut wame missinninnúog.
E.36.10 Then read Baruch in the book the words of Jeremiah in the house of the LORD, in the chamber of Gemariah the son of Shaphan the scribe, in the higher court, at the entry of the new gate of the LORD's house, in the ears of all the people.

α.36.11 Michajah wunnaumonuh Gemariah, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, n8tog wutch b8kut [vv]ame [vv]uttinn8[vv]aongash Jehovah.
E.36.11 When Michaiah the son of Gemariah, the son of Shaphan, had heard out of the book all the words of the LORD,

α.36.12 Neit w8msu en ketass8t weekit, ut wut-chamberumut Scribe, kah kusseh wame sontimóog na wutappinneau, Elishama noh Scribe, kah Del[a]jah wunnaumonuh Shemajah, kah Elnathan wunnaumonuh Achbor, kah Gemariah wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Zedekiah wunnaumonuh Hananiah, kah wame sontimóog.
E.36.12 Then he went down into the king's house, into the scribe's chamber: and, lo, all the princes sat there, even Elishama the scribe, and Delaiah the son of Shemaiah, and Elnathan the son of Achbor, and Gemariah the son of Shaphan, and Zedekiah the son of Hananiah, and all the princes.

α.36.13 Neit Michajah na 8wahteauwâhuun wame kutt8wongaṣh nish n8togish: Baruch ágkeetog b8k ut wuhtauogk8óut missinninnúog.
E.36.13 Then Michaiah declared unto them all the words that he had heard, when Baruch read the book in the ears of the people.

α.36.14 Newaj wame sontimóog negont8waog Jehudi wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, wunnaumonuh Cushi en Baruch$ut n8waog, nemunuṣh ut kenutcheg[a]nit tuttuppéquianaúsik ne agketaman ut wuhtauogk8[ó]ut missinninnuog, kah peyauṣh; neit Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah nemunum wuttuppequianaúsik ut wunnutcheganit, kah nah uppeyaonuh.
E.36.14 Therefore all the princes sent Jehudi the son of Nethaniah, the son of Shelemiah, the son of Cushi, unto Baruch, saying, Take in thine hand the roll wherein thou hast read in the ears of the people, and come. So Baruch the son of Neriah took the roll in his hand, and came unto them.

α.36.15 Kah nah wuttinóuh nummatappish, kah ogketaṣh ut nehtauogkinnónut.
E.36.15 And they said unto him, Sit down now, and read it in our ears. So Baruch read it in their ears.

α.36.16 Kah n$nih n8tamwehettit wame kutt8wongaṣh wabesuog nishnoh pasuk, kah nag unnaog Baruchoh, wunnamuhkut nuttinnonnánonaṣh ketass8t wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh.
E.36.16 Now it came to pass, when they had heard all the words, they were afraid both one and other, and said unto Baruch, We will surely tell the king of all these words.

α.36.17 Kah nag nat8tomauáog Baruchoh, n8waog, ussunan yeuyeu, uttoh kuttin wussukhumunas wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh ut wutt8nut?
E.36.17 And they asked Baruch, saying, Tell us now, How didst thou write all these words at his mouth?

α.36.18 Neit Baruch wunnamp8hamauoh, yeush wame kutt8wongaṣh nuttugqunaṣh nashpe wutt8n, kah niṣh n8sukkuhhumunaṣh nashpe ink ut b8kut.
E.36.18 Then Baruch answered them, He pronounced all these words unto me with his mouth, and I wrote them with ink in the book.

α.36.19 Neit sontimóog unnáog Baruchoh, puttogquesh, ken kah Jeremiah, kah howan wahteau8hkitch ut$toh apeóg.
E.36.19 Then said the princes unto Baruch, Go, hide thee, thou and Jeremiah; and let no man know where ye be.

α.36.20 Kah petutteaunaog ketass8toh, ut mishe-komukqut, qut ponamwog tuttuppequayânôsik ut wut[-]chamberumut Elishama noh Scribe, kah wussinnaoaṣh wame kutt8wongaṣh ut wuhtauogkut ketass8t.
E.36.20 And they went in to the king into the court, but they laid up the roll in the chamber of Elishama the scribe, and told all the words in the ears of the king.

α.36.21 Neit ketass8t ann8nau Jehudi neemskomunat tuttuppequianaúsik; kah wunnemunnumun wutch wut-chamberumut Elishama noh Scribe, kah Jehudi wutogketamun ut wehtauogut ketass8t, kah wame wehtauogk8óut sontimóog neg kéhchekompauwéhtauoncheg ketass8toh.
E.36.21 So the king sent Jehudi to fetch the roll: and he took it out of Elishama the scribe's chamber. And Jehudi read it in the ears of the king, and in the ears of all the princes which stood beside the king.

α.36.22 Kah ketass8t appu popone-komukqut, ut pasuk8gun adtahs8it nepauz, kah na n8tau ut ahohtag n8tau chikohteau, ut anaquabit.
E.36.22 Now the king sat in the winterhouse in the ninth month: and there was a fire on the hearth burning before him.

α.36.23 Kah n$nih Jehudi agketog shuoh asuh yauoh wunnepagwoh, w[u]ttummussumun nashpe méqunéhquog, kah wuttinnúhkon n8taut, ne ut ahohtag n8teau, nô pajeh mamusse tuttuppéquianuk mahchikuttaut, ut n8taut ne ahhohtag n8teau.
E.36.23 And it came to pass, that when Jehudi had read three or four leaves, he cut it with the penknife, and cast it into the fire that was on the hearth, until all the roll was consumed in the fire that was on the hearth.

α.36.24 Qut matta wabesuog asuh nehnekikkom8og wutohtk8un8aṣh, matta ketass8t asuh howae wuttinneumoh n8taminnit wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh.
E.36.24 Yet they were not afraid, nor rent their garments, neither the king, nor any of his servants that heard all these words.
