α.36.25 Qut onch Elnathan, kah Delajah, kah Gemariah wehquetumauópanneg ketass8toh matta wutchikkossum8unat tuttuppequiánunk, qut nah mat wunn8tauoh.
E.36.25 Nevertheless Elnathan and Delaiah and Gemariah had made intercession to the king that he would not burn the roll: but he would not hear them.

α.36.26 Qut ketass8t ann8team8 Jerahmeel wunnaumonuh Hammelech, kah Serajah wunnaumonuh Azriel, kah Shelemiah wunnaumonuh Abdiel, tohqunnónat Baruch noh Scribe, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen: qut Jehovah wutadtahshuh.
E.36.26 But the king commanded Jerahmeel the son of Hammelech, and Seraiah the son of Azriel, and Shelemiah the son of Abdeel, to take Baruch the scribe and Jeremiah the prophet: but the LORD hid them.

α.36.27 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jermiah, (mahche ketass8t chikkohsuk tuttuppéquianaúsik kah kutt8wongaṣh nish Baruch wasukk8hukupaṣh ut wutt8nut Jeremiah) n8wau,
E.36.27 Then the word of the LORD came to Jeremiah, after that the king had burned the roll, and the words which Baruch wrote at the mouth of Jeremiah, saying,

α.36.28 Nemunush wonk onkatuk tuttuppéquianausik, kah tanúhsukkuhwhush wame negonne kutt8wongaṣh nish ohtagkupaṣh negonne tuttuppéquianausik, ne Jehojakim Judae ketass8t châgkossik.
E.36.28 Take thee again another roll, and write in it all the former words that were in the first roll, which Jehoiakim the king of Judah hath burned.

α.36.29 Kah piṣh kuttin Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, yeu wussin Jehovah yeu kutchikkossumunáh tuttuppèquianaúsik kussip, tohwhutch na$ut wussukhuman, Babylone ketass8t pish wunnamuhkut peyau, kah piṣh yeu pagwadtauun ohke, kah piṣh wohkukquôsumau na wutch wosketompoh kah puppinashimwoh?
E.36.29 And thou shalt say to Jehoiakim king of Judah, Thus saith the LORD; Thou hast burned this roll, saying, Why hast thou written therein, saying, The king of Babylon shall certainly come and destroy this land, and shall cause to cease from thence man and beast?

α.36.30 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah papaume Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, matta pish wadchanóon howane appinneat wutappuonganit David, kah nupp8e wuhhogkuh piṣh sohwhôkauónuh ut kussittae kesukodtut, kah ut t8hpue nuhkonut.
E.36.30 Therefore thus saith the LORD of Jehoiakim king of Judah; He shall have none to sit upon the throne of David: and his dead body shall be cast out in the day to the heat, and in the night to the frost.

α.36.31 Kah noh piṣh nussasamatoh kah 8skannemunneoh, kah wuttinneumoh, wutch ummatcheseongan8, kah nunnuhkinnumauóog, kah ut wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, kah ut Judae wosketompaut, wame machuk ne ayeuuhkonittue únnog: qut matta kukkeihtam8og.
E.36.31 And I will punish him and his seed and his servants for their iniquity; and I will bring upon them, and upon the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and upon the men of Judah, all the evil that I have pronounced against them; but they hearkened not.

α.36.32 Neit Jehovah onkatog nemunum tuttuppéquianaúsik, kah wuttinnumauoh Baruchoh noh Scribe wunnaumonuh Neriah, kah na wuttit wussukhumun wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, wame b8ke kutt8wongaṣh niṣh Jehojakim Judae ketass8t châgossukupash ut n8taut, kah naut k8tnéhteauunash onkatogaṣh monaash kutt8wongaṣh neyaneyeu8gish.
E.36.32 Then took Jeremiah another roll, and gave it to Baruch the scribe, the son of Neriah; who wrote therein from the mouth of Jeremiah all the words of the book which Jehoiakim king of Judah had burned in the fire: and there were added besides unto them many like words.

α.37.1 KAh ketass8t Zedekiah wunnaumonuh Josiah nompinau Coniahoh wunnaumonuh Jehojakim, neh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t kóhtahs8tamwéhteóhpoh ut Judae ohkeit.
E.37.1 And king Zedekiah the son of Josiah reigned instead of Coniah the son of Jehoiakim, whom Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon made king in the land of Judah.

α.37.2 Qut matta nagum asuh wuttinneumoh, asuh ne ohkee missinninnuog kuhkeitamóog wuttinn8waongash Jehovah, nish án8wopash nashpe Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
E.37.2 But neither he, nor his servants, nor the people of the land, did hearken unto the words of the LORD, which he spake by the prophet Jeremiah.

α.37.3 Kah Zedekiah ketass8t an8team8 Jehucal wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, kah Zephaniah wunnaumonuh Maasejah sephausuaen, en Jeremiahut quoshodtumwaen, n8wop, yeuyeu peantamwanshinnean en Lord num-Manitt8munónut.
E.37.3 And Zedekiah the king sent Jehucal the son of Shelemiah and Zephaniah the son of Maaseiah the priest to the prophet Jeremiah, saying, Pray now unto the LORD our God for us.

α.37.4 Kah Jeremiah petutteau, kah sohham ut kenugke missinninnútu: newutche nag matta ukkupshagkinóuh.
E.37.4 Now Jeremiah came in and went out among the people: for they had not put him into prison.

α.37.5 Neit Pharaoh ukkenauwameumoh sohhamwop wutch Egypt: kah Caldeansog neg weenuhkogig Jerusalem n8tamwehettit unaunchem8k[o]naongan8, nag nukkodtumwog Jerusalem.
E.37.5 Then Pharaoh's army was come forth out of Egypt: and when the Chaldeans that besieged Jerusalem heard tidings of them, they departed from Jerusalem.

α.37.6 Neit wuttinnw8aonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, n8wau,
E.37.6 Then came the word of the LORD unto the prophet Jeremiah saying,

α.37.7 Yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, yeu piṣh kuttinnoneau Judae ketass8t noh an8nukquéog en nuhhogkat, nat8tamonteanat, kusseh, ukkenauwameonk Pharaoh ne sohham8m8uk kutann8munkqunnaóut, piṣh qushkeog en Egypt nehenwonche wutohtuóut.
E.37.7 Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel; Thus shall ye say to the king of Judah, that sent you unto me to enquire of me; Behold, Pharaoh's army, which is come forth to help you, shall return to Egypt into their own land.

α.37.8 Kah Caldeansog piṣh wonk peyaog, kah piṣh ayeuuhkontámwog yeu keitotan, kah piṣh wussohkomuneau, kah piṣh wutchikkossumuneau.
E.37.8 And the Chaldeans shall come again, and fight against this city, and take it, and burn it with fire.

α.37.9 Yeu wussin Jehovah, as8kekomuhteógk kuhhogkaóog, n8wáog, Caldeansog piṣh wunnamuhkut nunnukkonukqunnónog: newutche nag matta piṣh moncheog.
E.37.9 Thus saith the LORD; Deceive not yourselves, saying, The Chaldeans shall surely depart from us: for they shall not depart.

α.37.10 Tôhkônogque kuttogkomonáoh mamusse Caldeanse kenauwameonk, ne ayeuuhkonukqueógig, kah webe squsháhettis n8chumwehtahwhutcheg missinninnúog ut kenugke nagoh, qut onch nag woh neepóog nishnoh pasuk ut wekit, kah piṣh chikohsumwog yeu keitotan nashpe n8tau.
E.37.10 For though ye had smitten the whole army of the Chaldeans that fight against you, and there remained but wounded men among them, yet should they rise up every man in his tent, and burn this city with fire.

α.37.11 Kah n$nihyeup ukkenauwameongan8 Caldeansog neepauwehettit wutch anaquohtag Jerusalem, quhtamunat ukkenauwameonk Pharaoh.
E.37.11 And it came to pass, that when the army of the Chaldeans was broken up from Jerusalem for fear of Pharaoh's army,

α.37.12 Neit Jeremiah sohham wutch Jerusalem, ônat wutohkeit Benjamin, na$wutch chippeinat ut nashaue missinninnútu.
E.37.12 Then Jeremiah went forth out of Jerusalem to go into the land of Benjamin, to separate himself thence in the midst of the people.

α.37.13 Kah apit 8squontamut Benjamin, askuhwheteae mugquomp na wutappináh, noh ussoweu Irijah wunnaumonuh Shelemiah, wunnaumonuh Hananiah, kah tohqunau Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwaénuh, n8wau, kutontsehtau Caldeansog.
E.37.13 And when he was in the gate of Benjamin, a captain of the ward was there, whose name was Irijah, the son of Shelemiah, the son of Hananiah; and he took Jeremiah the prophet, saying, Thou fallest away to the Chaldeans.

α.37.14 Neit Jeremiah n8wau, ne pann8waonk, matta nutontsehtauoh, Caldeansog, qut matta ukkehketauoh: neit Irijah tohqunau Jeremiah kah uppas8uh sontimmouhtu.
E.37.14 Then said Jeremiah, It is false; I fall not away to the Chaldeans. But he hearkened not to him: so Irijah took Jeremiah, and brought him to the princes.

α.37.15 Newaj sontimoog musquanumaog Jeremiahoh, kah wuttogkomouh, kah ukkupshagkinau, ut wekit Jonathan noh Scribe, newutche ne ukkupshagkinegonuhkoneau.
E.37.15 Wherefore the princes were wroth with Jeremiah, and smote him, and put him in prison in the house of Jonathan the scribe: for they had made that the prison.

α.37.16 Jeremiah petuttead[t] pohkenaekomukqut, kah wonogquehtu, & Jeremiah na m8chetikqunohteadt,
E.37.16 When Jeremiah was entered into the dungeon, and into the cabins, and Jeremiah had remained there many days;

α.37.17 Neit Zedechiah ketass8t ann8team8 & uppohquohshagkunuh; & ketass8t ukkeme nat8tomauoh ut wékit, kah n8wop, sun ne teagwe kutt8onk wutch Jehovahut? kah Jeremiah n8wau, ohtau, newutche n8wau, ken pish kupponit ut wunnutcheganit Babylone ketass8t.
E.37.17 Then Zedekiah the king sent, and took him out: and the king asked him secretly in his house, and said, Is there any word from the LORD? And Jeremiah said, There is: for, said he, thou shalt be delivered into the hand of the king of Babylon.

α.37.18 Nano Jeremiah unnau ketass8toh Zedechiahhoh, toh kittinne matchenehesh, asuh kittinneumog, asuh yeug missinninnuog, waj kuppishagkinneog?
E.37.18 Moreover Jeremiah said unto king Zedekiah, What have I offended against thee, or against thy servants, or against this people, that ye have put me in prison?

α.37.19 Uttiyeug kukquoshodtumwaeneumog, neg quoshodtumunkqueaneg, n8wahettit, Babylone ketass8t matta pish kutayeuuhkonuk8 asuh yeu ohke.
E.37.19 Where are now your prophets which prophesied unto you, saying, The king of Babylon shall not come against you, nor against this land?

α.37.20 Newutch yeuyeu n8tash k8wehquetumoush, woi nul$Lordum ketass8t, nunnanumpanwaonk tapeneaumunach ut anaquabean k8wehquetumoush, onk woh mo kukqushkeahheu en wekit Jonathan noh Scribe, ishkont ná nuttit nuppun.
E.37.20 Therefore hear now, I pray thee, O my lord the king: let my supplication, I pray thee, be accepted before thee; that thou cause me not to return to the house of Jonathan the scribe, lest I die there.

α.37.21 Neit Zedechiah ketass8t ann8team8 woh pononat Jeremiah kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit, kah asekesukokish woh wutassamonaoont kodchuhki petukqunnunk wutch wuttaumaogkumut petukqununganehteaenuog, nô pajeh wame petukquneg keitotanat mahtshunk yeu wuttinne Jeremiah appin kuppishagkinnittue chippinneutunganit.
E.37.21 Then Zedekiah the king commanded that they should commit Jeremiah into the court of the prison, and that they should give him daily a piece of bread out of the bakers' street, until all the bread in the city were spent. Thus Jeremiah remained in the court of the prison.

α.38.1 NEit Shephatiah wunnaumonuh Mattan kah Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Pashur kah J[u]cal wunnaumonuh Shelemiah kah Pashur wunnaumonuh Malchiah, nag n8tamw[ô]g kutt8wongash nish Jeremiah an8wajish en wame missinninnuut, n8wau,
E.38.1 Then Shephatiah the son of Mattan, and Gedaliah the son of Pashur, and Jucal the son of Shelemiah, and Pashur the son of Malchiah, heard the words that Jeremiah had spoken unto all the people, saying,

α.38.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah, noh yeu apit keitotanat, pish nup nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, qut noh sohhog en Caldeansut pish pomantam: newutche noh pish ohto uppomantamoonk wutch toh an tohqunuk, kah pish pomantam.
E.38.2 Thus saith the LORD, He that remaineth in this city shall die by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence: but he that goeth forth to the Chaldeans shall live; for he shall have his life for a prey, and shall live.

α.38.3 Yeu wussin Jehovah, yeu keitotan pish wunnamuhkut magun en wunnutchegan8out Babylone ketass8t ukkenauwameonk, neg pish sohhogig
E.38.3 Thus saith the LORD, This city shall surely be given into the hand of the king of Babylon's army, which shall take it.

α.38.4 Newaj sontimoog unnahettit ketass8toh, k8wehquetumauunumun yeuoh wosketomp nushunach: newutche yeu wuttiñe n8chumwehteauun wunnutchegan8oash ayeuhteaenuog neg apitcheg yeu otanat, kah wunnutcheganooash wame missinninnuog, nish anont kutt8wongash newutche yeuoh wosketomp matta natinneham8 8niyeuongan8 yeug missinninnuog, qut woskehuonat.
E.38.4 Therefore the princes said unto the king, We beseech thee, let this man be put to death: for thus he weakeneth the hands of the men of war that remain in this city, and the hands of all the people, in speaking such words unto them: for this man seeketh not the welfare of this people, but the hurt.

α.38.5 Neit Zedechiah kétass8t n8wau, kusseh noh appu kenutchegan8out, newutche ketass8t matta woh toh kuttin wuttamhik8.
E.38.5 Then Zedekiah the king said, Behold, he is in your hand: for the king is not he that can do any thing against you.

α.38.6 Neit nag nemunaog Jeremiahoh, kah wuttinuhkonauh ut uppohkononogk8mut Malchiah wunnaumonuh Hammelech, ne [ó]htag kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutonganit, kah n8kompanaog Jeremiahoh nashpe pemuneahtonash: kah ut pohkenonogque matta nippen8, qut pisseogquanu8: neit Jeremiah quttaueu ut pisseogqu[a]nit.
E.38.6 Then took they Jeremiah, and cast him into the dungeon of Malchiah the son of Hammelech, that was in the court of the prison: and they let down Jeremiah with cords. And in the dungeon there was no water, but mire: so Jeremiah sunk in the mire.

α.38.7 Neit Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, pasuk euneuch ut ketass8t wekit, n8tog nag ponaog Jeremiahoh pohkinnaonogqut (ketass8t neit apit ut Benjamine squontamut.)
E.38.7 Now when Ebedmelech the Ethiopian, one of the eunuchs which was in the king's house, heard that they had put Jeremiah in the dungeon; the king then sitting in the gate of Benjamin;

α.38.8 Ebedmelech sohham wutch wekit ketass8t kah ken8nau ketass8toh n8wau,
E.38.8 Ebedmelech went forth out of the king's house, and spake to the king saying,

α.38.9 Nul$Lordum ketass8t yeug wosketompaog matche usseog wame ne anheahettit Jeremiahhoh quoshodtumwaenuh neh pánonteahetticheh en pohkinonogqut, kah noh nahen paskanontam ut ayeuonganit ne ayit, newutche matta wonk petukqununganun8 ut keitotanat.
E.38.9 My lord the king, these men have done evil in all that they have done to Jeremiah the prophet, whom they have cast into the dungeon; and he is like to die for hunger in the place where he is: for there is no more bread in the city.

α.38.10 Neit ketass8t ann8nau Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, n8wau, neemun yeu wutch nishwinchahkodtog wosketompaog, kah kuhkuhquin, Jeremiah quoshodtumwaenin wutch pohkenónog[p]ut, ash na nupp8kup.
E.38.10 Then the king commanded Ebedmelech the Ethiopian, saying, Take from hence thirty men with thee, and take up Jeremiah the prophet out of the dungeon, before he die.

α.38.11 Neit Ebedmelech neemunau wosketompuh, kah petutteau wekit ketass8t ut agwe nompak8unnekomukqut, kah na 8tinnumun nukkononákinaṣh, kah nukkonéwhiash, kah niṣh uppinnompánumaú[o]náoaṣh nashpe pemunneahtonaṣh en pohkinónogqut en Jeremiahut.
E.38.11 So Ebedmelech took the men with him, and went into the house of the king under the treasury, and took thence old cast clouts and old rotten rags, and let them down by cords into the dungeon to Jeremiah.

α.38.12 Kah Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian unnau Jeremiahoh, ponsh yeuyeu yeush nukkononakinash, kah nukkonéhwhiaṣh agwe kenukqueit agwe pemuneohtonit, kah Jeremiah ne wutussen.
E.38.12 And Ebedmelech the Ethiopian said unto Jeremiah, Put now these old cast clouts and rotten rags under thine armholes under the cords. And Jeremiah did so.

α.38.13 Neit kuhkuhqu[n]aoh Jeremiah nashpe pemuneohtanash, kah nag wunneemun[o]uh wutch pohkinónogqut, kah Jeremiah appu kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutunkanit.
E.38.13 So they drew up Jeremiah with cords, and took him up out of the dungeon: and Jeremiah remained in the court of the prison.

α.38.14 Neit Zedekiah ketass8t ann8team8, kah nemunumau, Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwanúh, ut nashwunnú8k ahhut petutteamuk Jehovah wekit, kah ketass8t unnau Jeremiahoh, kenat8tomouṣh ne teag adtahtiéhkon ne teag.
E.38.14 Then Zedekiah the king sent, and took Jeremiah the prophet unto him into the third entry that is in the house of the LORD: and the king said unto Jeremiah, I will ask thee a thing; hide nothing from me.

α.38.15 Neit Jeremiah unnau Zedekiahoh, wahteauwahunon sunnummatta woh wunnamuhkut kenusheu? kah kogkuhtimunon, sunnummatta woh kukkehketiyeu?
E.38.15 Then Jeremiah said unto Zedekiah, If I declare it unto thee, wilt thou not surely put me to death? and if I give thee counsel, wilt thou not hearken unto me?

α.38.16 Neit ketass8t kemu chadchekéimoh Jeremiahoh, n8wau, pomantog Jehovah noh ayimukquean yeuh keteahogkôunoh, matta kenushin8h, asuh matta nummag8 kuhhog en wunnutchegan8wóut yeug woskeompaog kod nushhukqueaneg.
E.38.16 So Zedekiah the king sware secretly unto Jeremiah, saying, As the LORD liveth, that made us this soul, I will not put thee to death, neither will I give thee into the hand of these men that seek thy life.

α.38.17 Neit Jeremiah unnau Zedekiahoh, yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteaog, um-Manitt8m8oh Isr[à]el, tohneit wunnamuhkut sohhaman en wussontim[ô]mut Babylone ketass8t, neit kukketeahogkou piṣh pomantam, kah yeu keitotan matta piṣh chikohtano n8taut, kah piṣh ken kuppomantam, kah kek. 
E.38.17 Then said Jeremiah unto Zedekiah, Thus saith the LORD, the God of hosts, the God of Israel; If thou wilt assuredly go forth unto the king of Babylon's princes, then thy soul shall live, and this city shall not be burned with fire; and thou shalt live, and thine house:

α.38.18 Qut matta sohham8an en wussontimómut Babylone ketass8t, neit piṣh yeu keitotan magun en wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, kah nag piṣh wutchi[k]kossùmuneau ut n8taut, kah matta piṣh kuppohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8out.
E.38.18 But if thou wilt not go forth to the king of Babylon's princes, then shall this city be given into the hand of the Chaldeans, and they shall burn it with fire, and thou shalt not escape out of their hand.

α.38.19 Kah Zedekiah ketass8t unnau Jeremiahoh, n8wabesuon Jewsog neg anogquehcheg Caldeansog, ishkont nag nupponukquog wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, kah nuttôontohkônukquog.
E.38.19 And Zedekiah the king said unto Jeremiah, I am afraid of the Jews that are fallen to the Chaldeans, lest they deliver me into their hand, and they mock me.

α.38.20 Qut Jeremiah n8wau, nag matta piṣh magwog kuhhog, n8swetaṣh k8wehquetumoush 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Lord, ne ânun: neit piṣh k8nihukqun, kah kukketeahogkou piṣh pomantam.
E.38.20 But Jeremiah said, They shall not deliver thee. Obey, I beseech thee, the voice of the LORD, which I speak unto thee: so it shall be well unto thee, and thy soul shall live.

α.38.21 Qut sekeneaman sohhamun, yeu kutt8onk ne Jehovah nahtussit.
E.38.21 But if thou refuse to go forth, this is the word that the LORD hath shewed me:

α.38.22 Kah kusseh, wame mittamwussissog sekqshoncheg ut Judae ketass8t wekit piṣh sohh8wunóog ut wussontimóm8ut Bablyone ketass8t, kah yeug piṣh n8waog, keetompaog kukkitchittôusháhikquog, kah kussohkunkquog, kusseetash quttauushauṣh ut pissagquanit, kah nag qushkeog.
E.38.22 And, behold, all the women that are left in the king of Judah's house shall be brought forth to the king of Babylon's princes, and those women shall say, Thy friends have set thee on, and have prevailed against thee: thy feet are sunk in the mire, and they are turned away back.

α.38.23 Neit nag piṣh sohh8wunaog wame kummittamwussoh kah kummukkiésumoh en Caldeansut, kah matta piṣh kuppohquohham8 wutch wunnutchegan8out, qut piṣh ken kuttohqunit nashpe wunnutcheg Babylone ketass8t: kah yeu piṣh kutchikkossumwáhtauun keitotan ut n8taut.
E.38.23 So they shall bring out all thy wives and thy children to the Chaldeans: and thou shalt not escape out of their hand, but shalt be taken by the hand of the king of Babylon: and thou shalt cause this city to be burned with fire.

α.38.24 Neit Zedekiah unnau Jeremiahoh, howan wohteau8hkitch yeush kutt8wongaṣh kah matta piṣh kenupp8.
E.38.24 Then said Zedekiah unto Jeremiah, Let no man know of these words, and thou shalt not die.

α.38.25 Qut sontimóog n8tamwehettit kukkeket8hkouṣh, kah nag peyaonukquean, kah unnukquean, wahteauwáhenan uttoh âun adt ketass8t: ahque adtohtaiinnean, kah matta kenushin8mun, kah wonk toh ánukquean ketass8t.
E.38.25 But if the princes hear that I have talked with thee, and they come unto thee, and say unto thee, Declare unto us now what thou hast said unto the king, hide it not from us, and we will not put thee to death; also what the king said unto thee:

α.38.26 Neit nag piṣh kuttinnóog, nupponamup n8wehquetum8onk anaquabit ketass8t, woh mo nukqushkeáhik8unat en [J]onathan wekit naut nuppunat.
E.38.26 Then thou shalt say unto them, I presented my supplication before the king, that he would not cause me to return to Jonathan's house, to die there.

α.38.27 Neit wame sontimóog peyaonóog Jeremiahoh, kah nag wunat8tomauóuh, kah wuttinónash wame niṣh neaunak ketass8t ánann8nont: neit wutahque keket8hkauóuh, newutche matta wahsham8 ne teag.
E.38.27 Then came all the princes unto Jeremiah, and asked him: and he told them according to all these words that the king had commanded. So they left off speaking with him; for the matter was not perceived.

α.38.28 Neit Jeremiah appu kuppishagkinittue chippinnutunkanit pajeh nâ kesukok Jerusalem sohkomuk, kah na wutappineah Jerusalem sohkomuk.
E.38.28 So Jeremiah abode in the court of the prison until the day that Jerusalem was taken: and he was there when Jerusalem was taken.

α.39.1 PAsuk8gun wutteashe kodtum8muk Zedekiah Judae ketass8t, ut piogqussit nepauz, Nebuchádrezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah wame ukkenauwameónk ayeuuhkonittue peyaontamwog Jerusalem, kah nag 8wéenuhkomuneau.
E.39.1 In the ninth year of Zedekiah king of Judah, in the tenth month, came Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon and all his army against Jerusalem, and they besieged it.

α.39.2 Nabowunnukqutte kodtum8mit Zedekiah, ut yaue nepauzsaut, kah pasuk8gun adtashikqunohhog, keitotan pokqsheau.
E.39.2 And in the eleventh year of Zedekiah, in the fourth month, the ninth day of the month, the city was broken up.

α.39.3 Kah wame wussontimom[ô]h Babylone ketass8t petutteaog, kah appuog nasha[ú]e usquontamut, Nergal-Sharezer, Samger-Nebo, Sarsechim, Rabsaris, Nergal-Sharezer, Rabmag, kah wame onkatogig Babylone ketass8t wussontimómoh.
E.39.3 And all the princes of the king of Babylon came in, and sat in the middle gate, even Nergalsharezer, Samgarnebo, Sarsechim, Rabsaris, Nergalsharezer, Rabmag, with all the residue of the princes of the king of Babylon.

α.39.4 Kah n$nih[,] Zedekiah Judae ketass8t noh nauont, kah wame ayeuhteénúh, neit nag wussem8og, kah sohhamwog wutch [ó]tanat nukkonáeu, en may$ut ne kishke ketass8t tanohketeaonganit, en squontamut ut nashaue neese qussukquaneuntunkanit, kah en sohham mukoshquttae may$ut.
E.39.4 And it came to pass, that when Zedekiah the king of Judah saw them, and all the men of war, then they fled, and went forth out of the city by night, by the way of the king's garden, by the gate betwixt the two walls: and he went out the way of the plain.

α.39.5 Qut Caldeansog ukkenauwameongan8 nah wunn8swuttahwhóuh, kah mattanáog Zedekiahoh ut Jerichoe mukoshquttaut, k[á]h tohqunáhettit, nag uppas8óuh Nebuchadnezzarut Babylone ketass8t ut Riblah ut ohkeit Hamath, uttoh adt wussumomp.
E.39.5 But the Chaldeans' army pursued after them, and overtook Zedekiah in the plains of Jericho: and when they had taken him, they brought him up to Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon to Riblah in the land of Hamath, where he gave judgment upon him.

α.39.6 Neit Babylone ketass8t nushau wunnaumonuh Zedekiah ut anaquabit, ut Riblah, kah wonk Babylone ketass8t nushau wame Judae sontimuh.
E.39.6 Then the king of Babylon slew the sons of Zedekiah in Riblah before his eyes: also the king of Babylon slew all the nobles of Judah.

α.39.7 Nano, skojkesukquánau Zedekiahoh, kah wutáhtogkuppanuh chainsaṣh wutuss8unónat Babylon.
E.39.7 Moreover he put out Zedekiah's eyes, and bound him with chains, to carry him to Babylon.

α.39.8 Kah Caldeansog chikkossumwog ketass8t wek, kah wek8oash missinninnuwog ut n8taut, kah n8konteaog Jerusaleme pummeneutunk.
E.39.8 And the Chaldeans burned the king's house, and the houses of the people, with fire, and brake down the walls of Jerusalem.

α.39.9 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp missinóhteau ashqshoncheg missinninnuog, neg apitcheg keitotanat, kah yeug amaéhcheg, ummosogquéhtunkquoh, kah onkatogig missinninnuog neg ashqshoncheg.
E.39.9 Then Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard carried away captive into Babylon the remnant of the people that remained in the city, and those that fell away, that fell to him, with the rest of the people that remained.

α.39.10 Qut Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp nukkonau matchekue missinninnúh neg monteag ohtau8gig ut ohkeit Judah, kah nah wuttinnumauoh weenominneohtekonaṣh kah ohteukonash ne nan ahquompág.
E.39.10 But Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard left of the poor of the people, which had nothing, in the land of Judah, and gave them vineyards and fields at the same time.

α.39.11 Kah Nebuchanezzar ketass8t ann8nau papaume Jeremiah, Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, n8wau,
E.39.11 Now Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon gave charge concerning Jeremiah to Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard, saying,

α.39.12 Nemun kah wunádchan, kah woskeheúhkon, qut unneh ne woh ánukquean.
E.39.12 Take him, and look well to him, and do him no harm; but do unto him even as he shall say unto thee.

α.39.13 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, ann8team8, kah Nebushazban, Rabsaris, kah Nergal-Sh[a]rezer, Rabmag, kah wame wussontimómuh Babylone ketass8t.
E.39.13 So Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard sent, and Nebushasban, Rabsaris, and Nergalsharezer, Rabmag, and all the king of Babylon's princes;

α.39.14 Nag ann8team8og kah neemunoog Jeremiahoh wutch kuppishagkinnittue chippinnutunkanit, kah wutáhtashónuh ut Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, woh nummonchanónat en weekit, neit weechayeumau missinninnúh.
E.39.14 Even they sent, and took Jeremiah out of the court of the prison, and committed him unto Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan, that he should carry him home: so he dwelt among the people.

α.39.15 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah ash kophâusit kuppishagkinnittue chippinnútunkanit, n8wau,
E.39.15 Now the word of the LORD came unto Jeremiah, while he was shut up in the court of the prison, saying,

α.39.16 Monchish ken8s Ebedmelech wut-Ethiopian, n8wash, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nunnuhkinnumau nuttinn8waongaṣh yeuoh keitotan, wutche machuk kah matta wanegik, kah nish pish pakodche n$niyeuash ut anaquabean.
E.39.16 Go and speak to Ebedmelech the Ethiopian, saying, Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will bring my words upon this city for evil, and not for good; and they shall be accomplished in that day before thee.

α.39.17 Qut kupppohquohwhunush ne kesukok wussin Jehovah, kah matta pish kupponitteoh wunnutchegan8óut yeug wosketompaog quoshadcheg.
E.39.17 But I will deliver thee in that day, saith the LORD: and thou shalt not be given into the hand of the men of whom thou art afraid.

α.39.18 Newutche wunnamuhkut kuppohquohwhunush, kah matta piṣh kuppenushoh n[a]shpe togkodteg, qut pish kuppomantam 8w[o]ntam kuttohqunnum8onk, newutche kuppabuhtanumeh wussin Jehovah.
E.39.18 For I will surely deliver thee, and thou shalt not fall by the sword, but thy life shall be for a prey unto thee: because thou hast put thy trust in me, saith the LORD.

α.40.1 WUttinn8wank ne pauhónukqut Jeremiah wutch Jehovahut, mahche Nebuzaradan askuhwhetae mugquomp moncheáheont wutch Ramath, noh nemunont tohtogkuppissit chainsaṣh, ut kenugke wame neg masinohteamukeg wutch Jerusalem kah Judah, nag masinohteamukeg en Babylon.
E.40.1 The word that came to Jeremiah from the LORD, after that Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard had let him go from Ramah, when he had taken him being bound in chains among all that were carried away captive of Jerusalem and Judah, which were carried away captive unto Babylon.

α.40.2 Kah askuhwheteae mugquomp nemunau Jeremiahoh, kah wuttinuh, Lord kum-Manitt8m matche ken8tam ne machuk yeu ut ayeuonganit.
E.40.2 And the captain of the guard took Jeremiah, and said unto him, The LORD thy God hath pronounced this evil upon this place.

α.40.3 Yeuyeu Jehovah uppaudtauun, kah wutussen ne an8wop: newutche kummatcheneheomw8 Jehovah, kah matta ken8swehtam8mw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, newaj yeu nuhkuhkongqueóg.
E.40.3 Now the LORD hath brought it, and done according as he hath said: because ye have sinned against the LORD, and have not obeyed his voice, therefore this thing is come upon you.

α.40.4 Kah yeuyeu kusseh, kutompenush yeu kesukok wutch chainsash ohtagish kenutcheganit; wekontaman k8weechaiinneat Babylon, peyaush, kah k8ne nanauwuhhesh; qut matta wekontam8an k8weechaiinneat en Babylon, ne nohtaj: kusseh wame ohke anaquabean; uttoh wekontaman ónat ne âush.
E.40.4 And now, behold, I loose thee this day from the chains which were upon thine hand. If it seem good unto thee to come with me into Babylon, come; and I will look well unto thee: but if it seem ill unto thee to come with me into Babylon, forbear: behold, all the land is before thee: whither it seemeth good and convenient for thee to go, thither go.

α.40.5 Kah asquam quashkeit, n8wop, qushkish wonk en Gedaliahut wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunumwaheumpoh wame Judae keitotanash, kah noh weetom ut kenugke missinninnuog: asuh aush uttoh an tapeneaman ônat neit askuhwheteae mugquomp wuttinnumauoh m[é]echum, kah onkquatunk, kah ummoncheaheuh.
E.40.5 Now while he was not yet gone back, he said, Go back also to Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan, whom the king of Babylon hath made governor over the cities of Judah, and dwell with him among the people: or go wheresoever it seemeth convenient unto thee to go. So the captain of the guard gave him victuals and a reward, and let him go.

α.40.6 Neit Jeremiah âonau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam en Mizpah, & 8weetomuh ut kenugke missininnuh neg asqunutcheg ut ohkeit.
E.40.6 Then went Jeremiah unto Gedaliah the son of Ahikam to Mizpah; and dwelt with him among the people that were left in the land.

α.40.7 Neit wame kenauwamee mukquompaog ut ohteuhkontu, nag kah 8wosketomp8m8uh, n8tamohettit Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwaheau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, ut ohkeit: & wutahtohshuh wosketompoh, kah mittamwussissoh kah mukkiesoh, madchekitcheg ut óhkeit, neg sequnutcheg wutche ma[u]nohteamukeg ut Bablyon;
E.40.7 Now when all the captains of the forces which were in the fields, even they and their men, heard that the king of Babylon had made Gedaliah the son of Ahikam governor in the land, and had committed unto him men, and women, and children, and of the poor of the land, of them that were not carried away captive to Babylon;

α.40.8 Neit nag peyaonaog Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah, Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, & Johanan kah Jonathan wunnaumonuh Kareah, & Serajah wunnaumonuh Tanhumeth; & wunnaumonuh Ephai, wut-Netophathite[,] kah Jezaniah wunnaumonuh wut-Maachathite, nag kah 8wosketompom8uh,
E.40.8 Then they came to Gedaliah to Mizpah, even Ishmael the son of Nethaniah, and Johanan and Jonathan the sons of Kareah, and Seraiah the son of Tanhumeth, and the sons of Ephai the Netophathite, and Jezaniah the son of a Maachathite, they and their men.

α.40.9 Kah Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, nah wutchadchekeimuh, kah wuttinninneum8uh, n8wau, wabesehteok k8tinninneumuhkauonaoont Caldeansog: wutohkek yeu ohkeit, kah wuttinninneumuhkok Babylone ketass8t, & pish k8niyeuwontamuneau.
E.40.9 And Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan sware unto them and to their men, saying, Fear not to serve the Chaldeans: dwell in the land, and serve the king of Babylon, and it shall be well with you.

α.40.10 Kah nen, kusseh, nuttai Mizpah wuttinninneumuhkauonat Caldeansog, neg pish páuh[ó]nukqueagig: qut kenaau mauinne[á]k wine, kah neepunné meechummuongash kah pummee, kah nish ponam8k k8wishquaout kah ayek kukkeitotanahtu, nish attumunumogish.
E.40.10 As for me, behold, I will dwell at Mizpah, to serve the Chaldeans, which will come unto us: but ye, gather ye wine, and summer fruits, and oil, and put them in your vessels, and dwell in your cities that ye have taken.

α.40.11 Nano wame Jewsog ut Moab, kah kenugke Ammonitsog, kah ut Edom, & neg ayitcheg wame ohkeit, nag n8tamwehettit Babylone ketass8t, sequnau Judae sequnutcheg, kah nanawunnumwaheau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan.
E.40.11 Likewise when all the Jews that were in Moab, and among the Ammonites, and in Edom, and that were in all the countries, heard that the king of Babylon had left a remnant of Judah, and that he had set over them Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan;

α.40.12 Wame Jewsog qushkeog wutch wame ayeuonganehtu uttoh an8kauuttus, kah nag peyaog Judae ohkeit, en Gedaliahut, en Mizpah, kah nag mukkinnumwog wine, kah neepunne meechummuongash m8naash.
E.40.12 Even all the Jews returned out of all places whither they were driven, and came to the land of Judah, to Gedaliah, unto Mizpah, and gathered wine and summer fruits very much.

α.40.13 Nano, Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog ut ohteuhkontu, nag peyaonaog Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah.
E.40.13 Moreover Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces that were in the fields, came to Gedaliah to Mizpah,

α.40.14 Kah wuttinuh, sun kuppahke wahteoh, Baal Ammonitse ketass8t, ann8nau Ishmaeloh wunnaumonuh Nethaniah kenushikqunat qut Geadliah wúnnaumonuh Ahika matta wunnamptauoh.
E.40.14 And said unto him, Dost thou certainly know that Baalis the king of the Ammonites hath sent Ishmael the son of Nethaniah to slay thee? But Gedaliah the son of Ahikam believed them not.

α.40.15 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, keme ken8nau Gedaliahoh ut Mizpah, n8wau, k8wehquetumoush moncheti, kah nunnush Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, kah matta howan pish 8wahteau8un, tohwutch woh noh nushikquean, neg wame Jewsog miaehtunkquéaneg, woh noswaiyeuog, kah yeug sequnutcheg ut Judah woh pagwanoog.
E.40.15 Then Johanan the son of Kareah spake to Gedaliah in Mizpah secretly saying, Let me go, I pray thee, and I will slay Ishmael the son of Nethaniah, and no man shall know it: wherefore should he slay thee, that all the Jews which are gathered unto thee should be scattered, and the remnant in Judah perish?

α.40.16 Qut Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam, unnau Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, matta yeu pish kutussein, newutche kuppann8wáh Ishmael.
E.40.16 But Gedaliah the son of Ahikam said unto Johanan the son of Kareah, Thou shalt not do this thing: for thou speakest falsely of Ishmael.

α.41.1 KAh n$nih, ut nesausuk adtahs8it nepauz, Ishmael, wunnaumonuh Nethaniah wunnaumonuh Elishamah, ketass8tamwe wuskannem, kah wussontimausoh ketass8t piogqussuoh woskeotmpuh weechog, peyaonog Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam ut Mizpah, kah na meechwog petukqunneg ut Mizpah.
E.41.1 Now it came to pass in the seventh month, that Ishmael the son of Nethaniah the son of Elishama, of the seed royal, and the princes of the king, even ten men with him, came unto Gedaliah the son of Ahikam to Mizpah; and there they did eat bread together in Mizpah.

α.41.2 Neit Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah kah piogqussuh wosketompuh weechogqutcheh neepoog, kah togkomaog Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam wunnaumonuh Shaphan nashpe togkodteg, kah wunnushouh, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwaheompoh ut ohkeit.
E.41.2 Then arose Ishmael the son of Nethaniah, and the ten men that were with him, and smote Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan with the sword, and slew him, whom the king of Babylon had made governor over the land.

α.41.3 Ishmael wonk nushau wame Jewsoh, neh weechayeumumpoh, weeche Gedaliah ut Mizpah, kah Caldeansog neg na apitcheg, kah ayeuhteaenuog.
E.41.3 Ishmael also slew all the Jews that were with him, even with Gedaliah, at Mizpah, and the Chaldeans that were found there, and the men of war.

α.41.4 Kah n$niyeup, nahohtôeu kesukok mahche nushit Gedaliah, k[á]h matta howan 8wahteauouun.
E.41.4 And it came to pass the second day after he had slain Gedaliah, and no man knew it,

α.41.5 Na 8muneau nawhutche wutch Shechem, wutch Shiloh, kah wutch Samaria, shwosuk tahshinchagkodtog, m8sôsik 8weeshitt8un8òash, wuthogk8un8ash nehneekuhkôsuash, kah neekussôsik wuhhogkauh, mag8ongash kah weetemungquok ohtag wunnutchegan8óut, nish paudtauunat wekit Jehovah.
E.41.5 That there came certain from Shechem, from Shiloh, and from Samaria, even fourscore men, having their beards shaven, and their clothes rent, and having cut themselves, with offerings and incense in their hand, to bring them to the house of the LORD.

α.41.6 Kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, sohham wutch Mizpah nah wunnogskauonat, nauwadtohpausu ne ayont, kah n$nih nah nogskauo[n]t, nah wuttinuh, peyaón8k Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam.
E.41.6 And Ishmael the son of Nethaniah went forth from Mizpah to meet them, weeping all along as he went: and it came to pass, as he met them, he said unto them, Come to Gedaliah the son of Ahikam.

α.41.7 Kah n$nih paahettit nô|8tâni, Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah nah wuñushoh, kah wuttinuhkonuh ut nanashaue pasáhtheganit, nagum, kah wosketompuh neh weechógqutcheh.
E.41.7 And it was so, when they came into the midst of the city, that Ishmael the son of Nethaniah slew them, and cast them into the midst of the pit, he, and the men that were with him.

α.41.8 Qut piukqussuog ut kenugke wuhhogkaout neg anoncheg Ishmaeloh, ahque nushinnean, nutohtomun nompak8unash ut ohteuhkontu, wheatash, kah barlyhash, kah pummee kah hony, neit kehchithau, kah matta wunnushoh ut kenugke wematut.
E.41.8 But ten men were found among them that said unto Ishmael, Slay us not: for we have treasures in the field, of wheat, and of barley, and of oil, and of honey. So he forbare, and slew them not among their brethren.

α.41.9 Kah ne passohtheg ne Ishmael petuhteadt wame nupp8e wuhhogkauh (neh nashoncheh newutche Gedaliah) né Asa ketass8t ayikup wutche u[k]qushaonk Baashahoh Israelle ketass8toh, kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah wunnumwamechumuhkon neh nashómukeh.
E.41.9 Now the pit wherein Ishmael had cast all the dead bodies of the men, whom he had slain because of Gedaliah, was it which Asa the king had made for fear of Baasha king of Israel: and Ishmael the son of Nethaniah filled it with them that were slain.

α.41.10 Neit Ishmael missinohteau wame sekqshonutcheh missinninúh ut Mizpéh, ketass8t wuttaunoh, kah wame missinninúog, neg sekqshoncheg ut Mizpah: neh Nebuzaradan askuhwhete[a]e mugquomp ohtúhshau Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam; kah Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah ummissinóhkonu[h] kah monchu qushkogkonat en Ammonitsut.
E.41.10 Then Ishmael carried away captive all the residue of the people that were in Mizpah, even the king's daughters, and all the people that remained in Mizpah, whom Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard had committed to Gedaliah the son of Ahikam: and Ishmael the son of Nethaniah carried them away captive, and departed to go over to the Ammonites.

α.41.11 Qut Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenawamee mugquompaog, n8tamwehettit wame ne machuk Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah ne asit,
E.41.11 But when Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces that were with him, heard of all the evil that Ishmael the son of Nethaniah had done,

α.41.12 Neit nemunaog wame wosketompuh, kah ayeuuhkonaog Ishmaeloh wunnaumonuh Neth[a]niah, kah nag wunnamheouh ut kishke mishe nippeut ne ut Gibeon.
E.41.12 Then they took all the men, and went to fight with Ishmael the son of Nethaniah, and found him by the great waters that are in Gibeon.

α.41.13 Kah n$nihyeup, wame missinninnuog neg weechayeumoncheg Ishmaeloh, n[a]uahettit Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, neh weetómukqutcheh, neit weekontamwog.
E.41.13 Now it came to pass, that when all the people which were with Ishmael saw Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces that were with him, then they were glad.

α.41.14 Neit wame missinninnúog neh Ishmael masinohteacheh wutch Mizpah, quinnuppeog, kah qushkeog, kah auog Johananut wunnaumonuh Kareah.
E.41.14 So all the people that Ishmael had carried away captive from Mizpah cast about and returned, and went unto Johanan the son of Kareah.

α.41.15 Qut Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah pohquohham wutch Johananut, kah weeche shwosuk tahsuog, kah auog Ammonitsut.
E.41.15 But Ishmael the son of Nethaniah escaped from Johanan with eight men, and went to the Ammonites.

α.41.16 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, nag neemunáog wame ashqshonutcheh missinninnúh, neh pohquohwhunoncheh wutch Ishmaelut wunnaumonuh Nethaniah, wutch Mizpah, (mahche nushont Gedaliah wunnaumonuh Ahikam) menuhkesue ayeuhteaenúog, kah mittamwussissog, kah mukki[é]sog, kah Eunuchsog neh wôs8oncheh Gibeon.
E.41.16 Then took Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces that were with him, all the remnant of the people whom he had recovered from Ishmael the son of Nethaniah, from Mizpah, after that he had slain Gedaliah the son of Ahikam, even mighty men of war, and the women, and the children, and the eunuchs, whom he had brought again from Gibeon:

α.41.17 Kah nag monch[é]og, kah appuog wutappuonganit Chimham, ne kishke Bethlehem, woh wutch petutteamuk en Egypt.
E.41.17 And they departed, and dwelt in the habitation of Chimham, which is by Bethlehem, to go to enter into Egypt,

α.41.18 Wutch Caldeansog: newutche nag ukqushóuh, newutche Ishmael wunnaumonuh Nethaniah nushop Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, neh Babylone ketass8t nanawunnumwáheumpoh ut ohkeit.
E.41.18 Because of the Chaldeans: for they were afraid of them, because Ishmael the son of Nethaniah had slain Gedaliah the son of Ahikam, whom the king of Babylon made governor in the land.

α.42.1 NEit wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, kah Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, Jeremiah wunnaumonuh Hoshajah, kah wame missinninnuog wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk, nag pas8tshaog.
E.42.1 Then all the captains of the forces, and Johanan the son of Kareah, and Jezaniah the son of Hoshaiah, and all the people from the least even unto the greatest, came near,

α.42.2 Kah unnaog J[e]remiahoh quoshodtumwaénuh, k8wehquetumunumun, n8wehquetum8onganun tapeneunkqutch ut anaquabean, kah peantamwanshinnean en Jehovah kum-Manitt8mut, wutche wame yeug ashqshoncheg (newutche nutogguhse sekqshomun wutch mattaanukuppanneg, neh kuskesukquash yeuyeu nauoncheh)
E.42.2 And said unto Jeremiah the prophet, Let, we beseech thee, our supplication be accepted before thee, and pray for us unto the LORD thy God, even for all this remnant; (for we are left but a few of many, as thine eyes do behold us:)

α.42.3 Onk woh Jehovah kum-Manitt8m nunnáhtinukqun may uttoh woh aôog, kah ne woh aséog.
E.42.3 That the LORD thy God may shew us the way wherein we may walk, and the thing that we may do.

α.42.4 Neit Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen nah wuttinuh, ken8tauunumw8, kusseh, nuppeantamau Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8 neaunak kukkutt8wonganooash, kah pish nnih, uttoh áne Jehovah namp8hamunkqueóg, pish k8wahteauwáhenuneau: wanne teag kukkogkôununumauun8mw8.
E.42.4 Then Jeremiah the prophet said unto them, I have heard you; behold, I will pray unto the LORD your God according to your words; and it shall come to pass, that whatsoever thing the LORD shall answer you, I will declare it unto you; I will keep nothing back from you.

α.42.5 Neit nag unnáog Jeremiahoh, Lord noh wunnamuhkutee, kah pabuhtánumwe wauwaeni[e]ch nashauwe ut nenawun, matta usseog neaunak wame nish Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, ann8nukqueániṣh en nuhhogkanónut.
E.42.5 Then they said to Jeremiah, The LORD be a true and faithful witness between us, if we do not even according to all things for the which the LORD thy God shall send thee to us.

α.42.6 Wanegik asuh machuk n8swehtamumun 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, noh ánunn8nunog, onk woh n8niyeuhhikqunan n8swehtomog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun.
E.42.6 Whether it be good, or whether it be evil, we will obey the voice of the LORD our God, to whom we send thee; that it may be well with us, when we obey the voice of the LORD our God.

α.42.7 Kah n$nihyeup mahche piogkukquinogok, wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaónuk Jeremiah.
E.42.7 And it came to pass after ten days, that the word of the LORD came unto Jeremiah.

α.42.8 Neit wehkomau Johananoh wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah kenauwamee mugquompaog, neh weechayeumukqutcheh, kah wame missinninnuog wutch peississit pajeh masugkenuk.
E.42.8 Then called he Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces which were with him, and all the people from the least even to the greatest,

α.42.9 Kah nah wuttinuh, yeu wussin Lord um-Manitt8moh Israel, noh ánano8seógkup, kupponamunat k8wehquetumo8ongan8 [ú]t anaquabit.
E.42.9 And said unto them, Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel, unto whom ye sent me to present your supplication before him;

α.42.10 Ash yeu pumappeóg ohkeit, neit k8wekikónunumw8, kah matta ken8kinin8mw8, kah kutohteuhkonunumw8, kah matta kuppohqunun8mw8, newutche nutáuskoiantam wutche machuk ne anhén[n]óg.
E.42.10 If ye will still abide in this land, then will I build you, and not pull you down, and I will plant you, and not pluck you up: for I repent me of the evil that I have done unto you.

α.42.11 Wabesuonúhteok Babylone ketass8t, noh quoshog, noh wabesuonúhteogk wussin Jehovah, newutche k8weetómunumw8 k8wadchanunaóont, kah kuppohquohwhununnaóont wutch wunnutcheganit.
E.42.11 Be not afraid of the king of Babylon, of whom ye are afraid; be not afraid of him, saith the LORD: for I am with you to save you, and to deliver you from his hand.

α.42.12 Kah kummonanumunumw8, onk woh kummonánumukou, onk woh kukqushkeáhik8 en nehenwonche kutohtkeout,
E.42.12 And I will shew mercies unto you, that he may have mercy upon you, and cause you to return to your own land.

α.42.13 Qut unn8waog matta n8tohtéumun yeu ohkeit, kah matta n8swehtam8mun 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8.
E.42.13 But if ye say, We will not dwell in this land, neither obey the voice of the LORD your God,

α.42.14 N8waog, matchaog, qut nutômun ohkeit Egypt, uttoh mo adt naum8og mattompog, kah matta nunn8tam8mun mishont8wae trumpet, kah matta pish nukkodtitteam8mun petukquneg, kah na nutáyinnean.
E.42.14 Saying, No; but we will go into the land of Egypt, where we shall see no war, nor hear the sound of the trumpet, nor have hunger of bread; and there will we dwell:

α.42.15 Kah yeuyeu newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau askqshéogish Judah, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, tohneit mamusse ponamok kuskesukooaṣh petukonat en Egypt na$ut keohteainneat.
E.42.15 And now therefore hear the word of the LORD, ye remnant of Judah; Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; If ye wholly set your faces to enter into Egypt, and go to sojourn there;

α.42.16 Neit pish n$nih, togkodteg ne quohtamóg, ne pish kummattan[ú]kqunneau ut ohkeit Egypt, kah mahshagquodt ne quohtamóg, pish môsogque asuhkongquneau ut Egypt, kah na pish kuttit nuppuneau.
E.42.16 Then it shall come to pass, that the sword, which ye feared, shall overtake you there in the land of Egypt, and the famine, whereof ye were afraid, shall follow close after you there in Egypt; and there ye shall die.

α.42.17 Ne pish wuttinniinneau wame nag anaquohtunkeg wuskesuk88aṣh ônat Egypt, na ut kéohteáinneat, nag pish nupwog nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, kah matta howan nag pish wusseksqshoh, asuh pohquohhamóh machuk ne nóhkenumauog.
E.42.17 So shall it be with all the men that set their faces to go into Egypt to sojourn there; they shall die by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence: and none of them shall remain or escape from the evil that I will bring upon them.

α.42.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, neane nummusquantamóonk kah nunnisquétuonk sókenumauoneau wadohkitcheg Jerusalem; ne ne nunnisquétuonk pish kussókenumonteaneau petutteaóg Egypt; kah kenaau pish kummattanumitteae utteamw8, kah kutchepshónitteamw8, kah kummatchenànumitteamw8 kah kutushpinanitteamw8, kah matta pish wonk yeu ayeuonk kenaum8uneau.
E.42.18 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; As mine anger and my fury hath been poured forth upon the inhabitants of Jerusalem; so shall my fury be poured forth upon you, when ye shall enter into Egypt: and ye shall be an execration, and an astonishment, and a curse, and a reproach; and ye shall see this place no more.

α.42.19 Jehovah n8wau papaume kenaau, woi kenaau sekqshaógish Judah, onteógk Egypt, pahke wahteau8k, kukquosháe amaumunnumw8 yeu kesukok.
E.42.19 The LORD hath said concerning you, O ye remnant of Judah; Go ye not into Egypt: know certainly that I have admonished you this day.

α.42.20 Newutche kuteiantoge ussemw8 kuttahh8wout án8néóg en Lord kum-Manitt8m8wóut, an8waog, peantamwanshinnean en Lordut núm-Manitt8munónut, kah neaunak wame ne Jehovah an8wadt, ne ne w[e]ahteauwáhinan, kah mos nutussenan.
E.42.20 For ye dissembled in your hearts, when ye sent me unto the LORD your God, saying, Pray for us unto the LORD our God; and according unto all that the LORD our God shall say, so declare unto us, and we will do it.

α.42.21 Kah yeuyeu yeu kesukok k8wahteauwáhenuneau, qut matta ken8swehtamomw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah kum-Manitt8mw8, asuh ne teag ne ann8sit en kuhhogkaóut.
E.42.21 And now I have this day declared it to you; but ye have not obeyed the voice of the LORD your God, nor any thing for the which he hath sent me unto you.

α.42.22 Newutche yeuyeu pahke wahteau8k, pish kenup[m]w8 nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahashagquodt, kah nashpe enninneaonk, ut ne ayeuonganit ne an kodtantamóg penuwohteainneat.
E.42.22 Now therefore know certainly that ye shall die by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence, in the place whither ye desire to go and to sojourn.

α.43.1 KAh n$nih, Jeremiah mahche ken8nont wame missinninnùh, wame ukkutt8wongaṣh Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh, wutche nish Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh an8teamwutcheh nah en, wame yeush kutt8wongaṣh
E.43.1 And it came to pass, that when Jeremiah had made an end of speaking unto all the people all the words of the LORD their God, for which the LORD their God had sent him to them, even all these words,

α.43.2 Neit Azariah wunnaumonuh Hoshajah, kah Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame pahtuánumwutcheg, nag keket8kaog unnáog Jeremiahoh, kuppann8wayim: Jehovah num$Manitt8mun, matta kutann8nuk8h n8wonat, onteógk Egypt na$ut kéohteaineat.
E.43.2 Then spake Azariah the son of Hoshaiah, and Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the proud men, saying unto Jeremiah, Thou speakest falsely: the LORD our God hath not sent thee to say, Go not into Egypt to sojourn there:

α.43.3 Qut Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah kenushquáh en kutáyeuuhkónukqunnanónut, ummagunat kuhhogkaunonash en wunnutchegan8óut Caldeansog, onk woh nag kenushikqunnónog kah kummissinóhkonukqunnanonut en Babylon.
E.43.3 But Baruch the son of Neriah setteth thee on against us, for to deliver us into the hand of the Chaldeans, that they might put us to death, and carry us away captives into Babylon.

α.43.4 Neit Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, kah wame missinninnúog matta n8swehtamóog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, wutohkinneat Judae ohkeit.
E.43.4 So Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces, and all the people, obeyed not the voice of the LORD, to dwell in the land of Judah.

α.43.5 Qut Johanan wunnaumonuh Kareah, kah wame kenauwamee mugquompaog, nag neemunáog wame askqushóncheg ut Judah, kah neg quashkécheg wutch wame wutohtimóinneat uttoh ann8kauut, ayinneat Judae ohkeit.
E.43.5 But Johanan the son of Kareah, and all the captains of the forces, took all the remnant of Judah, that were returned from all nations, whither they had been driven, to dwell in the land of Judah;

α.43.6 Wosketompaog, kah mittamwussissog, kah peississog, kah ketass8t wuttaunoh, kah nishnoh howan, neg Nebuzaradan askuhwheteáe mugquomp sequnnumauoncheh Gedaliahoh wunnaumonuh Ahikam, wunnaumonuh Shaphan, kah Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, kah Baruch wunnaumonuh Neriah.
E.43.6 Even men, and women, and children, and the king's daughters, and every person that Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard had left with Gedaliah the son of Ahikam the son of Shaphan, and Jeremiah the prophet, and Baruch the son of Neriah.

α.43.7 Neit peyaog ohkeit Egypt, newutche matta n8swehtam8og 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah: neit peyaog Taphnes.
E.43.7 So they came into the land of Egypt: for they obeyed not the voice of the LORD: thus came they even to Tahpanhes.

α.43.8 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Jeremiah ut Taphnes, n8wau,
E.43.8 Then came the word of the LORD unto Jeremiah in Tahpanhes, saying,

α.43.9 Nemunush mogke qussukquanash ut kenutcheganit, kah niṣh adtahtaaṣh ut man8skut ut ahhutchikkoswut bricksog, ne ahhut petutteamuk Pharaoh wek ut Taphnes, ut anaquabhettit Judae wosketompaog:
E.43.9 Take great stones in thine hand, and hide them in the clay in the brickkiln, which is at the entry of Pharaoh's house in Tahpanhes, in the sight of the men of Judah;

α.43.10 Kah nag us, yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um$Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nutann8team, kah nunneemun Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, nuttinneum, kah nukquenahtóh wutappuonk ut woskeche yeush qussukquanaṣh nish adtahtauoniṣh, kah ne woskeche piṣh wuttit sepágenumun wussontimóe kommuk.
E.43.10 And say unto them, Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will send and take Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon, my servant, and will set his throne upon these stones that I have hid; and he shall spread his royal pavilion over them.

α.43.11 Kah peyont piṣh togkodtam Egypte ohke: neg woh napukeg en nuppunnat, neg woh masinácheg en missinnáinneat, neg woh wutch togkodteg en togkodteganit.
E.43.11 And when he cometh, he shall smite the land of Egypt, and deliver such as are for death to death; and such as are for captivity to captivity; and such as are for the sword to the sword.

α.43.12 Kah nunn[a]shqunánum n8teau en wekuóut Egypte manitt8og, kah niṣh piṣh wutchikkossumunaṣh, kah piṣh ummissinóhkonuh, kah pish hogk8 Egypte ohke, onatuh nanaushepsaen ágqut wuthogk8onk, kah na 8ch piṣh wunohteáe sohhamun.
E.43.12 And I will kindle a fire in the houses of the gods of Egypt; and he shall burn them, and carry them away captives: and he shall array himself with the land of Egypt, as a shepherd putteth on his garment; and he shall go forth from thence in peace.

α.43.13 Kah piṣh wonk pokshanáog Bethshemeshe unneukontunkanog, ne ohtag Egypte ohkeit, kah wek8óash um-manitt8m8uh Egyptiansog pish wutchikkossumunaṣh n8taut.
E.43.13 He shall break also the images of Bethshemesh, that is in the land of Egypt; and the houses of the gods of the Egyptians shall he burn with fire.

α.44.1 WUttinn8waonk ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah papaume wame Jewsog neg wadohkitcheg Egypte ohke, neg wadohkitcheg Migdol, kah Tahpanhes, kah Noph, kah ut wutohkeit Pathros, n8wau,
E.44.1 The word that came to Jeremiah concerning all the Jews which dwell in the land of Egypt, which dwell at Migdol, and at Tahpanhes, and at Noph, and in the country of Pathros, saying,

α.44.2 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kenaumw8 wame machuk ne án nuhkinnumauog Jerusalem, kah wame Judae keitotanéhtu: kah kusseh yeu kesukok touushin, kah matta howan na 8tohkéin.
E.44.2 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Ye have seen all the evil that I have brought upon Jerusalem, and upon all the cities of Judah; and, behold, this day they are a desolation, and no man dwelleth therein,

α.44.3 Newutche ummatcheseonganooash niṣh asehettichish, numm8m8sqhikqunnaóut, newutche chikossumauópanneg weetemungquok wuttinneumuhkauónat onkatogig manitt8og, neh matta waheáhettegeh matta nag, asuh kenaau, asuh k8sh8woog.
E.44.3 Because of their wickedness which they have committed to provoke me to anger, in that they went to burn incense, and to serve other gods, whom they knew not, neither they, ye, nor your fathers.

α.44.4 Qut nutann8nomp en kuhho[g]kaóut wame quoshodtumwae nuttinneumog, nompoae omohkeon, kah ann8nog, nussip, ussehteogk ne nishkeneunkquok ne sekeneam.
E.44.4 Howbeit I sent unto you all my servants the prophets, rising early and sending them, saying, Oh, do not this abominable thing that I hate.

α.44.5 Qut nag matta n8tamoog, kah matta ahchusittam8og, quinnuppenat wutch ummatcheseongan8óut, matta chikohsumauónat weetemungquok onkatogig manittoog.
E.44.5 But they hearkened not, nor inclined their ear to turn from their wickedness, to burn no incense unto other gods.

α.44.6 Newaj nunnishquetuonk kah nummusquantamoonk sohkenumomp kah nasqunop ut Judae keitotanáhtu, kah Jerusalem[e] toumáogquehtu, kah niṣh mohchim8ash kah touishineash neane yeu kesukok.
E.44.6 Wherefore my fury and mine anger was poured forth, and was kindled in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem; and they are wasted and desolate, as at this day.

α.44.7 Newutche yeuyeu yeu wussin Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteáog, um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, tohwaj yeu unayeúhkone matchenéheog kukketeahogkôn8, tummehtahwhonat wutche kuhhogkaout wosketomp kah mittamwossis, mukkies kah n8nuk wutch Judah, matta kussequnitteaunnaóut.
E.44.7 Therefore now thus saith the LORD, the God of hosts, the God of Israel; Wherefore commit ye this great evil against your souls, to cut off from you man and woman, child and suckling, out of Judah, to leave you none to remain;

α.44.8 Newutche kumm8m8sqhimw8, nashpe kenutchegane anakausuwonganooash, châgossumauog weetemungkquok onkatogig manitt8og, ut ohkeit Egypt, uttoh a[ó]og kutayeinneaóut, onk woh kuttummetahwhomw8 kuhhogkaoog, onk woh kummattanumitteamw8, kah kukkehkômitteamw8 ut kenugke wame ohkee wutohtimóneáhtu.
E.44.8 In that ye provoke me unto wrath with the works of your hands, burning incense unto other gods in the land of Egypt, whither ye be gone to dwell, that ye might cut yourselves off, and that ye might be a curse and a reproach among all the nations of the earth?

α.44.9 Sun k8wananittamw8 ummatchetowongan8 k8sh8[ô]og, kah ummatchetowongan8 Judae ketass8tamwog kah ummittamwuss8uh ummatchetowongan8, kah nehenwonche kummatchetowongan8, kah kummittamwuss8oog ummatchetowongan8, niṣh aséhetticheh ut Judae ohkit, kah ut Jerusaleme toumáogquehtu.
E.44.9 Have ye forgotten the wickedness of your fathers, and the wickedness of the kings of Judah, and the wickedness of their wives, and your own wickedness, and the wickedness of your wives, which they have committed in the land of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem?

α.44.10 Nag matta pohqueteahá8og pajeh yeu kesukok, kah matta wabeséog, kah matta pomushaóntam8og nuttinnaumatuonk, kah nukkuhk8waongash niṣh ponamónish anaquabeóg kah anaqu[a]hettit k8sh8óog.
E.44.10 They are not humbled even unto this day, neither have they feared, nor walked in my law, nor in my statutes, that I set before you and before your fathers.

α.44.11 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, kutayeuuhkonittue ponamauonumw8 nuskesuk wutche machuk, kah tummetahwhonat wame Judah.
E.44.11 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will set my face against you for evil, and to cut off all Judah.

α.44.12 Kah nunneemun ashqshoncheg ut Judah, neg anaquoushácheg Egypt na$ut penuwohteáinneat, kah nag piṣh wame mohtuppaéog, kah penushaog ut ohkit Egypt: nag piṣh mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, kah nag piṣh nupwog wutch peississut pajeh masugkenut, nashpe togkodteg kah nashpe mahshagquodt kah nag piṣh mattanittuonk, chepshaonk, kah matánum8[utt]uonk, kah ushpunadtuonk.
E.44.12 And I will take the remnant of Judah, that have set their faces to go into the land of Egypt to sojourn there, and they shall all be consumed, and fall in the land of Egypt; they shall even be consumed by the sword and by the famine: they shall die, from the least even unto the greatest, by the sword and by the famine: and they shall be an execration, and an astonishment, and a curse, and a reproach.

α.44.13 Newutche nag nussasamatahwhóog wadohkiitcheg Egypte ohkeit, neane sasamatahwhogkup Jerusalem nashpe togkodteg, nashpe mahshagquodt kah nashpe enninneaonk.
E.44.13 For I will punish them that dwell in the land of Egypt, as I have punished Jerusalem, by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence:

α.44.14 Newaj matta howan ashqshoncheg ut Judah neg aóncheg Egypte ohkeit, na$ut n8sausinneat, piṣh pohquohhamm8 asuh sekqshó[o]u, woh nag qushkenóont en Judae ohkeit, ne kodtantamw[é]hettit, en qushkénat, na ayinneat newutch matta piṣh howan qushkeu, qut neg pohquohhogig.
E.44.14 So that none of the remnant of Judah, which are gone into the land of Egypt to sojourn there, shall escape or remain, that they should return into the land of Judah, to the which they have a desire to return to dwell there: for none shall return but such as shall escape.

α.44.15 Neit wame wosketompaog neg wáheoncheg ummittamwuss8oh chikossumau[á]og weetemungquok onkatogeh manitt8h, kah wame mittamwussissog neg na kishke neepauticheg, mattaánukeg, wame missinninnúog neg wadohkitcheg Egypt, ut Pathros, nag namp8hamauâog Jeremiahoh, n8wau,
E.44.15 Then all the men which knew that their wives had burned incense unto other gods, and all the women that stood by, a great multitude, even all the people that dwelt in the land of Egypt, in Pathros, answered Jeremiah, saying,

α.44.16 Kutt8onk ne áseog ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah, matta kukkuhkeitauunómun.
E.44.16 As for the word that thou hast spoken unto us in the name of the LORD, we will not hearken unto thee.

α.44.17 Qut wunnamuhkut pish nutussenan uttoh án sohham8m8uk wutch nutt8nunónut chikkohsumauónat weetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sókenumauónat wuttattamoe sephausuongaṣh, ne mahche usséog, nenawun kah n8shunónog: nukketass8timómunónog kah nussontimomunonog ut Judae keitotanahtu, kah Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu: newutche neit nummishe meechumumunónup kah n8niimunónup, kah matta naum8mun machuk.
E.44.17 But we will certainly do whatsoever thing goeth forth out of our own mouth, to burn incense unto the queen of heaven, and to pour out drink offerings unto her, as we have done, we, and our fathers, our kings, and our princes, in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem: for then had we plenty of victuals, and were well, and saw no evil.

α.44.18 Qut nádteuh ahque chikossumauogkut weetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sókenumauonat wuttattamwe mag8ongaṣh, nukquenauhikkumun wame teanteaquassinish, kah nummahche mohchimumun nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt.
E.44.18 But since we left off to burn incense to the queen of heaven, and to pour out drink offerings unto her, we have wanted all things, and have been consumed by the sword and by the famine.

α.44.19 Kah chôgossumauógut weetemungquok kesukque kuhchi[s]sonkusq, kah sokenumauogkut wuttattamoe mag8ongash, sun nuttáyimauóunónus petukqunegaṣh wowussumónat, kah sun nussokanumauóunónus wuttattamoe mag8ongash ne toh ut matta násukôunonog?
E.44.19 And when we burned incense to the queen of heaven, and poured out drink offerings unto her, did we make her cakes to worship her, and pour out drink offerings unto her, without our men?

α.44.20 Neit Jeremiah unnau wame missinninnúh, wosketompuh, kah mittamwossissoh, kah wame missinnúh neh namp8hamunutcheh, n8wau,
E.44.20 Then Jeremiah said unto all the people, to the men, and to the women, and to all the people which had given him that answer, saying,

α.44.21 Weetemungquok ne chôgossumogkup, ut Judae keitotanahtu, kah ut Jerusaleme toumaogquehtu kenaau, kah kussontim8m8oog, kah ohkee missinninnúog, sunnummatta Jehovah ummequanumuh, kah sunnummatta peyomunóus ut wuttenantam8onganit?
E.44.21 The incense that ye burned in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem, ye, and your fathers, your kings, and your princes, and the people of the land, did not the LORD remember them, and came it not into his mind?

α.44.22 Newaj Jehovah matta sepe kehchithog, wutche machuk kutusseongan8, kah wutche ne unkquánumukquok ne aséog: newaj touushik kutohtu, kah chepshaonganu8, kah matanittuonganu8, matta wutohkéin, neane yeu kesukok.
E.44.22 So that the LORD could no longer bear, because of the evil of your doings, and because of the abominations which ye have committed; therefore is your land a desolation, and an astonishment, and a curse, without an inhabitant, as at this day.

α.44.23 Newutche kutchikkossumw8 weetemungquok, newutche kummatcheneheomw8 Jehovah, kah matta ken8swetamomw8 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, kah matta kuppomushomw8 wuttinna[u]matuonganit, kah matta ukkuhk8waonganit, asuh 8wauwaonganit, newaj yeu machuk peyaonukqueóg, neane yeu kesukok.
E.44.23 Because ye have burned incense, and because ye have sinned against the LORD, and have not obeyed the voice of the LORD, nor walked in his law, nor in his statutes, nor in his testimonies; therefore this evil is happened unto you, as at this day.

α.44.24 Nano Jeremiah unnau wame missinninnúh, kah wame mittamwussissoh: n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame Judah neg apitcheg ohkeit Egypt.
E.44.24 Moreover Jeremiah said unto all the people, and to all the women, Hear the word of the LORD, all Judah that are in the land of Egypt:

α.44.25 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuhteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, kenaau kah kummittamwuss8oog, naneeswe kussimw8 nashpe kutton8wout, kah kummahche usseneau nashpe kenutchegan8, kussimw8: wunnamuhkut nutussenan nukquoshomuwaonganunonaṣh, niṣh quoshoáogiṣh, chikohsumauonat wetemungquok kesukque kehchissonkusq, kah sokanumauónat wuttattamoe mag8ongaṣh: wunnamuhkut piṣh kuppahkodchehteomw8 kukquoshomuwaongan8oaṣh, kah wunnamuhkut piṣh kutussemw8 kukquoshomuonganooaṣh.
E.44.25 Thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, saying; Ye and your wives have both spoken with your mouths, and fulfilled with your hand, saying, We will surely perform our vows that we have vowed, to burn incense to the queen of heaven, and to pour out drink offerings unto her: ye will surely accomplish your vows, and surely perform your vows.

α.44.26 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, wame Judah neg wadohkitcheg Egypt ohkeit, kusseh, nutchadchekéyeuop nashpe nummishe wesuonk, wussin Lord, n8wesuonk matta piṣh wonk missohham8un ut wutt8nut, howae Judae wosketomp ut wame Egypte ohkeit, unn8wadt Jehovah Manit pomantam.
E.44.26 Therefore hear ye the word of the LORD, all Judah that dwell in the land of Egypt; Behold, I have sworn by my great name, saith the LORD, that my name shall no more be named in the mouth of any man of Judah in all the land of Egypt, saying, The Lord GOD liveth.

α.44.27 Kusseh, nag nutaskwhonóog wutche machuk, qut matta wanegik, kah wame Judae wosketompaog ut ohkeit Egypt, nag piṣh mahchim8og nashpe togkodteg, kah nashpe mahshagquodt, nô pajeh 8wohkukquossinunaóont[.]
E.44.27 Behold, I will watch over them for evil, and not for good: and all the men of Judah that are in the land of Egypt shall be consumed by the sword and by the famine, until there be an end of them.

α.44.28 Qut ogguhsikeg neg pohquohhogig togkodteg, nag pish qushkeog wut-Egypte ohkeit en Judae ohkeit: kah wame ashqshoncheg Judah neg aoncheg Egypt na$ut n8sausinneat, nag pish wa[h]teauog howan ukkutt8onk manuhkohtag, nukkutt8onk asuh nagumau.
E.44.28 Yet a small number that escape the sword shall return out of the land of Egypt into the land of Judah, and all the remnant of Judah, that are gone into the land of Egypt to sojourn there, shall know whose words shall stand, mine, or their's.

α.44.29 Kah yeu pish kukkehkinneasuongan8, wussin Jehovah, kussasamatahwhush yeu$ut ayeuonganit, onk woh k8wahteomw8, wunnamuhkut pish nuttinn8waonk, kummenuhtikkompauwehtunkquneau wutche machuk
E.44.29 And this shall be a sign unto you, saith the LORD, that I will punish you in this place, that ye may know that my words shall surely stand against you for evil:

α.44.30 Yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, Pharoh-Hophra Egypte ketass8t nuppon wunnutchegan8wout ummatwomoh, kah en wunnutchegan8out neg kodnushoncheg, neane mag8omp Zedechiah Judae ketass8t en wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzer Babylone ketass8t ummatwomoh noh kodnushomp.
E.44.30 Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will give Pharaohhophra king of Egypt into the hand of his enemies, and into the hand of them that seek his life; as I gave Zedekiah king of Judah into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, his enemy, and that sought his life.

α.45.1 WUttinn8waonk ne JEremiah quoshodtumwaen anont Baruchoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, mahche wâsukkuhh8k ut B8kut yeush wuttinn8waongash, wutch wutt8nut Jeremiah, ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t, n8wau,
E.45.1 The word that Jeremiah the prophet spake unto Baruch the son of Neriah, when he had written these words in a book at the mouth of Jeremiah, in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah, saying,

α.45.2 Jehovah um-Manitt8muh Israel yeu kuttugqun, woi Baruch.
E.45.2 Thus saith the LORD, the God of Israel, unto thee, O Baruch:

α.45.3 Kussip, yeuyeu missi nutonkapunaonk, newutche Lord k8tnehtau neuantam8onk en nutonkquanum8onganit, nussauunumup mahshanomweon, kah matta nunnampteo8 anwôsin8onk.
E.45.3 Thou didst say, Woe is me now! for the LORD hath added grief to my sorrow; I fainted in my sighing, and I find no rest.

α.45.4 Yeu woh kuttinnon, yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, ne ayimomp nuppohquenumun, kah ne ahketeaomp nuppohqunumun, yeu mamusse ohke.
E.45.4 Thus shalt thou say unto him, The LORD saith thus; Behold, that which I have built will I break down, and that which I have planted I will pluck up, even this whole land.

α.45.5 Kah kenatinneaham magogish? wutch kuhhog natiñeham8hkon: newutche kusseh, nunnuhkenumau machuk wame weyaus wussin J[é]hovah, qut kuppomantamoonk kuttinnumauunun wutch kuttohqunnumoonk ut wame ayeuonganéhtu uttoh aoan.
E.45.5 And seekest thou great things for thyself? seek them not: for, behold, I will bring evil upon all flesh, saith the LORD: but thy life will I give unto thee for a prey in all places whither thou goest.

α.46.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah, ne peyaonuk Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ayeuuhkonittue penuwohteaog.
E.46.1 The word of the LORD which came to Jeremiah the prophet against the Gentiles;

α.46.2 Ayeuuhkonittue Egypt ayeuuhkone ukkenauwameonk Pharoh$Necho Egypte ketass8t, noh ayeup kishke Euphratese sepuut, ut Carcemish, ne Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t togkodtogkup ut weyaue kodtum8mut Jehojakim wunnaumonuh Josiah Judae ketass8t.
E.46.2 Against Egypt, against the army of Pharaohnecho king of Egypt, which was by the river Euphrates in Carchemish, which Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon smote in the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah king of Judah.

α.46.3 Wunohto8k bukler kah ogqunneg, kah pas8tshagk ayeuwuttinneat.
E.46.3 Order ye the buckler and shield, and draw near to battle.

α.46.4 Wunneheuk horsesog, kuhkuhquegk naiyeumutteaogish, kah neepauwehtam8k nashpe kuppuhkukk8out ahohtagish, wunnehteogk qunuhtugquash, kah hogk8k brigandinsash.
E.46.4 Harness the horses; and get up, ye horsemen, and stand forth with your helmets; furbish the spears, and put on the brigandines.

α.46.5 Tohwutch nag nauog wutchepshonaoont, kah qushkeog? kah ummissugken8m8uh n8ketahwhoninneuh, kah kenuppe puhh8waog, kah matta ompamuhquaeog, newutche wabesuonk quinuppohtop, wussin Jehovah.
E.46.5 Wherefore have I seen them dismayed and turned away back? and their mighty ones are beaten down, and are fled apace, and look not back: for fear was round about, saith the LORD.

α.46.6 Neg kakenupshoncheg, wusseemohettekitch, kah mas[ú]gkenuk, pohquohhogitch, nag pish togkussittassunwog, kah penushaog nogque nanummiyeu, kishke Euphrates.
E.46.6 Let not the swift flee away, nor the mighty man escape; they shall stumble, and fall toward the north by the river Euphrates.

α.46.7 Howan yeuoh ogque kuhkuhquit tomogkonit noh wunnuppeash agque mamonchem88g sepuut?
E.46.7 Who is this that cometh up as a flood, whose waters are moved as the rivers?

α.46.8 Egypt ohque waapem8 tommogkonit, kah wunnuppemash ogque mamonchem8ash sepuut, kah n8wau, nukkuhkuhquem, nunnuhkuhkom ohke, nuppagwatoh keitotan kah wame neg na wadohkitcheg.
E.46.8 Egypt riseth up like a flood, and his waters are moved like the rivers; and he saith, I will go up, and will cover the earth; I will destroy the city and the inhabitants thereof.

α.46.9 Kuhkuhquegk kenaau horsesog, kah mishont8wag kenaau chariotsash, kah manuhkesitcheg sohhamwehettich, Ethiopiansog kah Lybiansog, neg nohtonukeg ogqunneg, kah Lydiansog neg nahtuhtunkig, kah p8tunkanoncheg ohtompeh.
E.46.9 Come up, ye horses; and rage, ye chariots; and let the mighty men come forth; the Ethiopians and the Libyans, that handle the shield; and the Lydians, that handle and bend the bow.

α.46.10 Newutche yeu ukkesukkodtum Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, ann8tôadtue kesukod onk woh ann8tauau ayeuuhkonukqutcheh: kah togkodteg pish mahchipp8m8, kah pish wamep8h[,] kah kogkeissippam8 nag 8sqheongan8: newutche Lord JEhovah ayeuteaunit sephausuonk ohtoou ut nanum ohkeit, ut kishke Euphratise sepuut.
E.46.10 For this is the day of the Lord GOD of hosts, a day of vengeance, that he may avenge him of his adversaries: and the sword shall devour, and it shall be satiate and made drunk with their blood: for the Lord GOD of hosts hath a sacrifice in the north country by the river Euphrates.

α.46.11 Kuhkuhquegk en Gilead, kah neemunuṣh balme woi penomp Egypte wuttaunin: tahn8che piṣh kutauwóhteam iyánaskéhtuaṣh: newutche matta piṣh keneetskesu.
E.46.11 Go up into Gilead, and take balm, O virgin, the daughter of Egypt: in vain shalt thou use many medicines; for thou shalt not be cured.

α.46.12 Wutohtimóneunk n8tamwog kutakodchuonk, kah kummauonk numwohtau ohkeit: newutche menuhkesuen ayeuuhkonittue togkussittassum8óneau masugkenutcheh, kah nag neeswe moeu kepshaog.
E.46.12 The nations have heard of thy shame, and thy cry hath filled the land: for the mighty man hath stumbled against the mighty, and they are fallen both together.

α.46.13 Wuttinn8waonk ne Jehovah ánont Jeremiahoh quoshodtumwaenúh, uttoh an piṣh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t peyont, kah togkodteg Egypte ohke.
E.46.13 The word that the LORD spake to Jeremiah the prophet, how Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon should come and smite the land of Egypt.

α.46.14 Wahteauwáhuwagk ut Egypt, kah n8tamwahuw[a]gk ut Migdol, kah n8tamwahuwag ut Noph, kah ut Taphnes, n8wagk, menehtikkompauṣh, kah nanashwiṣh, newutche tokkodteg piṣh mahchipp8 ut k8wohkôiyeumut.
E.46.14 Declare ye in Egypt, and publish in Migdol, and publish in Noph and in Tahpanhes: say ye, Stand fast, and prepare thee; for the sword shall devour round about thee.

α.46.15 Tohwaj kummenuhkesuenúmog chékuhwhut? matta neepau8og, newutche wutáma8hkauópuh Jehovah.
E.46.15 Why are thy valiant men swept away? they stood not, because the LORD did drive them.

α.46.16 Monaoh penusháheau, nux, papenush[a]ónittuog, kah n8waog, omohkek, kah wonk óntuh nehenwonche kummissinninnumunónut, kah ut keneetue ohkéunnonut wutch sunukkutchoh8wae togkodteganit.
E.46.16 He made many to fall, yea, one fell upon another: and they said, Arise, and let us go again to our own people, and to the land of our nativity, from the oppressing sword.

α.46.17 Nag na wuttit mauunáop, Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t noh webe wuttauatonkqussuonk, noh paumuhkom kuhquttum8e ahquompi.
E.46.17 They did cry there, Pharaoh king of Egypt is but a noise; he hath passed the time appointed.

α.46.18 Pomantamon, wussin ketass8t noh ás8wesit Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnamuhkut neane Tabor ut kenugke wadchuuhkontu, kah neane Carmel kishke ketahhannit, ne piṣh wuttinne peyon.
E.46.18 As I live, saith the King, whose name is the LORD of hosts, Surely as Tabor is among the mountains, and as Carmel by the sea, so shall he come.

α.46.19 Woi ken wuttaunin áyean Egypt, tâpauwamish en missinnainneat, newutche Noph piṣh mahchim8, kah touwushin, matta wutohkéinneat.
E.46.19 O thou daughter dwelling in Egypt, furnish thyself to go into captivity: for Noph shall be waste and desolate without an inhabitant.

α.46.20 Egypt tatuppeyeu8og wunnetue heifer$ut, qut paguanuonk peyau: 8m88 nanummiyeu.
E.46.20 Egypt is like a very fair heifer, but destruction cometh; it cometh out of the north.

α.46.21 Kah wonk ann8nutcheg ut wunnashómut, nag tatuppeyeu8og wunnogque oxenat, newutche nag wonk qushkeog, kah m[ó]eu wussem8og, nag matta neepau8og, newutche uppaguanúe kesukkodtum8 nuhkuhkongquog, kah natauwahaongane ahquompi.
E.46.21 Also her hired men are in the midst of her like fatted bullocks; for they also are turned back, and are fled away together: they did not stand, because the day of their calamity was come upon them, and the time of their visitation.

α.46.22 Ne wuttauatonkqussuonk piṣh ohque monchem8 ask8kut: newutche nag piṣh moncheog weeche kenauwameonk, kah piṣh wutayeuuhkonittue uppeyaun[ó]uh nashpe togungaṣh, kah pogkomshaenúog.
E.46.22 The voice thereof shall go like a serpent; for they shall march with an army, and come against her with axes, as hewers of wood.

α.46.23 Nag piṣh tummehtamwog wuttouohkomuk8 wussin Jehovah, tohkônogque woh mo pannuppadtinneuhkóntam8un, newutche nag ánuánwog onk neg chantsampsog, kah ahantanwog.
E.46.23 They shall cut down her forest, saith the LORD, though it cannot be searched; because they are more than the grasshoppers, and are innumerable.

α.46.24 Egypte wuttaunin piṣh chepshau, noh piṣh ponau ut wunnutchegan8out nanummiyeue missinninnuog.
E.46.24 The daughter of Egypt shall be confounded; she shall be delivered into the hand of the people of the north.

α.46.25 Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, n8wau, kusseh, nussasamatoh mataánukeg No, kah Pharaoh, kah Egypt, weeche um-manitt8m8uh, kah ukketass8tam8m8uh, Pharaoh kah wame neh pabuhtanumukqutche.
E.46.25 The LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, saith; Behold, I will punish the multitude of No, and Pharaoh, and Egypt, with their gods, and their kings; even Pharaoh, and all them that trust in him:

α.46.26 Kah nag nummagunununk ut wunnutchegan8out neg kodnushoncheg, kah ut wunnutcheganit Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t, kah ut wunnutchegan8out wuttinneumoh, kah ompetak piṣh wutohkim, neane nôadt wussin Jehovah.
E.46.26 And I will deliver them into the hand of those that seek their lives, and into the hand of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, and into the hand of his servants: and afterward it shall be inhabited, as in the days of old, saith the LORD.

α.46.27 Qut wabeséhkon, ken woi nuttinneum Jakob, kah chepshuhkon woi Israel, newutche kusseh, k8wadchāsh wutche n8adtit, kah k8skannem wutch ummissinnáe ohkéyeuóut, kah Jakob piṣh qushkeu, kah piṣh anwôsin, kah mánunniyeu, kah matta piṣh howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
E.46.27 But fear not thou, O my servant Jacob, and be not dismayed, O Israel: for, behold, I will save thee from afar off, and thy seed from the land of their captivity; and Jacob shall return, and be in rest and at ease, and none shall make him afraid.

α.46.28 Wabesehkon, woi Jakob nuttinneum wussin Jehovah, newutche k8weetomsh, newutche n8wohkukquossum wame wutohtimoneash uttoh ann8hkauun, qut matta ken kuppapaquanne wohkukquossumunn8, qut quttuh[h]am8e kussasamatoush onch matta kummamusse mat sasamatahwhun8.
E.46.28 Fear thou not, O Jacob my servant, saith the LORD: for I am with thee; for I will make a full end of all the nations whither I have driven thee: but I will not make a full end of thee, but correct thee in measure; yet will I not leave thee wholly unpunished.

α.47.1 WUttinn8waonk Jehovah ne pauhonukqut Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, ayeuuhkonittue Philistiansog, asquam Pharaoh togkomunk Gaza.
