E.47.1 The word of the LORD that came to Jeremiah the prophet against the Philistines, before that Pharaoh smote Gaza.

α.47.2 Yeu wussin Lord, kusseh, nippeash waapém8aṣh wutch nanummiyeu, kah niṣh piṣh anúchuwáne tommogkon, kah piṣh anúchuan ohke, kah wame na na ohtag keitotan kah neg na wadohkitcheg: neit piṣh wosketompaog mauog, kah wadohkitcheg ohkeit pish 8n8og.
E.47.2 Thus saith the LORD; Behold, waters rise up out of the north, and shall be an overflowing flood, and shall overflow the land, and all that is therein; the city, and them that dwell therein: then the men shall cry, and all the inhabitants of the land shall howl.

α.47.3 Wadtauatongqussinit wúhkass8oh menuhke wut-horsesumoh, kah kogunkshik wut-chariotsumash, kah téqunum8m8uk 8wheelumash, wut8shimau matta piṣh ompamuhquaéhtauau wunneechanuh wutche n8chumwiyeuut wunnutchegaṣh.
E.47.3 At the noise of the stamping of the hoofs of his strong horses, at the rushing of his chariots, and at the rumbling of his wheels, the fathers shall not look back to their children for feebleness of hands;

α.47.4 Newutche kesukod peyaum8 matcheheonaoont wame Philistiansog, kah tummehtahwhonat wutch Tyrus, kah Zidon, nish$noh anninnohsuen noh sekqshont: newutche Jehovah pish matcheheau Philistiansoh, wutusk[q]shaongan8 Caphtore wutohtimoin.
E.47.4 Because of the day that cometh to spoil all the Philistines, and to cut off from Tyrus and Zidon every helper that remaineth: for the LORD will spoil the Philistines, the remnant of the country of Caphtor.

α.47.5 M8sontuppaonk nuhkuhkom Gaza: Ashkalon tummetahwhou, weeche 8nouhkoiyeue askqshonutcheh: toh utt8ch pish kuttummetah kuhhog?
E.47.5 Baldness is come upon Gaza; Ashkelon is cut off with the remnant of their valley: how long wilt thou cut thyself?

α.47.6 Woi ken wuttogkodtegoh Jehovah, toh utt8che pish kutchonchequnap? pechish pechehquogkunganit, anwôsish kah chequnapsh.
E.47.6 O thou sword of the LORD, how long will it be ere thou be quiet? put up thyself into thy scabbard, rest, and be still.

α.47.7 Uttoh woh en chequnohteau, newutche Jehovah ummechumuhkontamun ayeuuhkone Ashkelon, kah ayeuuhkone ketahhanne unnunohkomuk? na wuttit kukquttumun.
E.47.7 How can it be quiet, seeing the LORD hath given it a charge against Ashkelon, and against the sea shore? there hath he appointed it.

α.48.1 AYeuuhkone Moab yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel missi wutonkapunaonk Nebo newutche matchehteauun: Kirjathaim chepshaum8, kah sohkomun: Misgab chepshaum8 kah quequena[u]onum8m8.
E.48.1 Against Moab thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Woe unto Nebo! for it is spoiled: Kiriathaim is confounded and taken: Misgab is confounded and dismayed.

α.48.2 Matta pish wonk waeenomoun Moab, ut Heshbon wutayeuuhkonittue natwontammontamunneau machuk: peyunk tummehthamuttuh, matta wutohtimoinneayeu8 ut ken wonk pish kuttummetahwhit, woi Madmen, togkoteg pish k8naumatuhkunk.
E.48.2 There shall be no more praise of Moab: in Heshbon they have devised evil against it; come, and let us cut it off from being a nation. Also thou shalt be cut down, O Madmen; the sword shall pursue thee.

α.48.3 Maue wadtauatonkqussuonk wtuch Horonaim, mukk8kinnuwaonk, kah mishe pagwanuonk.
E.48.3 A voice of crying shall be from Horonaim, spoiling and great destruction.

α.48.4 Moab pagwanau, uppeissesumoh n8tamwahuwon ummauongan8.
E.48.4 Moab is destroyed; her little ones have caused a cry to be heard.

α.48.5 Newutche ahhut kuhkuhquemuk Luhith maue mauonk kuhkuhquem8: newutche ahhut w8mussimuk Horonaim, matwaog n8tamwog pagwunue mauonk.
E.48.5 For in the going up of Luhith continual weeping shall go up; for in the going down of Horonaim the enemies have heard a cry of destruction.

α.48.6 Wusseem8k, pohquohwuttau8k kuppomantam8ongan8, ogqueneunkqussek poskissuwontugqut tou$ohkomukqut.
E.48.6 Flee, save your lives, and be like the heath in the wilderness.

α.48.7 Newutche newaj pabuhtantaman kutanakausuongash, kah kenompak8unash, ken wonk pish kuttogquinit, Chemosh pish sohham en missinnainneat weeche wussephausueneumoh, kah wussontimomoh moeu.
E.48.7 For because thou hast trusted in thy works and in thy treasures, thou shalt also be taken: and Chemosh shall go forth into captivity with his priests and his princes together.

α.48.8 Kah woskehuwaenin piṣh nuhkuhkom nishnoh keitotan, kah matta otan piṣh pohquohham8mun8; 8nóuhkôi wonk piṣh paguanum8, kah mukoshqut piṣh pagwatauun, ne an8wop Jehovah.
E.48.8 And the spoiler shall come upon every city, and no city shall escape: the valley also shall perish, and the plain shall be destroyed, as the LORD hath spoken.

α.48.9 Wunnuppawhunuhkok Moab onk woh pt8wu, kah monchasseau, newutche ukkeitotanaṣh piṣh touishinneash, matta howan wutayeineat.
E.48.9 Give wings unto Moab, that it may flee and get away: for the cities thereof shall be desolate, without any to dwell therein.

α.48.10 Matánumunach noh mehshane usseit wutanakausuonk Jehovah: kah matan[ú]munach noh kohkôunuk wuttogkodteg wutch wusqueheonganit.
E.48.10 Cursed be he that doeth the work of the LORD deceitfully, and cursed be he that keepeth back his sword from blood.

α.48.11 Moab manunaiyeup wutch wuskenúuneat, áhtoteapáshitteau wul-leesum, kah matta wuttuhhòntsu sequnnum8un en wishquadt, kah matta missinoou, newaj wuttishpukqussuonk ash pumohtunk, kah wuttussumunkqussuonk matta ôs8wemun8.
E.48.11 Moab hath been at ease from his youth, and he hath settled on his lees, and hath not been emptied from vessel to vessel, neither hath he gone into captivity: therefore his taste remained in him, and his scent is not changed.

α.48.12 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8 wussin Lord, negonshhúam en wuhhogkat kogkeompoh, nag piṣh ukkogkéompohéouh, kah nag piṣh sequnnumwog 8wishquaṣh, kah piṣh soquttahhamwog 8wishquaṣh.
E.48.12 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will send unto him wanderers, that shall cause him to wander, and shall empty his vessels, and break their bottles.

α.48.13 Kah Moab akodchuwonau Chemoṣh, neane Israelle wek akodchuwontogkup Bethel uppabahtantamoonk.
E.48.13 And Moab shall be ashamed of Chemosh, as the house of Israel was ashamed of Bethel their confidence.

α.48.14 Tohwaj n8waog, nenawun nummissugkénimun kah nummenuhkesimun en ayeú[h]konat.
E.48.14 How say ye, We are mighty and strong men for the war?

α.48.15 Moab matcheheau, kah kuhkuhqueu wutch ukkeitotanáhtu, kah uppepénamwe wuskeneumoh womsuog en pagwanittiñeat, n8wau ketass8t, noh [á]s8wesit, Jehovah ayeuhteaunit.
E.48.15 Moab is spoiled, and gone up out of her cities, and his chosen young men are gone down to the slaughter, saith the King, whose name is the LORD of hosts.

α.48.16 Wutunkquanumoonk Moab pas8cheyeu8, kah wutonkapunaonk kenupshaum8.
E.48.16 The calamity of Moab is near to come, and his affliction hasteth fast.

α.48.17 Wame kenaau weenuhkauógiṣh mauunitteaunshúk, kah wame kenaau wahteauógiṣh 8wesuonk, n8wak, uttoh en menuhke anwohhou poksheau, kah wunnegenne pogkommunk.
E.48.17 All ye that are about him, bemoan him; and all ye that know his name, say, How is the strong staff broken, and the beautiful rod!

α.48.18 Ken wuttaunin áyean Dibon womsish wutch kussohsum8onganit, kah kunkutt8n8e appish: newutch noh matcheneheont Moaboh piṣh kenuhkuhkunk, kah noh piṣh pagwatau k8wonkon8sinaṣh.
E.48.18 Thou daughter that dost inhabit Dibon, come down from thy glory, and sit in thirst; for the spoiler of Moab shall come upon thee, and he shall destroy thy strong holds.

α.48.19 Woi ken wadohkean Aroer, neepaush kishke mayut, kah askuhwheteaṣh, nat8tomau noh waseemuk, kah noh pohquohhuk, toh mahche n$nih?
E.48.19 O inhabitant of Aroer, stand by the way, and espy; ask him that fleeth, and her that escapeth, and say, What is done?

α.48.20 Moab quequenauánum8 newutche pohquetahwhôu; 8n8k kah mau8k, unnok ut Arnon, Moab matcheheau.
E.48.20 Moab is confounded; for it is broken down: howl and cry; tell ye it in Arnon, that Moab is spoiled,

α.48.21 Kah wussittumoonk nuhkuhkom mukoshqutáe wutohtimóin, ut Holon, kah ut Jahazah, kah ut Mephaath,
E.48.21 And judgment is come upon the plain country; upon Holon, and upon Jahazah, and upon Mephaath,

α.48.22 Kah ut Dibon, kah ut Nebo, kah ut Beth$diblithaim.
E.48.22 And upon Dibon, and upon Nebo, and upon Bethdiblathaim,

α.48.23 Kah ut Kirjathaim, kah ut Beth[-]gamul, kah ut Beth-meon,
E.48.23 And upon Kiriathaim, and upon Bethgamul, and upon Bethmeon,

α.48.24 Kah ut Kirjoth, kah ut Bozrah, kah ut wame Moabe keitotanahtu, noóhkish kah pás8giṣh
E.48.24 And upon Kerioth, and upon Bozrah, and upon all the cities of the land of Moab, far or near.

α.48.25 Wutaskonoh Moab tummetahwhôu, kah 8hpit pohquetahhamun wussin Jehovah.
E.48.25 The horn of Moab is cut off, and his arm is broken, saith the LORD.

α.48.26 Kogkeissippamwéheúk, newutche mishehheau wuhhogkuh ayeuhkonónat Jehovah; Moab wonk piṣh ôômeu ummenádtam8onk, kah noh wonk piṣh ahanehtauôu.
E.48.26 Make ye him drunken: for he magnified himself against the LORD: Moab also shall wallow in his vomit, and he also shall be in derision.

α.48.27 Newutche sunnummatta Israel kutáhanehtauómus? sun noh nameheous kenugke komm8towanúut? newutche nadteuh weadtimadt, kukquequeshomp wutche wekontam8onk.
E.48.27 For was not Israel a derision unto thee? was he found among thieves?  for since thou spakest of him, thou skippedst for joy.

α.48.28 Woi kenaau wadohkéogiṣh Moab, nukkodtum8k keitotanaṣh, kah ayégk qussukquannéhtu, kah ogqueneunkqussek wuskuhwhununáut, noh ádtanadsháteadt sussippôeu wônogquehtu.
E.48.28 O ye that dwell in Moab, leave the cities, and dwell in the rock, and be like the dove that maketh her nest in the sides of the hole's mouth.

α.48.29 Nunn8tamumun[ó]nup uppehtuanum[o]onk Moab (noh mishe pittuánum8) ukqunnunkquanumoonk ummish[á]numoonk, kah uppehtuánumoonk, kah ukqunuhqutteaháonk.
E.48.29 We have heard the pride of Moab, (he is exceeding proud) his loftiness, and his arrogancy, and his pride, and the haughtiness of his heart.

α.48.30 N8wahteoh ummusquanittam8onk wussin Lord, qut ne matta piṣh nano uppann8waongaṣh matta piṣh ussémun8.
E.48.30 I know his wrath, saith the LORD; but it shall not be so; his lies shall not so effect it.

α.48.31 Newaj 8n8wanshok Moab, kah nummishont8wam wutche wame Moab, nuttah mauunnitteauwánshau Kir-hereze wosketompaog.
E.48.31 Therefore will I howl for Moab, and I will cry out for all Moab; mine heart shall mourn for the men of Kirheres.

α.48.32 Woi Sibmahhe weenomwussippog, kummauunitteauwanshish nashpe Jazere mauonk: niṣh adtannegikish kuhhogkat naish qushkodteam8aṣh kehtahhannit, nash weeksqhineash Jazere kehtahhannit, matchehuwaen penushadtam keneepunne meechummuongaṣh, kah ut k8wenominne kepenum8onganit.
E.48.32 O vine of Sibmah, I will weep for thee with the weeping of Jazer: thy plants are gone over the sea, they reach even to the sea of Jazer: the spoiler is fallen upon thy summer fruits and upon thy vintage.

α.48.33 Kah weekontam8onk kah muskouantam8onk amaunumun wutch missegunne ohteuhkonit, kah wutch Moabe ohkeit, kah wine monteagwunnuóhtauóuun wutch wine-pressut, matta howan mishont8wae wuttahtaskuhkom8un, ummishont8ongan8 matta piṣh mishont8womun8.
E.48.33 And joy and gladness is taken from the plentiful field, and from the land of Moab, and I have caused wine to fail from the winepresses: none shall tread with shouting; their shouting shall be no shouting.

α.48.34 Wutch ummauonganit Heshbon wehque Elealeh, kah wehque Jahaz, mishont8waog wutch Zoar wehque Horonaim, ogque heifer nashwe kodtumwohkog: newutche wunnippem8aṣh Nimrim piṣh touishinneash.
E.48.34 From the cry of Heshbon even unto Elealeh, and even unto Jahaz, have they uttered their voice, from Zoar even unto Horonaim, as an heifer of three years old: for the waters also of Nimrim shall be desolate.

α.48.35 Nano, n8wohkukquossum ut Moab, wussin Jehovah, noh sephausit ut qunuhqui ayeuongan[e]htu, kah noh chôgossumauont weetemungquok, ummanitt8moh.
E.48.35 Moreover I will cause to cease in Moab, saith the LORD, him that offereth in the high places, and him that burneth incense to his gods.

α.48.36 Newaj piṣh nuttah ogque mishont8wag puhpekquónit, wutche Moab: kah nuttah piṣh ogque mishont8wau puhpequonit, wutche Kir-hereze wosketompahtu: newutch 8weenauwetuongash niṣh ohtunkish mahtshaaṣh.
E.48.36 Therefore mine heart shall sound for Moab like pipes, and mine heart shall sound like pipes for the men of Kirheres: because the riches that he hath gotten are perished.

α.48.37 Newutche nishnoh muhpuhkuk piṣh mukukki, kah nishnoh weeshitt8n m8sumun; ut wame menutcheganéhtu piṣh tannogkussim8onganú8, kah ut wame musseganit man8tionakinnú8.
E.48.37 For every head shall be bald, and every beard clipped: upon all the hands shall be cuttings, and upon the loins sackcloth.

α.48.38 Pish maumuttam8onganú8 mamusseu wame woskéche kommukquehtu Moab, kah ut toumaogquehtu: newutche nutogque pohquttoh Moab wishquadt, uttoh adt matta weekontam8onganin8k, wussin Jehovah.
E.48.38 There shall be lamentation generally upon all the housetops of Moab, and in the streets thereof: for I have broken Moab like a vessel wherein is no pleasure, saith the LORD.

α.48.39 Nag piṣh 8n8wog, uttoh en pohquetahhamun? uttoh en Moab uppisk ukquinnuppinnumun en akodchuonganit: nein pish Moab ahanéhtauon kah chepshaonou wame neg quánuppuhkauoncheg
E.48.39 They shall howl, saying, How is it broken down! how hath Moab turned the back with shame! so shall Moab be a derision and a dismaying to all them about him.

α.48.40 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, noh piṣh ogque pt8wu wompesikkuhquait, kah piṣh anue sephagkenau wunnuppewhunoh ut Moab.
E.48.40 For thus saith the LORD; Behold, he shall fly as an eagle, and shall spread his wings over Moab.

α.48.41 Kirjoth sohkomun, kah wonkon8sinash sohkomunaṣh: kah wuttahhou Moabe menuhkesuenuog piṣh tatuppeyeu8 mittamwussis wuttahhut, ut wutonkquommom8onganit.
E.48.41 Kerioth is taken, and the strong holds are surprised, and the mighty men's hearts in Moab at that day shall be as the heart of a woman in her pangs.

α.48.42 Kah Moab pish paguanau matta ummissinninnueneat, newutche noh ayeuuhkonittue misheheau wuhhogkuh Jehovah$ut.
E.48.42 And Moab shall be destroyed from being a people, because he hath magnified himself against the LORD.

α.48.43 Wabesuonk, kah passohtheg, kah ahpeh pish kenuhkuhkunk, woi wadohkean Moab wussin Jehovah.
E.48.43 Fear, and the pit, and the snare, shall be upon thee, O inhabitant of Moab, saith the LORD.

α.48.44 Noh wasemwut wutche wabesuonk petshau pass[o]theganit, kah noh kájeit wutch passohtheganit, pish puttahwho[u] ut appehhannit, newutche nunnuhkinnuamau, Moab natauwahae ukkodtum8m8 wussin Jehovah.
E.48.44 He that fleeth from the fear shall fall into the pit; and he that getteth up out of the pit shall be taken in the snare: for I will bring upon it, even upon Moab, the year of their visitation, saith the LORD.

α.48.45 Neg wasemwutcheg nepoog ut agwe Heshbonne onkauohtaut, newutche chekee usseonk, qut n8tau pish sohham8m8 wutch Heshbon, kah n8n8nau wutch nashaue Sihon, kah pish mahchipp8m8 wunnashinneum Moab, kah ukkodtantupp[ô]un8 wogkouitcheg.
E.48.45 They that fled stood under the shadow of Heshbon because of the force: but a fire shall come forth out of Heshbon, and a flame from the midst of Sihon, and shall devour the corner of Moab, and the crown of the head of the tumultuous ones.

α.48.46 Missi kutonkapunaonk woi Moab, ummissinninnumoh Chemosh pagwanuog: kah kenaumonuh missinohkonunk kah kuttaunog missinoowog.
E.48.46 Woe be unto thee, O Moab! the people of Chemosh perisheth: for thy sons are taken captives, and thy daughters captives.

α.48.47 Qut wonk nukquehchuwuttoh ummissinooonk Moab ut ogkomae kesuko[k]tut wussin Lord yeu sohke wussumon Moab.
E.48.47 Yet will I bring again the captivity of Moab in the latter days, saith the LORD. Thus far is the judgment of Moab.

α.49.1 PApaume Ammonitsog yeu wussin Jehovah, Israel sun mo wunnaumoniyeu? sun mo howane nompenukkou? tohwhuech neit ukketass8tamom8uh nompenumunit Gad, kah ummissinninnumoh ayeuoh wutotanahtu?
E.49.1 Concerning the Ammonites, thus saith the LORD; Hath Israel no sons?  hath he no heir? why then doth their king inherit Gad, and his people dwell in his cities?

α.49.2 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtash peyaum8 wussin Jehovah n8tamwahuwam mattompagwe wadtauatonkqussuonk ut Rahab ut Ammonitsut, kah ne pish touushinne numwunkquau, kah wuttaunoh pish chikkossuoh ut n8taut: neit pish Israel nompenau neh nompinukqutcheh wussin Jehovah.
E.49.2 Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will cause an alarm of war to be heard in Rabbah of the Ammonites; and it shall be a desolate heap, and her daughters shall be burned with fire: then shall Israel be heir unto them that were his heirs, saith the LORD.

α.49.3 OOnsh woi Heshnon, newutche Ai matchitteauun, mau8k kenaau wuttaun8oh Rabbah, puttukquobpissuwontam8k man8tionak: maumuttam8k, kah ahahsukqueu ussishunk pum̃enutunkanehtu: newutche ukketass8tam8m8uh pish missino8oh, wussephausueneumoh kah wussontimomoh moeu.
E.49.3 Howl, O Heshbon, for Ai is spoiled: cry, ye daughters of Rabbah, gird you with sackcloth; lament, and run to and fro by the hedges; for their king shall go into captivity, and his priests and his princes together.

α.49.4 Tohwutch waeenowaan ut 8nouhkôiyeutu, kuttommogkonne 8nouhkoiyeum, woi as8epósue wuttaunin: noh pabahta[n]tog wunnompak8unash, n8wau, howan woh pauhausit?
E.49.4 Wherefore gloriest thou in the valleys, thy flowing valley, O backsliding daughter? that trusted in her treasures, saying, Who shall come unto me?

α.49.5 Kusseh, kenuhkenumoush wabesuonk wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wutch wame yeug weenuhkongqueaneg, kah pish kenaau kussohh8konteamw8, nish$noh pasuk, piuhsuke, kah matta howan pish ummuhkinuh neh naswaiyinitch[e]h.
E.49.5 Behold, I will bring a fear upon thee, saith the Lord GOD of hosts, from all those that be about thee; and ye shall be driven out every man right forth; and none shall gather up him that wandereth.

α.49.6 Kah ompetagk pish wonk nukqushkinnum ummissin8onk wunnaumonuh Ammon, wussin Jehvoah.
E.49.6 And afterward I will bring again the captivity of the children of Ammon, saith the LORD.

α.49.7 Papaume Edom, yeu wusin Jehovah ayeuteaunit sun waantamoonk matta wonk ohtano ut Teman? ukkogahqutteam8onk sun mahchem8 wutch waantamwehtu, sun mahtshaau 8waantam8ongan8?
E.49.7 Concerning Edom, thus saith the LORD of hosts; Is wisdom no more in Teman? is counsel perished from the prudent? is their wisdom vanished?

α.49.8 Wussem8k, qushken, ayek monaiyeuut wói wadohkeogish Dedan: neuwtche nunnuhkenumau wutonkquanum8onk Esau, ahquompi ne adt n8tauwaheog.
E.49.8 Flee ye, turn back, dwell deep, O inhabitants of Dedan; for I will bring the calamity of Esau upon him, the time that I will visit him.

α.49.9 Mainneacheg weenominneash peogqueog, sunnummatta sequnnum8og mukkupashquaeu weenomineash komm8towaenuog nukkonaeu, nag mukk8kinnuwaog nô pajeh wamepwunneaoont.
E.49.9 If grapegatherers come to thee, would they not leave some gleaning grapes? if thieves by night, they will destroy till they have enough.

α.49.10 Qut Esau nupp8skissuah, nupposkinum ukkôussuongash, kah noh matt apish tapenum8 upputtogquenat: 8skannem match[é]hteanun, kah weematoh, kah weetatteamungoh, kah noh matta appu.
E.49.10 But I have made Esau bare, I have uncovered his secret places, and he shall not be able to hide himself: his seed is spoiled, and his brethren, and his neighbours, and he is not.

α.49.11 Nukkodtumah kuttouiesumog, nuppomantamwahheoog: kah kussekous[q]omog pabahtanumehettich.
E.49.11 Leave thy fatherless children, I will preserve them alive; and let thy widows trust in me.

α.49.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah kusseh, nag wásumitcheg matta wuttattam8unat wuttattamwaitch, wunnamuhkut wuttattamwog, kah sun ken woh matta sasamatahwhont, qut wunnamuhkut pish k8tattamun.
E.49.12 For thus saith the LORD; Behold, they whose judgment was not to drink of the cup have assuredly drunken; and art thou he that shall altogether go unpunished? thou shalt not go unpunished, but thou shalt surely drink of it.

α.49.13 Newutche nashpe nen nehenwonche nutchadchekeyeuwam wussin Jehovah, Bozra pish touwushin, kekontuonk mahchumm8onk, matanittuonk, kah wame ukkeitotaneumash, pish michemohtae touishinneash.
E.49.13 For I have sworn by myself, saith the LORD, that Bozrah shall become a desolation, a reproach, a waste, and a curse; and all the cities thereof shall be perpetual wastes.

α.49.14 Nunn8tamup wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch Lordut, kah ann8naenin ann8nau en pen8wohteaut, n8wau, miyaek, ayeuuhkon8k, kah waabpek en ayeuwuttinneat.
E.49.14 I have heard a rumour from the LORD, and an ambassador is sent unto the heathen, saying, Gather ye together, and come against her, and rise up to the battle.

α.49.15 Newutche kusseh, kuppéhesh ut kenugke penuwohteaut, kah kutjishanumukqush ut kenugke wosketompaog.
E.49.15 For, lo, I will make thee small among the heathen, and despised among men.

α.49.16 Kutunkqueneunkqussuonk kuppûhch8unuk, kuppetuánumwutteaháonk woi ken wadohkean, passipskodtut,, ken wadchanumon koduhkôag, t[ó]konogque ogque qunuhqueu wadjishóhteáan wompsikukquaut, nâ k8ch n8kinunin, wussin Lord.
E.49.16 Thy terribleness hath deceived thee, and the pride of thine heart, O thou that dwellest in the clefts of the rock, that holdest the height of the hill: though thou shouldest make thy nest as high as the eagle, I will bring thee down from thence, saith the LORD.

α.49.17 Edom wonk pish touwushin: nishnoh pasuk nâ kishke paumushadt piṣh chepshau, kah piṣh quequssumau wáme enninneaongash na$ut.
E.49.17 Also Edom shall be a desolation: every one that goeth by it shall be astonished, and shall hiss at all the plagues thereof.

α.49.18 Neane képuhteamukup Sodom kah Gomorrah, kah weene keitotanash, wussin Jehovah: matta howan na piṣh wutappein, kah matta wosketompae wunnaumonain piṣh 8tohkein.
E.49.18 As in the overthrow of Sodom and Gomorrah and the neighbour cities thereof, saith the LORD, no man shall abide there, neither shall a son of man dwell in it.

α.49.19 Kusse[h], piṣh ogque kuhkuhqueu qunnónouut, wutch ummogquesuonk Jordan, ayeuuhkonittue wutáyeuongan8 manuhkesitcheg: qut nukkenuppe wussémowah wutch nahoh, kah howan pepenaue wosketomp, onk woh nah nanawunnumwahéonuh? newutche howan yâninneunkqusseh? kah howan woh kohquttumiit ahquompi? howan noh nanaushepsaen woh neepauit anaquabeh?
E.49.19 Behold, he shall come up like a lion from the swelling of Jordan against the habitation of the strong: but I will suddenly make him run away from her: and who is a chosen man, that I may appoint over her? for who is like me? and who will appoint me the time? and who is that shepherd that will stand before me?

α.49.20 Newutche n8tamok ukkogáhqutteám8onk Jehovah, ne ayeuuhkonittue nemunum Edom, kah uppogkodtantam8onk ne pagkodtantog ayeuuhkonittue wadohkinitcheh Teman: wunnamuhkut peississit ut flockut, piṣh nah ukkódtinuh: wunnamuhkut piṣh touwushitteau wutáyeuongan8 weeche nahoh.
E.49.20 Therefore hear the counsel of the LORD, that he hath taken against Edom; and his purposes, that he hath purposed against the inhabitants of Teman: Surely the least of the flock shall draw them out: surely he shall make their habitations desolate with them.

α.49.21 Ohke ontohteau panusháhettit: mauuhhettit, ne wadtauatonkqussuonk wuttussittamun mishque ketahhanit.
E.49.21 The earth is moved at the noise of their fall, at the cry the noise thereof was heard in the Red sea.

α.49.22 Kusseh, noh piṣh kuhkuhqueu, kah pt8wu onatuh wompsikukquáut, kah piṣh woskeche sepagenau umméqunuh Bozrah: kah n[è] kesukok wuttahhou Edome menuhkesuenuog, piṣh ogqutteahaog mittumwossis onkquonomit.
E.49.22 Behold, he shall come up and fly as the eagle, and spread his wings over Bozrah: and at that day shall the heart of the mighty men of Edom be as the heart of a woman in her pangs.

α.49.23 Papaume Damaskus, Hamath chepshau kah Arpad: kah newutche nag n8tamwog matchissetonkquot, nag sohqutteaháog, onkquanumoonk ohteau ketahhannit, matta woh chequnohtan8.
E.49.23 Concerning Damascus. Hamath is confounded, and Arpad: for they have heard evil tidings: they are fainthearted; there is sorrow on the sea; it cannot be quiet.

α.49.24 Damaskus nano n8chumwesu, quinnuppinnum wuhhog wussémunneat, kah wabesuonk nuhkuhkunk; onkquanum8onk kah onkquommom8ongaṣh wutogque tohqunukqun[a]ṣh mittamwossis neechadt.
E.49.24 Damascus is waxed feeble, and turneth herself to flee, and fear hath seized on her: anguish and sorrows have taken her, as a woman in travail.

α.49.25 Uttoh en waeenomae keitotan matta nukkodtum8un, n8weekontam8e keitotan?
E.49.25 How is the city of praise not left, the city of my joy!

α.49.26 Newaj piṣh 8skeneumoh penushonit ut toumaogquehtu, kah wame ayeuteaenuog piṣh tummetahwhôog ne kesukok, wussin Lord ayeuhte[a]unit.
E.49.26 Therefore her young men shall fall in her streets, and all the men of war shall be cut off in that day, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.49.27 Kah nunnashqunánum n8teau, ut Damaskusse hassunnútunkanit; kah piṣh mahchikkussum8m8 ummishe kommuk8maṣh Benhadad.
E.49.27 And I will kindle a fire in the wall of Damascus, and it shall consume the palaces of Benhadad.

α.49.28 Papaume Kedar, kah papaume Hazore ass8tam8ongaṣh, niṣh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t piṣh tôkodtogiṣh, yeu wussin Jehovah: omohkek, kuhkuhquek en Kedar, kah mukk8kin8k wutcheksue wosketompaog.
E.49.28 Concerning Kedar, and concerning the kingdoms of Hazor, which Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon shall smite, thus saith the LORD; Arise ye, go up to Kedar, and spoil the men of the east.

α.49.29 Week8oaṣh kah uf-flocksum8oaṣ nag piṣh amaunáog, nag piṣh nemunumoog wutonkwhongan8, kah wame 8wishqua8ash, kah Camelsum8uh, kah nag ummishont8wánumauóuh, wabesuonk quinnuppeyeu8.
E.49.29 Their tents and their flocks shall they take away: they shall take to themselves their curtains, and all their vessels, and their camels; and they shall cry unto them, Fear is on every side.

α.49.30 Wusseem8k, nôadtut onkq, m8nôiyeuut ayék, woi wadohkéógiṣh Hazor wussin Jehovah: newutche Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue k8weadtimuk8, kah missantam pogkodtantamoonk ayeuuhkonittue kenaau.
E.49.30 Flee, get you far off, dwell deep, O ye inhabitants of Hazor, saith the LORD; for Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon hath taken counsel against you, and hath conceived a purpose against you.

α.49.31 Neepok kuhkuhquek wenauwetue wutohtimoineat[,] neg matta nan[a]uw[ó]ntamwe ayitcheg, wussin Jehovah, neg matta ohto8gig squontamash asuh barsash, neg nâsiitcheg.
E.49.31 Arise, get you up unto the wealthy nation, that dwelleth without care, saith the LORD, which have neither gates nor bars, which dwell alone.

α.49.32 Kah uk-Camelsum8uh piṣh tohqunnum8onganú8oh kah mataánukeg uppuppinashim8m8uh piṣh mukk8kinittuonganu8, kah nag nusseahwhôog ut wame wabanéhtu, neg aongkoue adt nashik, kah nuppaudto, wutonkquanum8ongan8 wutch waeenu, wussin Lord.
E.49.32 And their camels shall be a booty, and the multitude of their cattle a spoil: and I will scatter into all winds them that are in the utmost corners; and I will bring their calamity from all sides thereof, saith the LORD.

α.49.33 Kah Hazor piṣh wutáyeuongan8 dragonsog, kah micheme touwushin, matta na piṣh howan wutappein, kah matta wosketompae wunnumoniin piṣh 8tohkéin.
E.49.33 And Hazor shall be a dwelling for dragons, and a desolation for ever: there shall no man abide there, nor any son of man dwell in it.

α.49.34 Wuttinn8waonk Jehovah uppeyaonukqun Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen, ayeuuhkonittue Elam; n8che nanauwunnuadt Zedechiah Judae ketass8t, n8wau,
E.49.34 The word of the LORD that came to Jeremiah the prophet against Elam in the beginning of the reign of Zedekiah king of Judah, saying,

α.49.35 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kusseh, nuppohqun wutahtompeh Elam, kehche ummenuhkesueneúm8uh.
E.49.35 Thus saith the LORD of hosts; Behold, I will break the bow of Elam, the chief of their might.

α.49.36 Kah nunnúhkinumau Elam yauoh wuttinoh, wutch yaue kesukque chippiyeuut, kah nag nusseahwhôog nogque wame yeuh wabanehtu, kah na piṣh mat wutohtimoinneaèn8, uttoh en pogkénitcheg wutch Elam matta piṣh peyôuneau.
E.49.36 And upon Elam will I bring the four winds from the four quarters of heaven, and will scatter them toward all those winds; and there shall be no nation whither the outcasts of Elam shall not come.

α.49.37 Newutche nutchepsháheaog Elam ut anaquabenit ummatwom8oh, kah ut anaquabinit kodnushikqutcheh: kah nunnuhkinnumauóog machuk, nummishe musquantamoonk wussin Lord, kah nag n8suhqunóog togkodteg, nô pajeh nummohtupponónaóont.
E.49.37 For I will cause Elam to be dismayed before their enemies, and before them that seek their life: and I will bring evil upon them, even my fierce anger, saith the LORD; and I will send the sword after them, till I have consumed them:

α.49.38 Kah nupponam nutappuonk ut Elam, kah na n8ch paguanon ketass8t kah sontimóog, wussin Jehovah.
E.49.38 And I will set my throne in Elam, and will destroy from thence the king and the princes, saith the LORD.

α.49.39 Qut piṣh n$nih, ut majish kesukodtásh, piṣh wonk nukquehchuwutto ummissinóonk Elam, wussin Jehovah.
E.49.39 But it shall come to pass in the latter days, that I will bring again the captivity of Elam, saith the LORD.

α.50.1 KUtt8onk ne ayeuuhkonittue Babylonut unn8wadt Jehovah, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutohtuout Caldeansog, nashpe Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen.
E.50.1 The word that the LORD spake against Babylon and against the land of the Chaldeans by Jeremiah the prophet.

α.50.2 Wahteauwahu8k ut kenugke wutohtimôineat, kah n8tamwahuwagk, kah nepatto8k muttaagk, n8tamwahuwagk, kah attáhta8hkon; n8wagk, Babylon sohkomun, Bel chepshau, Merodach sokqshau, wuttinneukontunkoh chepsháoh, wuttinneukontunkanouh sokqsháoh.
E.50.2 Declare ye among the nations, and publish, and set up a standard; publish, and conceal not: say, Babylon is taken, Bel is confounded, Merodach is broken in pieces; her idols are confounded, her images are broken in pieces.

α.50.3 Newutche wutch nanummiyeu ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtunk wutohtim[ô]in, nah piṣh touishitte[a]uohteauinit wutohke, kah matta howan na piṣh wutaiin: nag piṣh ontappuog, nag piṣh amaéog naneeswe wosketomp kah puppinashim.
E.50.3 For out of the north there cometh up a nation against her, which shall make her land desolate, and none shall dwell therein: they shall remove, they shall depart, both man and beast.

α.50.4 Yeush ut kesukodtaṣh, kah na ahquompak wussin Jehovah, wunneechanoh Israel piṣh peyaoh, nag kah wunneechanoh Judah moeu, monchehettit, kah mauhettit, nag piṣh moncheog kah natinnewhaog Jehovah um-Manitt8m8uh.
E.50.4 In those days, and in that time, saith the LORD, the children of Israel shall come, they and the children of Judah together, going and weeping: they shall go, and seek the LORD their God.

α.50.5 Nag pish nat8tamuhteaog may ánshik Zion, ne nogque anaquosháhettit, n8wahettit, peyonk, weech8whuttitteuh en Jehovahut nashpe michemohtae wunn8waonk, ne matta wanhuwómun8g.
E.50.5 They shall ask the way to Zion with their faces thitherward, saying, Come, and let us join ourselves to the LORD in a perpetual covenant that shall not be forgotten.

α.50.6 Nummissinninnúmog mahche wunneheáog shepsoh, wunnanaushepsaéneum8oh nanwushahukquog, nah wuttinn8hkauóuh wadchuuhkontu nag ahóntsadchuwâusháog, nag wanantamwog wutanwôsin8e ayeuongan8.
E.50.6 My people hath been lost sheep: their shepherds have caused them to go astray, they have turned them away on the mountains: they have gone from mountain to hill, they have forgotten their restingplace.

α.50.7 Wame neh nahnamheoncheg ummahchipwunneaóuh, kah a8kqhetticheh n8waoh matta nummatcheseumun: newutche nag matcheneheaog Jehovah, wutáyeuonk sampweusseonk, Jehovah wutannoósuongan8 8sh8oh.
E.50.7 All that found them have devoured them: and their adversaries said, We offend not, because they have sinned against the LORD, the habitation of justice, even the LORD, the hope of their fathers.

α.50.8 Ontappek wutch nashauwe Babylon, kah sohham8k wutch wutohtuóut Caldeansog, kah tatuppéyeuk nomposhimwut ut anaquohtag flock.
E.50.8 Remove out of the midst of Babylon, and go forth out of the land of the Chaldeans, and be as the he goats before the flocks.

α.50.9 Newutche kusseh, n8waábeh kah nukkuhkuhqueáh ayeuuhkonittue Babylon, mishe wutohtimóinne mukkinneunk, wutch nanumohkeit, kah nag piṣh, wutayeuuhkonittue wunappehtauóuh, nâ wutch piṣh amaunou: nag ukkôuhquodt8aṣh piṣh tatuppeyeu8aṣh noh pagwohteadt, matta piṣh tahn8che qushkemu8.
E.50.9 For, lo, I will raise and cause to come up against Babylon an assembly of great nations from the north country: and they shall set themselves in array against her; from thence she shall be taken: their arrows shall be as of a mighty expert man; none shall return in vain.

α.50.10 Kah Caldea piṣh matchehteauonganu8, wame neg magk8kinoncheg piṣh wamep8og, wussin Jehovah.
E.50.10 And Chaldea shall be a spoil: all that spoil her shall be satisfied, saith the LORD.

α.50.11 Newutche k8wekontamumwop, newutch kummuskouantamumwop, woi kenaau pagwatauógish wutohtóonk, newutche nano konohkumw8, onatuh heiferut maskuhkuhkontu, kah kutogque chequttumumw8 nomposhimwut.
E.50.11 Because ye were glad, because ye rejoiced, O ye destroyers of mine heritage, because ye are grown fat as the heifer at grass, and bellow as bulls;

α.50.12 K8kás8 piṣh mishe chepshau, noh nekhikqueóg piṣh akodchu, kusseh, aongkoue wutohtimoin piṣh touohkomuk88, kunkohteâadteáe ohke, kah touishinne ohke.
E.50.12 Your mother shall be sore confounded; she that bare you shall be ashamed: behold, the hindermost of the nations shall be a wilderness, a dry land, and a desert.

α.50.13 Newutche ummusquanittam8onk Jehovah matta piṣh ayeuonganinn8, qut piṣh mamusse touwushin: nishnoh pasuk noh kezqush[a]dt Babylon piṣh chepshau, kah pish quequssumau wame wuttininneaongoh.
E.50.13 Because of the wrath of the LORD it shall not be inhabited, but it shall be wholly desolate: every one that goeth by Babylon shall be astonished, and hiss at all her plagues.

α.50.14 Ayeuuhkonittue wunappéhtók Babylon waeenu: wame kenaau wonki[n]ógish ohtomp, pumók, wohquánittadteohk kounkquodtash, newutche matcheneheau Jehovahoh.
E.50.14 Put yourselves in array against Babylon round about: all ye that bend the bow, shoot at her, spare no arrows: for she hath sinned against the LORD.

α.50.15 Mishont8wak waéenu: noh magou wunnutcheg, ukquenohtagómash penushaash, ukqussukqunneutunkaṣh penushaash: newutche ne wutann8taonk Jehovah; ann8tók, ne ásit, ne unnéheuk.
E.50.15 Shout against her round about: she hath given her hand: her foundations are fallen, her walls are thrown down: for it is the vengeance of the LORD: take vengeance upon her; as she hath done, do unto her.

α.50.16 Tummehtoh8k ohkehteaénin wutch Babylon, kah noh nohtónuk sickle, kepenumuk: newutche wabesuóntamwog sunukkutchóh8wae togkodteg, nag piṣh quinnuppeog nishnoh pasuk en ummussinninnúmut, kah nag piṣh ushpuhh8waog nishnoh pasuk en nehenwonche wutohtuóut.
E.50.16 Cut off the sower from Babylon, and him that handleth the sickle in the time of harvest: for fear of the oppressing sword they shall turn every one to his people, and they shall flee every one to his own land.

α.50.17 Israel naswáiyeue sheep, qunnon8og wutama8hkauóuh: negonne Assyriae ketass8t ummahchipwunneàpuh kah maumachish noh Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t uppohquétahhamauoh wuskonaṣh.
E.50.17 Israel is a scattered sheep; the lions have driven him away: first the king of Assyria hath devoured him; and last this Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon hath broken his bones.

α.50.18 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Jehovah ayeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, kusseh, nussasametah Babilone ketass8t & wutohke, neane sasamatahwhogkup Assyriae ketass8t.
E.50.18 Therefore thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; Behold, I will punish the king of Babylon and his land, as I have punished the king of Assyria.

α.50.19 Kah wonk nuppas8 Israel ut wutáyeuonganit, kah noh piṣh nadtupp8wongam Carmel kah Bashan, kah ukketeahogkounoh piṣh taphéoneuh ut Ephraimme kah Gileade wadchuut.
E.50.19 And I will bring Israel again to his habitation, and he shall feed on Carmel and Bashan, and his soul shall be satisfied upon mount Ephraim and Gilead.

α.50.20 Ut yeush kesukkodtash, kah na ahquompag, wussin Jehovah, ummatcheseonk Israel piṣh natinnehamun, kah piṣh wannehenn8: kah ummatcheseongash Judah, kah matta piṣh namehteauouunash; newutche nutahquontamauoog neg wadchanogeg.
E.50.20 In those days, and in that time, saith the LORD, the iniquity of Israel shall be sought for, and there shall be none; and the sins of Judah, and they shall not be found: for I will pardon them whom I reserve.

α.50.21 Ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquéhtam8k wutohke Merathaim, ayeuuhkontamunat, kah ayeuuhkonittue wadohkitcheg Pekod, mahtupán8k kah papaquanne paguan8k asuhk8e nag, wussin Jehovah, kah ussish wame neanann8nun.
E.50.21 Go up against the land of Merathaim, even against it, and against the inhabitants of Pekod: waste and utterly destroy after them, saith the LORD, and do according to all that I have commanded thee.

α.50.22 Mishont8wae mattompog ut ohkeit, kah mishe pagu[a]nuonk.
E.50.22 A sound of battle is in the land, and of great destruction.

α.50.23 Uttoh en wut-hammerum mamusse ohke poskehthamun, kah pohquenumun? uttoh en Babilon tauishitteauun ut kenugke wutohtimóneat.
E.50.23 How is the hammer of the whole earth cut asunder and broken! how is Babylon become a desolation among the nations!

α.50.24 Kupponamoush ahpeh, kah kuppitham woi Babilon, kah matta k8wâun, kenamhetteap kah wonk kuppitham, newutche kutáyeuuhkon Jehovah.
E.50.24 I have laid a snare for thee, and thou art also taken, O Babylon, and thou wast not aware: thou art found, and also caught, because thou hast striven against the LORD.

α.50.25 Jehovah pohquánum ukkenauwameekommuk, kah sohh8wuttau ummusquanittam8e auwohteaongash, newutche yeu wutanakausuonk Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, ut wutohtuóut Caldeansog.
E.50.25 The LORD hath opened his armoury, and hath brought forth the weapons of his indignation: for this is the work of the Lord GOD of hosts in the land of the Chaldeans.

α.50.26 Ayeuuhkon8k wutch aongkoue s[ù]ssippoiyeuut, wôshinum8k ummaumachiekommukquash; ogque unnúhteagk nomwunkquag; kah papaquanne paguanok: ahque teag sequnnum[ó]k.
E.50.26 Come against her from the utmost border, open her storehouses: cast her up as heaps, and destroy her utterly: let nothing of her be left.

α.50.27 Nehtók wame wutoxinumoh: womussehettich en ahhut nushit: missi wutonkapunnaongan8 newutche ukkesukkodtum peyom8, natauwaháe wutaquompiyeum8.
E.50.27 Slay all her bullocks; let them go down to the slaughter: woe unto them! for their day is come, the time of their visitation.

α.50.28 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg wasemwutcheg wutch Babilone ohkeit: wahteauwáhuónat ut Zion wuttann8taonk Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, wut-Templumme [á]nn8taonk.
E.50.28 The voice of them that flee and escape out of the land of Babylon, to declare in Zion the vengeance of the LORD our God, the vengeance of his temple.

α.50.29 Miyáe wehkomok pepummuwaenuog ayeuuhkonittue Babilon: wame kenaau w[o]o[n]kinogish ahtomp, weenuhkók: howán pohquohhogitch: ununkquodtok neaunak wutanakausuonk: neaunak wame wutusseonk ne unnéhúk: newutche noh pehtuanum8óneau Jehovah, ayeuuhkonittue 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.50.29 Call together the archers against Babylon: all ye that bend the bow, camp against it round about; let none thereof escape: recompense her according to her work; according to all that she hath done, do unto her: for she hath been proud against the LORD, against the Holy One of Israel.

α.50.30 Newaj piṣh 8skeneumoh penushónit ut mayit, kah wame wutayeúhteaenéumoh piṣh tummehtahwhóninneuh ne kesukok, wussin Jehovah.
E.50.30 Therefore shall her young men fall in the streets, and all her men of war shall be cut off in that day, saith the LORD.

α.50.31 Kusseh, kutayeuuhkonsh woi ken mahshe pittuanumweon wussin Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit: newutche kukkesukodtum peyom8, ahquompi neadt nátauwáhhun.
E.50.31 Behold, I am against thee, O thou most proud, saith the Lord GOD of hosts: for thy day is come, the time that I will visit thee.

α.50.32 Kah mahshe pittuanumwit piṣh togkussittassun kah penushau, kah matta piṣh howan wutomohkinuh: kah piṣh nunnashqunnanum n8tau ut ukkeitotanahtu, kah piṣh mahchikussum8m8 wame waeenu.
E.50.32 And the most proud shall stumble and fall, and none shall raise him up: and I will kindle a fire in his cities, and it shall devour all round about him.

α.50.33 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wunnaumonuh Israel, kah wunnaumonuh Judah, moeu sunnukkutchahwhoog, kah wame neg masinóuhteacheg, ummenuhkinóuh, sekenamwog ummoncheáhónaóont.
E.50.33 Thus saith the LORD of hosts; The children of Israel and the children of Judah were oppressed together: and all that took them captives held them fast; they refused to let them go.

α.50.34 Uppohquohwussuaéneumoh menuhkesuoh, Jehovah ayeuhteaunit ussowesu, noh piṣh papannuppe ukken8tamwanshuh onk woh wutanwôhsiteauunat ohke, kah woh 8wogkouwéhheonat wadohkinitche Babilon.
E.50.34 Their Redeemer is strong; the LORD of hosts is his name: he shall throughly plead their cause, that he may give rest to the land, and disquiet the inhabitants of Babylon.

α.50.35 Togkodteg nuhkuhkongquog Caldeansog, wussin Jehôvah, kah wadohkitcheg Babilon, ut wussontimomut kah 8waantam8mut.
E.50.35 A sword is upon the Chaldeans, saith the LORD, and upon the inhabitants of Babylon, and upon her princes, and upon her wise men.

α.50.36 Togkodteg nuhkuhkongquog pann8waenuog, kah nag piṣh as8ke usseog, togkodteg nuhkuhkauau ummenuhkesueneumoh, kah nag piṣh chepshaog.
E.50.36 A sword is upon the liars; and they shall dote: a sword is upon her mighty men; and they shall be dismayed.

α.50.37 Togkodteg nuhkuhkauau wut$horsesumoh[,] kah wut[-]chariotumash, kah ut wame kenukshae missinninnùut ut wunnash[ó]mut, kah nag piṣh tatuppeyeu8og mittamwossisut: togkodteg nuhkuhkom8m8 wunnompekouunash, kah piṣh mukk8kinnuwontamunash.
E.50.37 A sword is upon their horses, and upon their chariots, and upon all the mingled people that are in the midst of her; and they shall become as women: a sword is upon her treasures; and they shall be robbed.

α.50.38 Nunohteau ut wunnippemut, kah niṣh piṣh nunnohtaash, newutche ne nunneukontunkanne ohke, kah nag kogkee ahchuánumaog wuttinneukontunkanóuh.
E.50.38 A drought is upon her waters; and they shall be dried up: for it is the land of graven images, and they are mad upon their idols.

α.50.39 Newaj piṣh touohkomukque puppinashimwog kah munnahhanne puppinashimwog na pish 8tohkinneau, kah k8k8kh[â]usog na piṣh 8tohkinneau: & matta pish wonk wutohkei[n] micheme, kah matta piṣh wutohkein wutch pometuonganit onk yaan pometuonganit.
E.50.39 Therefore the wild beasts of the desert with the wild beasts of the islands shall dwell there, and the owls shall dwell therein: and it shall be no more inhabited for ever; neither shall it be dwelt in from generation to generation.

α.50.40 Neane God kepuhteop Sodom kah Gomorrah kah weetatteamunguh, wussin Lord? ne ne matta pish howan wutappein kah matta wosketompae wunnaumoniin pish 8tohkein[.]
E.50.40 As God overthrew Sodom and Gomorrah and the neighbour cities thereof, saith the LORD; so shall no man abide there, neither shall any son of man dwell therein.

α.50.41 Kusseh, missinninnuog pish 8mwog nannumiyeu, kah mishe wutohimoin, kah monaog ketass8tamwog pish tahshinon, wutch sussippoi ohkeit.
E.50.41 Behold, a people shall come from the north, and a great nation, and many kings shall be raised up from the coasts of the earth.

α.50.42 Nag pish kogkôunnaog ohtompe, kah qunuhtug, nag onkapunuhteaenu8og, kah matta monanetea8og: 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 pish ogque mishont8wom8 keitahhannit, kah nag pish nayeumukquog horsesoh nish$noh pasuk ogquhhausu ayeuittimuk, ayeuuhkonittue ken woi Babylone wuttaunin.
E.50.42 They shall hold the bow and the lance: they are cruel, and will not shew mercy: their voice shall roar like the sea, and they shall ride upon horses, every one put in array, like a man to the battle, against thee, O daughter of Babylon.

α.50.43 Babylone ketass8t n8tam unaunchem8wonaongan8, kah wunnutchegash n8chumwiyeuash onkquommom8onk wuttohqunuh, kah ogque onkquommom8 mittamwossis neechadt.
E.50.43 The king of Babylon hath heard the report of them, and his hands waxed feeble: anguish took hold of him, and pangs as of a woman in travail.

α.50.44 Kusseh noh pish ogque kuhkuhqueu qunnon8ut wutch ummogquesuonganit Jordan, ut wut[a]yeuong[a]nit manuhkesit: qut nag teanuk n8semowaheaog: kah howan noh pepenaue wosketomp onk woh nah nanawunnumwaheonuh, newutche howan aniit, kah howan kohquttumiit ahquompi, kah howan noh nanaushipseaen noh neepauit anaquabeh?
E.50.44 Behold, he shall come up like a lion from the swelling of Jordan unto the habitation of the strong: but I will make them suddenly run away from her: and who is a chosen man, that I may appoint over her? for who is like me? and who will appoint me the time? and who is that shepherd that will stand before me?

α.50.45 Newut[c]he n8tam8k ukkogahqutteam8onk Jehovah, ne nemunuk ayeuuhkonittue Babylon, kah ukkesantam8ongash nish ayeuuhkonittue kesantogish wutohke Caldeansog: wunnamuhkut noh peississit ut flockut pish wussohwhunuh, wunnamuhkut pish touwishittea8 wutayeuonk weeche nahoh.
E.50.45 Therefore hear ye the counsel of the LORD, that he hath taken against Babylon; and his purposes, that he hath purposed against the land of the Chaldeans: Surely the least of the flock shall draw them out: surely he shall make their habitation desolate with them.

α.50.46 Ut 8wadtauatonkqussuonganit Babylone tohqunnumunat, ohke ontohteau, kah mauonk n8tunkquadt ut kenugke wutohtimoneat.
E.50.46 At the noise of the taking of Babylon the earth is moved, and the cry is heard among the nations.

α.51.1 YEu wussin Lord, kusseh nutayéuuhkonittue waabenumau Babylon, kah nag nashaue ayitcheg, neg waabehtunkqueâneg, pagwohteae waban.
E.51.1 Thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will raise up against Babylon, and against them that dwell in the midst of them that rise up against me, a destroying wind;

α.51.2 Kah nutann8n fanonuhsuenuog en Babylon nah pish fa[u]nonahetticheh, kah pish sequnnumwog wutohke: newutche wuttamehpunae kesukodtut pish waeenu wutayeuuhkonouh.
E.51.2 And will send unto Babylon fanners, that shall fan her, and shall empty her land: for in the day of trouble they shall be against her round about.

α.51.3 Ayeuuhkonittue noh wadtu[u]kinont ahtompe, pepummuwaenin wuttunkinonch wutohtompeh: kah ayeuuhkonittue noh waapinuk up-brigandineum: wohquanumuhkon 8skeneumoh, papaquane pagwohteau wame ukkenauwameumoh.
E.51.3 Against him that bendeth let the archer bend his bow, and against him that lifteth himself up in his brigandine: and spare ye not her young men; destroy ye utterly all her host.

α.51.4 Yeu pish wuttinne penushoneau nashitcheg ut wutohtuout C[a]ldeansog, kah neg pannuppetawhutcheg ut wuttaumaogk8mut.
E.51.4 Thus the slain shall fall in the land of the Chaldeans, and they that are thrust through in her streets.

α.51.5 Newutche Israel matta ohquanumau[,] kah Judah um-Manitt8moh, kah nashpe Jehovaoh ayeuteaunittoh tohkonogque wutohk8 numwohteau ummatcheketeaongan8 8neetup[a]natam8moh Israel
E.51.5 For Israel hath not been forsaken, nor Judah of his God, of the LORD of hosts; though their land was filled with sin against the Holy One of Israel.

α.51.6 Wusseemok wutch nashauwe Babylon, kah pohquohwhunonch, nishnoh pasuk ukketeahogkôunoh, tummetawhutteateok ut ummatcheseonganit: newutche yeu ahquompi wutann8táonk Jehovah; neh piṣh wutonkquatauoh.
E.51.6 Flee out of the midst of Babylon, and deliver every man his soul: be not cut off in her iniquity; for this is the time of the LORD's vengeance; he will render unto her a recompence.

α.51.7 Bablyon ne golde wuttattamwaitch ut wunnutcheganit Jehovah, ne kogkeissippamwáheont wame ohke: wutohtimoinneunk wuttattamwog 8wineum, newaj wutohtimoineash kogkey[ô]m8uk.
E.51.7 Babylon hath been a golden cup in the LORD's hand, that made all the earth drunken: the nations have drunken of her wine; therefore the nations are mad.

α.51.8 Babylon kenuppe penusheau, kah paguatauun: 8n8wansh8k, neemunum8k balme wutch wutonkquommom8onk, tohneit woh neetskéhit.
E.51.8 Babylon is suddenly fallen and destroyed: howl for her; take balm for her pain, if so be she may be healed.

α.51.9 Nukkodneetskéheómun Babylon, qut noh matta neetskeheuh: ohquanumok, kah ontuh nishnoh pasuk wutohkit: newutche wussumáonk mussishin kesukqut, kah tohshinnumun wehque pohkuhqut.
E.51.9 We would have healed Babylon, but she is not healed: forsake her, and let us go every one into his own country: for her judgment reacheth unto heaven, and is lifted up even to the skies.

α.51.10 Jehovah sohh8wuttau nussampweusseonganun: peyunk kah wahteauwáhuwadtuh ut Zion wutusseonk Jehovah um-Manitt8m.
E.51.10 The LORD hath brought forth our righteousness: come, and let us declare in Zion the work of the LORD our God.

α.51.11 Wôóhsuppánumok kôuhquodtaṣh: moenum8k ogqunnegash Jehovah tahshinau wuttahh8uh Medse ketass8tamwog: newutche ukkesantam8onk ayeuhkontam8m8 Babylon pagwatauunat, newutche ne wutann8taonk Jehovah, wut-templumme ann8taonk.
E.51.11 Make bright the arrows; gather the shields: the LORD hath raised up the spirit of the kings of the Medes: for his device is against Babylon, to destroy it; because it is the vengeance of the LORD, the vengeance of his temple.

α.51.12 Neepattau8k muttaag ut Babylone hassunneutunkanit, menehketeau8k askuhwheteaonk: wunash8k askuhwheteaénin: quagwashwehtam8k tummushkôsuongash, newutche Lord kesantam kah mahche ussen, ne ayeuhkonittue [à]nomp Babylon.
E.51.12 Set up the standard upon the walls of Babylon, make the watch strong, set up the watchmen, prepare the ambushes: for the LORD hath both devised and done that which he spake against the inhabitants of Babylon.

α.51.13 Woi ken wadohkéan eiyáne nippekontu, monatash kenompak8unash, k8wohkukquossin8onk peyom8, kah numwohtae kutaháhchuwontam8onk.
E.51.13 O thou that dwellest upon many waters, abundant in treasures, thine end is come, and the measure of thy covetousness.

α.51.14 Lord ayeuhteaunit chadchekeyeuau nashpe nehenwonche nagum, n8wau, wunnamuhkut kutogque numwohtoush wosketompaog m8paut, kah nag piṣh kussáshquónukquog.
E.51.14 The LORD of hosts hath sworn by himself, saying, Surely I will fill thee with men, as with caterpillers; and they shall lift up a shout against thee.

α.51.15 Ayimup ohke nashpe ummenuhkesuonk, menehketeauop ohke nashpe 8waantamoonk, noh sepágenumup kesukquaṣh nashpe 8wohwohtam8onk.
E.51.15 He hath made the earth by his power, he hath established the world by his wisdom, and hath stretched out the heaven by his understanding.

α.51.16 Mishant8adt, móneau nippeash ut kesukqut, waabehteau ouwan, wutch weekqshik ohke, ukkutshámunáhteau nashpe sokanon, sohh8wunau wabanoh wutch wunnompak8unéhtu.
E.51.16 When he uttereth his voice, there is a multitude of waters in the heavens; and he causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth: he maketh lightnings with rain, and bringeth forth the wind out of his treasures.

α.51.17 Nishnoh pasuk puppinashimweyeu8 ut wohwohtam8onganit: nishnoh pasuk noh sabahsausit chepshau nashpe wuttinneukontungok, newutche wussabassumwe wuttinneukontunkoh, pann8waongannù8oh, kah matta wunnashaonganéog.
E.51.17 Every man is brutish by his knowledge; every founder is confounded by the graven image: for his molten image is falsehood, and there is no breath in them.

α.51.18 Nag tahn8cheyeu8og, pann8wáe usseonk, natauwáhit piṣh pagwan[ù]og.
E.51.18 They are vanity, the work of errors: in the time of their visitation they shall perish.

α.51.19 Wuchippiyeum Jakob matta tatuppéi[n]8, newutche noh kahkénauwéhteunk wame, kah Israel uppogkomungane ohtoonk: Jehovah ayeuhteaunit ne 8wesuonk.
E.51.19 The portion of Jacob is not like them; for he is the former of all things: and Israel is the rod of his inheritance: the LORD of hosts is his name.

α.51.20 Ken nummattompágwe togkunk, kah nummattompagwe auwohteaonk, newutche nashpe ken nuppohquetahham wutohtimóneash, kah nashpe ken nuppagwadtoh ass8tam8ongash.
E.51.20 Thou art my battle axe and weapons of war: for with thee will I break in pieces the nations, and with thee will I destroy kingdoms;

α.51.21 Kah nashpe ken nussukquttoh horses kah neh na8moncheh, kah nashpe ken nuppohquttahham chariotsash, kah neh na8mukqut.
E.51.21 And with thee will I break in pieces the horse and his rider; and with thee will I break in pieces the chariot and his rider;

α.51.22 Nashpe ken wonk nussukquttoh wosketomp kah mittamwossis, kah n[a]shpe ken nussukquttoh kutchis kah wusken, kah nashpe ken nussukqutt[o]h wusken, kah|peaomp.
E.51.22 With thee also will I break in pieces man and woman; and with thee will I break in pieces old and young; and with thee will I break in pieces the young man and the maid;

α.51.23 Nashpe ken wonk nussukquttoh nanáushepsaen kah uf-flockum, kah nashpe ken nussukquttoh ohkehteaen, kah we-yoke oxinumoh, kah nashpe ken nussoquetoh mugquompaog, kah nananuwaénuoh.
E.51.23 I will also break in pieces with thee the shepherd and his flock; and with thee will I break in pieces the husbandman and his yoke of oxen; and with thee will I break in pieces captains and rulers.

α.51.24 Kah nutonkquttau Babylon, kah wadohkitcheg Caldea, wame machuk ne asehettit ut Zion, anaquabeóg wussin Jehovah.
E.51.24 And I will render unto Babylon and to all the inhabitants of Chaldea all their evil that they have done in Zion in your sight, saith the LORD.

α.51.25 Kusseh, kutayeuhkonsh woi ken pagwohteae wadchu, wussin Lord, ken pagwatauan wame ohke, kah nussumagkinum nuhpit ut kuhhogkat, kah k8w8mhenuṣh wutch qussukquanóhtu, kah kutchikohtaé wadchukonsh.
E.51.25 Behold, I am against thee, O destroying mountain, saith the LORD, which destroyest all the earth: and I will stretch out mine hand upon thee, and roll thee down from the rocks, and will make thee a burnt mountain.

α.51.26 Kah nag matta piṣh neemunumóog náshine qussuk wutch ken, asuh quenohtagane qussuk, qut piṣh kummicheme touwushin wussin Jehovah.
E.51.26 And they shall not take of thee a stone for a corner, nor a stone for foundations; but thou shalt be desolate for ever, saith the LORD.

α.51.27 Neepatto8k muttaagk ut ohkeit, p8tantam8k monopuhpegk ut kenugke wutohtimóineash: ayeuhkonittue nanashwunnumok wutohtimóneash, ayeuhkonittue moeu wehquetumok Araratte ketass8tamwog, Minni kah Ashkenaz; ayeuhkonittue kukquttumok mugquompuh: 
E.51.27 Set ye up a standard in the land, blow the trumpet among the nations, prepare the nations against her, call together against her the kingdoms of Ararat, Minni, and Ashchenaz; appoint a captain against her; cause the horses to come up as the rough caterpillers.

α.51.28 Ayeuhkonittue nanashwunnumok wutohtimóneash, weeche Medse ketass8tamwog, umummugquompomuh, kah wunnanauwunnuaéneumoh, kah wame wunnanauwunnumóe ohkeit.
E.51.28 Prepare against her the nations with the kings of the Medes, the captains thereof, and all the rulers thereof, and all the land of his dominion.

α.51.29 Kah ohke piṣh nunnuksheau, kah neuantam: newutch nishnoh ukkesantam8onk Lord piṣh wutussen ayeuhkonittue Babylon, touishitteauunat Babylone ohke, matta wutohkeéinneat.
E.51.29 And the land shall tremble and sorrow: for every purpose of the LORD shall be performed against Babylon, to make the land of Babylon a desolation without an inhabitant.

α.51.30 Babylone menuhkésuenuog ahquiyeuhteáog: nag appuog 8wonkon8sinn8óut: ummenuhkesuongan8 mahtsheau, tatuppeyeu8og mittamwussisut, nag chikossumwog wutáyeuongan8, up-barsumash pokqshaash.
E.51.30 The mighty men of Babylon have forborn to fight, they have remained in their holds: their might hath failed; they became as women: they have burned her dwellingplaces; her bars are broken.

α.51.31 Pasuk quogqueaenin pish quogqueu nogkishkauonat onkatogeh, kah pasuk ann8naen nogkushkauonat onkatuk, nahtinonat Babylone ketass8t, ukkeitotan sohkomun ut nequtchippaiyeuut.
E.51.31 One post shall run to meet another, and one messenger to meet another, to shew the king of Babylon that his city is taken at one end,

α.51.32 Kah pomushaongash kuppuhhausuash, kah weekinaskquash chikohtaash n8taut, & ayeuhteaenuog t8weshaog.
E.51.32 And that the passages are stopped, and the reeds they have burned with fire, and the men of war are affrighted.

α.51.33 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah áyeuteaunit um-Manitt8moh Israel, wuttaunoh Babylon tatuppeyu8oh tanuppogguhham8onganit, utt8cheyeu8 ne adt woh pogguhwhut, qut pasweyeu8 kah kepenumwae ahquompi peyaum8.
E.51.33 For thus saith the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel; The daughter of Babylon is like a threshingfloor, it is time to thresh her: yet a little while, and the time of her harvest shall come.

α.51.34 Nebuchàdnezar Babylone ketass8t, nummahchipuk nussunukkuhhuk, nummachishquohkonuk: nutogque misheashquonuk dragonsut, wameechummehteau wunnogkus n8nummeechumash, nussohwhuhkonuk.
E.51.34 Nebuchadrezzar the king of Babylon hath devoured me, he hath crushed me, he hath made me an empty vessel, he hath swallowed me up like a dragon, he hath filled his belly with my delicates, he hath cast me out.

α.51.35 Chekee unnehettuonk, kah ut neyausut nuhkuhkaj Babylon, wadohkitcheg Zion ne pish n8waog; kah n8sqheonk nuhkuhkonkqhettich wadohkitcheg Caldea, ne Jerusalem n8wau.
E.51.35 The violence done to me and to my flesh be upon Babylon, shall the inhabitant of Zion say; and my blood upon the inhabitants of Chaldea, shall Jerusalem say.

α.51.36 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh nukken8tamwontam kuttinniyeuonk, kutann8tauwanshush, kah nunnanassum ukkethann8m, kah nunnunassum wuttuhkekomeumash.
E.51.36 Therefore thus saith the LORD; Behold, I will plead thy cause, and take vengeance for thee; and I will dry up her sea, and make her springs dry.

α.51.37 Kah Babylon pish numwonkquaenu8, wutayeuongan8 Dragonsog, chepshaonk, kah quekqs[u]ontam8onk, matta ayeinat.
E.51.37 And Babylon shall become heaps, a dwellingplace for dragons, an astonishment, and an hissing, without an inhabitant.

α.51.38 Nag pish moae ogque chequttumwog qunnon8ut, kah pish ogque 8nwog qunnonuemesit.
E.51.38 They shall roar together like lions: they shall yell as lions' whelps.

α.51.39 Kósobpishettit, nummishadtup, kah nukkogkeissippamwaheaog, onk woh weekontámwog, kah woh micheme koueog, kah matta t8hkeog, wussin Jehovah.
E.51.39 In their heat I will make their feasts, and I will make them drunken, that they may rejoice, and sleep a perpetual sleep, and not wake, saith the LORD.

α.51.40 Nag nutogque womussuunoog Lambsut nushonaout, onatuh ramsog weeche nomposhimwe goatsut.
E.51.40 I will bring them down like lambs to the slaughter, like rams with he goats.

α.51.41 Uttoh en Sheshak tohqunau? kah uttoh en mamusse ohkee waéenoaonk sohkomun? uttoh en Babylon chépshontamun ut kenugke wutohtimoineat.
E.51.41 How is Sheshach taken! and how is the praise of the whole earth surprised! how is Babylon become an astonishment among the nations!

α.51.42 Keitoh kuhkuhquemo Babylon: noh puttogguhkunk nashpe monacheg tuhk8oh.
E.51.42 The sea is come up upon Babylon: she is covered with the multitude of the waves thereof.

α.51.43 Ukkeitotan8mash touishineash, nunohtae ohke, kah touohkomuk, ohke ne matta howan ayek, kah matta wosketompae wunnaumoniin na pomushaun.
E.51.43 Her cities are a desolation, a dry land, and a wilderness, a land wherein no man dwelleth, neither doth any son of man pass thereby.

α.51.44 Kah nussasamatah Bel ut Babylon, kah nussohh8wauttau wutch wutt8nut, ne mase[a]shqut, kah wutohtimoinneash matta pish wonk moae miyaehtunk8h, nux Babylone hassunneutu[u]k pish penusheau.
E.51.44 And I will punish Bel in Babylon, and I will bring forth out of his mouth that which he hath swallowed up: and the nations shall not flow together any more unto him: yea, the wall of Babylon shall fall.

α.51.45 Nummissinninnúmog sohham8k wutch wunnashómut, kah pohquohwhunok nishnoh ukketeahogkôunoh wutch ummishe musquantam8onganit Jehovah.
E.51.45 My people, go ye out of the midst of her, and deliver ye every man his soul from the fierce anger of the LORD.

α.51.46 Kah ishkont kuttahhou nupp8m8, kah kukquehtamumw8 nashpe wadtaúatonkquodt ne piṣh n8tamuk ut ohkeit: wadtauatonkquodt piṣh peyaum8 nequt kodtumwae, kah ompetak onkatog kodtumm8 piṣh peyaum8 wadtauatonkquodt, kah chekeeusseonk ut ohkeit, nanawunnuwaén ayeuuhkóne nanawunnuaènúh.
E.51.46 And lest your heart faint, and ye fear for the rumour that shall be heard in the land; a rumour shall both come one year, and after that in another year shall come a rumour, and violence in the land, ruler against ruler.

α.51.47 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyaum8, n8sum kogoksumwe nunneukontunkanog ut Babylon, kah mamusse wutohke piṣh chepshaog, kah wame neh náhtaúutcheh piṣh penushauh ut wunnashómut.
E.51.47 Therefore, behold, the days come, that I will do judgment upon the graven images of Babylon: and her whole land shall be confounded, and all her slain shall fall in the midst of her.

α.51.48 Neit kesuk kah ohke, kah wame ne na ohtag piṣh ket8hamwóntamwog Babylon: newutche neg magk8kinoncheg piṣh uppeyaóunouh wutch nanummiyeu, wussin Jehovah.
E.51.48 Then the heaven and the earth, and all that is therein, shall sing for Babylon: for the spoilers shall come unto her from the north, saith the LORD.

α.51.49 Neane Babylon penusháheont adt nushitcheg Israel: ne piṣh wuttinne ut Babylon penushoneau nashitcheg ut wame ohkeit.
E.51.49 As Babylon hath caused the slain of Israel to fall, so at Babylon shall fall the slain of all the earth.

α.51.50 Kenaau pohquohhamógish togkodteg, monchegk, neepo8k, nôadtit en ne mehquánumok Lord, kah Jerusalem peyom8utch kummequontam8ongan8óut.
E.51.50 Ye that have escaped the sword, go away, stand not still: remember the LORD afar off, and let Jerusalem come into your mind.

α.51.51 Nutchepshámun newutche n8tamumun kekont8onk, akodchuonk nukkuhkom nuskesukqunónash, newutche penuwohteaog petutteaog ut wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganéhtu Jehovah wekit.
E.51.51 We are confounded, because we have heard reproach: shame hath covered our faces: for strangers are come into the sanctuaries of the LORD's house.

α.51.52 Newutche kusseh, kesukodtaṣh peyom8, wussin Jehovah, piṣh n8sum ukkogoksumwe nunnúkontunkoh, kah pannuppe wame wutohkeit n8chumwéhtahhamauitcheh piṣh ha[u]uhhóm8oh.
E.51.52 Wherefore, behold, the days come, saith the LORD, that I will do judgment upon her graven images: and through all her land the wounded shall groan.

α.51.53 Tôkonoguqe Babylo[n] woh kuhkuhquem8ut en kesukqut, kah tôkô piṣh unogque ummenuhkehteauun ukqunuhqui menuhkesuonk, onch wutch nuhhogkat woskehuaénúh piṣh peyaónuk wussin Jehovah.
E.51.53 Though Babylon should mount up to heaven, and though she should fortify the height of her strength, yet from me shall spoilers come unto her, saith the LORD.

α.51.54 Maue wadtauatonkqussuonk 8m88 Babylon, kah mishe pagwanuonk wutch wutohtuout Caldeansog.
E.51.54 A sound of a cry cometh from Babylon, and great destruction from the land of the Chaldeans:

α.51.55 Newutche Jehovah matchehteo Babylon, kah pagwodtau mishe wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch wuhhogkat, wuttukk8moh agque mishont8ánit mishe nippéit, mishont8wae 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 sohwhunumun.
E.51.55 Because the LORD hath spoiled Babylon, and destroyed out of her the great voice; when her waves do roar like great waters, a noise of their voice is uttered:

α.51.56 Newutche woskehuwaen wunnuhkuhkauuh, ut Bablyon, kah ummenuhkesuéneumoh tohqunóneuh, nishnoh pasuk wutohtompeh pohquésuoh, newutche Jehovah ôadtehteáe Manit, piṣh wunnamuhkut wutonkquatauoh.
E.51.56 Because the spoiler is come upon her, even upon Babylon, and her mighty men are taken, every one of their bows is broken: for the LORD God of recompences shall surely requite.

α.51.57 Kah nukkogkeissippamwáh wussontimomoh, kah 8waantam8moh, ummugquompomo[h], kah w[u]nnanawunn[u]énúh, kah ummenuhkesuénúmoh: kah nag piṣh micheme kouéog, kah matta t8hkeog, wussin ketass8t noh as8wénit Lord ut ayeuteaunit.
E.51.57 And I will make drunk her princes, and her wise men, her captains, and her rulers, and her mighty men: and they shall sleep a perpetual sleep, and not wake, saith the King, whose name is the LORD of hosts.

α.51.58 Yeu wussin Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Babylone mishe kishkinneutongash piṣh pokshaash kah ukqunuhkqui squontamash piṣh chikohtaash n8taut, kah missinninnúog piṣh tahn8tanakausuog, kah auwâog n8taut, kah piṣh sauunumwog.
E.51.58 Thus saith the LORD of hosts; The broad walls of Babylon shall be utterly broken, and her high gates shall be burned with fire; and the people shall labour in vain, and the folk in the fire, and they shall be weary.

α.51.59 Wuttinn8waonk ne Jeremiah quoshodtumwaen ann8nau Serajahoh wunnaumonuh Neriah, wunnaumonuh Maasejah, weechauont Zedechiahoh, Judae ketass8toh en Babylon, yaue kodtumwae nanauwinnuwadt, kah yeuoh Serajah manunnissue Sontimó8.
E.51.59 The word which Jeremiah the prophet commanded Seraiah the son of Neriah, the son of Maaseiah, when he went with Zedekiah the king of Judah into Babylon in the fourth year of his reign. And this Seraiah was a quiet prince.

α.51.60 Neit Jeremiah wussukhum ut b8kut wame machuk ne piṣh nohkuhkom8m8uk Babylon: wame yeush kutt8wongash nish wasukkuhwhosikish ayeuhkonittue Babylon.
E.51.60 So Jeremiah wrote in a book all the evil that should come upon Babylon, even all these words that are written against Babylon.

α.51.61 Kah Jeremiah unnau Serajahoh, pey[o]an Babylon, kah nauman, kah ogketaman wame yeush kutt8wongash.
E.51.61 And Jeremiah said to Seraiah, When thou comest to Babylon, and shalt see, and shalt read all these words;

α.51.62 Neit pish kussim, woi Jehovah, yeu kutayeuhkonittue ken8tamun ayeuonk, tummehthamunat, onk woh mo howan wutappein, wosketomp asuh puppinashim, kah ne piṣh touwushin micheme.
E.51.62 Then shalt thou say, O LORD, thou hast spoken against this place, to cut it off, that none shall remain in it, neither man nor beast, but that it shall be desolate for ever.

α.51.63 Kah piṣh nnih mahche ogketaman yeu b8k, piṣh k8wéenadtippinun qussuk, kah kuttinuhkon nashaue Euphrates.
E.51.63 And it shall be, when thou hast made an end of reading this book, that thou shalt bind a stone to it, and cast it into the midst of Euphrates:

α.51.64 Kah piṣh kussim, yeu pish wuttinne quttauwushun Babylon, kah matta piṣh omohku wutch machuk ne piṣh nohkinnumauog, kah nag pish sauunumwog, yeu wéhque ukkutt8wongaṣh Jeremiah.
E.51.64 And thou shalt say, Thus shall Babylon sink, and shall not rise from the evil that I will bring upon her: and they shall be weary. Thus far are the words of Jeremiah.

α.52.1 ZEdechiah neesneechage kah nequtta kodtumwohkomup n8che nanauwunn[u]wadt, kah nabo nequtta kodtumwaeu nanawunnuau ut Jerusalem, kah ohkasoh ussowesuoh Hamutall wuttaunoh Jeremiah wul[-]Libnah.
E.52.1 Zedekiah was one and twenty years old when he began to reign, and he reigned eleven years in Jerusalem. And his mother's name was Hamutal the daughter of Jeremiah of Libnah.

α.52.2 Kah ussu ne machuk ut wuskesukqut Jehovah, neaunak wame wutusseonk Jehojakim.
E.52.2 And he did that which was evil in the eyes of the LORD, according to all that Jehoiakim had done.

α.52.3 Newutche nashpe ummusquantam8onk Jehovah n$niyeup ut Jerusalem, kah ut Judah, nô pajeh uppogkenónat wutch anaquabit, Zedechiah cheketauau Babylone ketass8toh.
E.52.3 For through the anger of the LORD it came to pass in Jerusalem and Judah, till he had cast them out from his presence, that Zedekiah rebelled against the king of Babylon.

α.52.4 Kah n$niyeup pasuk8gun adtahshe kodtumwae nanawunnuadt, piogqussit nepauz, piogquequinohhog nepauz, Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t peyau, nagum kah wame ukkenauwammúmoh, ayeuhkontamunat Jerusalem, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutappehtamun, kah 8wonkon8sinuhkontamun waéenu.
E.52.4 And it came to pass in the ninth year of his reign, in the tenth month, in the tenth day of the month, that Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon came, he and all his army, against Jerusalem, and pitched against it, and built forts against it round about.

α.52.5 Neit keitotan wéenuhkomunáh, nô pajeh nabowunnukqutte kodtum8mit Zedechiah.
E.52.5 So the city was besieged unto the eleventh year of king Zedekiah.

α.52.6 Kah ut yaue nepauzsaut, pasuk8gun adtahshikqunúhhog nepauz, mahshagquodt unkqueneunkquodt ut otanat, newaj matta petukqunneganinn8g wutche ohkee missinninnuog.
E.52.6 And in the fourth month, in the ninth day of the month, the famine was sore in the city, so that there was no bread for the people of the land.

α.52.7 Neit keitotan sohqshau, kah wame ayeuhteaenuog wussem8og, kah sohhamwog wutch otanat nuhkonaeu, squontame mayut nashaue neutunkanit, ne kishkohtag ketass8t wuttittanohketeaonganit (kah Caldeansog weenuhkomog otan) kah auog mukoshquttae mayut.
E.52.7 Then the city was broken up, and all the men of war fled, and went forth out of the city by night by the way of the gate between the two walls, which was by the king's garden; (now the Chaldeans were by the city round about:) and they went by the way of the plain.

α.52.8 Qut Caldeanse kenauwameonk n8swetahwhaog ketas8toh, kah mattanaog Zedechiahoh ut Jerichoe mukoshquttaut, kah wame ukkenauwamumoh seahsh[á]uh.
E.52.8 But the army of the Chaldeans pursued after the king, and overtook Zedekiah in the plains of Jericho; and all his army was scattered from him.

α.52.9 Neit tohqunaog ketass8t, kah wutuss8unouh en Babylone ketass8tamwut ut Riblah ut Hamathe ohkeit: uttoh ad wussumup.
E.52.9 Then they took the king, and carried him up unto the king of Babylon to Riblah in the land of Hamath; where he gave judgment upon him.

α.52.10 Kah Babylone ketass8t, nushau wunnaumonuh Zedechiah ut anaquabenit: nushau wonk wame Judae Sontimuh ut Riblah
E.52.10 And the king of Babylon slew the sons of Zedekiah before his eyes: he slew also all the princes of Judah in Riblah.

α.52.11 Neit kajkesukquanau Zedechiahoh, kah Babylone ketass8t wuttattogkuppinuh chainsash wutuss8unuh Babylon, kah ukkupshagkinuh, nó pajeh wunnupinat.
E.52.11 Then he put out the eyes of Zedekiah; and the king of Babylon bound him in chains, and carried him to Babylon, and put him in prison till the day of his death.

α.52.12 Kah napanna tahshe nepauz piogquequinohhog nepauz (ne nabo pasuk8gun tahshe ukkodtum8m Nebuchadnezzar Babylone ketass8t) Nebuzarradan askuhwheteae mugquomp, noh wadtininneumuhkauont Babylone ketass8t, petutteau Jerusalem.
E.52.12 Now in the fifth month, in the tenth day of the month, which was the nineteenth year of Nebuchadrezzar king of Babylon, came Nebuzaradan, captain of the guard, which served the king of Babylon, into Jerusalem,

α.52.13 Kah chikkossum wek Jehovah, kah ketass8t wek, kah wame Jerusalemme wetuomash, kah wame wekuoash masugkenukeg chikossumunash ut n8taut.
E.52.13 And burned the house of the LORD, and the king's house; and all the houses of Jerusalem, and all the houses of the great men, burned he with fire:

α.52.14 Kah wame Caldeanse kenauwameog, neg weetomoncheg askuhwheteae mugquompoh nag pohqshadtauog Jerusaleme hassunneutongash waeenu.
E.52.14 And all the army of the Chaldeans, that were with the captain of the guard, brake down all the walls of Jerusalem round about.

α.52.15 Neit Nebuzarradan askuhwhetae mugquomp, missinohteau matchekuoh, kah askqshoncheg missinninnuog neg apitcheg otanat kah neg amashoncheg en Babylone ketass8tamut, kah sekqshoncheg monacheg.
E.52.15 Then Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard carried away captive certain of the poor of the people, and the residue of the people that remained in the city, and those that fell away, that fell to the king of Babylon, and the rest of the multitude.

α.52.16 Qut Nebuzarradan askuhwhetae mugquomp sequnau machekinitcheh ut ne ohkeit, wanteunkeg weenominneash kah ohkehteaenuog.
E.52.16 But Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard left certain of the poor of the land for vinedressers and for husbandmen.

α.52.17 Wonk brasse pillarsash wonk nish ohtagish wekit Jehovah, kah basesash kah brasse keitoh, nish ohtagish wekit Jehovah Caldeansog sohquttahhamunaash kah monchadtoog wame brasse en Babylon.
E.52.17 Also the pillars of brass that were in the house of the LORD, and the bases, and the brasen sea that was in the house of the LORD, the Chaldeans brake, and carried all the brass of them to Babylon.

α.52.18 Cauldronsash wonk, kah shovelsash, kah snuffersash, kah wunnonkanash, kah kenamoog, kah brasse auwohteaongash, nish nashpe wowussumahetticheh, nash wunnemunnumunaoash.
E.52.18 The caldrons also, and the shovels, and the snuffers, and the bowls, and the spoons, and all the vessels of brass wherewith they ministered, took they away.

α.52.19 Kah bas[i]nsash, kah n8taeponsash kah wu[sin]onkanash kah cauldronsash, kah wequananteganuhtugquash, kah kenamog, kah cupsash, nish goldu8hish, ut goldut, nish silvereu8gish, ut silverut, askuhwheteae mugquomp wutamaunumussash. 
E.52.19 And the basons, and the firepans, and the bowls, and the caldrons, and the candlesticks, and the spoons, and the cups; that which was of gold in gold, and that which was of silver in silver, took the captain of the guard away.

α.52.20 Neenash pillersash, pasuk keitoh, nabo nees8og brasse bulsog, neg agwapehcheg basesut, nish ketass8t Solomon ayikupash ut wekit Jehovah, ne brasse ut wame yeu auwohteaonganit, matta quttuhwhosin8.
E.52.20 The two pillars, one sea, and twelve brasen bulls that were under the bases, which king Solomon had made in the house of the LORD: the brass of all these vessels was without weight.

α.52.21 Kah papaume pillarsash ne sohkunkqussit pasuk pillar nabo swosuk tashishquanogkut, kah pemuneat nabo neesihquanogog weenompósu, ne an8ke kishkag yauunash muttinwhunutcheash: puhpuhtiyeup.
E.52.21 And concerning the pillars, the height of one pillar was eighteen cubits; and a fillet of twelve cubits did compass it; and the thickness thereof was four fingers: it was hollow.

α.52.22 Brasse muhpuhkuk quenahtop nesohkunkquok pasuk muhpuhkuk napanna tashishquanogok, hashabanakausuonk, kah pomgranatsash quenohtopash muhpuhkukqut waeenu, wame wompohshag: kah nahohtoeu wonk pillar, & pomgranatsash, neyaneyeu8.
E.52.22 And a chapiter of brass was upon it; and the height of one chapiter was five cubits, with network and pomegranates upon the chapiters round about, all of brass. The second pillar also and the pomegranates were like unto these.

α.52.23 Kah pask8gun tahshinchagkodtash kah nequtta pomgranatsash sussippoeu, kah wame Pomgranatsash ut hashabpae anakausuongánit nequt pasuk88ash quinnuppu.
E.52.23 And there were ninety and six pomegranates on a side; and all the pomegranates upon the network were an hundred round about.

α.52.24 Kah askuhwhetae Mugquomp tohqunau Serajah kehche sephausuenuh, kah Zephaniah nahohtôeu sephausuen, kah nishuog nanawehteunkig ushsquont.
E.52.24 And the captain of the guard took Seraiah the chief priest, and Zephaniah the second priest, and the three keepers of the door:

α.52.25 Amaunau wonk wutch otanat Eunuch, noh nanawunont ayeuhteaenutcheh, kah nesausuk tahsuog neg kishkappehtauoncheg ketass8toh, neg namhetcheg ut keitotanat, kah kehche kenauwamee Scribe, maiyapheont ohkee missinninnuog, kah nequtta tahshinchagkodtog ohkee missinninnuog, neg namhetcheg ut nashaue otanat.
E.52.25 He took also out of the city an eunuch, which had the charge of the men of war; and seven men of them that were near the king's person, which were found in the city; and the principal scribe of the host, who mustered the people of the land; and threescore men of the people of the land, that were found in the midst of the city.

α.52.26 Neit Nebuzaradan askuhwheteae mugquomp nah wunneemunuh, kah nah uppas8uh ut Babylone ketass8tamwut ut Riblah.
E.52.26 So Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard took them, and brought them to the king of Babylon to Riblah.

α.52.27 Kah Bablyone ketass8t nah wutt[o]gkomuh, kah wunnush[u]h ut Riblah, ut Hamathe ohkeit, yeu unne Judah missinohkonuh wutch nehenwonche wutohkeit.
E.52.27 And the king of Babylon smote them, and put them to death in Riblah in the land of Hamath. Thus Judah was carried away captive out of his own land.

α.52.28 Yeug missinninnuog Nebuchadnezzar masinóhteapah ut nesausuk tahshe kodtum8ut, nishwudt muttannonganog kussuog Jewsog, kah neesneechagkodtog kah shuog.
E.52.28 This is the people whom Nebuchadrezzar carried away captive: in the seventh year three thousand Jews and three and twenty:

α.52.29 Nabo shwosuk wutteashe kodtum8mut Nebuchadnezzar, missinóhteauup wutch Jerusalem shwosuk tahshe pasuk88oh, shwinchagkodtoh kah neesuoh.
E.52.29 In the eighteenth year of Nebuchadrezzar he carried away captive from Jerusalem eight hundred thirty and two persons:

α.52.30 Neesneechage kah nishwe kodtum8mut[,] Nebuchadnezzar, Nebuzaradan askuhwheteae mugquomp missinóhteau Jewsoh, nesausuk tahshe pasuk88oh yauunchag, kah napanna tahsuoh, wame missinninnúog yauut muttannonganog kussuog kah nequtta tahshit pasuk88og.
E.52.30 In the three and twentieth year of Nebuchadrezzar Nebuzaradan the captain of the guard carried away captive of the Jews seven hundred forty and five persons: all the persons were four thousand and six hundred.

α.52.31 Kah n$nihyeup, shwinchage kah enatuh tahshe kodtum8 ummissinnoóonk Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, ut naboneese nepauzsaut, naboneesnechage kah napanna adtahshikquinok, Evil$merodach Babylone ketass8t, negonne kodtum8e nanawunnuadt, tahshinum uppuhkuk Jehojakim Judae ketass8t, kah wussohh8wunuh wutch kuppishagkinittuonganit.
E.52.31 And it came to pass in the seven and thirtieth year of the captivity of Jehoiachin king of Judah, in the twelfth month, in the five and twentieth day of the month, that Evilmerodach king of Babylon in the first year of his reign lifted up the head of Jehoiachin king of Judah, and brought him forth out of prison.

α.52.32 Kah 8womoausuont8wanumauoh, kah wut[á]nuwonkquottauoh wutappuonk, wuttappuongan8 ketass8tamwog, neh weetomukqutcheh ut Babylon.
E.52.32 And spake kindly unto him, and set his throne above the throne of the kings that were with him in Babylon,

α.52.33 Kah ôs8wunum ukkuppishagkinae hogk8ongash: kah nagwutteae meechwoh petukqununk ut anaquabit, nisohke pomantog.
E.52.33 And changed his prison garments: and he did continually eat bread before him all the days of his life.

α.52.34 Kah wutch ummeetsuonk, nagwutteae wutchippiyeum aninnumauau nashpe Babylone ketass8t, pajeh kesukodte wunnupp8onganit, tohsohkepomantog.
E.52.34 And for his diet, there was a continual diet given him of the king of Babylon, every day a portion until the day of his death, all the days of his life.
